# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Phase separation seeded by Z2 and U(1) topological defects from holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00163)
*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Zhang-Yu Nie,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过全息对偶（holography）中的双淬火协议（double-quench protocol），研究了自发对称破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）与相分离动力学（phase separation dynamics）之间的相互作用，发现拓扑缺陷（topological defects）能够作为相分离的普适动力学种子，且在Z₂和U(1)对称系统中表现出相同的普适动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自发对称破缺过程中产生的拓扑缺陷如何影响后续的相分离动力学，以及这种影响是否具有普适性。

Method: 采用全息对偶框架，设计双淬火协议：第一次快速穿过临界点（critical point）以生成拓扑缺陷，第二次将系统驱动至非线性不稳定区引发旋节分解（spinodal decomposition）。分别研究Z₂对称和U(1)对称两类系统。

Result: 拓扑缺陷动态决定了相分离的成核位置（nucleation sites）；随着不稳定性增长，缺陷核（defect cores）膨胀为宏观尺度的相分离畴（phase-separated domains）。尽管Z₂和U(1)体系的对称性与拓扑性质不同，两者表现出相同的普适动力学行为。

Conclusion: 拓扑缺陷可以作为后续相分离的普适动力学种子（dynamical seeds），其影响不依赖于具体的对称性类型，揭示了一种非平衡态下的普适动力学机制。

Abstract: We study the interaction between spontaneous symmetry breaking and phase separation dynamics in holography. Using a double-quench protocol, the system first rapidly crosses the critical point and generates topological defects, while a second quench drives the system into a nonlinear unstable regime with spinodal decomposition. We investigate both $\mathbb{Z}_2$ and $U(1)$ symmetric systems, where different types of topological defects emerge during symmetry breaking. We show that topological defects dynamically determine the nucleation sites of phase separation. As the instability grows, the defect cores expand into macroscopic phase-separated domains. Despite the distinct symmetries and topological properties of these defects, both systems exhibit the same universal dynamical behavior, indicating that topological defects can universally serve as dynamical seeds for subsequent phase separation.

</details>


### [2] [Constraints on four-party entanglement in holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00210)
*Vijay Balasubramanian,William K. L. Chan,Monica Jinwoo Kang,Chitraang Murdia,Simon F. Ross*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 在纯时间反演对称的全息（holographic）态中，所有已知的四体纠缠信号均以三重信息$I_3$非零为必要条件。$I_3$是四体纠缠存在的最强已知信号，并定量限制所有基于多熵（multi-entropy）构建的四体纠缠信号，但残余熵$Q_4$不受$I_3$限制，尽管$I_3=0$时$Q_4$也为零（除测度为零的奇异集外）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨全息态（holographic states）中四体纠缠信号之间的层次关系，尤其是三重信息$I_3$在探测和约束四体纠缠中的角色。

Method: 在全息框架中，分析纯时间反演对称态下已知四体纠缠信号的行为，并比较$I_3$与其他信号（如多熵构造和残余熵$Q_4$）之间的约束关系。

Result: $I_3$非零是所有已知四体纠缠信号存在的必要条件；$I_3$定量限制所有基于多熵的四体纠缠信号；$I_3=0$蕴含$Q_4=0$，但反之不成立，$I_3$不限制$Q_4$的大小。

Conclusion: $I_3$是目前已知最强、最基础的四体纠缠信号；残余熵$Q_4$独立于$I_3$之外提供互补信息。

Abstract: We show that in pure time-reflection-symmetric holographic states all known four-party entanglement signals vanish unless the triple information $I_3$ is non-zero. In this sense, our results show that $I_3$ is the strongest known signal of the presence of quadripartite entanglement. Additionally, $I_3$ quantitatively bounds all four-party entanglement signals built from the multi-entropy. However, the residual entropy $Q_4$, also a measure of four-party entanglement, is not bounded by $I_3$, although $I_3=0$ does imply $Q_4=0$ for holographic states (except on a set of measure zero for which $Q_4$ is ill-defined).

</details>


### [3] [Dynamical Sauter-Schwinger pair creation process from Feynman perspective: Comparison of boundary- and initial-value approaches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00236)
*J. Z. Kamiński,A. Bechler,M. M. Majczak,K. Krajewska*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过两种方法研究动态Sauter-Schwinger对产生过程：一是基于费曼正电子诠释与量子电动力学时空描述的边界条件方法，二是基于狄拉克方程标准化初始条件的初值方法。两种方法在自旋求和动量分布上近似一致，但自旋分辨分布存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电磁背景场下真空中动态Sauter-Schwinger对产生（dynamical Sauter-Schwinger pair creation）过程的严格理论描述，并比较两种不同方法的等价性与差异。

Method: 第一种方法基于费曼（Feynman）正电子诠释与量子电动力学（Quantum Electrodynamics, QED）时空描述，将自旋与动量概率幅表达为关于背景场的无穷Born级数，并通过求解具有费曼或反费曼边界条件的狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）来精确求和该级数。第二种方法则通过具有归一化初始（或终末）条件的狄拉克方程求解，该方法源于将费曼传播子替换为推迟（或超前）传播子的修改版费曼时空方法。

Result: 两种方法在自旋求和（spin summed up）动量分布上几乎一致但并非完全等同；然而在自旋或螺旋度分辨（spin- or helicity-resolved）的动量分布上，二者表现出显著差异。数值结果基于均匀电场脉冲（homogeneous electric field pulse）展示。

Conclusion: 费曼边界条件方法等价于散射矩阵理论（scattering matrix theory）并与世界线形式（worldline formalism）一致；初值方法则对应于狄拉克海（Dirac sea）诠释。两种方法在自旋求和层面近似等价，但在自旋分辨层面存在本质差异，需谨慎选择适用方法。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical Sauter-Schwinger pair creation process from the vacuum by an electromagnetic background field using two alternative approaches. The first one is based on the Feynman interpretation of positrons and the space-time description of Quantum Electrodynamics, which leads to the spin and momentum probability amplitudes expressed as the infinite Born series with respect to the background field. We demonstrate that in order to sum up this series exactly, the problem can be reduced to solving the Dirac equation with uniquely defined Feynman or anti-Feynman boundary conditions. The use of these boundary conditions leads to the results that are equivalent to the scattering matrix theory and consistent with the worldline formalism. Alternative way of investigating the dynamical Sauter-Schwinger process consists in solving the Dirac equation with normalized initial (final) conditions. It is shown that this method follows from the suitably modified Feynman space-time approach, in which the Feynman propagators are replaced by the retarded (advanced) propagators. By doing so it is implicitly assumed that negative energy solutions describe electrons filling the Dirac sea (i.e., representing the Dirac vacuum) and the process of pair creation consists in the excitation of these electrons to the positive energy states. For both the boundary- and initial-value approaches the helicity-entangled momentum distributions are discussed and compared. Predictions of the two approaches are illustrated numerically for the homogeneous electric field pulse and for parameters such that for the spin summed up distributions both methods lead to nearly the same, although not identical, results. It is shown that even in such cases the spin- or helicity-resolved momentum distributions exhibit significant differences.

</details>


### [4] [Casimir effect near spontaneously Lorentz-breaking magnetic vacua in Plebański nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00361)
*C. A. Escobar,Román Linares,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性电动力学中磁真空态附近电磁涨落的Casimir响应。在Plebański一阶表示下，通过分析磁分支中对称性破缺条件$S_m(P)=0$的退化行为，计算了平行板Casimir能量。结果显示，当背景场趋近精确的Lorentz破缺真空时，奇异分支发散，但该发散并非真实物理预言，而是正则量子化与约束条件先后顺序不可交换的诊断标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究规范不变非线性电动力学中，磁真空态自发破缺Lorentz对称性时的Casimir效应；探究在接近或处于对称性破缺真空时，电磁涨落的物理行为是否出现发散及其物理意义。

Method: 采用Plebański一阶表示形式（Plebański first-order representation），以单不变Hamiltonian势$\widehat V(P)$为基础；通过$S_m(P) \equiv \widehat V_P(P)+2P\widehat V_{PP}(P)$控制磁分支的对称性破缺条件；在正则磁背景$\bar P$（$S_m(\bar P)\neq0$）附近线性化，得到普通Maxwell分支和受$\alpha(\bar P)$控制的各向异性奇异分支；计算垂直和平行于板面的两种平行板构型下的正规化Casimir能量。

Result: 正则背景趋近精确Lorentz破缺真空$P_\star$（$S_m(P_\star)=0$）时，奇异分支变得奇异；在平行板平行于背景场构型中，Casimir能量在正则描述下发散。但在退化曲面上的直接分析表明，奇异分支对一般动量并非独立的物理传播模式；该发散并非精确Lorentz破缺态下无限真空能量的预言，而是先正则量子化后施加约束条件与先施加约束后量子化之间非对易性的诊断标志。

Conclusion: 磁真空态Lorentz对称性破缺附近电磁涨落的Casimir能量发散，反映的是量子化顺序的非对易性（noncommutativity），而非真实的物理发散。该工作为理解非线性电动力学中对称性破缺真空的量子涨落提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study the Casimir response of electromagnetic fluctuations near magnetic vacua that spontaneously break Lorentz symmetry in gauge-invariant nonlinear electrodynamics. The theory is formulated in the Plebański first-order representation, with a single-invariant Hamiltonian potential $\widehat V(P)$ taken as the fundamental nonlinear object. This formulation is particularly useful because the nontrivial vacua are obtained as stationary points of the effective Hamiltonian, rather than as extrema of $\widehat V(P)$ itself. In the magnetic branch, the symmetry-breaking condition is governed by $S_m(P) \equiv \widehat V_P(P)+2P\widehat V_{PP}(P)$, whose vanishing also signals the degeneracy of the Hamiltonian constraint structure and the loss of rank of the longitudinal magnetic response. We first linearize around a regular purely magnetic background $\bar P$, with $S_m(\bar P)\neq0$, and obtain an ordinary Maxwell-like branch together with an extraordinary anisotropic branch controlled by $α(\bar P)=\widehat V_P(\bar P)/S_m(\bar P)$. We then compute the regularized parallel-plate Casimir energy for magnetic backgrounds perpendicular and parallel to the plates. As the regular background approaches the exact Lorentz-breaking vacuum $P_\star$, where $S_m(P_\star)=0$, the extraordinary branch becomes singular and, in the parallel configuration, the Casimir energy diverges within the regular-sector description. A direct analysis on the degenerate surface shows, however, that the extraordinary branch does not survive as an independent physical propagating mode for generic momenta. The divergence is therefore not a prediction of an infinite vacuum energy at the exact Lorentz-breaking state, but a diagnostic of the noncommutativity between quantizing the regular theory and imposing $S_m(P_\star)=0$ before quantization.

</details>


### [5] [Massless Islands in Wedge Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00488)
*Naman Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无鬼影（ghost-free）、无DGP项的机制，通过在楔形全息（wedge holography）的余维二角落引入局域化的幺正缺陷共形场论（unitary defect conformal field theory），使无质量引力子（massless graviton）理论中也能出现非视界（non-horizon）的纠缠岛（entanglement island）鞍点，从而证明阻碍无质量岛出现的并非质量为零本身，而是缺乏额外的健康熵项来平衡极值面（extremal surface）趋于视界的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在楔形全息（wedge holography）中，双膜上的诺伊曼边界条件（Neumann boundary conditions）会产生可归一化的无质量引力子（massless graviton），但纯几何Ryu-Takayanagi问题的岛鞍点（island saddle）会坍缩到视界（horizon）；负DGP项虽能恢复非平凡岛，却会引入有质量鬼影（massive ghost）。因此，亟需一种无鬼影、健康的机制，在无质量引力理论中实现非视界岛鞍点。

Method: 保持楔形引力作用量（wedge gravitational action）不含DGP项，在余维二角落添加一个局域化的幺正缺陷共形场论（unitary defect conformal field theory）。该缺陷扇区的熵贡献到广义熵（generalized entropy）中；若缺陷理论是全息的，其熵由辅助的体Ryu-Takayanagi曲面计算。通过调整楔形端点位置来确定缺陷的纠缠区域（entangling region），使辅助面积与楔形面积呈现相反的变化趋势，同时保持所有耦合常数和中心荷（central charges）为正。

Result: 局域端点模型（local endpoint model）展示出一个孤立的稳定鞍点（isolated stable saddle），且后期占据主导地位，优于Hartman-Maldacena曲面。量子极值性条件（quantum extremality condition）取代纯正交性条件（pure orthogonality condition），在长程、无质量、无鬼影的引力理论中实现了一个非视界岛鞍点。

Conclusion: 阻碍最小楔形全息（minimal wedge holography）中出现无质量岛的并非无质量引力子本身，而是缺少一项能够平衡面积趋于视界变化的额外健康熵项。本文提出的缺陷共形场论机制提供了一种可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Entanglement islands are usually easiest to realize in doubly holographic models with massive gravitons or non-gravitating baths. In wedge holography, by contrast, Neumann boundary conditions on both branes give a normalizable massless graviton, but the island saddle of the purely geometric Ryu-Takayanagi problem collapses to the horizon. Negative Dvali-Gabadadze-Porrati (DGP) terms can restore nontrivial islands by changing the endpoint condition of the extremal surface, but this branch contains a massive ghost. We propose a different, manifestly healthy mechanism. We keep the wedge gravitational action free of DGP terms and add a unitary defect conformal field theory localized at the codimension-two corner. This sector is distinct from the standard corner CFT dual to the undeformed wedge, whose entropy is already represented by the wedge RT area; hence no double counting is involved. The entropy of this additional defect sector contributes to the generalized entropy. If the defect theory is holographic, this entropy is computed by an auxiliary bulk Ryu-Takayanagi surface. We show that when the wedge endpoint position determines the defect entangling region, the auxiliary area can have the opposite variation to the wedge area while all couplings and central charges remain positive. A local endpoint model exhibits an isolated stable saddle and its late-time dominance over the Hartman-Maldacena surface. The quantum extremality condition then replaces the pure orthogonality condition and allows a non-horizon island saddle in a long-range, massless, ghost-free gravitational theory. This demonstrates that the obstruction to massless islands in minimal wedge holography is not masslessness itself, but the absence of an additional healthy entropy term capable of balancing the horizon-minimizing area variation.

</details>


### [6] [The Triple $T\bar{T}$-Like Flow in Quantum Field Theories: Irrelevant, Marginal, and Relevant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00536)
*H. Babaei-Aghbolagh,Bin Chen,Song He,Jue Hou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文引入了一类单参数根-$T\bar T$型流（root-$T\bar T$-like flow），通过参数$α$将应力张量形变（stress-tensor deformation）组织为无关（irrelevant）、边缘（marginal）和相关（relevant）三个分支，并在对偶不变电动力（duality-invariant electrodynamics）与二维可积西格玛模型（integrable sigma model）中给出了闭合形式的解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于$T\bar T$形变的研究缺乏一个统一的理论框架来涵盖不同能标相关性的形变类型，尤其是那些不同于标准Born-Infeld型$T\bar T$流的形变。

Method: 构造了一个单参数流方程$\partial_λ\mathcal{L}=\mathcal{R}_λ^{1/α}$，其中$α$为可控参数；在四维对偶不变电动力学和二维可积西格玛模型中，该流可通过辅助方程（auxiliary equation）得到闭合形式的解。

Result: $α=1$时恢复根-$T\bar T$ / ModMax分支（边缘形变）；$α<1$时产生不同于标准Born-Infeld $T\bar T$流的无关形变；$α>1$时给出显式的相关$T\bar T$型拉格朗日量。

Conclusion: 根-$T\bar T$流为对偶不变形变与可积形变提供了一种统一的组织原则（organizing principle）。

Abstract: We introduce a one-parameter root-$T\bar T$-like flow, $ \partial_λ\mathcal{L}=\mathcal{R}_λ^{1/α}$, which organizes stress-tensor deformations into irrelevant, marginal, and relevant branches. Within duality-invariant electrodynamics in four dimensions, and equivalently within two-dimensional integrable sigma models, the flow admits a closed-form solution controlled by an auxiliary equation. The marginal point $α=1$ reproduces the root-$T\bar T$ / ModMax branch, while $α<1$ gives irrelevant deformations distinct from the standard Born-Infeld $T\bar T$ flow. For $α>1$, the same construction yields explicit relevant $T\bar T$-like Lagrangians. These results suggest that root-$T\bar T$ flows provide a common organizing principle for duality-invariant and integrable deformations.

</details>


### [7] [Spacetime torsion signatures in neutrino oscillation physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00617)
*Capolupo Antonio,Monda Simone,Pisacane Gabriele,Quaranta Aniello,Serao Raoul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文报告了在爱因斯坦-卡特理论（Einstein-Cartan theory）背景下，存在背景挠率（torsion）时中微子振荡（neutrino oscillation）的最新结果。针对恒定挠率和线性时间依赖挠率两种情形，推导了新的振荡公式，且这些公式依赖于自旋方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）中背景挠率场对中微子振荡的影响，以扩展标准量子场论框架下的中微子物理研究。

Method: 基于爱因斯坦-卡特理论，将背景挠率项引入中微子传播的拉格朗日量，求解了恒定挠率和线性时间依赖挠率两种情况下的中微子振荡方程，并分析了自旋取向对振荡概率的影响。

Result: 得到了依赖于自旋方向的、适用于恒定挠率和线性时间依赖挠率的新中微子振荡公式。

Conclusion: 背景挠率能够调制中微子振荡行为，振荡公式中的自旋依赖性可能为检验广义相对论（general relativity）的非黎曼拓展提供可观测信号。

Abstract: We report on recent results concerning neutrino oscillation in the presence of background torsion. In the context of Einstein-Cartan theory, we find new oscillation formulas for constant torsion and linearly time-dependent torsion. The oscillation formulas obtained depend on the orientation of the spin.

</details>


### [8] [Gauge Theory of Gravity and the AdS/CFT Correspondence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00929)
*Takeshi Fukuyama*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从引力作为规范对称性破缺相的角度审视AdS/CFT对偶，系统分析了AdS₂/CFT₁、AdS₄/CFT₃及AdS₅/CFT₄情形，揭示了Schwarzian导数、Cotton张量等边界共形不变量与体区几何结构之间的内在联系，提出了全息对偶性的统一几何诠释：边界作为破缺共形规范对称性的残余结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者试图从引力作为共形规范对称性（conformal gauge symmetry）破缺相的视角来重新理解AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）的几何本质，澄清不同维度下体区（bulk）与边界（boundary）之间对称性结构的对应关系，并探讨四维共形规范框架的适用边界。

Method: 研究者采用规范理论表述引力的方法，将引力视为破缺的共形规范对称性。在AdS₂/CFT₁中，通过边界外在曲率（extrinsic curvature）导出Schwarzian导数（Schwarzian derivative），并阐明Liouville几何（Liouville geometry）与边界射影结构（projective structure）的关系。在AdS₄/CFT₃中，从共形规范对称性破缺推导出含宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的Einstein–Hilbert作用量及全导数项，进而论证该结构诱导边界引力Chern–Simons项（gravitational Chern–Simons term），其变分自然给出Cotton张量（Cotton tensor）。

Result: 在AdS₂/CFT₁中，Schwarzian导数被识别为边界外在曲率的自然产物；体区共形规范代数（conformal gauge algebra）无中心扩张（central extension），而边界Virasoro结构（Virasoro structure）具有非零中心荷（central charge）。在AdS₄/CFT₃中，Cotton张量被解释为残余边界共形几何（residual boundary conformal geometry）的基本共形不变量（conformal invariant），其角色类似于AdS₂/CFT₁中的Schwarzian导数。AdS₅/CFT₄则可能超出四维共形规范框架，需要更高维的弦论启发结构（string-inspired structures）。

Conclusion: 本文提出全息对偶性可被统一理解为破缺共形规范对称性的边界残余（boundary remnants），为引力与共形场论之间的几何对应提供了新的理论视角，同时指出不同维度AdS/CFT对偶在对称性破缺框架下的定性差异。

Abstract: We discuss the AdS/CFT correspondence from the viewpoint of the gauge-theoretic formulation of gravity, in which gravity is interpreted as a broken phase of conformal gauge symmetry.
  In the AdS$_2$/CFT$_1$ case, we show that the Schwarzian derivative naturally emerges from the boundary extrinsic curvature of AdS$_2$ geometry. The relation between the bulk Liouville geometry and the boundary projective structure is clarified. We further discuss the distinction between the bulk conformal gauge algebra with vanishing central extension and the emergent boundary Virasoro structure with nonvanishing central charge.
  We then investigate the possible structure of the AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$ correspondence, which is directly related to the original four-dimensional formulation of gravity as a broken phase of conformal gauge symmetry. In this framework, the Einstein--Hilbert action with cosmological constant emerges together with a total derivative term. We argue that this structure induces the boundary gravitational Chern--Simons term, whose variation leads naturally to the Cotton tensor. The Cotton tensor is interpreted as the fundamental conformal invariant associated with the residual boundary conformal geometry, playing a role analogous to that of the Schwarzian derivative in AdS$_2$/CFT$_1$.
  We also discuss the qualitative difference between AdS$_4$/CFT$_3$ and AdS$_5$/CFT$_4$. While the former appears naturally connected with gravity arising from conformal symmetry breaking, the latter may require genuinely higher-dimensional, string-inspired structures beyond the four-dimensional conformal gauge framework. These observations suggest a unified geometrical interpretation of holography in terms of boundary remnants of broken conformal gauge symmetry.

</details>


### [9] [Black holes with quantum corrections in $3d$: The case of Page curve in Lindblad, greybody factor, and Lyapunov exponent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01025)
*Mahdis Ghodrati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文首先将含量子修正的黑洞视为开放量子系统，利用Lindblad形式论解释霍金-佩奇曲线与辐射过程中的“锯齿”行为（特别考虑异常点效应）；随后计算三维Cotler-Jensen理论（即带有重参量化模的AdS₃）中各参数的量子修正，并与Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）理论结果进行对比；接着计算多种黑洞解（尤其是Cotler-Jensen理论）的量子修正灰体因子；最后研究量子修正对黑洞Lyapunov指数、势函数及量子信息结构的影响。

Result: 描述了利用Lindblad形式论及异常点效应解释霍金-佩奇曲线“锯齿”行为的机制；给出了Cotler-Jensen理论中各参数的量子修正结果，并与JT理论进行了系统性对比；获得了多种黑洞解（特别是Cotler-Jensen理论情形）的量子修正灰体因子；得到了量子修正对Lyapunov指数、势函数及黑洞量子信息结构的影响结果。

Conclusion: 开放量子系统框架（Lindblad形式论）及异常点效应能够有效解释霍金-佩奇曲线中的“锯齿”行为；Cotler-Jensen理论在量子修正下与JT理论存在可对比的结构；量子修正显著影响黑洞的灰体因子、混沌特性（Lyapunov指数）和信息结构，为从量子层面理解黑洞信息悖论提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: In this work, first we discuss black holes with quantum corrections as an open quantum system and apply Lindblad formalism to explain the ``zig-zag" behavior in the Hawking- Page curve and radiation process, specially by considering the effects of exceptional points. Then, we calculate quantum corrections for various parameters of $3d$ Cotler-Jensen theory which is $\text{AdS}_3$ with reparametrized modes. At each step of the calculations, we compare the results with the case of JT. We then calculate quantum-corrected greybody factor for various black hole solutions, and specially for the case of Cotler-Jensen theory. Finally, we study the effects of quantum corrections on Lyapunov exponent, potential, and quantum information structure of black holes.

### [10] [Modular theory and affine representations on the Rindler horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01071)
*Michele Arzano,Paolo Palumbo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于光射线上的仿射对称性（affine symmetry）建立 Unruh 效应的群论解释，并将其与模理论（modular theory）联系起来。对于二维时空中的无质量标量场，惯性观测者和均匀加速观测者分别选择同一手征单粒子结构中的零平移（null translations）与膨胀（dilations）两种不同的流动，Minkowski 模和 Rindler 模分别适应这两种流动，而 Mellin 变换是两者之间的天然桥梁。模理论提供了相应的算子代数解释：在视界上，半线代数的模流由膨胀实现，受限真空满足 KMS 条件，因此仿射群可视为 Rindler 视界上热性背后的最小对称性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为 Unruh 效应寻找更深层的对称性基础，利用仿射群（affine group）解释加速观测者所感受到的热态，并将其与模理论中的算子代数框架统一起来。

Method: 采用群论方法分析惯性系与加速系中场的对称性选择：惯性观测者对应光射线上的零平移，均匀加速观测者对应膨胀；利用 Mellin 变换在 Minkowski 模和 Rindler 模之间建立联系；通过模理论分析半线代数的模流、受限真空的 KMS 条件，以及正频扇区内的非酉性。

Result: 发现 Minkowski 正频模限制到单个 Rindler 楔（Rindler wedge）后，与 Rindler 模在正频扇区内的比较是非酉的；模理论表明 Rindler 视界上的模流由膨胀实现，受限真空满足 KMS 条件；仿射群被确认为 Rindler 视界上热性所需的最小对称性结构。

Conclusion: 仿射群提供了 Rindler 视界上热效应的最小对称性解释，统一了 Unruh 效应中惯性系与加速系之间的对称性选择，并给出了相应的算子代数刻画。

Abstract: We develop a group-theoretic interpretation of the Unruh effect based on affine symmetry on a light ray and relate it to modular theory. For a massless scalar field in two spacetime dimensions inertial and uniformly accelerated observers select two different flows within the same chiral one-particle structure, respectively, null translations and dilations. Minkowski modes are adapted to translations, while Rindler modes are adapted to dilations, with the Mellin transform providing the natural bridge between them. When a Minkowski positive-frequency mode is restricted to a single Rindler wedge, its comparison with Rindler modes is non-unitary within the positive-frequency sector. Modular theory gives the corresponding operator-algebraic interpretation: on the horizon the modular flow of the half-line algebra is implemented by dilations, and the restricted vacuum satisfies the KMS condition. The affine group thus appears as the minimal symmetry structure underlying thermality on the Rindler horizon.

### [11] [Self-gravitating quantum stars with a globally relevant Bohm potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01103)
*Ilidio Lopes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于轨道自由密度泛函框架，推导了自旋1/2暗扇区费米子双组分薛定谔-泊松-汤川（Schrödinger-Poisson-Yukawa）体系，发现玻姆势（Bohm potential）贡献类核液滴模型的物种依赖表面能修正，并给出了可预测的质量-半径关系，为约束多组分暗扇区中的暗费米子质量提供了第一性原理参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非重子暗物质（non-baryonic dark matter）的微观物理机制仍然未知（unknown），本文旨在通过第一性原理推导建立可检验的理论框架。

Method: 在轨道自由密度泛函（orbital-free density-functional）框架下，采用Kirzhnits梯度系数λ_B=1/9，推导了通过标量中介子（scalar mediator）φ（质量m_φ）经通用汤川耦合（universal Yukawa coupling）连接的自旋1/2暗扇区费米子场ψ（质量m_1）和χ（质量m_2）的双组分薛定谔-泊松-汤川方程组。

Result: 玻姆势在托马斯-费米（Thomas-Fermi）机制下不可忽略，贡献了类似核液滴模型（nuclear liquid-drop model）的物种依赖表面能修正；单物种薛定谔-泊松极限下基态恢复基准不变量M_dim≈3.883和x_T≈2.562；多方指数γ=5/3时质量-半径关系满足R∝M^{-1/3}，γ=4/3时出现极限质量；构型覆盖质量M=10^{-8}-5 M_⊙、质量m_1∼10^{-14}-10^{-6} eV、半径从几km至∼10^3 R_⊙，引力波接触频率落入爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）和LISA频段。

Conclusion: 所得质量-半径关系具有预测刚性（predictive rigidity），单微观参数m_1即可在总质量给定后确定平衡半径，为约束多组分暗扇区中的暗费米子质量提供了可重复的第一性原理参考。

Abstract: The microphysics underlying non-baryonic dark matter remains unknown. I derive the two-species Schrödinger-Poisson-Yukawa system for spin-1/2 dark-sector fermion fields, $ψ$ (mass $m_1$) and $χ$ (mass $m_2$), coupled through a scalar mediator of mass $m_φ$ via a universal Yukawa coupling, within an orbital-free density-functional framework with the Kirzhnits gradient coefficient $λ_B=1/9$. A central result is that the Bohm potential, far from being negligible in the Thomas-Fermi regime, contributes a species-dependent surface-energy correction analogous to the nuclear liquid-drop model: the heavier fermion species generates an outward quantum-pressure wall whilst the lighter species provides an inward surface tension, with degeneracy pressure furnishing the bulk confinement. In the single-species Schrödinger-Poisson limit the ground state recovers the benchmarked invariants $M_{\mathrm{dim}}\simeq 3.883$ and $x_T\simeq 2.562$, yielding $M R_T\simeq 9.95\,λ_B\hbar^2/(G m_1^2)$. For polytropic index $γ=5/3$ the mass-radius relation satisfies $R\propto M^{-1/3}$; for $γ=4/3$ a limiting mass emerges above which no stable equilibrium exists. Illustrative configurations span $M=10^{-8}$-$5\, M_\odot$, $m_1\sim 10^{-14}$-$10^{-6}\, eV$, and radii from a few~km to $\sim 10^3\, R_\odot$, with gravitational-wave contact frequencies in the Einstein Telescope and LISA bands and microlensing signatures accessible to current surveys. The predictive rigidity of the resulting mass-radius relation, in which the single microphysical parameter $m_1$ determines the equilibrium radius once the total mass is specified, furnishes a reproducible, first-principles reference for constraining the dark-fermion mass in multi-component dark sectors.

### [12] [One-loop divergences for KK theories on $\mathrm{AdS}\times S$ spaces; a reanalysis of $\mathrm{AdS}_4 \times S^7$ /ABJM precision holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01167)
*Federico Arrighi,Lorenzo Casarin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个系统框架，用于计算任意维度乘积空间 $\mathrm{AdS}_{d_A} \times S^{d_S}$ 上单圈配分函数（one-loop partition function）的对数发散部分。通过球谐展开将高维动力学算子约化为无穷多个 AdS 行列式，并利用谱 $\zeta$ 函数（spectral $\zeta$-function）方法表示。将该框架应用于 11 维超引力（11-dimensional supergravity）在 $\mathrm{AdS}_4 \times S^7$ 上的完整多重态，恢复了已知的 $\frac{1}{4}\log N$ 修正结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为任意维度乘积空间 $\mathrm{AdS}_{d_A} \times S^{d_S}$ 上的单圈配分函数计算提供系统化方法，以便处理 AdS 行列式与无穷 KK 求和（Kaluza-Klein sum）之间相互作用所产生的对数发散。

Method: 将高维动力学算子（kinetic operators）在球谐函数（spherical harmonics）中展开，将 $(d_A+d_S)$ 维谱问题约化为无穷多个 $d_A$ 维行列式（determinants），并使用谱 $\zeta$ 函数方法表示这些行列式。在计算中仔细处理球面上零模（zero modes）产生的额外 AdS 行列式贡献。

Result: 在 $\mathrm{AdS}_4 \times S^7$ 上的 11 维超引力完整多重态中，唯一的非零对数发散完全来源于鬼扇区（ghost sector）中的 2-形式 AdS 模（2-form AdS mode），重现了超对称局域化（supersymmetric localization）预言的 ABJM 自由能 $\frac{1}{4}\log N$ 修正。

Conclusion: 该框架可推广至其他 AdS/CFT 对偶中的对数发散计算，为高维乘积空间中的量子引力修正分析提供系统工具。

Abstract: We provide a systematic framework for computing the logarithmically divergent part of one-loop partition functions on product spaces $\mathrm{AdS}_{d_A} \times S^{d_S}$ of arbitrary dimension. By expanding the higher-dimensional kinetic operators in spherical harmonics, we reduce the ($d_A+d_S$)-dimensional spectral problem to an infinite tower of $d_A$-dimensional determinants, which are then represented via spectral $ζ$-function methods. We isolate the logarithmic divergences arising from the interplay between the individual AdS determinants and the infinite Kaluza-Klein sum, carefully accounting for the contributions of zero modes on the sphere that produce additional AdS determinants. We test this framework on different fields and apply it to the complete multiplet of 11-dimensional supergravity on $\mathrm{AdS}_4 \times S^7$. We recover in a 4d language the result of arXiv:1210.6057, namely that the only non-vanishing logarithmic divergence originates entirely from the 2-form AdS mode in the ghost sector, reproducing the well-known $\frac{1}{4}\log N$ correction to the ABJM free energy predicted by supersymmetric localization.

### [13] [Notes on Wasserstein distance and wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01296)
*Ville Keranen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出玻尔兹曼-瓦瑟斯坦（Boltzmann–Wasserstein, BW）距离，一种依赖温度的量子理论空间度量，定义为玻尔兹曼加权能量谱之间的最优 W₂ 距离，并建立了它与黑洞面积差、热两/四点函数之间的解析关系，同时通过 Schwinger–Keldysh 虫洞（wormhole）构造给出了经典与量子修正的引力对偶解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子理论与引力对偶（gauge/gravity duality）的框架下，需要一种能同时捕捉能谱重排（spectral rearrangement）和本征态量子修正的度量，以刻画不同量子理论之间的"距离"，从而探索时空几何与量子信息结构之间的深层联系。

Method: 定义 BW 距离为玻尔兹曼加权能量谱间的 2-瓦瑟斯坦（Wasserstein-2, W₂）最优传输距离。对于熵位移微小变化的半经典理论，利用归一化 BW 距离推导出平方视界面积比较器（horizon-area comparator）公式；对于哈密顿量差为算子 V 的情形，通过时间平均得到热两/四点关联函数表达式；两种情形均通过 Schwinger–Keldysh 虫洞构造给出引力对偶。

Result: 归一化 BW 距离在熵位移微小变化时退化为平方视界面积比较器，与温度下黑洞面积差 δA/4G 的平方成正比；当哈密顿量差为算子 V 时，BW 距离等于 V 的时间平均热两点函数（thermal two-point function）；若该函数因共形不变性（conformal invariance）为零（主扰动情形），次阶贡献由四点函数给出。经典虫洞描述光谱重排，而两点函数公式捕获对扰动的本征向量敏感的真正量子修正。

Conclusion: BW 距离为量子理论空间提供了统一的度量框架，其引力对偶区分了经典几何信息（能谱重排）与量子信息（本征向量修正），两个具体例子（不同宇宙学常数的两个 BTZ 黑洞和 BTZ 的 T\bar{T} 形变）验证了公式的有效性。

Abstract: We develop the Boltzmann--Wasserstein (BW) distance, a temperature-dependent metric on the space of quantum theories defined as the optimal $W_2$ distance between Boltzmann-weighted energy spectra. For semiclassical theories differing by a small entropy shift, the normalised BW distance collapses to a squared horizon-area comparator, $\tilde{\mathcal{W}}^2 \approx (δA/4G)^2/8$, with the two areas evaluated at equal energy. When the Hamiltonians of the theories differ by an operator $V$, then the BW distance equals a time-averaged thermal two-point function of $V$; for primary perturbations where this vanishes by conformal invariance, a four-point representation appears at the next order. Both formulas arise from a similar gravitational picture but capture complementary content. The Schwinger--Keldysh wormhole that determines $C_{\max}$ -- two Euclidean caps sharing a single horizon, joined by a Lorentzian segment that adiabatically interpolates between the two theories -- sees only the rearrangement of the spectrum. The perturbative two-point formula computes the genuinely quantum correction sensitive to the eigenvectors of the perturbation, invisible to the classical gravity saddle. The Lorentzian part of the wormhole is essential for the construction. We work out two examples -- two BTZ black holes with different cosmological constants and a $T\bar{T}$ deformation of BTZ.

</details>


### [14] [Pseudo-Gauge Stabilizers and Fibration Structure of the Cooper--Frye Map at Freeze-Out](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01429)
*Jiahua Tian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过研究相对论自旋流体力学（relativistic spin hydrodynamics）中冻结态（freeze-out）的赝规范变换（pseudo-gauge transformation, PGT）自由性，建立了Cooper-Frye映射的纤维丛结构，将可观测量分为底空间（base）和纤维（fiber）两类，并应用于重离子极化数据，解释了Λ极化与φ-介子自旋排列之间的张力，表明涡度主导响应扇区可能需要通过局域场关联数据加以扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在相对论自旋流体力学中，冻结态的赝规范变换自由度（pseudo-gauge transformation freedom）尚未得到系统的数学结构分析与观测分类。作者旨在建立这一自由度的严格几何框架，并阐明其如何限制可观测量数量及导出交叉一致性关系，进而为重离子极化实验中的测量矛盾提供结构层面的解释。

Method: 作者证明Cooper-Frye映射可以通过冻结态数据模去一个泛在稳定化子（universal stabilizer）的商空间进行因子化，从而在热力学拉格朗日乘子（thermodynamic Lagrange multipliers）空间上诱导出一个分层纤维化结构（stratified fibration）。利用该纤维丛分类，可观测量被区分为底空间类型（base type）和纤维类型（fiber type），并推导出PGT敏感可观测量的数量上限由族受限纤维维数（family-restricted fiber dimension）界定，以及交叉可观测量一致性关系。

Result: 该纤维丛结构为Λ极化与φ-介子自旋排列之间的张力提供了一个结构性解释：表明涡度主导的响应扇区（vorticity-dominated response sector）可能需要通过局部场关联数据加以扩充。此外，近期由Weyl反常诱导的流（Weyl-anomaly-induced currents）被分类为底空间可观测量；从稳定化子条件可恢复已知的Belinfante-规范（Belinfante–canonical）障碍Ω_{ab} ≠ ϖ_{ab}。

Conclusion: 本文建立的纤维化分类框架系统地将赝规范变换自由度纳入了相对论自旋流体力学的可观测量理论，为理解重离子极化数据中的矛盾提供了几何基础，并指出了扩展响应扇区以包含局域场关联数据的必要性。

Abstract: We study the pseudo-gauge transformation (PGT) freedom at freeze-out in relativistic spin hydrodynamics. The Cooper--Frye map is shown to factor through the quotient of freeze-out data by a universal stabilizer, yielding a stratified fibration over the space of thermodynamic Lagrange multipliers. This classifies observables into base and fiber types, bounds the number of independent PGT-sensitive observables by the family-restricted fiber dimension, and implies cross-observable consistency relations. Applied to heavy-ion polarization data, the fibration structure provides a structural interpretation of the tension between $Λ$ polarization and $φ$-meson spin alignment as evidence that the vorticity-dominated response sector may need to be enlarged with local field-correlation data. We show that Weyl-anomaly-induced currents studied recently are classified as base observables and recover the known Belinfante--canonical obstruction $Ω_{ab}\neq\varpi_{ab}$ from the stabilizer condition.

</details>


### [15] [Approximate higher-form symmetries and dualities of massive p-forms in the holographic bulk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01486)
*André Oliveira Pinheiro*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于全息对偶（holographic duality）框架，发展了一套用于描述连续高阶形式对称性（continuous higher-form symmetries）及其低能有效理论的方法，核心工具包括体时空路径积分（bulk path integrals）、全息重整化（holographic renormalisation）以及边界条件改变形变（boundary-condition-changing deformations）。研究表明，与缺陷流（defect current）相关联的近似高阶形式对称性可通过有质量反对称张量场（massive antisymmetric tensor fields）在全息框架中实现；同时，体时空中的有质量/无质量霍奇对偶性（Hodge dualities）对应于边界理论中不同量子化选择之间的对偶关系，为近似对称性、对偶性和强-弱耦合关系提供了统一视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 连续高阶形式对称性在量子场论和引力理论中日益重要，但目前缺少一个统一的低能有效描述框架。本文旨在构建一个全息（holographic）方法来系统处理此类对称性及其破缺、对偶性等基本问题。

Method: 采用体时空路径积分和全息重整化技术，引入边界条件改变形变；利用有质量反对称张量场（massive $p$-forms）实现与缺陷流关联的近似高阶形式对称性；通过分析有质量/无质量霍奇对偶性，推导边界理论之间的对偶关系。

Result: 展示了近似高阶形式对称性可通过参数化小的体质量或与罗宾边界条件（Robin boundary conditions）相关的强形变来实现；导出了质量零和非零情形下霍奇对偶性对应的边界理论对偶关系；在精确对称性自对偶（self-dual）情形下，推导了存在双迹形变（double-trace deformations）时全息流-流关联函数（current-current correlators）的广义约束条件。

Conclusion: 该框架为全息理论中的近似对称性、对偶性及强-弱耦合关系提供了统一视角，特别是在有质量 $p$-形式场背景下。

Abstract: We develop a holographic framework for continuous higher-form symmetries and their low-energy effective descriptions, based on bulk path integrals, holographic renormalisation and boundary-condition-changing deformations. We show how approximate higher-form symmetries associated with a defect current can be realised holographically through massive antisymmetric tensor fields, either via parametrically small bulk masses or strong deformations associated with Robin boundary conditions. We further study the consequences of massless and massive Hodge dualities in the bulk, deriving the corresponding dualities between boundary theories related by different quantisation choices. Our results provide a unified perspective on approximate symmetries, dualities and strong/weak-coupling relations in holographic theories based on massive $p$-forms. In the self-dual case of an exact symmetry of degree $(d-3)/2$, we derive generalised constraints on holographic current-current correlators in the presence of double-trace deformations.

### [16] [Color Confinement and Massive Gluon in Superfield Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01795)
*Ichiro Oda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在超场形式论（superfield formalism）下重新审视量子色动力学（QCD）中的色禁闭现象，并将其与二次引力（QG）中大质量鬼场的禁闭问题相联系。研究表明，胶子场BRST变换中存在束缚态时，胶子获得质量并被禁闭；其渐近场满足大质量偶极子场方程，而非传统Klein-Gordon方程。夸克场在禁闭相中满足大质量旋量偶极子方程，暗示夸克-反夸克对形成束缚态并禁闭为介子。这些结果推测，二次引力中大质量鬼场的类似禁闭行为可能解决其物理S矩阵的幺正性（unitarity）问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本篇研究的动机源于二次引力（quadratic gravity, QG）中大质量鬼场（massive ghost）的禁闭问题，该问题破坏了物理S矩阵的幺正性（unitarity）。为了寻找解决该问题的线索，作者在超场形式论（superfield formalism）下重新审视了量子色动力学（QCD）中已被广泛研究的色禁闭（color confinement）现象。

Method: 研究采用超场形式论（superfield formalism）框架，对QCD中的胶子场和夸克场进行分析。通过考察胶子场BRST变换（BRST transformation）中束缚态的存在性，推导出胶子的质量生成与禁闭条件；进一步分析胶子渐近场所满足的场方程，并类比推导夸克场在禁闭相中的动力学行为。

Result: 结果显示，当胶子场的BRST变换中存在束缚态（bound state）时，胶子获得质量（massive）并被禁闭；其渐近场（asymptotic field）服从的场方程并非传统的大质量Klein-Gordon场方程，而是大质量偶极子（massive dipole）场方程。对于夸克禁闭，夸克场在禁闭相中满足大质量旋量偶极子方程（massive spinor dipole equation），暗示夸克-反夸克对构成束缚态并被禁闭为介子（meson）。

Conclusion: 基于QCD中色禁闭的上述结果，论文推测二次引力（QG）中可能发生类似的大质量鬼场（massive ghost）禁闭现象，这有望为二次引力中物理S矩阵的幺正性问题（unitarity problem）提供解决途径。

Abstract: In connection with the question of confinement of massive ghost in quadratic gravity (QG), color confinement in quantum chromodynamics (QCD) has been reconsidered in the superfield formalism. It is shown that when a bound state in the BRST transformation of the gluon field exists, the gluon becomes massive and is confined. It is also shown that the asymptotic field of the gluon field obeys the field equation for not the conventional massive Klein-Gordon field but the massive dipole field. In case of quark confinement, it is shown that the quark field satisfies the massive spinor dipole equation in the confinement phase, which might suggest a physical picture such that a pair of quark and anti-quark constitutes a bound state and is confined into a meson. These facts encourage us to conjecture that the similar phenomenon could take place in confinement of massive ghost, which violates the unitarity of the physical S-matrix, and might provide us with a resolution to the unitarity problem in QG.

</details>


### [17] [Quasi-bound States of Scalar field inside the Dyonic Kerr-Sen Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01877)
*David Senjaya,Tinnagrit Songkeaw,Piyabut Burikham*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在带电克尔-森黑洞（dyonic Kerr-Sen black hole, DKSBH）背景中发现了有质量标量场（massive scalar field）的精确解析准稳态解，利用视界正则的入射爱丁顿-芬克尔斯坦坐标（Eddington-Finkelstein coordinates）施加边界条件，通过级数截断实现准稳态频率的精确量子化，揭示了频谱的多分支结构及其对黑洞自旋与电荷的依赖关系，并基于模式增长/衰减行为支持了霍金的时间保护猜想（chronology protection conjecture）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在带电克尔-森黑洞背景中有质量标量场的准稳态（quasi-stationary states）行为，并探讨其对黑洞时空稳定性及霍金时间保护猜想（chronology protection conjecture）的含义。

Method: 采用视界正则的入射爱丁顿-芬克尔斯坦坐标（ingoing Eddington-Finkelstein coordinates）直接施加入射边界条件；径向解表示为合流黑根函数（confluent Heun functions）；通过无穷远处正则性条件导出级数截断条件（series truncation condition），实现准稳态频率的精确量子化（exact quantization）。

Result: 频谱呈现丰富的多分支结构（multi-branch structure），分为两类：对黑洞自旋与电荷不敏感的模式和显式依赖自旋与电荷的模式；发现共转与逆转构型之间存在明显不对称性，以及电荷引致的系统性频谱偏移；正实部频率模式具有正虚部，呈指数增长，负实部频率模式则呈阻尼衰减；纯虚模（purely imaginary modes）不含振荡分量，无法沿闭合类时曲线（closed timelike curves）传播。

Conclusion: 正能激发在视界后方区域（包括包含闭合类时曲线的内视界内部区域）会指数级地使背景时空失稳，支持霍金时间保护猜想（chronology protection conjecture）；纯虚模不传播，避免了沿闭合类时曲线的旅行激发，与猜想一致。

Abstract: We found sets of exact analytic quasi-stationary states of a massive scalar field in a dyonic Kerr-Sen black hole~(DKSBH) background in the maximally extended spacetime region. A central novelty is the use of horizon-regular ingoing Eddington-Finkelstein coordinates, which enables a direct and unambiguous imposition of the ingoing boundary condition at the horizon. The exact radial solutions are in the form of confluent Heun functions. Imposing regularity at spatial infinity enforces a series truncation condition, yielding an exact quantization of the quasi-stationary frequencies. The spectrum exhibits a rich multi-branch structure, which we show splits into two distinct classes: modes that are insensitive to the black hole spin and charges and modes that explicitly depend on them. We uncover a clear asymmetry between co-rotating and counter-rotating configurations, driven by the spin-angular momentum coupling, as well as a systematic shift of the spectrum induced by electric and magnetic charges. The physical branches exhibit a universal behavior: modes with positive real frequency possess positive imaginary parts and therefore grow exponentially in time, whereas modes with negative real frequency are damped and decay. This suggests that positive-energy excitations in the region behind the outer horizon including the inner region of the inner horizon which contains the closed-timelike-curve, exponentially destabilize the background spacetime, supporting Hawking's chronology protection conjecture. In addition, the purely imaginary modes contain no oscillatory component and hence do not propagate through the spacetime, preventing traveling excitations along closed timelike curves and remaining consistent with the conjecture.

### [18] [Successes and challenges of using Semidefinite Programming for the study of Spin Chain Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02013)
*David Berenstein,P. N. Thomas Lloyd*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文使用半定规划（semidefinite programming, SDP）方法研究自旋链哈密顿量，重点分析 transverse Ising 模型与 3-态 Potts 模型的基态能量、激发态荷态及基态关联函数。研究揭示 SDP 在可精确求解的自由费米子系统（free fermion theories）中能获得精确基态能量与两点函数，但在非自由费米子系统中性能退化，且面临输入量随晶格体积增大而显著增长的可扩展性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解 SDP 方法在自旋链哈密顿量分析中的工作机制与适用条件，明确其在何种情形下表现良好及其原因，特别是在引入电荷约束（charge constraints）和可积模型（integrable models）附加约束后是否有助于改进方法。

Method: 采用 SDP 方法分析 transverse Ising 模型和 3-态 Potts 模型。使用电荷约束获取激发态，探索可积模型的附加约束对方法的改进效果。在临界点（criticality）利用近似 Virasoro 关联函数（approximate Virasoro correlators）提取中心荷（central charge）和荷态临界指数，并识别相变位置。

Result: 在自由费米子系统中，SDP 精确给出基态能量和费米子两点函数。在非自由费米子理论中，SDP 对基态能量之外的数据（如关联函数）的估计质量逐步下降，尽管定性的匹配仍可保持。SDP 的有效性面临可扩展性（scaling）问题，即所需输入量随晶格体积增大而糟糕地增长。

Conclusion: SDP 在自由费米子系统中表现完美，但推广到非自由费米子系统时准确性有限；方法的实际应用受限于输入数据量随系统规模扩大而快速增长的问题。

Abstract: We study semidefinite programming (SDP) methods to analyze spin chain Hamiltonians. We examine the ground state energy, the first excited charged states and ground state correlators in two simple models: the Ising model in a transverse magnetic field and the closely related 3-state Potts model. Our goal is to understand precisely what the SDP program is doing and when it works well, why it does so. We focus on the following novel ingredients: using charge constraints to obtain excited states and to see if additional constraints from integrable models are effective at improving the method.
  At criticality we also explore to what extent we can use approximate Virasoro correlators to extract conformal data: the central charge and some critical exponents of charged states. We also use these to identify the location of the phase transition. In the special case where the system is made of free fermions we prove that the SDP finds the exact energy of the ground state and produces the correct two point functions of the fermions. Away from free fermion theories, the SDP gets progressively worse at estimating data beyond the value of the ground state energy (like correlation functions), although it qualitatively matches these. In order to be effective, the SDP seems to run into scaling issues where the amount of input needed scales poorly with the lattice volume.

</details>


### [19] [Boulder Lectures on Thermal Dynamics and Hydrodynamic EFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02391)
*Luca V. Delacretaz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统介绍了如何利用有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）构建涨落流体动力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics）的理论框架，强调其源于“强到弱”自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking）这一现代视角，并涵盖从自旋链到相对论性量子场论（relativistic quantum field theories）等多种物理系统中的推广，最后讨论了输运参数（Wilson系数）所受到的紫外/红外（UV/IR）约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任何非零温度下的局域多体系统都会涌现出涨落流体动力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics），但如何对该涌现过程进行定量的控制性研究仍是核心挑战。有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）方法为此提供了严格的框架，因此需要系统梳理其组织原则和现代构造方式。

Method: 采用有效场论（EFT）方法，以“强到弱”自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking）为核心视角构建涨落流体动力学。通过高能物理与凝聚态物理中的实例（如自旋链、相对论性量子场论、具有广义对称性或't Hooft反常的模型）展示该范式的广泛适用性。

Result: 展示了如何将涨落流体动力学统一地视为“强到弱”自发对称性破缺的体现，并说明了该框架可适用于多种物理系统。此外，给出了流体动力学有效场论中输运参数（Wilson系数）在连续理论和格点理论中各自受到的紫外/红外（UV/IR）约束。

Conclusion: 基于“强到弱”自发对称性破缺的现代有效场论（EFT）构造为理解平衡与非平衡热化系统中的涨落流体动力学提供了统一且可控的理论工具，其适用范围涵盖从高能到凝聚态物理的多种体系，同时输运参数的UV/IR约束为理论预测提供了重要边界条件。

Abstract: Fluctuating hydrodynamics emerges in essentially any local many-body system at nonzero temperature. Effective field theory (EFT) approaches enable the quantitative study of this emergence, providing a controlled framework to capture late-time observables. These lectures introduce the organizing principles behind equilibrium and out-of-equilibrium dynamics in these thermalizing systems. A central focus is the modern construction of these EFTs, which frames fluctuating hydrodynamics through the lens of "strong-to-weak" spontaneous symmetry breaking. Drawing examples from both high-energy and condensed matter physics, we show how this paradigm adapts to systems ranging from spin chains to relativistic quantum field theories, including models with generalized symmetries or symmetries with 't Hooft anomalies. Finally, we discuss UV/IR constraints on transport parameters -- viewed as the Wilson coefficients of hydrodynamic EFTs -- both in continuum and on the lattice.

### [20] [Cumulant dynamics in finite-memory diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02446)
*Navid Abbasi,Xin An,Shanjin Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将描述守恒荷涨落演化的标准基线从Fickian扩散扩展为Maxwell–Cattaneo扩散，引入有限流弛豫时间带来的记忆效应，发现电流记忆会抑制、偏移和重塑累积量的非单调行为，尤其在高阶累积量及其比值中效果显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 守恒荷涨落是量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）临界点的主要探针信号之一，但其解释需要涨落关联子在夸克-胶子等离子体（quark–gluon plasma, QGP）火球有限寿命期间如何演化的动力学描述。标准基线Fickian扩散假设扩散流瞬时跟随局域密度梯度，当流弛豫时间与相关涨落模的弛豫时间可比时，这种瞬时流极限会遗漏延迟响应效应。

Method: 将演化基线扩展为Maxwell–Cattaneo扩散，其中流在有限时间尺度上弛豫因而保留记忆；推导了多点Wigner函数（multi-point Wigner functions）的封闭演化方程；沿QCD相图中代表性轨迹将冻结关联子转化为依赖于接收度（acceptance）的累积量（cumulants）。

Result: Fickian扩散已使关联子滞后于瞬时平衡值，而有限流弛豫引入的额外记忆效应超越了这种扩散滞后。电流记忆会抑制、偏移和重塑累积量相对于瞬时平衡和Fickian扩散的非单调行为。

Conclusion: 电流记忆效应在涨落信号中不可忽略，最显著的效果出现在高阶累积量及其比值中，表明在解释QCD临界点信号时需考虑非Fickian扩散的动力学修正。

Abstract: Fluctuations of conserved charges are among the main proposed signatures of the quantum chromodynamics (QCD) critical point, but their interpretation requires a dynamical description of how fluctuation correlators evolve during the finite lifetime of the quark--gluon plasma (QGP) fireball. The standard baseline for this evolution is Fickian diffusion, in which the diffusive current follows the local density gradient instantaneously. This instantaneous-current limit can miss delayed-response effects when the current-relaxation time becomes comparable to the relaxation time of the relevant fluctuation modes. In this work we extend this baseline to Maxwell--Cattaneo diffusion, where the current relaxes on a finite time scale and therefore retains memory. We derive closed evolution equations for multi-point Wigner functions and convert the freezeout correlators into acceptance-dependent cumulants along representative trajectories in the QCD phase diagram. While Fickian diffusion already causes the correlators to lag behind their instantaneous equilibrium values, finite current relaxation introduces an additional memory effect beyond this diffusive lag. As a result, current memory can suppress, shift, and reshape the non-monotonic behavior of the cumulants relative to both instantaneous equilibrium and Fickian diffusion, with the most visible effects appearing in higher-order cumulants and their ratios.

</details>

### [21] [Photooxidative ageing of 3D printed polymers PLA, ABS, PET, HIPS and PC induced by long-term UV radiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00068)
*Jan Tomastik,Karolina Siskova,Lukas Vaclavek,Radim Ctvrtlik*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了长期紫外线辐射（UV radiation）对使用熔丝制造法（FFF）3D打印制备的五种聚合物材料（PLA、ABS、PC、PETG、HIPS）力学与结构性能的影响，实验时长超过10个月（322天），通过纳米压痕法评估力学性能，并借助拉曼散射与红外吸收光谱分析结构变化，发现PLA和PC具有最佳抗UV性能，而ABS和HIPS脆化明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有聚合物老化研究多关注多因素联合效应且时间尺度不超过数月，为了解材料变化动力学并设计提升材料抗性的策略，有必要分离单一因素（如UV辐射）的影响。

Method: 在控制湿度与温度的环境箱中对FFF制备的五种聚合物进行超过10个月（7744小时，322天）的UV辐射老化；采用局部灵敏度纳米压痕法评估力学性能，包括硬度、弹性模量、表面特性、深度性能剖面及蠕变；对PLA、ABS和PETG样本使用拉曼散射（Raman scattering）和红外吸收（infrared absorption）振动光谱分析结构变化。

Result: PLA和PC表现出最高的UV抗性；ABS和HIPS力学性能发生显著变化（甚至在大深度处），前者出现脆化；PETG的力学性能变化仅体现在深度<10 μm范围内。振动光谱支持力学测试结果：PLA无明显结构变化，ABS和PETG在特征振动与变形振动上均出现差异。

Conclusion: 长期单一UV辐射对FFF制备聚合物材料的力学与结构性能具有显著差异化影响，PLA和PC在长时间UV暴露下性能稳定，而ABS和HIPS易发生脆化，PETG的退化局限于浅表层。振动光谱分析为力学结果提供了结构层面的佐证。

Abstract: This article focuses on the influence of long-term UV radiation exposure on mechanical and structural properties of selected polymeric materials (PLA, ABS, PC, PETG, HIPS) prepared using 3D-print based Fused Filament Fabrication (FFF) method. Existing research in the field of polymers weathering has been focused more on the combined effects so far, moreover on time scales not exceeding units of months. However, it is important to separate individual effects to understand the dynamics of material changes and design strategies to improve material resistance. Our research thus focuses on UV-affected ageing of the selected polymers for time duration exceeding 10 months (7744 consecutive hours, i.e. 322 days), performed in an environmental cell with controlled humidity and temperature. Mechanical properties were evaluated by a locally sensitive nanoindentation method. Surface properties, depth property profiles, and creep were studied as well. Hardness and modulus of elasticity data were obtained for a wide range of samples. Based on our analysis of mechanical properties, the highest UV resistances are characteristic for PLA and PC. On the contrary, noticeable changes of mechanical properties occur in the ABS and HIPS samples (even at greater depths), leading to an embrittlement of the former material. Changes in mechanical properties even in strongly affected samples (PETG) were only evident to depths <10 um. For the selected samples (PLA, ABS, PETG), vibrational spectroscopies (Raman scattering and infrared absorption) were exploited to gain a deeper insight into polymers structural changes. Vibrational spectra supported the results of mechanical properties tests: while PLA revealed no significant changes from the structural viewpoint; ABS and PETG showed differences in characteristic as well as deformation vibrations.

</details>


<div id='cs.AI'></div>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [22] [Self-Revising Discovery Systems for Science: A Categorical Framework for Agentic Artificial Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01444)
*Fiona Y. Wang,Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于范畴论（category theory）的框架，将科学发现建模为表征体制（representational regime）的验证性转换，而非单纯的答案生成。通过在固定体制下的余预层（copresheaf）状态与体制变迁时的左Kan延拓（left Kan extension）对比，区分检索、搜索与发现。并在蛋白质力学与纤维网络两个系统中实例化该框架，展示了范畴论作为自修正AI发现系统数学语言与工程规范的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有科学发现模型多关注答案生成，忽略了发现涉及对证据、人工制品（artifacts）、操作和验证者（verifiers）类型化方式（typing）的根本性修订。本文旨在为材料科学中的自主发现（agentic discovery）提供一个严格的数学基础，以区分搜索、检索与真正的发现。

Method: 采用范畴论方法。在固定体制b下，系统状态定义为从模式范畴（schema category）S_b到集合范畴的余预层I_t: S_b → Set，其出处（provenance）由元素范畴（category of elements）∫_{S_b} I_t 刻画。固定体制操作是保持出处的自函子（endofunctor）更新。体制变迁则通过左Kan延拓Lan_u I_t 保留旧人工制品，并与新状态比较以识别超出函子迁移的剩余内容（residual content）。

Result: 在两个系统中实例化该框架：1) Builder/Breaker中，蛋白质力学世界模型在最小描述长度（Minimum Description Length, MDL）门控下修订，接受定律为模式条件柔量（mode-conditioned compliance）；2) CategoryScienceClaw中，类型化技能、人工制品、开放需求等构成带证明的知识计算图（proof-carrying knowledge-computation graph），纤维网络实例记录了候选模型、AIC门控、微扰测试及接受的各向异性取向张量替代模型。

Conclusion: 范畴论既可作为科学发现的数学语言，也可作为自修正AI发现系统的工程规范。该框架成功将科学发现从主观新颖性（subjective novelty）中分离出来，定义为验证性的体制转换。

Abstract: Scientific discovery is not only answer generation but revision of the representational regime in which evidence, artifacts, operations, and verifiers are typed. We develop a category-theoretic account of agentic discovery for materials science. In a fixed regime b with schema category S_b, the system state is a copresheaf I_t: S_b -> Set, and provenance is the category of elements \int_{S_b} I_t. Fixed-regime operation is an update on such states, endofunctorial only when provenance-preserving refinements are specified and preserved. Discovery is instead a verified regime transition u: S_b -> S_b': old artifacts are preserved, transported by the left Kan extension Lan_u I_t, and compared with the post-transition state to identify residual content beyond functorial transport. This separates retrieval, search, and discovery without subjective novelty. We instantiate the framework in two systems. In Builder/Breaker, a protein-mechanics world model is revised under a Minimum Description Length gate; the accepted law expresses within-chain flexibility as all-mode elastic compliance conditioned by slow collective-mode participation, or mode-conditioned compliance. In CategoryScienceClaw, typed skills, artifacts, open needs, workflow mutation, gates, stress tests, and public discourse become a proof-carrying knowledge-computation graph. A fiber-network example records candidate models, rejected alternatives, an AIC gate, perturbation tests, and an accepted orientation-tensor anisotropic stiffness surrogate over an isotropic fiber-count descriptor. Together, the cases show how category theory can be both a mathematical language for discovery and an engineering specification for self-revising AI discovery systems.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SLD实验数据存储于过时的遗留格式，难以被现代物理学与机器学习研究所利用，因此需要将数据转换为通用、易用的文件格式，并配套相关文档以促进粒子物理领域的研究。

Result: 生成了一个包含约66万重建事件的数据集（AI就绪格式）以及新近数字化的SLD内部文档语料库，并提供了物理验证演示以及它们在粒子物理和机器学习研究中的应用示例。

Conclusion: 该现代化数据发布有效降低了SLD实验数据的使用门槛，为粒子物理学与机器学习交叉领域的研究提供了宝贵资源。

Abstract: We present a modernized, AI-ready release of reconstructed data from the SLD experiment at the SLAC Linear Collider (SLC). The dataset comprises approximately 660{,}000 reconstructed events collected at $\sqrt{s}\approx 91.2$~GeV with a highly polarized electron beam from 1996--1998. The data have been translated from legacy formats into modern, widely-used file formats with the help of AI agents. The release also includes a corpus of newly digitized SLD internal documentation. We describe the contents of both components and provide physics validation demonstrations along with illustrations of their utility for physics and machine learning research in particle physics.

*D. Ruterbories,S. Akhter,Z. Ahmad Dar,M. Sajjad Athar,M. Betancourt,S. Boyd,H. da Motta,J. Felix,L. Fields,R. Fine,A. M. Gago,H. Gallagher,P. K. Gaur,S. M. Gilligan,R. Gran,E. Granados,D. A. Harris,A. L. Hart,A. Klustová,M. Kordosky,D. Last,Z. Lin,A. Lozano,S. Manly,W. A. Mann,C. Mauger,K. S. McFarland,M. Mehmood,O. Moreno,J. G. Morfín,J. K. Nelson,C. Nguyen,V. Paolone,G. N. Perdue,C. TL;DR: 该论文通过比较两种不同能区的中微子束流下的相同中微子荷电流准弹性类散射测量结果，揭示了核介质效应导致的与自由中子散射的偏离，并发现现有模型高估了末态质子和带电π介子的相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子荷电流准弹性类散射（neutrino charged-current quasielastic-like scattering）被广泛用于中微子振荡测量，但核介质效应（如多核子过程和末态相互作用）会导致观测结果偏离自由核子散射行为，从而影响中微子能量重建的准确性。本文通过对比两种能区的中微子束流测量，旨在分离并检验核介质效应对散射过程的影响。

Method: 作者在两种不同的宽能带中微子束流中进行了相同的测量：一种束流峰值约3 GeV且少有中微子能量超过6 GeV，另一种束流峰值约6 GeV且少有中微子能量超过10 GeV。通过比较μ子和质子运动学（muon and proton kinematics）的微分截面，来探测由核介质效应引起的与自由中子散射的偏离。

Result: 观测到实验数据与模型预言之间存在不一致，这些不一致表明模型高估了准弹性类事件中质子和带电π介子（charged pions）的末态相互作用（final state interactions）。

Conclusion: 核介质效应在准弹性类散射中不可忽略，现有中微子相互作用模型对末态相互作用的处理需要修正，以提高中微子振荡实验中能量重建的可靠性。

Abstract: Neutrino charged-current quasielastic-like scattering, a reaction category extensively used in neutrino oscillation measurements, receives contributions from single nucleon knockout processes, multinucleon processes, and inelastic scattering with subsequent rescattering or absorption in the nucleus to produce only nucleons in the final state. In this article, comparisons are presented of the same measurement in two different wideband neutrino beams: one beam peaks near 3 GeV with few neutrinos above 6 GeV; the other peaks near 6 GeV with few neutrinos above 10 GeV. Comparisons of differential cross sections in muon and proton kinematics for these two exposures probe deviations from free-neutron scattering that arise from the processes involving the nuclear medium, and provide a test of neutrino interaction models used to infer neutrino energies in oscillation experiments. Discrepancies are observed between the data and predictions that point to overestimates of the final state interactions of both protons and charged pions in quasielastic-like events.

</details>


### [25] [Search for single production of a vector-like B' quark decaying to a top quark and a W boson in the single-lepton final state in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01423)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了CMS实验利用13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对窄宽度矢量类B'夸克（vector-like B' quark）通过衰变至t夸克和W玻色子进行单产生（single production）的搜寻，最终态包含单个轻子，是目前对该过程最灵敏的搜寻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超出标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的新物理，寻找窄宽度的矢量类B'夸克，该粒子是标准模型中尚未发现的理论候选粒子，其单产生过程此前未被充分约束。

Method: 使用CMS探测器于2016–2018年收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为138 fb⁻¹。分析采用单轻子末态，B'夸克候选体由电子或缪子、缺失横动量（missing transverse momentum）、一个大半径喷注（large-radius jet）及一个小半径喷注（small-radius jet）重建。大半径喷注的起源粒子由基于神经网络的标记器（neural-network-based tagger）识别，主要本底贡献由数据驱动的神经自回归流网络（neural autoregressive flow network）建模。

Result: 未发现显著信号，设定了对窄宽度B'夸克单产生的排除限。在Γ/m_B' = 5%条件下，排除质量为0.8至1.23 TeV的单态B'夸克（singlet B' quark）。同时给出了B'夸克与t夸克关联产生的生产截面上限，以及B'夸克与电弱玻色子（electroweak bosons）耦合因子的约束。

Conclusion: 本研究是迄今为止对窄宽度B'夸克单产生过程最灵敏的搜寻，为相关新物理模型的参数空间提供了严格的实验限制。

Abstract: A search is presented for the single production of a narrow-width vector-like B' quark that decays to a t quark and a W boson, with one of the decay products yielding an electron or muon. The data were collected from 2016 to 2018 by the CMS experiment at the LHC in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-2}$. The search is performed in a single-lepton final state, where the B' quark candidate is reconstructed from an electron or muon, missing transverse momentum, one large-radius jet, and one small-radius jet if the t quark decays leptonically. The originating particles of large-radius jets are identified using a neural-network-based tagger, and the dominant background contributions are modeled from data using a neural autoregressive flow network. This search is the most sensitive to date to the single production of narrow-width B' quarks, excluding singlet B' quarks with $Γ/m_\mathrm{B'}$ = 5% for masses between 0.8 and 1.23 TeV. Limits are also placed on the production cross section of single B' quarks produced in association with t quarks, and on the coupling factor of the B' quark to electroweak bosons.

</details>


### [26] [HS3: A Descriptive, Interoperable Serialization Standard for Statistical Models in High-Energy Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01760)
*Carsten Burgard,Oliver Schulz,Giordon Stark,Jonas Rembser,Simon Cello,Cornelius Grunwald*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了高能物理统计序列化标准（HS3），一种与实现无关、可读性强且可扩展的统计模型序列化格式，旨在实现统计模型的跨框架交换、验证与长期保存，支持FAIR原则，并已在C++、Python和Julia中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理中基于似然（likelihood）的推断日益成为精度测量和有效场论拟合的核心工具，现有模型表示格式（如ROOT workspaces、pyhf JSON、CMS DataCards）虽功能丰富，但绑定于特定软件栈，缺乏跨框架交换、验证和长期保存的通用标准。

Method: HS3将似然表示为计算图（computational graph），由命名分布（distributions）、函数、数据集、定义域和分析方案构成；支持有分箱（binned）与无分箱（unbinned）似然及层次复合模型（hierarchical composite models）。设计上可通过后向兼容扩展纳入新统计结构，推断过程留给下游框架实现。

Result: HS3可与ROOT/RooFit互转，是pyhf的超集（superset），已在C++、Python和Julia中实现，并展示了在HEPData上的公开似然应用、跨框架验证及重现性方面的初步成果。

Conclusion: HS3为大型强子对撞机（LHC）及其他领域的统计模型提供了符合FAIR原则的长期保存基础，旨在服务更广泛的科学社区，并随应用需求持续演进。

Abstract: Statistical models in high-energy physics formally encode the relationship between observed data, physics parameters of interest, and experimental and theoretical uncertainties. Likelihood-based inference is the central tool for precision measurements, effective field theory fits, and cross-analysis combinations. Consequently, there is an increasing need for machine-readable, descriptive, and portable model representations. Existing formats such as ROOT workspaces, pyhf JSON, and CMS DataCards provide valuable capabilities but remain tied to specific software stacks and offer no universal standard for exchange, validation, or long-term preservation. We introduce HS3, the High-Energy Physics Statistics Serialization Standard, an implementation-agnostic, human-readable, and extensible serialization format for statistical models. HS3 is designed such that new statistical constructs can be incorporated through backward-compatible extensions, while inference procedures and implementation-specific execution details remain the responsibility of downstream frameworks. HS3 represents likelihoods as computational graphs composed of named distributions, functions, datasets, domains, and analysis prescriptions. It supports binned and unbinned likelihoods as well as hierarchical composite models. HS3 is convertible from and to ROOT/RooFit and is a superset of pyhf. We describe the design principles, structure, and semantics of HS3 and summarize existing implementations in C++, Python, and Julia. We also present early applications to public likelihoods on HEPData, cross-framework validation, and reproducibility efforts. HS3 provides a foundation for FAIR (Findable, Accessible, Interoperable, Reusable), long-lived statistical models at the LHC and beyond. The standard is intended to serve the broader scientific community and to evolve over time for application across a wide range of domains.

</details>


### [27] [Search for a leptoquark in events with a hadronically decaying $τ$-lepton and missing transverse momentum using $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02067)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 利用ATLAS探测器在质子-质子对撞中收集的13 TeV数据（积分亮度140 fb⁻¹），对衰变至强子衰变τ轻子与缺失横向动量的末态进行轻子夸克（leptoquark）信号搜索；在基准U₁矢量轻子夸克（vector-leptoquark）模型下，未发现超出标准模型预期的信号，并在95%置信水平上对1.5–3.0 TeV质量范围内的耦合参数设定了上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻子夸克（leptoquark）是超出标准模型（Standard Model）的新粒子，可能同时耦合至夸克与轻子，探索其存在有助于理解味物理（flavor physics）中的未解之谜。

Method: 利用大型强子对撞机（LHC）上ATLAS探测器记录的质心能量√s=13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（2015-2018年，积分亮度140 fb⁻¹），选取衰变产物中包含强子衰变τ轻子与缺失横向动量的末态事例；针对轻子夸克的共振产生（resonant production）和非共振t-道交换（non-resonant t-channel exchange）两种产生机制同时开展搜索。

Result: 未观测到显著超出标准模型背景预言的信号；在基准U₁矢量轻子夸克模型下，首次在1.5–3.0 TeV质量范围内对耦合参数设定了95%置信水平（CL）的上限。

Conclusion: 该搜索在较宽的耦合情景下排除了1.5–3.0 TeV质量区间内U₁矢量轻子夸克的存在可能性，为未来的高能对撞机搜索提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for leptoquark signals is performed in final states with a hadronically decaying $τ$-lepton and missing transverse momentum, using data from proton--proton collisions at a centre-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV recorded by the ATLAS detector at the Large Hadron Collider during Run 2 (2015--18), corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 140 fb$^{-1}$. The analysis is designed to probe both resonant production and non-resonant $t$-channel exchange of the leptoquark, covering a wide range of coupling scenarios. No excess above the Standard Model background prediction is observed. Limits are set on the couplings in the benchmark $U_1$ vector-leptoquark model at 95% confidence level for masses between 1.5 TeV and 3.0 TeV.

### [28] [Advances in electrical contacts to single crystals of emerging materials for transport measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00173)
*Huandong Chen,Abhay. N. Pasupathy,Jayakanth Ravichandran*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了在可剥离与非可剥离单晶上制备高质量、光刻定义的多端电极用于输运测量的最新技术进展，为研究人员针对不同晶体特性选择合适接触制备策略提供了实用指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 输运测量是凝聚态物理学中探测材料电子性质的关键实验技术，已推动超导电性（superconductivity）、量子振荡（quantum oscillations）等新奇现象的发现。然而，新合成的单晶因几何不规则、尺寸有限、结构特性及易降解等问题，在建立可靠电接触方面面临巨大挑战。

Method: 本文以综述形式梳理了在可剥离与非可剥离两类单晶上，通过光刻（lithography）技术定义多端电极（multi-terminal electrodes）以进行输运测量的最新接触制备方法。

Result: 系统总结了针对不同单晶特性（如形貌、尺寸、稳定性和可剥离性）的电极制备策略及其技术进展。

Conclusion: 该综述为研究人员在面对新兴晶体材料时，选择适配的电接触制备方案提供了实践性指导。

Abstract: Transport measurements that probe electrical resistivity of a material under varying external stimuli, such as temperature, magnetic field, optical illumination, and gate voltage, are among the most important experimental techniques in condensed matter physics. These measurements provide critical insights into the fundamental electronic properties of materials. In recent years, they have facilitated the discovery and exploration of intriguing physical phenomena (e.g., superconductivity and quantum oscillations) and unique device functionalities (e.g., photoresponse and electrostatic gating effects) in various emerging materials, particularly in the form of single crystals. However, unlike large-scale wafers or thin films, newly synthesized single crystals often pose substantial challenges in establishing reliable electrical contacts due to their irregular geometries, limited dimensions, inherent structural characteristics, and potential susceptibility to degradation. In this review, we highlight recent technological advancements in the fabrication of high-quality, lithographically defined multi-terminal electrodes on both exfoliable and non-exfoliable single crystals for transport measurements. Our work provides a practical guide for researchers seeking to select appropriate contact-fabrication strategies tailored to unique characteristics of emerging crystals.

</details>


### [29] [Co-adsorption mechanism drives CO oxidation on defective ZnS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00264)
*P. R. A. de Oliveira,C. Codeço,M. G. Menezes,P. Venezuela,F. Stavale,J. A. Boscoboinik*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合近常压X射线光电子能谱（NAP-XPS）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，发现缺陷ZnS单晶表面的CO氧化由氧覆盖度（oxygen coverage）而非单纯缺陷密度驱动，氧辅助的共吸附路径形成弱结合的CO₂类中间体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽禁带半导体表面的反应活性依赖于活性位点的生成，但在CO氧化中，仅存在缺陷不足以驱动反应。该研究旨在揭示缺陷ZnS表面上CO氧化的真正关键因素。

Method: 采用近常压X射线光电子能谱（NAP-XPS）测量缺陷ZnS单晶表面的CO氧化过程，并结合密度泛函理论（DFT）计算进行机理分析。

Result: NAP-XPS仅在富氧条件下检测到CO₂类表面中间体；DFT支持氧辅助共吸附路径，CO优先与Zn缺陷位点附近稳定的吸附氧物种相互作用，形成弱结合的CO₂类结构。

Conclusion: 氧覆盖度（oxygen coverage）而非缺陷密度是控制缺陷ZnS上CO₂类中间体形成的关键因素，缺陷ZnS可作为研究非氧化物半导体表面氧辅助化学的模型平台。

Abstract: Reactivity on wide-bandgap semiconductor surfaces relies critically on the generation of active sites. In the case of CO oxidation, however, the mere presence of defects is insufficient to drive reactivity. Here, we investigate CO oxidation on a defective ZnS single-crystal surface by combining near ambient pressure X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (NAP-XPS) and density functional theory (DFT) calculations. NAP-XPS measurements reveal CO$_2$-like surface intermediates only under oxygen-rich conditions, consistent with oxygen-assisted CO oxidation. DFT calculations support an oxygen-assisted co-adsorption pathway in which CO interacts preferentially with adsorbed oxygen species stabilized near Zn-deficient sites, forming weakly bound CO$_2$-like structures. These results identify oxygen coverage, rather than defect density alone, as the key factor controlling CO$_2$-like intermediate formation on defective ZnS and establish defective ZnS as a model platform for studying oxygen-assisted surface chemistry on non-oxide semiconductors.

Method: 采用模拟X射线光子相关光谱（simulated x-ray photon correlation spectroscopy, XPCS），通过对结构因子（structure factor）第一峰对应的全三维衍射球（full three-dimensional diffraction sphere）进行散斑图样分析（speckle-pattern analysis），揭示多态结构退相关（multi-state structural decorrelation）。

Abstract: Deciphering complex relaxation pathways in disordered solids is a central challenge across polymeric, oxide, and metallic glasses, which traditionally relies on the interpretation of mechanical spectroscopy and resulting damping modes. Here we demonstrate the direct observation of dominant atomic-scale relaxation mechanisms during isothermal annealing of an as-quenched binary model glass towards incipient crystallization. Assessed via simulated x-ray photon correlation spectroscopy, a multi-state structural decorrelation is uncovered via speckle-pattern analysis of the full three-dimensional diffraction sphere across the first peak of the structure factor. Over a simulation time of up to 10 $μ$s, three distinct and subsequent decorrelation stages of thermal vibration, glassy network evolution, and structural and chemical ordering towards crystallization are identified. These findings promote a picture where specific dynamically-separated mechanisms drive the microstructural evolution during glass relaxation and suggest a much richer multi-mode relaxation behavior of metallic glasses than hitherto identified.

### [31] [Robust control over polar skyrmion bubble density with a combined optical and electrical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00398)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于第一性原理的计算方法（first-principles-based calculations），引入具有空间非均匀场图案的扭曲光（twisted light），并在直流电场（DC electric field）辅助下，调控铁电超薄膜中极性斯格明子气泡的密度与成核速率。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了铁电纳米薄膜对光和电场的独特响应特性，对于将极性斯格明子气泡应用于下一代超高密度存储技术具有关键意义。

Abstract: Polar skyrmion bubbles are nanoscale ferroelectric domain configurations with swirling polarization textures, and often emerge in ferroelectric oxide systems. Owing to their inhomogeneous polarization patterns, which endow them with distinct topologies and electrical responses from homogeneous monodomains, polar skyrmion bubbles are envisaged to be promising candidates for non-volatile memory devices. In such device, the recorded information density is directly proportional to the density of bubbles, underscoring the need for precise control over bubble nucleation. Here, using first-principles-based calculations, we demonstrate that when assisted with a DC electric field, twisted light, which has a spatially inhomogeneous field pattern, can robustly tune the density of polar skyrmion bubbles in ferroelectric ultrathin films between $10^2\sim 10^4 \rm{bit}/μm^2$. Moreover, by modulating DC and optical field strengths together with the beam radius, the nucleation rate, which characterizes the creation and annihilation speed of polar skyrmion bubbles, can also be well controlled. These findings highlight the unique response of ferroelectric nanofilms to optical and electric fields, which is crucial for employing polar skyrmion bubbles in the next-generation of ultrahigh-density memory technologies.

### [32] [Microscopic origin of polytype-dependent melting in SiC revealed by machine-learning molecular dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00403)
*Ljiljana Stojanović,Samuel J. Magorrian,Lara Kabalan,Richard N. White,Fabian L. Thiemann,Viktor Zólyomi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合相共存机器学习分子动力学与有限温度声子分析，利用微调后的MACE原子间势能，揭示了SiC多型体的高温稳定性排序（3C > 2H > 9R），并阐明了层间滑移与横向声子模式在驱动熔化过程中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体结构如何影响高温稳定性是材料建模与设计中的关键挑战。SiC因其多种多型体（polytypes）在保持相似局域四面体键合的同时具有不同的长程堆垛几何结构，为研究该问题提供了理想模型体系。

Method: 采用相共存机器学习分子动力学（phase-coexistence machine-learning molecular dynamics）结合有限温度声子分析（finite-temperature phonon analysis），并借助微调后的MACE原子间势能（MACE interatomic potential），该势能精确描述了多种SiC多型体在晶体态、高温态和无序态下的构型。

Result: 确定了明确的相对稳定性排序：3C > 2H > 9R，并反映在结构无序化、层间滑移和有限温度声子谱中。熔化起始于短程C-C接触和富碳局域区域的形成，随后伴随四面体Si-C连接性的逐步丧失。9R稳定性降低归因于与双层滑移相关的低频横向声学剪切模（transverse-acoustic shear modes），这些模在0 K声子谱中已存在，并在高温下进一步软化，产生更大的横向双层位移。

Conclusion: 多型共价材料的高温稳定性不仅受局域键强度控制，还取决于依赖于堆垛方式的横向动力学（transverse dynamics）。高温稳定性由局域键强度和堆垛依赖的横向动力学共同决定。

Abstract: Predicting how crystal structure influences high-temperature stability remains a key challenge in materials modelling and design. Silicon carbide (SiC), one of the most thermally and chemically stable materials known, provides an ideal system for studying this problem because its many polytypes preserve similar local tetrahedral bonding while differing in long-range stacking geometry. Here, we combine phase-coexistence machine-learning molecular dynamics with finite-temperature phonon analysis, enabled by a fine-tuned MACE interatomic potential that accurately describes crystalline, high-temperature, and disordered configurations across multiple SiC polytypes. We identify a clear relative stability ordering, 3C > 2H > 9R, reflected consistently in structural disordering, interlayer sliding, and finite-temperature phonon spectra. Across all polytypes, melting initiates through the formation of short C-C contacts and carbon-rich local regions, followed by a progressive loss of tetrahedral Si-C connectivity. The reduced stability of the long-period 9R polytype is traced to low-frequency transverse-acoustic shear modes associated with relative bilayer sliding, which are already present in the 0 K phonon spectra and soften further at high temperature. These modes generate larger lateral bilayer displacements, linking enhanced interlayer sliding to local chemical disordering and ultimately melting. More broadly, our results show that high-temperature stability in polytypic covalent materials is governed not only by local bond strength, but also by stacking-dependent transverse dynamics.

### [33] [Data-Driven Discovery of Unconventional Antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00409)

TL;DR: 本文通过物理信息预筛选、高通量交换计算和Luttinger-Tisza分析，从Materials Project数据库中的37,163种磁性材料中筛选出189种共线反铁磁体，并进一步识别出36种交错磁体（altermagnets）和11种Luttinger补偿亚铁磁体（LCFs），其中包括22种先前未被报道的交错磁体和9种新的LCF，建立了从结构数据库到可实验验证的对称性分类补偿自旋分裂磁体的可扩展发现路线。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从Materials Project数据库中的37,163种磁体出发，结合物理信息预筛选（physics-informed prescreening）、高通量交换计算（high-throughput exchange calculations）和Luttinger-Tisza分析，将范围缩小至189种共线反铁磁体（collinear antiferromagnets）；随后通过对称性分析（symmetry analysis）进一步识别出36种交错磁体和11种Luttinger补偿亚铁磁体（Luttinger-compensated ferrimagnets, LCFs）。

Result: 识别出36种交错磁体和11种LCF，其中22种交错磁体和9种LCF为先前未报道的新材料。这些非常规反铁磁体能够支持非相对论性自旋霍尔效应（nonrelativistic spin Hall effects）以及具有可切换极化和巨各向异性的掺杂可调自旋输运（doping-tunable spin transport）。

Conclusion: 该框架将广泛的结构数据库转化为经过筛选和对称性分类的、可实验验证的补偿自旋分裂磁体（compensated spin-split magnets）集合，为高效发现功能性反铁磁体建立了一条可扩展的路线。

Abstract: Unconventional antiferromagnets combine zero net magnetization with spin-split electronic bands, offering a distinct, important platform for spintronics. Their discovery, however, has so far depended largely on case-by-case studies and on a limited number of compounds with experimentally resolved magnetic structures. Here, we overcome these bottlenecks by resolving magnetic ground states across a broad materials database. We narrow down 37163 magnets from the Materials Project to 189 collinear antiferromagnets by combining physics-informed prescreening, high-throughput exchange calculations and Luttinger-Tisza analysis. Among these, symmetry analysis identifies 36 altermagnets and 11 Luttinger-compensated ferrimagnets (LCFs), including 22 altermagnets and 9 LCFs that have not been reported previously. The identified unconventional antiferromagnets can support nonrelativistic spin Hall effects and doping-tunable spin transport with switchable polarization and giant anisotropy. Our framework converts broad structural databases into a curated, symmetry-classified set of experimentally testable compensated spin-split magnets, establishing a scalable route for the efficient discovery of functional antiferromagnets.

### [35] [Giant Thermal-Conductivity Enhancement from Pseudo-Angular Momentum Conservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00546)
*Tingting Wang,Dabao Zha,Hao Chen,Jiangbin Gong,Lifa Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现赝角动量（PAM）守恒在声子-声子散射中构成隐藏的选择定则，通过在第一性原理玻尔兹曼输运计算中施加该定则，可将手性晶体Te的晶格热导率在300 K下提升5.30倍，并揭示该机制是解释手性晶体热输运实验与理论偏差的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 赝角动量（pseudo-angular momentum, PAM）已知是手性声子（chiral phonons）光学选择定则的基础，但其是否约束热激发有限波矢（finite-q）声子-声子散射过程尚不明确。本文旨在揭示PAM守恒对热输运的隐藏选择作用。

Method: 从旋转或螺旋本征相位（eigenphase）守恒出发，推导出立方非简谐顶点（cubic anharmonic vertices）上的PAM残差定则（PAM residue rule）。将该规则作为投影算子（projector）嵌入第一性原理玻尔兹曼输运方程（first-principles Boltzmann transport）计算中，在保持声子谱和力常数不变的情况下筛选三声子散射过程。

Result: 在螺旋对称的Te（一种精确实现该定则的平台）中，施加PAM残差定则消除了约三分之二的运动学允许三声子散射三重态（triplets），抑制了电阻性Umklapp弛豫（resistive Umklapp relaxation），使晶格热导率在300 K下提升5.30倍，且在400 K以下保持超过5倍。在另一手性晶体基准测试中，显式本征相位组织可使计算热导率提升约24%，与文献中第一性原理低估实验值的幅度相当。

Conclusion: PAM守恒被确立为手性声子热输运中一种非简谐选择原理（anharmonic selection principle）。对称性分辨的PAM守恒为预测和调控手性晶体及纳米尺度声子学（nanoscale phononics）中的热导率提供了新路径。

Abstract: Pseudo-angular momentum (PAM) underlies optical selection rules for chiral phonons, but whether it also constrains thermally populated finite-q phonon-phonon scattering has remained unresolved. We show that rotational or screw eigenphase conservation imposes a PAM residue rule on cubic anharmonic vertices, revealing a hidden selection rule for heat transport. In screw-symmetric helical Te, an exact platform, implementing this rule as a projector in first-principles Boltzmann transport leaves spectra and force constants unchanged but removes roughly two thirds of kinematically allowed triplets, suppresses resistive Umklapp relaxation, and enhances lattice thermal conductivity by a factor of 5.30 at 300 K, remaining above fivefold up to 400 K. A bulk chiral-crystal benchmark further shows that explicit eigenphase organization can increase the calculated lattice thermal conductivity by about 24%, comparable to the reported first-principles underestimation of experiment. These results establish PAM conservation as an anharmonic selection principle for chiral-phonon heat transport and identify symmetry-resolved PAM conservation as a route to predicting and controlling thermal conductivity in chiral crystals and nanoscale phononics.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属配合物在催化、药物设计和材料科学中至关重要，其性质对三维几何结构高度敏感；然而，过渡金属配合物的电子多样性和非常规成键环境给准确的结构生成带来了重大挑战。

Method: TMCgen 将扩散过程（diffusion process）构建在金属-配体配位角流形上，并结合配体的扭转扩散（torsional diffusion）和旋转扩散（rotational diffusion），从而聚焦于过渡金属配合物的关键几何自由度。

Result: TMCgen 在多种实验来源的生物无机和有机金属配合物上生成了准确的配位环境，且仅需较少的推理步数（inference steps）即可实现高效生成。

Conclusion: 结果表明，基于流形的生成式建模（manifold-based generative modeling）在数据高效的几何结构生成方面具有潜力，为面向性质定制的过渡金属配合物设计铺平了道路。

Abstract: Transition metal complexes are central to catalysis, drug design, and materials science, with relevant properties strongly sensitive to their three-dimensional geometry. However, the electronic diversity and unconventional bonding environments of transition metal complexes pose a major challenge for accurate structure generation. In this work, we introduce TMCgen, a manifold diffusion machine learning model that efficiently and accurately generates geometries of transition metal complexes. By formulating the diffusion process over the metal-ligand coordination angles, combined with torsional and rotational diffusion of the ligands, TMCgen focuses on the key geometric degrees of freedom of transition metal complexes. TMCgen shows strong performance in generating accurate coordination environments on a diverse set of experimentally derived bioinorganic and organometallic complexes while requiring only few inference steps, enabling efficient generation. Our results demonstrate the potential of manifold-based generative modeling for data-efficient geometry generation, paving the way for property-conditioned design of transition metal complexes.

### [38] [A Visible-Frequency Excitonic Reststrahlen Band in (PEA)$_2$PbI$_4$ Slabs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00682)
*Michael Pfeufer,Patrick Grenzer,Friedrich Schöppler,Tobias Hertel*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明(PEA)₂PbI₄薄片在低温下展现出由激子（exciton）诱导的可见光波段Reststrahlen效应，即当强激子使介电常数实部变为负值时，材料形成无腔体的反射带，并通过传输矩阵分析重构了负Re(ε)窗口和近超强激子-光子耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文对(PEA)₂PbI₄薄片进行低温透射测量，观察随厚度增加从激子吸收谷到宽近零透射区（伴随压缩法布里-珀罗条纹）的演变；采用有效洛伦兹振子介电响应模型进行传输矩阵分析，并计算电场分布图。

Result: 传输矩阵分析重构出有限宽的负Re(ε)窗口，并暗示近超强激子-光子耦合（near-ultrastrong exciton-photon coupling）。电场图显示该区间内面内场穿透被抑制，并在高能(ε=0)边缘处出现驱动的纵向响应。

Conclusion: (PEA)₂PbI₄薄片是一种无需光学腔的可见光频段激子Reststrahlen材料，其激子共振可直接驱动介电常数实部变负并产生反射带。

Abstract: Layered halide perovskites host exceptionally strong excitons, whose optical signatures are usually interpreted as absorptive resonances on a smooth dielectric background. Strong excitons, however, can also reshape the dielectric response itself and drive the real permittivity negative, opening a reflective band: the visible, excitonic analogue of an infrared Reststrahlen band. Whether bare (PEA)$_2$PbI$_4$ slabs reach this regime has remained unclear. Here we show that low-temperature transmission of (PEA)$_2$PbI$_4$ slabs, driven by the intralayer-exciton manifold, evolves with increasing thickness from an excitonic dip into a broad near-zero-transmission interval with compressed Fabry-Pérot-like fringes. Transfer-matrix analysis with an effective Lorentz-oscillator dielectric response reproduces this crossover, reconstructs a finite negative-Re($\varepsilon$) window, and implies near-ultrastrong exciton-photon coupling. Calculated field maps show suppressed in-plane field penetration within this interval and a driven longitudinal response near the high-energy ($\varepsilon=0$) edge. These results identify (PEA)$_2$PbI$_4$ slabs as a cavity-free visible-frequency excitonic Reststrahlen material.

### [39] [Impact of Cu-Mn ratio on Structure and Defects in Layered Multiferroic Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00742)
