  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究揭示了Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3中存在强磁电耦合（magnetoelectric coupling）效应，但纳米尺度结构（nanoscale structure）和缺陷对宏观性质的影响尚不清楚。本研究旨在系统解析化学成分变化如何调控纳米结构缺陷，从而理解其与光学、电子和磁学响应的关联。

Method: 采用扫描/透射电子显微镜（scanning/transmission electron microscopy）和单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）分析Cu缺乏（Cu-deficient, Cu:Mn<1）和Cu富余（Cu-rich, Cu:Mn>1）两类Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3晶体的结构与缺陷；辅以密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算验证极性差异。

Result: Cu缺乏晶体中广泛存在堆垛层错（stacking faults），且与Mn/Cu化学不均匀性和Te堆垛变化相关；Cu富余晶体堆垛层错较少，但出现针状沉淀（needle-shaped precipitates）和环状特征（loop-like features）。DFT计算表明Cu富余结构比Cu缺乏结构更具极性（more polar）。

Conclusion: 化学成分的细微变化显著影响Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3的纳米结构、缺陷分布和功能特性，为通过成分调控设计具有定制性能的多铁材料（multiferroic materials）提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Multiferroic materials exhibit the coexistence of magnetic and ferroelectric order, enabling control of magnetism through electric fields and vice versa. These properties make them attractive for spintronic and memory device applications. Recent studies on Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3 (0.04 \leq x \leq 0.26; 0.03 \leq y \leq 0.15) have revealed strong magnetoelectric coupling, with variations in Mn-to-Cu concentration leading to variations in optical, electronic, and magnetic responses. Despite these findings, the influence of nanoscale structure and defects on the observed properties remains poorly understood. In this study, we investigate the structure and nanoscale defects in Cu-deficient Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3 (Cu:Mn ratio <1, i.e., with 0.04 \leq x \leq 0.26 and 0.03 \leq y \leq 0.15) and Cu-rich Cu1+xMn1-ySiTe3 (Cu:Mn ratio >1, i.e., with 0.04 \leq x \leq 0.3 and 0.13 \leq y \leq 0.31) crystals using scanning/transmission electron microscopy and single-crystal X-ray diffraction. Cu-deficient crystals exhibit extensive stacking faults correlated with chemical inhomogeneity between Mn and Cu, along with variations in Te stacking. In contrast, Cu-rich crystals show fewer stacking faults but contain other local structural variations, such as needle-shaped precipitates and loop-like features. These distinct local structural features between Cu-rich and Cu-deficient crystals can be correlated to variations in their observed properties. Complementary density functional theory calculations confirm that the Cu-rich structure is more polar than the Cu-deficient structure. Overall, this study provides a comprehensive understanding of how subtle changes in chemistry influence the nanoscale structure, defect distribution, and functional properties in Cu1-xMn1+ySiTe3, offering guidance for designing multiferroic materials with tailored performance.

### [40] [Neural Spectral Element Methods for stiff multiphysics PDEs with electrochemical transport benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02335)
*Conrard Giresse Tetsassi Feugmo,David Pankaczy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出神经谱元方法（Neural Spectral Element Method, NSEM），通过将神经网络固定在 Legendre-Gauss-Lobatto 求积节点上评估并用预计算谱微分矩阵替代所有导数运算，实现了确定性的损失函数，使 L-BFGS 优化器能够达到 10^-9 至 10^-10 的残差。在 Poisson-Nernst-Planck（PNP）基准测试上，NSEM 以比自适应重采样 PINN 基线少两个数量级的配点数，获得了 10^-4 至 10^-7 的相对逐点误差，并验证了 tanh 多层感知机（MLP）和 Legendre KAN 两种骨干网络均能在同一框架内达到谱精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有物理信息神经网络（PINN）方法在处理多尺度、多区域耦合的物理问题（如电化学中的 Poisson-Nernst-Planck 方程）时，面临配点效率低、优化收敛困难等问题。研究者希望通过结合谱元法（spectral element method）的数值精度与神经网络的灵活性，提升求解精度与计算效率。

Method: NSEM 在固定的 Legendre-Gauss-Lobatto（LGL）求积节点上评估网络输出，并使用预计算的谱微分矩阵（spectral differentiation matrices）替换自动微分中的导数计算，从而构造确定性损失函数。引入 Kosloff-Tal-Ezer 坐标映射处理电化学边界层，并采用无网格神经 mortar 框架（mesh-free neural mortar framework）实现多元素域之间的耦合。

Result: 在 Huang 等人提出的四示例 Poisson-Nernst-Planck（PNP）基准上，NSEM 达到 10^-4 至 10^-7 的相对逐点误差，所需配点数比自适应重采样 PINN 基线少两个数量级。使用 L-BFGS 优化器可获得 10^-9 至 10^-10 的残差。tanh MLP 和 Legendre KAN 两种骨干网络均能在 NSEM 框架内实现谱精度（spectral accuracy），其中 KAN 在 1D PNP 基准上进入 L-BFGS 吸引盆所需的 Adam 步数约为 MLP 的一半。

Conclusion: NSEM 通过将谱元法的离散化策略嵌入神经网络训练流程，有效提升了 PINN 求解偏微分方程（PDE）的精度与效率，尤其在多元素耦合和边界层解析方面表现出优势。该方法可兼容不同的神经网络骨干结构，且 KAN 在优化效率上更具潜力。

Abstract: The Neural Spectral Element Method (NSEM) evaluates each network only at fixed Legendre-Gauss-Lobatto quadrature nodes and replaces all derivative calls with precomputed spectral differentiation matrices. The resulting deterministic loss enables limited-memory BFGS (L-BFGS) to reach residuals of 10^-9 to 10^-10. A Kosloff-Tal-Ezer coordinate map resolves electrochemical boundary layers, while a mesh-free neural mortar framework couples multi-element domains. On the four-example Poisson-Nernst-Planck (PNP) benchmark of Huang and co-workers, NSEM attains 10^-4 to 10^-7 relative pointwise error with two orders of magnitude fewer collocation points than the adaptive-resampling PINN baseline. Both a tanh multilayer perceptron (MLP) and a basis-aligned Legendre Kolmogorov-Arnold Network (KAN) backbone attain spectral accuracy within the same NSEM infrastructure, with the KAN requiring roughly half the Adam steps to enter the L-BFGS basin of attraction on the 1D PNP benchmark.

### [41] [Thermodynamic origin of medium-entropy stabilization in multicomponent rock-salt oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00753)
*Supriya Ghosal,Swapan Pati,Ashutosh Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理热力学框架研究发现，岩盐结构氧化物的单相稳定性并不局限于传统高熵极限（五等摩尔阳离子），中熵组分（三、四种阳离子）在高温下同样可以通过熵驱动实现稳定，构型熵（$ΔS_{conf}$）本身并非相稳定性的普适描述符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验观察到中熵组分也能表现出熵稳定的岩盐相，这引发了一个重要问题：实现相稳定所需的最小熵值是多少？传统观点将高熵氧化物与高构型熵（$ΔS_{conf}\geq 1.61R$）紧密关联，但这一阈值是否具有普适性尚不清楚。

Method: 采用第一性原理热力学框架（first-principles thermodynamic framework），结合密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）、基于MCSQS的结构建模（MCSQS-based structural modeling）以及有限温度吉布斯自由能分析（finite-temperature Gibbs free-energy analysis），定量评估混合焓（$ΔH_{mix}$）、构型熵（$ΔS_{conf}$）、振动熵（$ΔS_{vib}$）和电子熵贡献（$ΔS_{elec}$）在相稳定性中的作用。

Result: $ΔS_{conf}$单独并非相稳定性的普适描述符。二阳离子体系为焓稳定（enthalpy-stabilized），而三、四、五阳离子体系在高温下因熵驱动的吉布斯自由能降低而变得热力学稳定。

Conclusion: 单相岩盐氧化物并不局限于传统高熵极限，中熵组分在合适的热力学条件下同样可以实现稳定化。

Abstract: High entropy oxides are commonly associated with high configurational entropy ($ΔS_{conf}\geq$ 1.61R) corresponding to five equimolar cations occupying a crystallographic sublattice. However, recent experimental observations indicate that medium-entropy compositions may also exhibit entropy-stabilized rock-salt phases, raising an important question regarding the minimum entropy required for phase stabilization. In this work, we employ a first-principles thermodynamic framework to investigate the stability of rock-salt oxides containing two to five principal cations components analogous to (Ni$_{0.8}$Cu$_{0.2}$)O, (Ni$_{0.6}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$)O, (Ni$_{0.4}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$)O, (Ni$_{0.2}$Cu$_{0.2}$Zn$_{0.2}$Co$_{0.2}$Mg$_{0.2}$)O. Density functional theory, MCSQS-based structural modeling, and finite-temperature Gibbs free-energy analysis are combined to quantify the roles of enthalpy mixing ($ΔH_{mix}$), configurational ($ΔS_{conf}$), vibrational ($ΔS_{vib}$), and electronic contributions towards ($ΔS_{elec}$) entropy change in governing phase stability. The results show that $ΔS_{conf}$ alone is not a universal descriptor of phase stability. While the two-cation system is enthalpy-stabilized but three-, four- and five-cation systems become thermodynamically stable at high-temperature due to entropy-driven reduction of the Gibbs free energy. These findings demonstrate that single-phase rock-salt oxides are not restricted to the conventional high-entropy limit and that medium-entropy compositions can also be stabilized under suitable thermodynamic conditions.

Abstract: Alloying is a central strategy in electrocatalysis, enabling fine-tuning of electronic structure. In particular, compositionally complex solid solutions (CCSS) often called high-entropy alloys are of high interest as they allow active site design. However, the "combinatorial explosion" in the number of possible compositions poses a critical bottleneck for the discovery of active CCSS electrocatalysts. We present an autonomous scanning electrochemical cell microscopy (SECCM) system for ultrahigh-throughput and large-scale CCSS activity screening. Embedding analytical expressions of voltammetry in the algorithm enables the learning of whole voltammograms rather than a single selected metric. As a demonstration, we investigated hydrogen evolution reaction (HER) activities of Au-Ir-Rh, where Ir and Rh exhibit strong metal-hydrogen binding and Au exhibits relatively weak binding as derived from the HER volcano plot. The composition-activity trend was accurately predicted after measuring only 15% of all 966 measurement areas. Au30Ir20Rh50 and Au10Ir35Rh55 exhibit highest activities with standard rate constants of about 0.012 cm/s, demonstrating positive synergistic contributions from elemental mixing. ### [43] [Compressibility and High-Pressure Structure of CaMg$_2$Bi$_2$ and YbMg$_2$Bi$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00785)

Method: 采用熔融金属助熔剂法（molten metal flux method）合成单晶，利用单晶同步辐射X射线衍射（single-crystal synchrotron X-ray diffraction）结合金刚石对顶砧（diamond anvil cell）技术，在最高20 GPa的压力下进行原位结构表征。

Conclusion: CaMg₂Bi₂和YbMg₂Bi₂在高压下发生相变，生成了与同类化合物不同的C2/m畸变结构，揭示了AM₂X₂体系高压相行为的多样性，为进一步理解该类材料的结构-压力关系提供了依据。

Abstract: Compounds with the formula $AM_2X_2$ in the CaAl$_2$Si$_2$ structure type have garnered increasing interest across various solid-state research domains, such as quantum topological and thermoelectric materials. Prior studies have identified high-pressure phase transitions in several compounds, including Mg$_3$Sb$_2$, Mg$_3$Bi$_2$, CaMn$_2$Bi$_2$, and SrAl$_2$Si$_2$. We synthesized crystals using the molten metal flux method and examined them through single-crystal synchrotron X-ray diffraction, employing diamond anvil cells to exert pressures up to 20 GPa. Our analysis reveals insights into the anisotropic compressibility of these materials, highlighting the more compressible and flexible octahedral $A$-Bi bonds as the primary contributors to this anisotropy. Moreover, we observed a phase transition in both CaMg$_2$Bi$_2$ and YbMg$_2$Bi$_2$ at pressures above 9.6 GPa and 8.7 GPa, respectively. The newly identified high-pressure phase exhibits a distortion of the original CaAl$_2$Si$_2$ structure with space group $C2/m$. This high-pressure structure is distinct from that of related compounds (e.g., CaMn$_2$Bi$_2$, MgMg$_2$Bi$_2$), the latter exhibiting a square pyramidal coordination for the $M$ site.

*Swati Goyal,Karam Veer Singh,Rajiv O. Dusane,Triratna P. Muneshwar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过动力学建模与实验验证发现，在热丝化学气相沉积（HWCVD）制备氢化非晶硅（a-Si:H）薄膜时，采用脉冲式硅烷（SiH4）气流比连续气流能显著提高薄膜厚度（从~175 nm增至~425 nm）并改善电学性能（暗电导率降低、光电导率提高）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在热丝化学气相沉积（hot-wire chemical vapor deposition, HWCVD）制备氢化非晶硅（a-Si:H）薄膜过程中，通过改变前驱体硅烷（SiH4）的引入方式（连续流 vs. 脉冲流）来优化薄膜生长速率与电学性能的可能性。

Method: 假设催化解离（catalytic dissociation）机制，构建SiH4解离及a-Si:H薄膜生长的动力学模型（kinetic model）；引入脉冲气流模型，以时间间隔t_ON（设定流速）和t_OFF（流速为零）表征脉冲式SiH4流动；并通过实验对比相同SiH4剂量（75 cm^3, STP）下连续流与脉冲流（15次脉冲, t_ON=15s, t_OFF=60s）沉积的薄膜厚度与电学性质。

Result: 模型计算与实验一致表明：相同SiH4剂量下，脉冲流沉积的a-Si:H薄膜厚度（425 ± 8 nm）显著高于连续流（175 ± 5 nm）；脉冲流沉积薄膜的暗电导率（dark conductivity, σ_d）为1.1×10⁻¹¹ S/cm，光电导率（photoconductivity, σ_ph）为~5.8×10⁻⁵ S/cm，均优于连续流薄膜（σ_d~2.5×10⁻¹⁰ S/cm, σ_ph~3.5×10⁻⁶ S/cm）。

Conclusion: 脉冲式SiH4气流可有效提升HWCVD沉积a-Si:H薄膜的厚度与电学性能，为薄膜沉积工艺优化提供了新的策略。

Abstract: Hot-wire Chemical vapor deposition (HWCVD) of hydrogenated amorphous silicon (a-Si:H) thin films utilizes the dissociation of silane (SiH4) precursor over heated tungsten or tantalum filaments (\geq 1600 °C). In this work, assuming catalytic dissociation mechanism, we present kinetic model for SiH4 dissociation and the resulting a-Si:H film growth. Our model calculations showed that for an identical dose of the introduced SiH4 precursor, a-Si:H thickness was considerably higher for the pulsed SiH4 flow as compared to the continuous SiH4 flow. The pulsed SiH4 flow is represented by time intervals t_ON and t_OFF, where the SiH4 flow rate (F_(SiH_4)) is at the set-point and zero, respectively. In agreement with our model calculations for an introduced 75 cm^3 (STP) SiH4 dose, the resulting a-Si:H film thickness was 175 \pm 5 nm under continuous precursor flow, whereas it considerably increased to 425 \pm 8 nm when this SiH4 dose was split into 15 shorter pulses (t_ON =15s ; t_OFF = 60s). Moreover, these a-Si:H films deposited using pulsed SiH4 flow exhibited improved electrical properties, with a dark conductivity ({σ_d}) of 1.1 \times 10^-11 S/cm and a photoconductivity ({σ_ph}) of \sim 5.8 \times 10^-5 S/cm, compared to films deposited under continuous SiH4 flow (σ_d \sim 2.5 \times 10^-10 S/cm and σ_ph \sim 3.5 \times 10^-6 S/cm).

Abstract: Merging first-principles calculations with machine learning (ML), we aim to accelerate the exploration of catalytic behaviour in novel materials. We focus on two-dimensional (2D) Ti$_2$CT$_y$ MXenes, whose versatile surface chemistry makes them particularly compelling candidates for catalysis. Resolving their composition and structure under realistic conditions exceeds the reach of standard density functional theory (DFT) due to computational cost. To address this challenge, we generate a comprehensive dataset of 50,000 DFT calculations for training and 10,000 for testing, encompassing both Ti$_2$CT$_y$ MXene configurations and molecular systems, along with an additional test dataset with 1000 genuinely new, larger systems to investigate how well models generalise. We train and validate widely used and competitive machine learning interatomic potential (MLIP) models, including EquiformerV2, MACE, MatRIS, and UPET, that accurately predict atomic forces and formation energies -- quantities that DFT must repeatedly compute for structural and catalytic investigations -- for these 2D materials. Moreover, we perform an extensive qualitative evaluation of the trained models, showcasing the importance of comprehensive simulation-based comparison beyond benchmark metrics. The dataset and the trained models with the code are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/CatalystAnonymous/catalyst_mxenes.

Abstract: We have investigated the electronic structure and magnetotransport properties of SnSb$_6$Te$_{10}$ single crystals using density functional theory (DFT), synchrotron-based angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES), and quantum transport measurements. Our DFT calculations reveal a clear spin-orbit coupling driven band inversion between the Sb-$p$ and Te-$p$ states together with a non-trivial $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological invariant. The calculated surface-state dispersion and hexagonally warped Fermi surface contours agree well with the ARPES measurements. Temperature-dependent transport measurements indicate dominant electron-phonon scattering, while Hall measurements confirm hole-type carriers with carrier density of the order of $10^{21}$ cm$^{-3}$. Both transverse and longitudinal magnetotransport exhibit weak antilocalization behavior, while Shubnikov-de Haas oscillations observed for $H \parallel c$ yield a Berry phase close to $π$, consistent with Dirac-like surface states. Furthermore, angle-dependent magnetotransport measurements reveal pronounced anisotropy associated with an anisotropic Fermi surface topology and mixed bulk-surface transport behavior. Our combined theoretical and experimental results establish SnSb$_6$Te$_{10}$ as a strong topological insulator and a promising platform for investigating topological transport phenomena in layered telluride systems.

Abstract: Defect-engineered TiO$_2$ photocatalysts are extensively investigated for photocatalytic hydrogen evolution; however, the highly heterogeneous nature of the literature, including inconsistent descriptors, diverse synthesis protocols, non-uniform activity metrics, and incomplete mechanistic reporting, limits the applicability of conventional machine-learning approaches based solely on statistical regression. Here, we present a literature-grounded large language model (LLM)-assisted scientific reasoning framework for defect-engineered TiO$_2$ photocatalysts integrating curated literature data, mechanistic rule extraction, and retrieval-augmented reasoning. *Sourav Rajat Subhra Maitra,Poulami Manna,Ravi Prakash Singh,Chandrasekhar Murapaka,Arabinda Haldar*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用溅射沉积（sputter-deposited）方法制备Bi2Se3/NiFe异质结构，中间插入钛（titanium）间隔层；通过微波驱动铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance）诱导自旋进动（spin precession），实现自旋泵浦（spin pumping）将纯自旋电流（pure spin current）经钛层注入Bi2Se3，并改变Bi2Se3厚度进行系统性研究。

Result: 在4 nm Bi2Se3厚度下，吉尔伯特阻尼参数（Gilbert damping parameter）显著增加55%，表明纯表面态贡献；插入钛间隔层后，自旋霍尔角（spin Hall angle）提升一个数量级，归因于钛层抑制了Bi2Se3与NiFe之间的互扩散（interdiffusion），从而保护了拓扑表面态。

Conclusion: 钛间隔层在基于拓扑材料的自旋电子学器件中具有重要作用，可有效保护拓扑表面态并显著提升自旋-电荷转换效率。

Abstract: Topological insulators have attracted significant attention in spintronics due to their topological surface states and spin-momentum-locking-driven spin-to-charge conversion. Among these, Bi2Se3 has been extensively investigated because of its large bulk bandgap and single Dirac cone band structure. However, spin-to-charge conversion strongly depends on the quality of the topological insulator/ferromagnet interface. Here, we investigate spin-to-charge conversion in a sputter-deposited heterostructure comprising a topological insulator (Bi2Se3) and a ferromagnetic NiFe thin film separated by a titanium spacer layer. The Bi2Se3 layer is deposited on a silicon substrate for industrial compatibility. Pure spin current is injected into the Bi2Se3 layer through the titanium spacer via spin pumping induced by spin precession during microwave-driven ferromagnetic resonance of the ferromagnetic film. Spin pumping studies are performed by varying the Bi2Se3 thickness. The Gilbert damping parameter exhibits a significant 55% increase at a Bi2Se3 thickness of 4 nm, indicating a pure surface-state contribution. The spin Hall angle, which quantifies the spin-to-charge conversion efficiency, increases by an order of magnitude upon insertion of the titanium spacer layer. This enhancement is attributed to the suppression of interdiffusion between the Bi2Se3 and NiFe layers by titanium, thereby preserving the topological surface states. These findings highlight the important role of titanium spacer layers in spintronic devices based on topological materials.

### [49] [Stationarity-constrained representative volume elements for image-based homogenization of granular microstructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01248)
*Fernando Alonso-Marroquin,Abdullah Alqubalee,Christian Tantardini*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于图像的工作流程，用于化学映射颗粒微结构中代表性单元体积（REV）的尺寸确定。该流程将REV视为有限窗口收敛尺度，通过局部均值和标准差筛选平稳域，并采用持久均值-谱准则选择代表性支撑尺寸。在沙丘砂BSE图像上验证得到REV长度约为2.01–2.04 mm，并通过QEMSCAN物性均匀化独立验证了该毫米尺度估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有REV尺寸确定方法通常将REV视为分配给整幅非平稳（non-stationary）图像的全局长度，忽略了微结构内部的局部平稳性。为更准确地从化学映射颗粒微结构中确定REV，需开发一种依赖图像平稳域（stationary domains）的可复现工作流程。

Method: 全分辨率背散射电子（BSE）灰度图通过局部均值与标准差兼容性筛选平稳域；候选窗口仅在这些域内采样；采用持久均值-谱准则（persistent mean-spectral criterion），要求视在均值残差和低波数协方差谱残差在非参考尾部保持在容差内；并采用系综可复现性（ensemble reproducibility）作为辅助检验。

Result: 在7张沙丘砂BSE图像上应用严格平稳域准则，得到L_REV=1536像素（约2.01 mm，像素尺寸1.31 μm）。QEMSCAN物性均匀化独立给出L_REV^prop=204像素（约2.04 mm），与前者吻合。该尺度位于表观电导率、刚度和定向杨氏模量曲线的大窗口区域。

Conclusion: 该工作流程为化学映射颗粒微结构的REV尺寸确定提供了可复现的路径，并明确揭示了REV对平稳性（stationarity）、图像视场、窗口序列和目标观测量（target observable）的依赖关系。

Abstract: We present an image-based workflow for Representative Elementary Volume (REV) sizing in chemically mapped granular microstructures. The REV is treated as a finite-window convergence scale within approximately stationary material domains, rather than as a global length assigned to a non-stationary image. Full-resolution backscattered-electron (BSE) gray-level maps are screened by local mean and standard-deviation compatibility to identify stationary domains. Candidate windows are sampled only inside these domains, and the representative support is selected using a persistent mean--spectral criterion requiring both the apparent-mean residual and the low-wavenumber covariance-spectrum residual to remain within tolerance over the non-reference tail. Ensemble reproducibility is used as an auxiliary check. Applied to seven full-resolution BSE images of dune-sand microstructures, the strict stationary-domain criterion gives $(L_{\rm REV}=1536~\mathrm{pixels})$, corresponding to $(\ell_{\rm REV}\approx2.01~\mathrm{mm})$ for a BSE pixel size of $(1.31~μ\mathrm{m})$. Property-level homogenization on QEMSCAN-derived numerical maps independently supports this millimetre-scale estimate: the converted support is $(L_{\rm REV}^{\rm prop}=201.2)$ pixels and is snapped to the nearest tested size, $(L_{\rm REV}^{\rm prop}=204)$ pixels $(\ell_{\rm REV}^{\rm prop}=2.04~\mathrm{mm})$. This length lies in the large-window regime of the apparent conductivity, stiffness, and directional Young-modulus curves. The workflow provides a reproducible route for REV sizing while making explicit its dependence on stationarity, image field, window sequence, and target observable.

### [50] [How Can Machine Learning Accelerate CALPHAD Free Energy Modeling?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01305)
*Chen Shen,Muhammad Waqas Qureshi,Mark Asta,Izabela Szlufarska,Dane Morgan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合机器学习策略（ML4RK），通过将物理信息描述符嵌入Redlich-Kister框架，在保持热力学形式体系的可解释性和数据效率的同时，实现对未知二元体系相互作用参数的预测，从而拓展CALPHAD方法对新化学组分体系的建模能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CALPHAD框架虽为热力学建模提供了严格基础，但其预测新化学组分（new chemistries）的能力受限于有限的数据以及仅依赖组分（composition）的函数形式。

Method: 采用混合策略，通过物理信息元素描述符（physically informed elemental descriptors）学习Redlich-Kister（RK）相互作用系数；使用通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine-learning interatomic potential, MLIP）生成的14元素FCC合金形成能数据，对三类模型进行基准测试。

Result: 留一元素交叉验证（Leave-one-element-out tests）表明：基于组分的RK模型在拥有二元信息时数据效率最高；基于描述符的ML模型可实现训练集中未出现元素的零样本外推（zero-shot extrapolation）；混合方法ML4RK则将描述符嵌入RK框架，统一了上述两种机制，实现对未知或数据稀缺二元体系的相互作用参数预测。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一条兼具物理基础与数据效率的途径，通过将机器学习的可迁移性与热力学形式体系的物理基础、可解释性、数据效率和鲁棒性相结合，扩展了CALPHAD模型的能力。

Abstract: The CALPHAD framework provides a rigorous basis for thermodynamic modeling, yet its ability to predict new chemistries is restricted by limited data and by functional forms that rely heavily on composition alone. Here, we show that machine learning (ML) can address these challenges through a hybrid strategy that learns Redlich-Kister (RK) interaction coefficients directly from physically informed elemental descriptors. Using formation energies of 14-element FCC alloys generated by a universal machine-learning interatomic potential (MLIP), we benchmark three classes of models: (1) composition-based RK and ML models, (2) descriptor-based ML models, and (3) a combined ML-augmented RK approach (ML4RK). Leave-one-element-out tests highlight complementary strengths. RK models, class (1), remain the most data-efficient when binary information is available, while descriptor-based ML models, class (2), enable genuine zero-shot extrapolation to elements absent from the training set. By embedding elemental descriptors into the RK framework, the hybrid approach unifies these regimes and enables prediction of interaction parameters for otherwise unknown or data-scarce binaries, class (3). This work demonstrates a physically grounded and data-efficient route to extend CALPHAD models by combining the transferability of ML with the physical grounding, interpretability, data efficiency, and robustness of thermodynamic formalisms.

### [51] [Orbital Hall effect-driven spin-orbit torque enhancement in Ti-based systems via rare-earth interface engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01308)
*Rohiteswar Mondal,Chennoju Raghu,Animesh Baral,Arabinda Haldar,Chandrasekhar Murapaka*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过在钛（Ti）轨道源与钴（Co）铁磁体之间插入钆（Gd）中间层，实现了轨道转矩效率的五倍提升，并观察到超过1的自旋（轨道）转矩效率，表明稀土中间层工程是增强轨道转矩效率的有效策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻金属中的轨道电流（orbital current）虽能产生较大的轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity），但将其转化为实用的自旋轨道转矩（spin-orbit torque, SOT）效率存在根本性限制。本研究旨在通过引入Gd中间层来突破这一瓶颈。

Method: 采用Ti作为轨道源（orbital source），Co作为铁磁层，在两者之间插入Gd中间层构建Ti/Gd/Co三明治结构。利用基于铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）的自旋（轨道）泵浦测量和自旋转矩铁磁共振（spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance, ST-FMR）测量表征轨道转矩效率。

Result: 最优Gd厚度约为4 nm时轨道-自旋转换效率（orbital-to-spin conversion efficiency）达到最大；Ti中逆轨道霍尔效应（inverse orbital Hall effect）信号证实了体轨道霍尔效应（bulk orbital Hall origin），轨道扩散长度（orbital diffusion length）超过20 nm；Ti(20 nm)/Co的SOT效率相比Gd(4 nm)/Co参考样品提升五倍；Ti/Gd/Co三层的自旋（轨道）转矩效率大于1，且高于所有双层结构。

Conclusion: 稀土中间层工程（rare-earth interlayer engineering）是增强轨道转矩效率的可行技术路线，为下一代自旋轨道电子学（spin-orbitronics）器件提供了新的设计思路。

Abstract: Orbital currents in light metals offer large orbital Hall conductivities, yet translating this into practical spin-orbit torque efficiency is hindered by fundamental limitations. In this work, we introduce a Gd interlayer between a Ti orbital source and a Co ferromagnet to enhance the orbital torque efficiency. Ferromagnetic resonance-based spin (orbital) pumping measurements identify an optimal Gd thickness of around 4 nm, where the orbital-to-spin conversion efficiency reaches its maximum. The Ti-thickness dependence of the inverse orbital Hall effect signal confirms a bulk orbital Hall origin in Ti and yields a qualitative orbital diffusion length exceeding 20 nm. Spin-torque ferromagnetic resonance measurements demonstrate a fivefold enhancement of the SOT efficiency in Ti(20 nm)/Co compared to a Gd(4 nm)/Co reference. Interestingly, the trilayer Ti/Gd/Co architecture exhibits a spin (orbital) torque efficiency greater than 1, which is higher than that of the bilayer Ti/Co and Gd/Co structures, irrespective of Ti thickness. These results establish rare-earth interlayer engineering as a viable route to enhanced orbital torque efficiency for next-generation spin-orbitronic devices.

</details>

Method: 采用可转移的高分辨率薄金属掩模（transferable thin metal masks）结合富氧Ar+铣削（oxygen-enriched Ar+ milling）的无溶剂（solvent-free）图案化工艺。

Result: 输运测量显示，所制备的器件保留了本征性质，包括高载流子迁移率（high carrier mobilities），性能退化可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 该技术为工程化高性能氧化物电子器件提供了一条便捷且稳健的路径，能够精确调控器件的输运特性。

However, these interfaces are extremely susceptible to contamination and defect formation during nanofabrication, which often compromises device performance. Here, we present a solvent-free method for patterning oxide interfaces by employing high-resolution transferable thin metal masks in conjunction with oxygen-enriched Ar+ milling, which enables a clean and well-controlled nanofabrication process. Transport measurements demonstrate that the fabricated devices preserve their intrinsic properties, including high carrier mobilities, with negligible degradation compared to the pristine interfaces. ### [53] [Resonant Raman scattering in bilayer 3R-MoS$_{2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01350)
*Chinmay K. Mohanty,Kacper Walczyk,Tomasz Woźniak,Chengcheng Jiang,Adam Babiński,Clement Faugeras,Zhaolong Chen,Maciej R. Molas*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过多波长拉曼光谱、光致发光测量和密度泛函理论计算，系统研究了双层3R-MoS₂的随温度变化的共振拉曼响应，揭示了激子-声子耦合（exciton-phonon coupling）中入射共振与出射共振过程的竞争机制，以及共振效应引起的有效声子温度与晶格温度的显著偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拉曼散射（Raman scattering）是研究二维材料中光-物质相互作用和晶格动力学的有力光谱技术，但温度依赖的共振拉曼响应及其背后的激子-声子耦合机制仍需要更深入的理解。

Method: 研究结合了多波长拉曼光谱（multi-wavelength Raman spectroscopy）、光致发光测量（photoluminescence measurements）和密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，用于追踪激子跃迁（excitonic transitions）和共振条件（resonance conditions）的演化。

Result: 观察到来自中心声子和有限动量声子（finite-momentum phonons）的贡献；斯托克斯强度（Stokes intensity）在低温下显著淬灭后趋于饱和；反斯托克斯散射（anti-Stokes scattering）在130 K以上出现；共振效应导致有效声子温度（effective phonon temperature）与晶格温度（lattice temperature）出现强烈偏离。

Conclusion: 拉曼响应由入射共振（incoming resonance）与出射共振（outgoing resonance）过程的相互作用主导，这为理解范德华材料（van der Waals materials）中的激子-声子耦合提供了更深入的见解。

Abstract: Raman scattering is a powerful spectroscopic technique widely employed to investigate light-matter interactions and lattice dynamics in two-dimensional materials. Here, we investigate the temperature-dependent resonant Raman response of bilayer 3R-MoS$_2$. The study combines multi-wavelength Raman spectroscopy, photoluminescence measurements, and density functional theory calculations to track the evolution of excitonic transitions and resonance conditions. We observe contributions from both zone-centre and finite-momentum phonons, a pronounced quenching of the Stokes intensity at low temperatures followed by saturation, the emergence of anti-Stokes scattering above 130~K, and a strong deviation of the effective phonon temperature from the lattice temperature induced by resonance effects. These results demonstrate that the Raman response is governed by the interplay between incoming and outgoing resonance processes, providing deeper insight into exciton-phonon coupling in van der Waals materials.

### [54] [Flat interface between amorphous ices and the role of MDA-like intermediate states in the LDA-HDA transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01401)
*Anastasiia Shupletsova,Vladimir Stegailov*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次表征了低密度无定形冰（LDA）与高密度无定形冰（HDA）之间的平坦界面，确定了其平衡厚度，并揭示了该界面与中等密度无定形冰（MDA）的联系。研究发现界面厚度在压缩下保持不变，但其位置可逆地向LDA区移动，呈现弹性响应及动力学迟滞；同时，利用基于SOAP描述符的神经网络分类器（neural network classifier），证实中间无定形态（IA）并非独立体相，而是局域于LDA-HDA界面上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低密度无定形冰（LDA）与高密度无定形冰（HDA）之间的压力诱导转变是多晶型相变（polyamorphic transition）的典型范例，但其微观机制——尤其是中间无定形态（intermediate amorphous, IA）的性质——长期未获解析。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟构建平坦的LDA-HDA界面并表征其平衡厚度；利用基于SOAP（Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions）描述符的神经网络分类器（neural network classifier）对无定形冰进行高精度区分，系统描述局域结构并融入氢键网络（hydrogen bond network）的取向信息。

Result: 界面厚度在压缩过程中保持恒定，但其位置随压缩可逆地向LDA区域移动，呈现弹性响应；减压时出现动力学迟滞（kinetic hysteresis），类似记忆效应（memory effect）。MDA-like的中间无定形态（IA）构型并非独立体相，而是局域化于LDA-HDA界面之上。

Conclusion: LDA-HDA转变的中间态本质上是一种界面局域现象，而非体相；SOAP结合神经网络的方法为区分无定形冰结构提供了高精度工具，并强调了氢键网络取向信息在描述局域结构中的关键作用。

Abstract: The pressure-induced transformation between low-density amorphous ice (LDA) and high-density amorphous ice (HDA) is a prototypical polyamorphic transition, yet its microscopic mechanism - and in particular the nature of intermediate amorphous (IA) states - has long remained unresolved. We present the first characterisation of a flat LDA||HDA interface, determining its equilibrium thickness and showing its link to medium-density amorphous ice (MDA). Interestingly, the thickness of the interfacial layer remains constant under compression, while its position shifts reversibly into the LDA region - an elastic response that exhibits kinetic hysteresis upon decompression, reminiscent of memory effects. For high-precision discrimination of amorphous ices, we use a neural network classifier based on SOAP (Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions) descriptors. The systematic description of the local structure emphasizes the importance of orientational information from the hydrogen bond network. Furthermore, this approach enables molecular dynamics analysis of the LDA-to-HDA transformation, directly mapping the spatial distribution of intermediate structures relative to growing HDA domains and the surrounding LDA matrix, and revealing that MDA-like IA configurations are not a distinct bulk phase but rather localise at the LDA-HDA interface.

### [55] [Altermagnetism in MnF$_2$: Band Splitting and Its Physical Consequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01515)
*Igor Solovyev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 基于电子结构计算，本文构建了描述MnF₂最小模型，发现其交变磁（altermagnetic）能带分裂参数较小；系统处于强耦合（strong-coupling）区间，交换作用按1/U标度，导致交变磁对反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）的贡献被压制；但在光子能量ℏω~U时，由于δt直接进入带间跃迁能量，光学电导率张量被显著重塑，磁光响应大幅增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MnF₂被广泛认为是候选交变磁体（altermagnet），但其交变磁能带分裂的大小和物理含义仍存在争议，亟需通过理论建模加以澄清。

Method: 采用电子结构计算（electronic-structure calculations），构建能够描述MnF₂磁性与电子性质的最小模型（minimal models）。

Result: 手征磁振子分裂（chiral magnon splitting）和电子能带自旋分裂（spin splitting）的参数均较小；电子系统处于强耦合区间（strong-coupling regime），多数磁性由比率t/U控制；交变磁跳跃δt仅产生成比例的小交换项；掺杂后交变磁对反常霍尔效应的贡献被抑制，比常规贡献小约δt/U量级；但在ℏω~U时，δt直接出现在带间光学跃迁能量中，显著重塑电导率张量并增强磁光响应。

Conclusion: MnF₂中交变磁参数在多数磁性响应中因t/U与δt/U的小比率而被压制，但在高频光学响应（ℏω~U）中由于δt的直接贡献，磁光效应可获得显著增强，这为实验探测交变磁分裂提供了可行的光学途径。

Abstract: MnF$_2$ is widely regarded as a candidate altermagnet, but the magnitude and implications of its altermagnetic band splitting remain debated. Using electronic-structure calculations, we construct minimal models that capture the magnetic and electronic properties of MnF$_2$. These models show that the parameters governing the chiral magnon splitting and the spin splitting of the electronic bands are relatively small. Moreover, the electronic system lies in the strong-coupling regime, where most magnetic properties are controlled by the ratio $t/U$ between the characteristic hopping amplitude $t$ and the large on-site Coulomb repulsion $U$. Consequently, all exchange interactions scale as $1/U$, so a small altermagnetic hopping $δt$ produces only a proportionally small exchange term. Upon doping, the altermagnetic contribution to the anomalous Hall effect is likewise suppressed, being smaller than the conventional (non-altermagnetic) contribution by a factor of order $δt/U$. In contrast, the behavior of the conductivity tensor $\hatσ(ω)$ at $\hbar ω\sim U$ differs qualitatively, because $δt$ enters the energies of interband optical transitions \emph{directly} rather than through the reduced ratio $δt/U$. This contribution strongly reshapes $\hatσ(ω)$, leading to a dramatic enhancement of the magneto-optical response.

### [56] [Hydrogen trapping and interfacial decohesion at the α-Al2O3(0001)/Fe(110) interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01748)
*Youngseok Hwang,Norihito Sakaguchi,Yuji Kunisada*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）系统研究了α-Al₂O₃(0001)/Fe(110)界面的热力学稳定性、氢陷阱能量学及氢致解聚（hydrogen-induced decohesion）机制。结果表明，单氢原子优先稳定于Fe中空位，氢浓度升高会逐渐减小自由体积并增大晶格畸变，最终导致界面解理能为负，发生自发性界面剥落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）和氚泄漏对聚变反应堆结构部件构成严重挑战，因此α-Al₂O₃/Fe界面作为氚渗透屏障（tritium permeation barrier）至关重要。理解该界面的氢致解聚机制，是优化高性能渗透屏障的理论前提。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）对α-Al₂O₃(0001)/Fe(110)界面进行系统性第一性原理计算，涵盖单氢和多氢原子掺入条件下的热力学稳定性、陷阱能（trapping energetics）以及模拟解理过程。

Result: 单氢情形下，Fe中空位（Fe-hollow site）是最稳定的陷阱区域，归因于局部自由体积（local free volume）和异质界面键合（heterogeneous interfacial bonding）。多氢分析表明陷阱行为具有浓度依赖性；随氢浓度增加，可用自由体积逐渐减少，局部晶格畸变增大。模拟解理能随氢积累单调下降，高浓度下解理能为负，表明界面发生自发性剥落（spontaneous interfacial exfoliation）。

Conclusion: 这些定量结果阐明了保护性氧化膜（protective oxide scales）的原子尺度退化机制，为优化聚变相关钢材中的高性能渗透屏障提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Hydrogen embrittlement and tritium leakage pose critical challenges for fusion reactor structural components, rendering α-Al2O3/Fe interfaces vital as tritium permeation barriers. Here, the thermodynamic stability, trapping energetics, and hydrogen-induced decohesion at the α-Al2O3 (0001)/Fe(110) interface were systematically investigated using density functional theory. Single-hydrogen incorporation reveals that the Fe-hollow site is the most stable trapping region, owing to local free volume and heterogeneous interfacial bonding. Multi-hydrogen analysis demonstrates that trapping behavior is concentration-dependent; increasing hydrogen concentration progressively reduces the available free volume and increases local lattice distortion. As a result, simulated cleavage processes show a monotonic decrease in cleavage energy with accumulation. At high hydrogen concentrations, cleavage energy turns negative, indicating spontaneous interfacial exfoliation. These quantitative insights clarify the atomistic degradation mechanisms of protective oxide scales, offering a theoretical framework for optimizing high-performance permeation barriers in fusion-relevant steels.

### [57] [Polaron Transport in TiO$_{2}$ from Machine Learning Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01763)
*Christian S. Ahart,Denan Li,Jochen Blumberger,Shi Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出DeepPolaron——一种机器学习框架，将绝热极化子输运的第一性原理分子动力学可模拟时间尺度提升三个数量级，并应用于金红石和锐钛矿二氧化钛中过剩电子与空穴的极化子输运研究，揭示了各自的局域化特征、迁移路径、激活能及室温迁移率，与实验吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属氧化物作为光电催化剂备受关注，但其低且各向异性的电荷迁移率阻碍了实际应用。深入理解此类材料中的过剩载流子输运需要超越标准方法的核运动动力学处理。

Method: 引入DeepPolaron机器学习框架，将绝热极化子输运（adiabatic polaron transport）的第一性原理分子动力学（first principles molecular dynamics）可模拟时间尺度提升三个数量级，且精度损失可忽略不计。

Result: 金红石中过剩电子弛豫为局域在单个Ti原子上的极化子，沿[001]方向跳跃输运，激活能（activation energy）为39 meV，室温迁移率（room temperature mobility）为$4.4 \times 10^{-2}$ cm²/Vs；锐钛矿中空穴极化子局域在单个O原子上，因O 2p轨道与第一近邻轨道重叠较差，电荷主要向第二近邻输运，激活能为139 meV，室温迁移率为$1.4 \times 10^{-3}$ cm²/Vs。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了金红石和锐钛矿中小极化子输运的有限温度第一性原理表征，所建立的方法可直接迁移至其他小极化子形成材料及界面电荷转移过程的研究中。

Abstract: Transition metal oxides have attracted much attention as photo(electrochemical)-catalysts but practical applications are typically hampered by their low and anisotropic charge mobility. A deep understanding of excess charge carrier transport in these materials requires a dynamical treatment of nuclear motion that goes well beyond standard approaches. Here we introduce DeepPolaron, a machine learning framework boosting the accessible time scale of first principles molecular dynamics of adiabatic polaron transport by three orders of magnitude at a virtually negligible loss in accuracy. We apply our method to excess electron and hole transport in titanium dioxide rutile and anatase. We find that the excess electron in rutile relaxes to a polaron predominantly localized on a single Ti atom with hopping occurring only along the [001] direction, associated with an activation energy of 39 meV and a room temperature mobility of $4.4 \times 10^{-2}$ cm$^2$/Vs in good agreement with experiment. In contrast the hole polaron in anatase is localized on a single O atom, and due to poor O 2p orbital overlap with first nearest neighbors charge transport occurs primarily to second nearest neighbors, with a large activation energy of 139 meV resulting in a small room temperature mobility of $1.4 \times 10^{-3}$ cm$^2$/Vs. This work provides a finite temperature first-principles characterization of small polaron transport in rutile and anatase, with a methodology that is directly transferable to other small polaron forming materials and interfacial charge-transfer processes.

### [58] [Iterative Thermodynamic Augmentation of Spatially Resolved Analytic Microscopy for Fast-Diffusing Solutes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01793)
*Santiago Benito,Louis Becker,Niels Jöns,Sebastian Weber*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出一种计算框架，通过热力学模型将实验测得的置换型溶质元素空间分布图转换为间隙型溶质元素的定量浓度分布图，以解决快速扩散溶质难以空间分辨定量的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 间隙型合金元素在物理冶金（physical metallurgy）中作用关键，但快速扩散溶质（fast-diffusing solutes）的空间分辨定量在分析显微术（analytic microscopy）中面临诸多挑战，现有实验手段难以高效获取其定量空间分布。

Method: 采用迭代热力学模型（iterative thermodynamic model）：利用固态扩散动力学（solid-state diffusion kinetics）的巨大差异，假设仅移动间隙物种（mobile interstitial species）处于部分化学平衡（partial chemical equilibrium）；通过优化方案迭代调整整个显微组织映射下的均匀间隙化学势（uniform interstitial chemical potential），直至局部浓度积分值与独立测量的体相值（bulk value）收敛。

Result: 该方法能从稳健、低噪声的显微术数据中提取热力学自洽的间隙浓度映射图（interstitial concentration maps），得到定量的空间阵列（quantitative spatial arrays）。

Conclusion: 该计算框架可有效弥补实验手段的不足，在时间和资源成本上具有显著优势，为快速扩散溶质的空间定量分析提供了可行的替代方案。

Abstract: The spatially resolved quantification of fast-diffusing solutes presents several challenges in analytic microscopy. Given the critical role of interstitially alloyed elements in physical metallurgy, we propose a computational framework that addresses this limitation by augmenting spatially resolved composition maps of substitutional elements with computationally derived interstitial distributions. The underlying methodology is an iterative thermodynamic model: exploiting the stark differences in solid-state diffusion kinetics, the model assumes a state of partial chemical equilibrium exclusively for the mobile interstitial species. An optimization scheme iteratively adjusts an uniform interstitial chemical potential across the mapped microstructure until the integrated local concentration converges with an independently measured bulk value. Ultimately, this approach extracts thermodynamically consistent interstitial concentration maps from robust, low-noise microscopy data, yielding quantitative spatial arrays that are otherwise time- and resource-intensive to obtain at best.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统二维过渡金属二硫族化物（TMDs）在柔性纳米电子应用中易因晶格变形发生间接-直接带隙跃迁，影响性能；Janus TMDs 虽因破缺镜面对称性和面外偶极矩具有静电调控潜力，但其在应变下的电子稳定性及异质结构中硫族堆叠序列的作用尚不清楚。

Method: 采用第一性原理（first principles）计算，系统研究了 MoSSe/WSSe 异质双层（heterobilayer）不同构型的应变容忍度和压电特性，分析了界面化学对层间耦合、动态电荷重分布和偶极相互作用的调制机制。

Result: 界面化学显著调控层间耦合与电荷重分布；内禀电场与界面静电效应的协同作用有效抑制了传统 TMDs 中典型的应变诱导带隙跃迁；面内压电响应几乎不受堆叠顺序影响，而剪切压电系数强烈依赖于界面对称性，并可通过应变调制进行有效调控。

Conclusion: 界面工程是设计抗应变 Janus 异质结构的有力途径，为新一代柔性光电子（optoelectronic）、谷电子（valleytronic）和压电电子（piezotronic）器件提供了理论指导。

Abstract: The electronic structure of conventional two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) is highly sensitive to lattice deformation, often leading to indirect-to-direct band-gap transitions that compromise performance in flexible nanoelectronic applications. Janus TMDs, with their broken mirror symmetry and intrinsic out-of-plane dipoles, offer a promising alternative platform for electrostatic tuning. However, their electronic stability under strain and the role of the chalcogen stacking sequence in their heterostructures remains poorly understood. Here, we study from first principles the strain tolerance and piezoelectric properties of MoSSe/WSSe heterobilayers. By examining different configurations, we demonstrate that the interface chemistry strongly modulates interlayer coupling, dynamic charge redistribution, and dipole interactions. Importantly, the combined effects of intrinsic electric fields and interface electrostatics effectively suppress the strain-induced band-gap transitions typical of conventional TMDs. Moreover, while the in-plane piezoelectric response remains nearly insensitive to the stacking order, the shear piezoelectric coefficient depends heavily on the interfacial symmetry and can be effectively tuned by strain modulation. Our results highlight interfacial engineering as a powerful route to design strain-resilient Janus heterostructures for next-generation flexible optoelectronic, valleytronic, and piezotronic devices.

</details>


### [60] [Room-Temperature Electric-Field Control of Anomalous Hall Effect in Py/BTO/LSMO Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02298)
*Kusampal Yadav,Kousik Das,Aditya Raj,Mainak Ghosh,Abhishek Kumar,Kartick Biswas,Kalyan Sarkar,Pavan Nukala,Sayantika Bhowal,Devajyoti Mukherjee*

TL;DR: 本文在Ni80Fe20/BaTiO3/La0.7Sr0.3MnO3异质结中实现了室温电场控制反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect），通过衬底诱导应变调控磁各向异性，在0.5 V和2 V低电压下实现了近93%的霍尔电阻率调制，密度泛函理论（DFT）计算揭示了铁电序（ferroelectric order）与Rashba自旋劈裂（Rashba spin splitting）之间的直接关联。

Method: 在MgO和LaAlO3衬底上外延生长Ni80Fe20 (Py)/BaTiO3 (BTO)/La0.7Sr0.3MnO3 (LSMO)薄膜异质结；利用压电力显微镜（piezoresponse force microscopy, PFM）确认BTO的铁电极化（ferroelectric polarization）；结合输运测量与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算进行分析。

Result: 衬底诱导的应变状态产生不同的磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropies），实现了反常霍尔效应与拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect）之间的电压驱动调控；BTO的强铁电极化与界面轨道重构（interfacial orbital reconstruction）及载流子再分布（carrier redistribution）强耦合，在0.5 V和2 V下实现近93%的霍尔电阻率（Hall resistivity）调制。

Conclusion: Py/BTO/LSMO异质结构是实现低功耗多功能自旋电子器件的候选体系，通过衬底工程（substrate engineering）可实现对涌现量子输运现象（emergent quantum transport phenomena）的调控。

Abstract: We demonstrate room temperature electric field control of the anomalous Hall effect in epitaxial Ni80Fe20 (Py) BaTiO3 (BTO) La0.7Sr0.3MnO3 (LSMO) thin film heterostructures grown on MgO and LaAlO3 substrates. Substrate induced strain states generate distinct magnetic anisotropies, enabling voltage driven tuning between anomalous and topological Hall contributions. Robust ferroelectric polarization in BTO, confirmed by piezoresponse force microscopy, couples strongly to interfacial orbital reconstruction and carrier redistribution. As a result, Hall resistivity exhibits giant low voltage tunability, with up to nearly 93 percent modulation at operating voltages of only 0.5 tand 2 V. Density functional theory calculations further reveal polarization controlled Rashba spin splitting, establishing a direct link between ferroelectric order and emergent quantum transport. These findings establish Py/BTO/LSMO heterostructures as promising candidates for low-power multifunctional spintronic devices, where substrate engineering enables control over emergent quantum transport phenomena.

### [61] [Surface Modification for III-V Selective Area Molecular Beam Epitaxy of Non-Selective Mask Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02317)
*Ashlee M. García,Byron D. Aguilar,William J. Doyle,Pernille Undrum Fathi,Federico Capasso,Daniel Wasserman,Seth R. Bank*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文评估了Al₂O₃、TiO₂和HfO₂作为分子束外延（MBE）选区生长替代掩膜材料的可行性，发现Al₂O₃在GaAs生长温度下具有良好选择性，而HfO₂和TiO₂则表现出非选择性或反应性。通过引入亚1 nm SiO₂覆盖层，成功实现了对非选择性及反应性掩膜材料的选区生长，并保留了其优异的光学响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统SiO₂和Si₃N₄掩膜在红外波段消光系数较高，限制了高对比度光子学器件的设计，因此需要探索具有更优光谱响应的替代掩膜材料，以拓展选区分子束外延（selective-area molecular beam epitaxy）在III-V半导体集成中的应用能力。

Method: 采用分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy, MBE）方法进行选区嵌入再生长，评估了Al₂O₃、TiO₂和HfO₂薄膜的沉积选择性；针对非选择性和反应性材料，通过沉积薄层SiO₂覆盖层（sub-1 nm capping layer）进行表面修饰以改善选择性生长特性。

Result: Al₂O₃在典型GaAs生长温度下表现出良好的选择性生长特性；HfO₂在高达650°C时呈现高非选择性，主要表现为Ga在掩膜上的吸附；TiO₂在沉积过程中具有反应性。通过施加薄SiO₂覆盖层，成功实现了Si₃N₄和TiO₂的选区生长，且亚1 nm覆盖层即可显著改变掩膜表面化学性质。

Conclusion: 沉积薄层SiO₂可以使任意掩膜材料实现类似SiO₂的选择性，同时不降低其光学响应，为高对比度红外光子学器件的设计提供了新的掩膜材料选择策略。

Abstract: Selective-area embedded regrowth of III-V semiconductors by molecular beam epitaxy enables the seamless integration of metals and dielectrics into crystalline material for novel design of optoelectronic devices. However, traditional masks like $SiO_2$ and $Si_{3}N_{4}$ limit the design of high-contrast photonics in the infrared due to their high extinction coefficients at technologically relevant wavelengths. Consequently, there is a need to explore alternative mask materials to expand the selective area molecular beam epitaxy capabilities beyond those traditionally used. This study evaluates the deposition selectivity of the alternative materials $Al_{2}O_{3}$, $TiO_2$, and $HfO_2$, films with preferable spectral responses but higher surface reactivity. It was found that $Al_{2}O_{3}$ exhibits promising selective growth characteristics within typical GaAs growth temperatures, $HfO_2$ demonstrated a high non-selectivity dominated by Ga adsorption on the mask at temperatures up to 650 $^\circ$C, and $TiO_2$ proved reactive during deposition. To achieve selective growth of highly non-selective and even reactive mask materials, a surface modification technique was employed to improve the selective growth characteristics of any given film. Selective growth of $Si_{3}N_{4}$ and $TiO_2$ films was achieved with the application of a thin $SiO_2$ capping layer utilizing growth conditions typical of the GaAs/$SiO_2$ system. The relationship between the thickness of $SiO_2$ caps and growth selectivity was examined, revealing that sub-1 nm capping layers can significantly influence the mask surface chemistry, indicating that by depositing a thin layer of $SiO_2$, $SiO_2$-like selectivity for any mask material can be realized without degrading its optical response.

### [62] [DPA4: Pushing the Accuracy-Cost Frontier of Interatomic Potentials with EMFA SO(2) Convolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02419)
*Tiancheng Li,Wentao Li,Anyang Peng,Jianming Xue,Linfeng Zhang,Duo Zhang,Han Wang*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出DPA4，一种基于SE(3)-等变和EMFA SO(2)-等变卷积的机器学习原子间势架构，通过低秩边缘-节点乘积、多焦点设计、包络门控注意力及Lebedev网格投影等技术，在训练效率（torch.compile加速约3倍）和精度-计算成本帕累托前沿上显著超越现有基线模型（如eSEN），成为大规模原子模型预训练的有力候选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有最具表现力的等变（equivariant）原子间势架构训练成本高，已成为严重瓶颈；需要在保持量子力学精度的前提下降低训练开销并提升计算效率。

Method: 引入DPA4架构，核心是EMFA（Edge-conditioned, Multi-Focus, Attention）SO(2)-等变卷积，包含低秩边缘-节点SO(2)-等变乘积、多焦点消息非线性设计、以及包络门控注意力（envelope-gated attention）用于消息聚合；此外采用Lebedev网格投影将非线性中的SO(3)-等变性保持至机器精度，并采用编译器友好的保守能量梯度训练路径以利用torch.compile实现约3倍加速。

Result: DPA4-Pro在Matbench Discovery榜单取得最佳综合性能分数（CPS）；DPA4-Air（2.76M参数）以10.9倍更少参数和42.9倍更少训练计算量超越eSEN-30M-MP（30.1M参数）的精度；在SPICE-MACE-OFF上，DPA4-Plus（5.4M参数）将分子能量和力误差分别降低29%和30%，DPA4-Air（2.7M参数）以约2.4倍更少参数仍超越6.5M参数的eSEN基线。

Conclusion: DPA4在Matbench Discovery上确立了新的精度-成本帕累托前沿（accuracy-cost Pareto frontier），并成为未来多任务大规模原子模型（large atomistic model, LAM）预训练的强有力候选骨干架构。

Abstract: Machine-learning interatomic potentials now approach quantum-mechanical accuracy on standard benchmarks, but the training cost of the most expressive equivariant architectures has become a serious bottleneck. We introduce DPA4, an SE(3)-equivariant interatomic-potential architecture with an EMFA (Edge-conditioned, Multi-Focus, Attention) SO(2)-equivariant convolution that combines a low-rank edge-node SO(2)-equivariant product, a multi-focus design for message nonlinearity, and envelope-gated attention for message aggregation. A Lebedev-grid projection further preserves SO(3)-equivariance in the nonlinearity to machine precision. A compiler-friendly conservative energy-gradient training path provides up to $\sim$3 times wall-clock speedup under torch.compile. On the compliant Matbench Discovery benchmark, DPA4-Pro attains the best Combined Performance Score (CPS) on the leaderboard, while the 2.76M-parameter DPA4-Air exceeds the accuracy of the 30.1M-parameter eSEN-30M-MP baseline with 10.9$\times$ fewer parameters and 42.9$\times$ less training compute. On SPICE-MACE-OFF, the 5.4M-parameter DPA4-Plus lowers the aggregate molecular energy and force errors of the 6.5M-parameter eSEN baseline by 29% and 30%, while the 2.7M-parameter DPA4-Air still surpasses that baseline with $\sim$2.4$\times$ fewer parameters. Together these results place DPA4 on a new accuracy-cost Pareto frontier on Matbench Discovery and position it as a strong candidate backbone for future multi-task large atomistic model (LAM) pretraining.

### [63] [Aharonov-Casher Chern bands for ultracold dark state atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00207)
*Domantas Burba,Dominykas Borodinas,Gediminas Juzeliūnas*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究超冷原子在Λ型原子-光耦合方案中绝热跟随暗态时的Aharonov-Casher条件，推导了该条件成立的一般要求，并发现通过适当组合两种非理想因素（偏离精细调谐和有限耦合强度），可以获得完全平坦的最低能带，其拓扑性质适合模拟分数量子霍尔态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Λ型原子-光耦合方案中，超冷原子绝热跟随暗态时会受到几何标量势（geometric scalar potential）和合成磁场（synthetic magnetic field）的影响。Aharonov-Casher条件建立了二者之间的关系，但该条件在何种原子-光耦合下成立尚不明确，且如何在实际系统中实现完全平坦的最低能带以模拟分数量子霍尔态（fractional Hall states）仍有待探索。

Method: 从理论上推导了Aharonov-Casher条件对原子-光耦合的一般要求，即Λ方案中的Rabi频率（Rabi frequencies）必须是具有适当振幅和相位的平面波叠加。特别考察了由N=3, 4, 6个精细调谐平面波构成的Rabi频率情形，并分析了偏离精细调谐以及有限原子-光耦合强度对最低能带的影响。

Result: 精细调谐的N=3, 4, 6个平面波可获得符号确定的平滑背景磁场及一组不可测量的Aharonov-Bohm通量奇点（Aharonov-Bohm flux singularities）。偏离精细调谐时，奇点展宽为相反磁场的窄亚波长斑块，从而展宽最低能带。精细调谐时由于偏离绝热近似，有限耦合强度也会展宽最低能带。适当组合这两种非理想因素可使最低能带完全平坦，且具有模拟分数量子霍尔态所需的完美拓扑性质（topology）。

Conclusion: Aharonov-Casher条件在Rabi频率为特定平面波叠加时成立。通过调控偏离精细调谐和有限原子-光耦合强度这两个非理想因素的组合，可以在实验中实现完全平坦的最低朗道能级（lowest Landau-level-like band），为模拟分数量子霍尔态提供了可行的理论方案。

Abstract: We consider the Aharonov-Casher (AC) condition for ultracold atoms adiabatically following the dark-state in a $Λ$-type atom-light coupling scheme. The AC condition establishes a relation between the geometric scalar potential and the synthetic magnetic field, resulting in a fully degenerate lowest Landau-level-like band even if the magnetic field is inhomogeneous but has a proper sign. We derive a general requirement for the atom-light coupling under which the AC condition applies. The requirement holds if the Rabi frequencies of the $Λ$ scheme are the superposition of plane waves with the appropriate amplitudes and phases. In particular, the Rabi frequencies made of $N=3,\,4,\,6$ fine tuned plane waves yield a smooth background magnetic field of definite sign, as well as an array of non-measurable Aharonov-Bohm flux singularities. Departing from the fine tuning, the latter singularities broaden into narrow subwavelength patches of the opposite magnetic field, which broaden the lowest energy band. The lowest band is broadened also for the fine tuned situation due to deviation from the adiabatic approach because of the finite atom-light coupling strength. It is shown that a proper combination of the two imperfections (departure from fine tuning and finite atom-light coupling strength) can lead to a completely flat lowest band, which furthermore is characterized by the perfect topology needed for simulating the fractional Hall states.

</details>


### [64] [Energy spectra and cascade in the spin turbulence of a driven spinor Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00766)
*Junghoon Lee,Jongmin Kim,Donggyu Lee,Yong-il Shin*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文通过实验驱动自旋-1玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体，观测到自旋相互作用的能量谱遵循 -7/3 幂律标度，并在撤去驱动后观察到向高波数方向传递的自旋相互作用能量级联，从而确立了自旋湍流的能量谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深入理解自旋湍流（spin turbulence）这一非平衡稳态系统中的能量谱行为及其级联（cascade）动力学。

Method: 对自旋-1玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（spinor Bose-Einstein condensate）施加连续自旋驱动，产生具有空间起伏磁化强度的非平衡稳态，随后撤去驱动跟踪自由衰变（free-decay）演化过程。

Result: 观测到与自旋波湍流（spin-wave turbulence）预测的 -7/3 指数一致的幂律标度（power-law scaling）；该标度在全部驱动强度范围内持续存在，且不依赖谱各向异性（spectral anisotropy）的显著变化；撤去驱动后，观测到自旋相互作用能量向高波数方向的直接级联（direct cascade）证据。

Conclusion: 确立了自旋湍流的一个能量谱标志性特征，为自旋超流体（spinor superfluids）中级联动力学的定量研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We investigate the spin-interaction energy spectrum of spin turbulence in a driven spinor Bose-Einstein condensate. Continuous spin driving of a spin-1 condensate produces a nonequilibrium steady state with spatially fluctuating magnetization. We observe a power-law scaling consistent with the $-7/3$ exponent predicted for spin-wave turbulence, which persists across our full range of drive strengths despite substantial changes in the spectral anisotropy. After switching off the drive, we track the free-decay evolution and find evidence consistent with a direct cascade of spin-interaction energy toward higher wavenumbers. These results establish an energy-spectral hallmark of spin turbulence and enable quantitative studies of cascade dynamics in spinor superfluids.

### [65] [Three- and four-boson systems expanded around the unitarity limit: Application to $^4$He](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00854)
*Feng Wu,Xincheng Lin,Ubirajara van Kolck,Sebastian König*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在短程有效场论（Short-Range Effective Field Theory）框架下，系统研究了大散射长度、短有效力程的三体和四体玻色子系统。通过将领头阶取为通用的幺正极限（unitarity limit），并微扰引入有限散射长度、有效力程及四体力修正，结合Faddeev-Yakubovsky形式与图解方法，计算了束缚能与半径。结果表明，$^4$He原子团簇的物理仅受离散尺度不变性（discrete scale invariance）的小偏差支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 摘要未明确提及动机，但隐含动机是：在有效场论框架下统一描述大散射长度玻色子系统的三体和四体特性，并检验$^4$He原子团簇是否接近离散尺度不变性极限。

Method: 领头阶（leading order）取为通用的幺正极限（unitarity limit），此时两体系统无自由参数，仅需一个三体参数；次领头阶（next-to-leading order）微扰引入有限散射长度和有效力程修正，以及重整化所需的四体力。使用Faddeev-Yakubovsky（FY）形式及其互补的图解方法求解三体基态及四体基态和第一激发态；在四体计算中移除深度三聚体贡献以扩展截止值范围。

Result: $^4$He三原子和四原子团簇的束缚能与半径计算结果与使用复杂唯象势得到的结果良好收敛。

Conclusion: $^4$He原子团簇的物理仅由离散尺度不变性（discrete scale invariance）的小偏差主导，表明有效场论方法能成功描述此类系统。

Abstract: The three- and four-boson systems with a large scattering length and a short effective range in the two-body sector are studied in the framework of Short-Range Effective Field Theory. The starting point (leading order) of the EFT is taken to be the universal unitarity limit, where the two-body sector is parameter-free and only one three-body parameter enters. In this limit, physical systems manifests discrete scale invariance. Deviations from universality arising from finite scattering-length and effective-range corrections, as well as a four-body force required by renormalization, are included perturbatively at next-to-leading order. The three-body ground state and its associated four-body ground and first-excited states are studied using the Faddeev-Yakubovsky formalism and a complementary diagrammatic approach. By employing techniques to remove contributions from deep trimers in tetramer calculations, we extend our analysis to larger cutoffs than previously accessible within the FY approach. Our results for binding energies and radii of $^4$He three- and four-atom systems converge well to results obtained with sophisticated phenomenological potentials. These successes suggest that the physics of $^4$He atomic clusters is governed by only small deviations from discrete scale invariance.

### [66] [Ground-state phase diagram of Rydberg atoms in a triangular-prism array](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01116)
*Qing-Yuan Zuo,Shuo Geng,Shan-Wen Tsai,Jin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）研究了三角棱柱光镊阵列中里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）的基态相图，揭示了由D₃对称性驱动的丰富密度波相、多种临界行为及浮游相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索三角棱柱几何中里德伯原子阵列的基态相图，该几何具有D₃对称性（而非两腿里德伯梯子的Z₂对称性），以揭示更丰富的有序相和相变结构。

Method: 使用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法进行数值模拟，通过调节失谐与拉比频率之比（detuning-to-Rabi-frequency ratio）以及里德伯阻塞半径（Rydberg blockade radius）来扫描相图。

Result: 发现多种密度波相：在大失谐下出现交替双占位与单占位相，该相经两次Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless相变融化，中间存在由Z₆钟模型描述的临界相；在更大阻塞半径下，出现每个三角形一个里德伯激发的相，经历了第一类相变；还发现了rung-trimerized密度波相，其融化行为对应于Z₂情况下的伊辛临界线，以及Z₃和Z₄情况下的手征临界线，仅在相应有理线上存在Potts和Ashkin-Teller点；在Z₂ rung-trimerized相内部，纠缠熵峰值标示了交叉区域；在周期不同的trimerized相之间出现了具有不可公度准长程序（incommensurate quasi-long-range order）的浮游相（floating phases）。

Conclusion: 三角棱柱里德伯原子阵列因其D₃对称性，展示出比两腿里德伯梯子更丰富的相图，包括多重密度波相、BKT相变、手征临界线以及浮游相，为研究量子多体系统中对称性与相变的关系提供了新的平台。

Abstract: We study the ground-state phase diagram of Rydberg atoms in a triangular-prism optical tweezer array using the density matrix renormalization group. By tuning the detuning-to-Rabi-frequency ratio and the Rydberg blockade radius, the system realizes several density-wave phases with spontaneous breaking of translational and leg-exchange symmetries. Unlike two-leg Rydberg ladders with $\mathbb{Z}_2$ leg-exchange symmetry, the triangular prism has $\mathbb{D}_3$ symmetry, leading to a richer set of ordered phases and transitions. For blockade radius moderately larger than the lattice spacing, a phase with alternating double and single Rydberg occupancy appears at large detuning. It breaks $\mathbb{Z}_2$ translational and $\mathbb{Z}_3$ rotational symmetry while preserving a rung reflection symmetry. Upon decreasing detuning, it melts through two Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless transitions with an intermediate critical phase described by a $\mathbb{Z}_6$ clock model. At larger blockade radius, a phase with one Rydberg excitation per triangle and broken $\mathbb{D}_3$ symmetry appears through a first-order transition. When double occupation of neighboring triangles is suppressed, rung-trimerized density waves develop as detuning increases from the disordered phase. Their melting follows the same structure as in Rydberg chains and two-leg ladders: the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ case has Ising critical lines, while the $\mathbb{Z}_3$ and $\mathbb{Z}_4$ cases have chiral critical lines, with Potts and Ashkin-Teller points only on the corresponding commensurate lines. Inside the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ rung-trimerized phase, an entanglement-entropy peak signals a crossover regime with enhanced period-2 density modulation before a first-order transition into a $\mathbb{Z}_2\times\mathbb{D}_3$ phase. Floating phases with incommensurate quasi-long-range order appear between trimerized states of different periods.

</details>


### [67] [Negative Interaction Quench Dynamics of Density-Ordered Dipolar Bosons in a One-Dimensional Optical Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01712)
*Rhombik Roy,N. D. Chavda,Barnali Chakrabarti,Arnaldo Gammal*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用多组态含时Hartree方法，数值精确研究了有限一维光晶格中密度有序的偶极玻色气体在负相互作用猝灭（quench）后的非平衡动力学，发现晶态关联在猝灭后仍保持鲁棒性，并识别出局域呼吸和偶极振荡等激发模式，揭示了隧穿与关联动力学的直接联系，展示了偶极晶格系统在非平衡量子模拟中的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索密度有序偶极玻色气体在相互作用猝灭后的非平衡动力学行为，特别是从长程相互作用到短程相互作用的交叉过程中所产生的复杂隧穿动力学和关联演化，并评估偶极晶格系统作为非平衡量子模拟平台的可能性。

Method: 采用数值精确的多组态含时Hartree方法（multiconfigurational time-dependent Hartree method for bosons），对有限一维光晶格中的偶极玻色气体进行模拟，通过负相互作用猝灭（即相互作用符号反转）驱动系统从长程相互作用向短程相互作用交叉。

Result: 发现晶态关联在猝灭后仍然保持鲁棒性；在实空间和动量空间观测到局域呼吸和偶极振荡等涌现激发模式；通过位点分辨的位置方差定量刻画了隧穿行为；利用单体和两体Glauber关联函数揭示了隧穿与关联动力学之间的直接联系。

Conclusion: 结合相互作用猝灭与晶格深度斜坡（lattice-depth ramping）可实现可控的动力学调控，偶极晶格系统是非平衡量子模拟的一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: We explore the nonequilibrium dynamics of a density-ordered dipolar Bose gas in a finite one-dimensional optical lattice following a negative interaction quench, using the numerically exact multiconfigurational time-dependent Hartree method for bosons. The interaction sign reversal, effectively driving a crossover from long-range to short-range interactions, generates rich intra- and interwell tunneling dynamics spanning superfluid, Mott-insulating, and fragmented regimes. A striking finding is the robustness of the underlying crystal-state correlations against the quench, despite the strong dynamical response. We identify emergent excitation modes, including local breathing and dipole-like oscillations, via real- and momentum-space observables, and quantify tunneling through site-resolved position variance. One- and two-body Glauber correlation functions further uncover a direct connection between tunneling and correlation dynamics. Moreover, we show that combining interaction quenches with lattice-depth ramping enables controllable dynamical engineering, establishing dipolar lattice systems as a promising platform for nonequilibrium quantum simulation.

Method: 采用从头算（ab initio）的含时显式关联高斯（time-dependent explicitly correlated Gaussian, TDECG）方法，利用适度数量的关联高斯基函数（correlated Gaussian basis functions）对最多六粒子系统进行数值模拟。

Conclusion: TDECG方法能够有效模拟超出两粒子的少体费米子系统非平衡动力学，并揭示动态BCS-BEC渡越（dynamical BCS-BEC crossover）的微观机制。

Abstract: Recent experiments simulating two-dimensional few-fermion systems have observed emergent hydrodynamic behavior, i.e., interaction-driven elliptic flow by adding fermions two at a time [S.~Brandstetter et al., Nat. Phys. (2025)]. Due to the curse of dimensionality and strong correlations, capturing such phenomena beyond two particles remains challenging. Here, we use the ab initio time-dependent explicitly correlated Gaussian (TDECG) method to quantitatively reproduce these experimental observations. With only a moderate number of correlated Gaussian basis functions, our approach obtains converged dynamical observables for systems up to six particles. Furthermore, real-time access to the many-body wavefunction and two-point correlation functions enables us to visualize the transformation from a strongly interacting gas to a stream of paired molecules, i.e., a dynamical BCS-BEC crossover.

### [69] [Noise spectroscopy of two-body loss as a probe of dynamical bulk viscosity in ultracold atomic gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01835)
*Tingyu Zhang,Hiroyuki Tajima,Takeo Kato*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文从弱耗散量子气体中的二体损耗电流噪声出发，推导出其超过泊松散粒噪声的部分正比于接触算符（contact operator）的平衡关联函数，并结合接触涨落与体粘滞（bulk viscosity）之间的精确关系，建立了可测量的损耗电流噪声与动力学体粘滞之间的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动力学体粘滞（dynamical bulk viscosity）在实验中一直难以测量，本文旨在通过弱耗散量子气体中二体损耗电流的高阶涨落（higher-order fluctuation）为其提供一种可行的探针。

Method: 从弱非弹性损耗的林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）出发，推导损耗流算符（loss-current operator）；扣除泊松散粒噪声（Poissonian shot-noise）背景后，分析损耗电流噪声功率谱与接触算符平衡关联函数的关系，进而利用接触与体粘滞的精确关系建立对应。

Result: 二体损耗电流的非泊松噪声功率谱正比于接触算符的平衡关联函数，而该关联函数通过精确关系与体粘滞相联系，因此损耗电流噪声可作为动力学体粘滞的可测量探针。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上确认了二体损耗的二阶涨落能够用于探测长期难以实验测量的动力学体粘滞，为冷原子体系中的输运测量提供了新途径。

Abstract: We show that the correlated noise of the two-body loss current provides access to the dynamical bulk viscosity in weakly dissipative quantum gases. Starting from the Lindblad equation for weak inelastic losses, we derive the loss-current operator. After subtracting the leading Poissonian shot-noise background, the remaining noise power spectrum of two-body loss current is found proportional to the equilibrium correlation function of the contact operator. Combining this result with the exact relation between contact correlations and bulk viscosity, we demonstrate the correspondence between the measurable loss-current noise and the bulk-viscosity. Our result identifies the higher-order fluctuation of two-body loss as a probe of dynamical bulk viscosity, whose measurement has remained elusive in experiments.

</details>

### [70] [Development and integration of the NA64-DTC automation controller for the CERN "DESY Table'' motorized platform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02148)

Result: 该设备已在CERN的PS-T9和SPS-H4束线设施完成成功调试（commissioning），验证了其在真实束流环境中的性能。设备支持远程自动化操作，可与手动系统并行工作，无需修改原有硬件。

Abstract: We report on the development, construction, and integration of a remote automation controller \texttt{NA64-DTC} for the so-called ``DESY Table'' motorised platform widely used at CERN East-Area and North-Area experimental installations. The device is based on an ESP32-C3 System-on-Module that interfaces with the table manual control panel via a signal duplication connector. Button presses are emulated through opto-isolated switches, to allow for simultaneous operation with the manual system without modifying the original hardware. A \texttt{HTTP} server running on the controller allows interfacing with the device, enabling experiment-specific integration solutions. \\ The device was successfully commissioned at CERN, exploiting the experimental installations at PS-T9 and SPS-H4 beamlines. This work describes in detail the device technical design and operation, as well as the performance obtained during the commissioning operations. Although initially conceived for the NA64 experiment, the proposed solution can be of interest to all CERN experiments making use of the DESY Table platform, enabling remote and automated operation while reducing manual intervention during beam activities.

### [71] [Full Characterization of a Mock Nuclear Waste Barrel with Muon Tomography using Micromegas Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02557)
*Raphaël Bajou,David Attié,Héctor Gómez,Irakli Mandjavidze,Philippe Mas*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文基于μ子散射断层成像（muon scattering tomography）技术，使用Micromegas探测器对205升核废料模拟桶进行实验成像，结合蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟定义鉴别阈值，通过角度统计重建算法（Angle Statistics Reconstruction algorithm）实现了10 mm空间分辨率的三维成像，对铅、钢等高密度金属夹杂物实现了高识别效率（AUC ≥ 0.96），并建立了从仿真到实验验证的定量化框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核废料表征（nuclear waste characterization）需要对致密、屏蔽物体进行非破坏性成像，现有方法在穿透性和材料鉴别能力上存在局限。自然宇宙射线μ子（cosmic-ray muons）基于多重库仑散射（multiple Coulomb scattering）原理，可穿透高密度材料并提供材料密度信息，因此本研究旨在利用μ子散射断层成像实现对核废料桶内部异常结构的定位与材料鉴别。

Method: 研究采用1 m²专用μ子散射断层成像测试平台，使用复用型电阻式Micromegas探测器进行高精度μ子径迹（muon tracking）。首先通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）表征材料依赖的散射特征，并基于统计重建（statistical reconstruction）定量评估鉴别性能；依据模拟结果定义客观鉴别阈值（discrimination thresholds），再将该阈值应用于实验数据。使用角度统计重建算法（Angle Statistics Reconstruction algorithm）实现三维成像，并通过接收者操作特征分析（receiver operating characteristic analysis）评估材料区分性能。

Result: 实现了10 mm的空间分辨率，成功对包含低辐射长度（low-radiation length）和高辐射长度（high-radiation length）材料的内部结构进行三维成像。铅和钢等高密度金属夹杂物的AUC（area under the curve）≥ 0.96，空腔也表现出强对比度。实验数据与蒙特卡洛模拟结果吻合良好，在数天采集时间内实现了高识别效率。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一条从仿真性能表征到实测数据应用的无缝工作流，为μ子散射断层成像在复杂屏蔽物体（尤其是核废料表征）中的应用提供了定量验证的框架。该方法在内部异常定位、材料鉴别和三维成像方面表现出优异性能，具有良好的实际应用前景。

Abstract: Muon tomography based on multiple Coulomb scattering provides a non-destructive method to image dense and shielded objects using naturally occurring cosmic-ray muons. In the context of nuclear waste characterization, we present the experimental imaging of a 205-L mock waste barrel using a dedicated 1m$^2$ muon scattering tomography test bench. The system employs multiplexed resistive Micromegas detectors, enabling stable and high-precision muon tracking. Monte Carlo simulations are first used to characterize material-dependent scattering signatures and to quantitatively assess identification performance using statistical reconstruction. These simulation-based results are then used to define objective discrimination thresholds, which are subsequently applied to experimental data for the localization and identification of internal anomalies. Using an Angle Statistics Reconstruction algorithm, we achieve a spatial resolution of 10 mm and demonstrate the three-dimensional imaging of an internal structure containing both low- and high-radiation length materials. Material discrimination performance is evaluated using receiver operating characteristic analysis, yielding high identification efficiency for dense metallic inclusions such as lead and steel (AUC $\geq$ 0.96) within acquisition times of a few days, while cavities also exhibit strong contrast. Experimental results show good agreement with detailed Monte Carlo simulations. By establishing a continuous workflow from simulation-based performance characterization to practical application on measured data, this work provides a quantitatively validated framework for muon scattering tomography applied to complex, shielded objects.

</details>

### [72] [Eigenfunction correlators under power-law SULE and localization for lattice operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00650)
*M. Aloisio,C. R. de Oliveira,R. Matos,D. Oliveira,M. Pigossi*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个确定性框架，证明特征函数的半均匀局域化（semi-uniform localization of eigenfunctions, SULE）的幂律形式对晶格算子的结构与动力学施加了强约束。具体证明了幂律SULE可导出局域中心的几何约束、特征函数关联子的定量界及位置算子的有限矩意义下的幂律局域化；反之，特征函数关联子的适当界也蕴含对应形式的幂律SULE，从而揭示了两者间的紧密联系。作为应用，在不依赖微扰方法的情况下，获得了具有亚线性增长Stark型势的长程晶格算子的幂律局域化，并讨论了在长程随机算子中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有局域化理论主要关注指数局域化（exponential localization），而对介于指数与扩展态之间的幂律局域化（power-law localization）的机制理解尚不充分。本文旨在建立一套确定性框架，以揭示SULE的幂律形式作为局域化结构机制的核心作用。

Method: 采用确定性分析框架，从幂律SULE出发导出局域中心几何约束、特征函数关联子（eigenfunction correlators）定量界以及位置算子（position operator）有限矩条件；同时证明反向蕴含关系，从而建立幂律SULE与关联子界之间的等价联系。

Result: 证明了幂律SULE可导出几何约束与幂律局域化，且特征函数关联子的适当界蕴含对应形式的幂律SULE。应用于亚线性增长Stark型势的长程晶格算子，无需微扰方法即获得幂律局域化，并推广至长程随机算子。

Conclusion: 幂律局域化本质上是几何性的：局域中心的空间分布直接影响特征函数关联子与输运性质。幂律SULE是一种超越指数区间的局域化结构机制，可涵盖Anderson型模型的相关特征。

Abstract: We develop a deterministic framework showing that a power-law form of semi-uniform localization of eigenfunctions (SULE) imposes strong structural and dynamical constraints on lattice operators. In particular, we prove that power-law SULE yields geometric constraints on localization centers, quantitative bounds on eigenfunction correlators, and power-law localization in the sense of finite moments of the position operator. Conversely, suitable bounds on eigenfunction correlators imply a corresponding form of power-law SULE, establishing a close connection between these notions. This highlights the role of power-law SULE as a structural mechanism governing localization beyond the exponential regime, including features typically associated with Anderson-type models. Our results reveal that power-law localization is intrinsically geometric: the spatial distribution of localization centers directly influences eigenfunction correlators and transport properties. As an application, we obtain power-law localization for long-range lattice operators with Stark-type potentials of sublinear growth whose spectral regime exhibits asymptotically collapsing spectral gaps and quasi-resonant structures, without relying on perturbative methods. Applications to long-range random operators are also discussed.

### [73] [Structure, Composition, and High-Field Superconductivity in Metal-Rich $\mathrmη$-Carbide-Type Compounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00894)
*Manuele Balestra,KeYuan Ma,Harald O. Jeschke,Fabian O. von Rohr*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: η-碳化物型化合物作为金属富集量子材料（metal-rich quantum materials）的新兴类别，表现出由复杂金属键合产生的异常超导性质，因此有必要对其进行系统综述。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，综合分析了晶体对称性、合成挑战、过渡金属组成和电子结构对η-碳化物型超导相性质的影响。

Result: 已有多种η-碳化物型相被确认为体超导体（bulk superconductor），如Nb₄Rh₂C_{1-δ}、Ta₄Rh₂C_{1-δ}、Ti₄Ir₂O_{1-δ}和Ti₄Co₂O_{1-δ}，其超导转变温度（T_c）最高约10 K，上临界场（upper critical field）μ₀H_{c2}(0)最高约30 T。这些材料在晶体学上具有高对称性，并显著违反了弱耦合泡利极限（weak-coupling Pauli limit）。

Conclusion: η-碳化物型超导相的转变温度虽与典型金属间化合物超导体相当，但其对弱耦合泡利极限的显著违背值得关注。未来方向包括可能发现新的η-碳化物型材料。

Abstract: $\mathrmη$-Carbide-type compounds have recently emerged as a diverse class of materials in the study of superconductivity. These phases contribute to a growing family of metal-rich quantum materials that exhibit unusual superconducting properties emerging from complex metallic bonding. Several members of the $\mathrmη$-carbide-type phases have been found to be bulk superconductors -- such as Nb$_4$Rh$_2$C$_{1-δ}$, Ta$_4$Rh$_2$C$_{1-δ}$, Ti$_4$Ir$_2$O$_{1-δ}$, and Ti$_4$Co$_2$O$_{1-δ}$ -- with transition temperatures up to $T_{\rm c} \approx$ 10 K and upper critical fields as high as $μ_0 H_{\rm c2}(0) \approx$ 30 T. Whereas the transition temperatures may fall within the range typical for intermetallic superconductors, the pronounced violation of the weak-coupling Pauli limit in many of these crystallographically high-symmetry materials is noteworthy. Here, we review recent progress on superconducting $\mathrmη$-carbide-type phases, emphasizing how crystal symmetry, synthetic challenges, transition-metal composition, and electronic structure govern their superconducting properties. Furthermore, we outline open questions and future directions, including the possible discovery of new $\mathrmη$-carbide-type materials.

</details>


### [74] [Interplay between Quantum Metric and Hybridized Collective Modes in Flat-Band Superfluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01235)
*Yi Liu,Mingyan Wang,Penghui Hu,Yao Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究平带超流体（flat-band superfluids）中的集体激发（collective excitations），发现无论何种时间反演对称的孤立平带超流体系统，在长波极限下仅存在一个低能集体模式。该模式在零动量处无能隙（gapless），但在小动量下呈二次色散（$\omega\propto q^2$），且其色散系数由正常态的量子度量（quantum metric）决定。分析结果与数值计算高度一致，并普适于任何与分散带（dispersive bands）能量隔离的$s$波平带超流体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超流体（conventional superfluids）中的Goldstone模式呈线性色散，而平带超流体的集体激发行为尚未被充分理解。本文旨在揭示平带超流体中低能集体激发的普适行为及其与量子几何（quantum geometry）的内在联系。

Method: 通过耦合配对（相位与振幅）涨落与密度涨落的动力学，研究平带超流体中的集体激发。采用分析推导与数值计算相结合的方法，揭示低能集体模式的色散关系及其与正常态量子度量的关系。

Result: 对于任何时间反演对称的孤立平带超流体，长波极限下仅存在一个低能集体模式；该模式在零动量处无能隙，但在小动量下呈二次色散（$\omega\propto q^2$），区别于传统超流体的线性Goldstone模式。色散系数由正常态平带的量子度量（quantum metric）决定。解析预测与数值计算吻合。

Conclusion: 上述结果普适适用于任何与分散带能量隔离的$s$波平带超流体。平带超流体的低能集体激发由量子几何主导，为理解平带系统中的超流特性提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We investigate collective excitations in flat-band superfluids by incorporating the coupled dynamics of pairing (phase and amplitude) and density fluctuations. We demonstrate that for any time-reversal symmetric superfluid system with an isolated flat band, only a single low-energy collective mode emerges in the long-wavelength limit. In contrast to the linearly dispersive Goldstone mode in conventional superfluids, this hybridized mode is gapless at zero momentum but exhibits a quadratic dispersion ($ω\propto q^2$) at small momenta. Analytically, we reveal that the dispersion coefficient of this collective mode is governed by the normal-state quantum metric of the flat band. These analytical predictions are in excellent agreement with numerical calculations. Our results are universally applicable to any generic $s$-wave flat-band superfluid, provided the flat band is energetically well separated from other dispersive bands.

### [75] [Excitonic-Superconducting Coexistence and Emergent Nematic Superconductivity Driven by Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01785)
*Fei Yang,Ruigang Li,Junwei Liu,Binghai Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过自洽微观理论研究表明，在激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator, EI）中引入超导配对（superconducting pairing）时，电子-空穴费米面的内在失配会稳定FFLO型电子-空穴配对，打破EI态的对称性，从而重构超导与EI的配对相空间，使二者在费米面不同区域互补共存，并自发产生向列超导性（nematic superconductivity），无需外加对称性破缺场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为激子绝缘体（EI）与超导（SC）序相互排斥，然而实际材料中两者可能共存。本文旨在从微观理论层面揭示EI与SC竞争关系的本质，并探索二者共存的可能性及其物理后果。

Method: 采用自洽微观理论（self-consistent microscopic theory），在存在超导配对的情况下研究包含EI相的电子系统，分析电子与空穴费米面失配（mismatch）对竞争的影响。

Result: 电子-空穴费米面失配稳定了FFLO型电子-空穴配对，破坏了EI态的对称性。对称性破缺重构了SC与EI的配对相空间，使费米面不同区域互补地支持EI或SC关联，实现二者共存。SC态因此自发打破旋转对称性，发展出内禀向列超导性（intrinsic nematic superconductivity），无需外加磁场、自旋-轨道耦合或能带各向异性等显式对称性破缺场。

Conclusion: 该机制揭示了竞争多体序（competing many-body orders）产生电子向列性（electronic nematicity）的新途径。单层1T$'$-MoTe$_2$和方网半金属NaAlSi等候选材料可能成为观测该现象的有前景平台。

Abstract: Excitonic insulating (EI) and superconducting (SC) orders are generally regarded as mutually exclusive electronic instabilities. Within a self-consistent microscopic theory, we study electronic systems hosting an EI phase in the presence of SC pairing and show that an intrinsic mismatch between electron and hole Fermi surfaces fundamentally reshapes this competition. This mismatch stabilizes FFLO-like electron-hole pairing and drives spontaneous symmetry breaking of the EI state. The resulting symmetry breaking reconstructs the pairing phase space for SC and EI state, such that different regions of the Fermi surface complementarily support either EI or SC correlations, leading to a natural coexistence of the two orders. Notably, the emergent SC state consequently breaks rotational symmetry and develops intrinsic nematic superconductivity, even in the absence of explicit symmetry-breaking fields (such as magnetic fields, spin-orbit coupling, or bare band-structure anisotropy). Our results suggest that candidate materials such as monolayer 1T$'$-MoTe$_2$ and the square-net semimetal NaAlSi may provide promising platforms for observing this phenomenon. More broadly, these findings reveal a unique mechanism by which competing many-body orders generate electronic nematicity, suggesting a broader route toward spontaneous anisotropic electronic states in correlated quantum materials.

</details>


### [76] [Evolution of the intertwining correlated topological phases in iron-based superconductor Fe(Te,Se)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01786)
*Yue Sun,Shiying He,Zhongyi Zhang,Yong Huang,Jingheng Chen,Weixiang Yan,Chunbo Yu,Yuyang Dong,Kohei Aido,Xin Zhou,Zhengtai Liu,Mao Ye,Jishan Liu,Haruhisa Kitano,Zhixiang Shi,Hong Ding,Takeshi Kondo,Xianxin Wu,Peng Zhang*
