<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单个量子材料中可共存多种拓扑电子相并诱导不同的拓扑超导态，这为探索拓扑超导态与马约拉纳模（Majorana modes）之间的相互作用提供了更深层次的视角，且关联效应可能影响和改变这些现象。铁基超导体同时兼具拓扑态与关联效应，是研究上述问题的理想体系。

Method: 采用高分辨率角分辨光电子能谱（high resolution angle resolved photoelectron spectroscopy, ARPES）直接解析钴掺杂铁基超导体 Co-doped Fe(Te,Se) 中两种不同的交织拓扑电子态，并研究它们在电子掺杂（electron doping）下的演化。

Result: 确定了拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）表面态与拓扑狄拉克半金属（topological Dirac semimetal）态均穿越费米能级（Fermi level）的区域；拓扑态受到强关联效应（strong correlation effect）影响，并与平庸体态（trivial bulk states）隔离。

Conclusion: 不同拓扑相之间的演化为研究来自不同超导相的各种马约拉纳模（Majorana modes）提供了良好的契机，本工作为探索多种拓扑超导态及其相关马约拉纳模的相互作用建立了理想平台。

Abstract: Multiple topological electronic phases can coexist within a single quantum material and induce different topological superconducting states, offering deeper insights into interplay of topological superconducting states and Majorana modes, which may also be influenced and modified by correlation effect. Iron-based superconductors, with both topological states and correlation effect, is an ideal platform to study these phenomena. Here, with high resolution angle resolved photoelectron spectroscopy, we directly resolve two distinct intertwining topological states in iron-based superconductor Co-doped Fe(Te,Se), and study their evolution with electron doping. We identify a region where both topological insulator surface states and topological Dirac semimetal states intersect the Fermi level. The topological states are affected by the strong correlation effect and are isolated from trivial bulk states. The evolution between distinct topological phases offers a good opportunity to study various Majorana modes from different superconducting phases according to theoretical analysis. Our findings establish an ideal platform for exploring the interaction between multiple topological superconducting states and the related Majorana modes.

### [77] [Equilibrium Gibbs Bifurcations of Bardeen-AdS Black Holes at Fixed Pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00099)
*J. -K. Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在直接水平约定（direct horizon convention）下，系统分析了四维Bardeen-AdS黑洞的固定压强Gibbs曲线结构，识别出三个关键边界（g_*, g_c, g_s）并通过降维变量揭示了其压强依赖规律，最终定义了该热力学系统的Gibbs分岔结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解正则化尺度（regularization scale）变化时，Bardeen-AdS黑洞在Reissner-Nordstrom-AdS（RN-AdS）型类燕尾（swallow-tail）结构与单分支（single-branch）区域之间的中间序列的热力学相变行为。

Method: 通过分类壳上曲线（on-shell curve）的转向点（turning points）和自交点（self-intersections），结合局部热容过滤（local heat-capacity filtering）和稳定分支上的Lower Gibbs包络线（lower Gibbs envelope）构建，识别三个边界并采用降维变量分析（reduced-variable analysis）。

Result: 三个边界分别由g_*(P)（RN-AdS拓扑丢失）、g_c(P)（c形扇区起始）和g_s(P)（正温多分支结构终止）定义；降维变量分析表明这些边界由无量纲组合8πPg²控制，呈反平方根压强依赖性，并给出了单分支边界的解析值。

Conclusion: 稳定的小/大黑洞共存可以在第一次拓扑变化后存活，而c形扇区不存在稳定跨越；这些结果在直接水平约定下定义了Bardeen-AdS热力学的Gibbs分岔结构（Gibbs bifurcation structure）。

Abstract: In the direct horizon convention, the fixed-pressure Gibbs curve of the four-dimensional Bardeen-AdS black hole passes through an intermediate sequence between the Reissner-Nordstrom-AdS swallow-tail class and the single-branch regime as the regularization scale is increased. The on-shell curve is classified by its turning points and self-intersections, followed by local heat-capacity filtering and construction of the lower Gibbs envelope over stable branches. The deformation is resolved into three boundaries: g_*(P), where the RN-AdS-like topology is lost; g_c(P), where the c-shaped sector begins; and g_s(P), where the positive-temperature multibranch structure terminates. A reduced-variable analysis shows that these boundaries are controlled by the dimensionless combination 8 pi P g^2, accounting for their inverse-square-root pressure dependence and giving an analytic value for the final single-branch boundary. The equilibrium construction further shows that stable small/large coexistence can survive the first topology change, whereas the representative c-shaped regime has no stable crossing. Within the direct convention, these results define a Gibbs bifurcation structure for Bardeen-AdS thermodynamics.

### [78] [Cascading amplification of gravitational waves triggered by environment in dynamical Chern-Simons gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00166)
*Han-Wen Hu,Chen Lan,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在动力学陈-西蒙斯（dCS）引力理论的有效场论框架下，研究由外部动力学环境驱动的引力波级联放大机制。研究发现黑洞势垒与外部振荡壳层共同构成有效谐振腔，引发dCS标量场的Mathieu不稳定性，进而通过源项激发轴向引力扰动，产生延迟的次级爆发。该机制揭示了超弱耦合下的dCS修正可通过长期参量放大在引力波信号中留下可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索dCS引力修正如何在动力学环境中被显著放大，从而在引力波信号中产生可观测的效应。

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）框架，研究环境场与dCS赝标量场的耦合；通过数值方法分析谐振腔中的Mathieu不稳定性（Mathieu instability）及其驱动频率阈值；分别在频域和时域对标量扰动和轴向引力扰动进行分析。

Result: 最优驱动频率由谐振腔长度决定；环境场过于靠近黑洞时，能流泄漏至事件视界会抑制共振增长，从而给出不稳定性存在的动力学阈值；频域中标量扰动呈现Floquet边带结构；时域中放大的标量场作为源项驱动轴向引力扰动，产生延迟的次级爆发。

Conclusion: dCS引力在超弱耦合下的修正可以通过动力学环境中的长期参量放大机制累积，并在引力波信号中留下可辨别的特征。

Abstract: Within the effective field theory framework of dynamical Chern-Simons (dCS) gravity, we investigate the cascading amplification mechanism of gravitational waves driven by an external dynamical environment. Considering the interaction between the environmental field and the dCS pseudoscalar, we find that the black hole barrier and the external oscillating shell collectively form an effective resonant cavity, which triggers Mathieu instability in the dCS scalar sector. Numerical results show that the optimal driving frequency is set by the length of the resonant cavity. When the environmental field lies too close to the black hole, leakage toward the event horizon suppresses the resonant growth, thus giving a dynamical threshold for the existence of the instability. In the frequency domain, scalar perturbations display the Floquet sideband structures. In the time domain, the amplified scalar field further acts as a source term to drive axial gravitational perturbations, generating a delayed secondary burst. This mechanism reveals that dCS corrections at ultraweak coupling can still accumulate via long-term parametric amplification in a dynamical environment, leaving discernible signatures in gravitational wave signals.

### [79] [Future global stability of Maxwell-Jüttner equilibria and vacuum for the massless Boltzmann equation on FLRW spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00175)
*Robert M. Strain,Martin Taylor,Renato Velozo Ruiz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在线性减速膨胀的弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃尔克（Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker, FLRW）时空（空间拓扑为 $\mathbb{T}^3$）中研究无质量玻尔兹曼方程（massless Boltzmann equation），证明其非稳态麦克斯韦-尤特纳（Maxwell-Jüttner）平衡态的小扰动在未来全局时间存在唯一性，并在不同膨胀指数 $\mathfrak{q}$ 下给出超多项式或多项式的时间衰减率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在宇宙学背景下，理解相对论性玻尔兹曼方程在膨胀时空中的非线性稳定性与衰减行为，对早期宇宙动力学和非平衡统计力学具有重要意义。

Method: 在空间拓扑为 $\mathbb{T}^3$ 的 FLRW 时空上，考虑无质量玻尔兹曼方程，采用硬球相互作用（hard ball interaction）且不引入对称性假设；通过定义合适的基于 $L^2_p$ 的能量范数（energy norm）来度量扰动，并针对不同膨胀指数 $\mathfrak{q} \in [0,1]$ 分别分析时间衰减行为。

Result: 对 $0 \leq \mathfrak{q} \leq 1$，证明了小扰动在未来全局时间的存在唯一性。对 $0 \leq \mathfrak{q} < 1/3$，扰动的能量范数以超多项式速率 $t^{-3\mathfrak{q}}\exp(-t^{1-3\mathfrak{q}})$ 衰减；对 $1/3 < \mathfrak{q} \leq 1$，则以多项式速率 $t^{-3\mathfrak{q}}$ 衰减；边界情形 $\mathfrak{q}=1/3$ 的衰减速率为 $t^{-3\mathfrak{q} -c}$（$c>0$ 为均匀常数）。此外，对 $1/3 < \mathfrak{q} \leq 1$，还证明了真空解小扰动在未来全局时间的存在唯一性。

Conclusion: 无质量玻尔兹曼方程在 FLRW 时空上的长时间行为强烈依赖于膨胀指数 $\mathfrak{q}$：慢膨胀（$\mathfrak{q}<1/3$）导致超多项式衰减，快膨胀（$\mathfrak{q}>1/3$）导致多项式衰减，临界点 $\mathfrak{q}=1/3$ 处出现指数修正。

Abstract: In this work we study the general relativistic massless Boltzmann equation on Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker spacetimes with spatial topology $\mathbb{T}^3$ in the linear and decelerated expanding regimes, where the scale factor is $t^{\mathfrak{q}}$ with $\mathfrak{q}\in [0,1]$. The massless Boltzmann equation on these backgrounds admits non-stationary Maxwell-Jüttner equilibria of the form $\exp(- |t^{2\mathfrak{q}}p|)$. For $0 \leq \mathfrak{q} \leq 1$, we prove future global-in-time existence and uniqueness of small perturbations of these equilibria in the case of hard ball interaction without symmetry assumptions. For $0\leq \mathfrak{q} < 1/3$, we prove that the perturbation -- measured in a suitable $L^2_p$ based energy norm -- decays at the superpolynomial time-decay rate of $t^{-3\mathfrak{q}}\exp(-t^{1-3\mathfrak{q}})$, whereas for $1/3< \mathfrak{q} \leq 1$ we obtain the polynomial time-decay rate of $t^{-3\mathfrak{q}}$. In the borderline case $\mathfrak{q}=1/3$, we show the time-decay of $t^{-3\mathfrak{q} -c}$ with a uniform constant $c>0$. Finally, for $\frac{1}{3}< \mathfrak{q}\leq 1$, we prove future global-in-time existence and uniqueness of small perturbations of the vacuum solution on $\mathbb{T}^3$.

</details>


### [80] [Traversable Wormholes Supported by Entropy-Inspired Effective Matter Sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00178)
*Jonathan A. Rebouças,Francisco Bento Lustosa,Celio R. Muniz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文基于熵-几何对应关系，将修改后的熵（entropy）诱导的有效密度分布作为Morris-Thorne虫洞（wormhole）的现象学源，系统分析了Barrow、Tsallis、Kaniadakis、对数和指数五种熵模型，发现修改熵廓线可为可穿越虫洞提供可行的有效源，其支撑机制依赖于熵的形变方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，修改的Bekenstein-Hawking熵可诱导出形变的黑洞几何及各向异性物质场（anisotropic matter sector）。受此启发，本文旨在探究这些熵诱导的密度分布能否作为可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）的现象学源。

Method: 不直接引入原黑洞框架的全各向异性物质场，仅保留有效密度分布，将其作为Morris-Thorne度规中的熵灵感源。径向压力由压稳态方程（barotropic equation of state）p_r=wρ重建，其余物质变量由虫洞场方程和各向异性平衡条件确定。对Barrow、Tsallis、Kaniadakis、对数和指数五种熵模型，推导了形状函数（shape function）、红移方程（redshift equation）、能量条件诊断（energy-condition diagnostics）、嵌入行为（embedding behavior）及Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff平衡。

Result: Barrow和Tsallis熵产生幂律负密度源，Kaniadakis和指数熵产生局域化负密度分布，对数熵呈现负密度和正密度类幻像（phantom-like）区域。所有正则构型中，喉部处径向零能量条件（null energy condition）破坏与flare-out条件关联，而切向零能量条件和强能量条件（strong energy condition）组合揭示了每种熵形变如何通过各向异性应力重新分布奇异物质（exoticity）。

Conclusion: 修改熵廓线可作为可穿越虫洞的有效源，其支撑机制依赖于熵形变的具体类型。

Abstract: The entropic interpretation of gravity suggests that spacetime geometry may encode thermodynamic information from microscopic degrees of freedom. In this context, the entropy--geometry correspondence developed in Ref. [1] and extended in Ref. [2] shows that modified Bekenstein--Hawking entropy can induce deformed black-hole geometries and anisotropic matter sectors of entropic origin. Motivated by this result, we investigate whether the corresponding entropy-induced density profiles can act as phenomenological sources for traversable wormholes. We do not import the full anisotropic matter sector of the original black-hole framework; instead, we retain only the effective density profiles and use them as entropy-inspired sources in the Morris--Thorne spacetime. The radial pressure is reconstructed from the barotropic equation of state $p_r=wρ$, while the remaining matter variables follow from the wormhole field equations and anisotropic equilibrium. We analyze five sectors: Barrow, Tsallis, Kaniadakis, logarithmic, and exponential. For each case, we derive the shape function, redshift equation, energy-condition diagnostics, embedding behavior, and Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff balance. Barrow and Tsallis generate power-law negative-density sources, Kaniadakis and exponential yield localized negative-density distributions, and the logarithmic sector allows negative-density and positive-density phantom-like regimes. In all regular configurations, radial null energy condition violation at the throat is linked to the flare-out condition, whereas the tangential null energy condition and strong-energy-condition combination show how each entropy deformation redistributes exoticity through anisotropic stresses. The results show that modified entropy profiles can provide viable effective sources for traversable wormholes, with the supporting mechanism depending on entropy deformation.

</details>


### [81] [Analytical calculation of the observational parameters for tachyon inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00195)

Result: 新提出的测试哈勃率函数相比以往有显著改进，并与最新观测数据达到合理一致；对于其中一类函数成功完成了解析计算，获得了$n_{\rm s}$和$r$的显式表达式；解析与数值预测均与Planck观测约束相符。

Abstract: We investigate the possibility of analytically calculating observational parameters in tachyon inflation cosmology, using the Hubble expansion rate as a function of the tachyon field. First, in light of the newer Planck results, we analyze previous investigations in which the test Hubble rate functions were confronted with Planck 2013 data. We propose and analyze a number of new test Hubble rate functions, finding considerable improvement and approaching reasonable agreement with recent observational data. For a class of these functions, we were able to carry out analytical calculations. As a novelty, we introduce a functional dependence of the slow-roll Hubble flow parameters as an input, which facilitates an analytical study of inflation. In this way, we obtain explicit expressions for the scalar spectral index ($n_{\rm s}$) and the tensor-to-scalar ratio ($r$). We confront our analytical and numerical predictions with Planck observational constraints. Finally, we discuss the proposed linear dependence between the first two slow-roll parameters in light of recent data from ACT DR6, DESI, and others, as well as the potential to generalize this dependence to other inflation models.

### [82] [Constraints on the Phenomenology of Dissipative Cosmological Memory from BAO (BOSS + DESI 2024) and Pantheon+ Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00227)
*S. M. Ponomarenko*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个由振幅$ε$、衰减标度$z_*$和陡峭指数$β$三个参数描述的现象学流体模型，其红移演化服从德拜定律（Debye law）$f(z) = \exp[{-(z/z_*)^β}]$；采用联合贝叶斯分析（joint Bayesian analysis），综合使用来自BOSS DR12和DESI 2024的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation，BAO）数据、Pantheon$+$的光度距离（photometric distances）以及SHOES和Planck的$H_0$测量数据。

Abstract: We propose and test a phenomenological model of ``dissipative memory'' in the gravitational field, where early quantum gravitational processes leave a relic signature in the cosmic expansion rate. The model is parameterized by an additional fluid with amplitude $ε$, decay scale $z_*$, and a steepness index $β$, decaying according to a Debye law $f(z) = \exp[{-(z/z_*)^β}]$. We perform a joint Bayesian analysis using baryon acoustic oscillation data from BOSS DR12 and DESI 2024, photometric distances from Pantheon$+$, and $H_0$ measurements (SHOES and Planck). A global optimization reveals that the best fit is identical to $Λ$CDM: the memory correction vanishes across the entire observable range $z \in [0.3,\,2.3]$ ($Δχ^2 < 0.01$ with three extra parameters, $Δ\mathrm{AIC}=+6.0$, $Δ\mathrm{BIC}=+9.9$). We discuss the physical interpretation of this constraint and point out observational channels where the memory effect could potentially manifest.

Abstract: The spacetime behavior at very extreme conditions, such as the regions near a black hole, can be very difficult to modelize. In this work we introduce a new geometric method that allows to calculate the parameters of photon spheres, massive particle surfaces and shadow radius of black holes. We build upon a perturvative approach but bases in intrinsic curvatures, such as the geodesic and Gaussian curvatures. In the null case we are able to recover the results found by the perturvative method only. ### [85] [Relativistic transformation of temperature revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00521)
*Soroor Pouryazdan,Babak Vakili*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文从相对论热力学与统计视角重新审视温度的相对论变换问题，通过分析光子气体、相对论理想气体和电子气体的能量-动量张量，发现有效温度随速度增加而增大，支持Ott-Eddington解释，并指出温度是依赖于观测者的物理量，而非洛伦兹不变标量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 温度的相对论变换长期以来存在争议，Planck-Einstein、Ott-Eddington-Moller和Landsberg等经典定律给出了相互矛盾的结果，亟需从更一致的理论框架重新审视这一问题。

Method: 从各向同性系统的能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）出发，定义有效温度（effective temperature）Teff为运动观测者从变换后的能量密度中推断出的温度，并分别对光子气体、相对论理想气体（relativistic ideal gas）和电子气体（electron gas）进行分析。

Result: 三种系统的有效温度均随速度增加而增大，支持Ott-Eddington解释，且具体行为依赖于系统的状态方程（equation of state）。

Conclusion: 温度不是洛伦兹不变标量（Lorentz-invariant scalar），而是依赖于观测者的量；将温度与逆温度四维矢量（inverse-temperature four-vector）β相关联，可在统一的热力学框架内衔接操作性与不变性视角。

Abstract: The relativistic transformation of temperature has long remained controversial, with the classical laws of Planck-Einstein, Ott-Eddington-Moller and Landsberg yielding conflicting results. We reexamine this issue from a relativistic thermodynamic and statistical perspective, starting from the energy-momentum tensor of an isotropic system and defining the effective temperature Teff as that inferred by a moving observer from the transformed energy density. Analyses of a photon gas, a relativistic ideal gas and an electron gas show that Teff consistently increases with velocity, supporting the Ott-Eddington interpretation while depending on the system's equation of state. These results indicate that temperature is not a Lorentz-invariant scalar but an observer-dependent quantity. A consistent relativistic description emerges when temperature is related to the inverse-temperature four-vector beta, linking operational and invariant viewpoints within a unified thermodynamic framework.

### [86] [Searching for a waveform-agnostic gravitational wave signal in pulsar timing arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00577)
*Heling Deng,Bence Becsy,Yuri Levin,Neil J. Cornish,Xavier Siemens*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种不依赖波形模板（waveform-agnostic）的贝叶斯分层框架，利用傅里叶展开（Fourier expansion）和洛伦兹型超先验（Lorentzian hyperprior）分析脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array, PTA）数据，可同时推断引力波源的天区位置、频率成分和随机背景，并处理非建模脉冲星噪声。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays, PTAs）近期为纳赫兹随机引力波背景提供了令人信服的证据，推动了对局部引力波源（localized sources）的搜索。然而，现有搜索大多依赖特定的波形模板（waveform templates），计算成本高，且可能对预料之外的信号不敏感。

Method: 采用波形无关（waveform-agnostic）框架，通过傅里叶展开（Fourier expansion）对信号引起的计时残差（timing residuals）进行建模；对傅里叶系数的方差施加洛伦兹型超先验（Lorentzian hyperprior），以灵活捕捉信号的频率主峰和带宽；通过对傅里叶系数进行解析边际化（analytical marginalization），建立贝叶斯分层模型（Bayesian hierarchical framework），同时推断源的天区位置、频率成分和随机背景；此外，为每个脉冲星引入额外的平坦谱特征以减轻非建模噪声的污染。

Result: 在模拟数据集上的测试表明，该方法鲁棒性强，对预期及未预期的引力波现象均具有敏感性，为未来脉冲星计时阵列搜索提供了一种灵活工具。

Conclusion: 该波形无关框架兼具灵活性与鲁棒性，有望在无需预设波形模板的前提下，有效探测多种类型的纳赫兹引力波信号。

Abstract: Pulsar timing arrays have recently provided compelling evidence for a nanohertz stochastic gravitational wave background, motivating searches for gravitational waves from localized sources. Most existing searches assume specific waveform templates, which can be computationally demanding and potentially insensitive to unexpected signals. We introduce a waveform-agnostic framework that models signal-induced timing residuals via a Fourier expansion. A Lorentzian hyperprior is imposed on the variances of the Fourier coefficients, providing a flexible spectral envelope that captures the signal's dominant frequency and bandwidth while remaining agnostic to its exact shape. Analytical marginalization over the Fourier coefficients then yields a Bayesian hierarchical framework that concurrently infers the source sky location, its frequency content, and the stochastic background. To mitigate contamination from unmodeled pulsar noise, we further allow for additional flat-spectrum features for each pulsar. Tests on simulated datasets show that the method is robust and provides a flexible tool for future PTA searches, with sensitivity to both expected and unexpected gravitational wave phenomena.

### [87] [Bekenstein-Hawking temperature from the Schwarzian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00911)
*Donato Bini,Giampiero Esposito*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文论证黑洞视界（Killing horizon）上的射影结构（projective structure）完全决定了贝肯斯坦-霍金温度（Bekenstein-Hawking temperature），并通过施瓦西（Schwarzschild）和克尔（Kerr）几何中施瓦茨导数（Schwarzian derivative）与表面引力（surface gravity）的关系提供证据，为黑洞热力学建立射影几何基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 霍金关于黑洞粒子创生的原始推导依赖于零测地线仿射参数（affine parameter）对延迟时间变量（retarded time）的指数依赖，该指数律蕴含施瓦茨导数与表面引力平方的特定关系，表明黑洞热力学可能源于黑洞视界的射影几何结构。

Method: 通过分析施瓦西时空中零测地线仿射参数λ与延迟时间变量u之间的施瓦茨导数关系，引入Killing视界的射影结构；在可变质量参数时空模型中推导表面引力对数导数的表达式；详细研究施瓦西和克尔几何中的施瓦茨导数性质。

Result: 表面引力平方是Killing视界射影结构的不变量；在可变质量时空模型中，表面引力的对数导数由仿射参数的施瓦茨导数决定；施瓦西和克尔几何中的施瓦茨导数性质被完整刻画。

Conclusion: 这些性质是证明黑洞热力学奠基于Killing视界射影几何的第一步；该研究框架可推广至黑洞辐射功率、黑洞质量随视界面积变化率、以及类正规模（quasinormal modes）基频虚部（即黑洞扰动的衰减率）。

Abstract: Hawking's original derivation of particle creation by black holes in Schwarzschild spacetime exploits, among various concepts, the exponential dependence on the retarded time variable u of the affine parameter λof the null geodesics that are integral curves of the null vector field orthogonal to the Killing horizon. This exponential law implies that the Schwarzian derivative of λwith respect to u is minus a half the square of surface gravity. The black hole Killing horizon inherits an intrinsic projective structure, and the squared surface gravity is the invariant characterizing such a structure. There is therefore evidence that the Bekenstein-Hawking temperature is completely determined from the projective structure on the Killing horizon. As a further test, it is here shown that, in a spacetime model with variable mass parameter, the logarithmic derivative of surface gravity is determined by the Schwarzian of the affine parameter. The Schwarzian in Schwarzschild and Kerr geometries is also studied in detail. All these properties are a first step towards proving that black hole thermodynamics finds its mathematical foundations in the projective geometry of Killing horizons. Such a research program can be applied to the power radiated from a black hole, the rate of change of the black hole mass with respect to the area of the event horizon, the fundamental imaginary frequency of quasinormal modes (and hence the decay rate of black hole perturbations).

### [88] [Planckian Gravitons from an Imaginary-Time Clock](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01052)
*Michael R. R. Good,Eric V. Linder*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过非相对论运动点质量的四极辐射，推导出与普朗克分布完全一致的引力波谱（gravitational wave spectrum），证明该谱纯属运动学效应，无需热平衡、视界或随机源假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力辐射谱通常依赖热平衡或黑洞视界等物理机制，本文试图探索是否存在更基本的运动学起源，以纯解析方式导出普朗克型（Planck-type）能谱。

Method: 从标准爱因斯坦四极辐射公式出发，将运动点质量的轨迹通过乘积-对数函数（product-log trajectory）引入虚时周期性（imaginary-time periodicity），在频域中计算辐射功率，最终得到正比于普朗克分布的形式。

Result: 推导出四极辐射功率谱正比于 $ω^3/(e^{2πcω/κ}-1)$，即普朗克分布；对应的引力子（graviton）能谱总能量和数目均有限；该频谱纯粹由运动学决定，与平衡态、视界或随机源无关。

Conclusion: 非相对论点质量的四极辐射可以精确产生普朗克谱，表明普朗克分布并不必然需要统计力学（statistical mechanics）或热力学背景，而可能源于纯运动学约束。

Abstract: We present a simple derivation of the exact Planck spectrum of the quadrupole radiation from point masses moving apart nonrelativistically, essentially an analog for gravitational radiation. The standard Einstein quadrupole radiation formula gives emitted power proportional to the square of the third derivative of $x(t)^2$. In our moving-mass picture, imaginary-time periodicity appears as a product-log trajectory of a quadrupole source. In the frequency domain, the power becomes proportional to the Planck distribution, $ω^3/(e^{2πcω/κ}-1)$. The resulting Planckian graviton energy spectrum has finite total energy and finite graviton number. The emitted spectrum is purely kinematic in origin: no equilibrium, horizon, or stochastic source is assumed.

### [89] [Revisiting Schwarzschild's constant density star in isotropic coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01061)
*Christopher Simmonds,Matt Visser*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了拥有110年历史的Schwarzschild常密度星问题，强调在各项同性坐标（isotropic coordinates）下分析该时空比传统的Hilbert–Droste面积坐标（area coordinates）更为简便。作者展示了线元（line element）的简洁形式，分析了恒星内部的局域与准局域性质，并探讨了零密度星、裸奇点（naked singularity）以及压力本身产生引力效应等特殊情形，指出该主题具有被低估的物理丰富性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视Schwarzschild常密度星这一经典问题，指出其在各向同性坐标下分析更为简便，并揭示该模型中被低估的多种物理特性，包括压力引力效应（pressure gravitates）和裸奇点等特殊解。

Method: 采用各向同性坐标（isotropic coordinates）而非传统的Hilbert–Droste面积坐标来推导和分析Schwarzschild常密度星时空的线元，该线元包含两个简单的径向坐标有理函数，且其中的两个物理参数可直接由恒星的中心密度（central density）和中心压强（central pressure）解释。

Result: 局域性质（如压强剖面）在形式上非常简洁；准局域性质（如Misner–Sharp质量）略有复杂。存在零密度星解，直接验证了压力即使在质量-能量密度为零时也能产生引力效应。存在满足除一个标准经典能量条件之外所有条件的裸奇点解，且零密度与裸奇点可共存，此时仅需违背主能量条件（dominant energy condition）。

Conclusion: Schwarzschild常密度星具有诸多被低估的物理特征，采用各向同性坐标的分析方法在简洁性和清晰度方面优于传统方法，并且具有显著的教学价值。

Abstract: Herein we shall revisit the venerable 110-year-old topic of Schwarzschild's constant density star, emphasizing that for many (though not quite all) purposes it is much easier to analyze this spacetime in isotropic coordinates (\emph{versus} the more usually adopted Hilbert--Droste area coordinates). The relevant line element is particularly transparent, containing two simple rational functions of the radial coordinate, and the two physical parameters appearing in this line element are easily and readily interpretable in terms of the central density and central pressure of the star. Local properties in the stellar interior (such as the pressure profile) will be seen to be remarkably simple, though quasi-local properties like the Misner--Sharp mass are just a little bit trickier. Apart from its simplicity and clarity, the analysis is also of considerable pedagogical interest. For instance, there are a number of interesting special cases. Mathematically there is a perfectly good solution corresponding to a zero density star -- which can physically be interpreted as an explicit verification of the fact that pressure gravitates, even in the absence of mass-energy density. Additionally, there is a singular solution containing a naked singularity that satisfies all but one of the standard classical energy conditions. Furthermore you can even do both, combining zero density with a naked singularity -- so that pressure by itself can generate naked singularities -- at the cost of merely violating the dominant energy condition, the least physical of the standard energy conditions. We argue that many physically interesting features of Schwarzschild's star are very much under-appreciated.

</details>


### [90] [The Heuristic Approach to General Relativity in the Laplace-Beltrami Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01129)
*Noah M. MacKay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨将拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米形式（Laplace-Beltrami formalism）从并合致密双星（CCBs）推广至广义相对论中其他系统，通过对爱因斯坦场方程（EFEs）进行全阶（零阶、一阶、二阶）变分分析，并利用代表性度规假设检验该形式论的实用性与局限性。结果表明一阶分解可启发式地展示弯曲时空中矢量场与标量场的动力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米形式此前已成功应用于并合致密双星（CCBs）的引力波能量计算，将CCB建模为有效奇异体（中空质量壳层），所得表面辐射能与引力波并合能高度吻合。基于这一成功，作者自然希望将该形式论推广至其他广义相对论系统，包括“简单”系统和“微扰”系统，以检验其通用性。

Method: 在拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米形式下，将爱因斯坦场方程（EFEs）中的里奇张量（Ricci tensor）以偏微分拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的主导阶进行表述。假设CCB为遵循克尔度规假设（Kerr metric Ansatz）的有效奇异体（中空质量壳层），通过变分法处理EFEs，使得度规假设的几何特征通过$G_{μν}=8πGT_{μν}$决定能量输出。本文将分析扩展至所有微分阶（零阶、一阶、二阶），对二阶变分方法进行深入分析，并对一阶和零阶项进行基准检验，使用代表性示例和选择性度规假设探索形式论的实用性与局限性。

Result: 一阶分解可启发式地展示弯曲时空中矢量场与标量场的动力学机制。对于CCB质量壳层表示，产生的引力波能量被处理为辐射表面能（$E:=T_{00}V$），该表面能量与已编录的引力波并合能高度接近。

Conclusion: 拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米形式论具有从CCBs推广至其他广义相对论系统的潜力。全阶分析表明，该方法在二阶变分层面已有先前成功应用，而一阶分解则揭示了弯曲时空中矢量场与标量场的启发式动力学图像。该形式论的实际适用范围与局限性需通过代表性示例和选择性度规假设进一步检验。

Abstract: The Laplace-Beltrami formalism, in which the Ricci tensor in the Einstein field equations (EFEs) is formulated at leading-order in terms of the partial-differential Laplace-Beltrami operator, was previously applied to coalescing compact binaries (CCBs) generating gravitational waves (GWs). Supposing that the CCB is an effective singular body -- a hollow mass-shell -- that follows a Kerr metric Ansatz, the EFEs were approached variationally such that the Ansatz geometric signature dictates the energetic output via $G_{μν}=8πGT_{μν}$. For the CCB mass-shell representation, the generated GW energy is treated as radiated surface energy via $E:=T_{00}V$. This surface energy yielded a close approximation to the cataloged GW coalescence energy, as previously shown in past comparisons. Given this success, it is logical to ask whether the Laplace-Beltrami formalism can be applied to other general relativistic systems, whether ``simple" or ``perturbative", beyond CCBs.
  This heuristic work focuses broadly on the EFEs themselves under the Laplace-Beltrami formalism, considering all differential orders up to second-order. This namely includes a deeper analysis on the variational methodology employed on the EFEs in the second-order sector, utilized in previous works, and the benchmark analysis of the lower first- and zeroth-order terms. This all-order report utilizes representative examples and select metric Ansätze to explore the formalism's practicality and its limitations; this is shown that the first-order decomposition showcases heuristically the mechanics of vector and scalar fields upon a curved spacetime.

</details>


### [91] [Rotating traversable wormholes and particle dynamics in $f(R,T)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01141)
*G. G. L. Nashed,Waleed El Hanafy,Amare Abebe,Kazuharu Bamba,Emmanuel N. Saridakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 $f(R,T)$ 引力理论的慢转近似下构造了稳态且轴对称的可穿越旋转虫洞解，表明此类虫洞可在无需奇异物质（exotic matter）的情况下由各向异性流体支撑，满足零能量条件（null energy condition）和强能量条件（strong energy condition），并分析了粒子运动、参考系拖曳（frame dragging）、影子形变及引力透镜等可观测特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论（General Relativity）框架下，可穿越虫洞通常需要违反零能量条件的奇异物质，这限制了其物理可行性。为克服这一困难，作者转向具有物质-几何耦合的修正引力理论，探索无需奇异物质的虫洞解是否可能存在。

Method: 采用慢转近似（slow-rotation approximation），在 $f(R,T)$ 引力（其中 $R$ 为标量曲率，$T$ 为能量-动量张量的迹）中构造由各向异性流体（anisotropic fluid）支撑的稳态（stationary）且轴对称（axisymmetric）的虫洞解。

Result: 所得虫洞几何是正则（regular）、渐近平坦（asymptotically flat）且无极（horizonless）的，并在喉部满足耀出条件（flare-out condition）。物质部分同时满足零能量条件和强能量条件，表明无需奇异物质即可支撑该类虫洞。基于声速条件的初步稳定性分析也支持解的物理可行性。

Conclusion: 旋转虫洞在 $f(R,T)$ 引力中是物理自洽的致密结构，具有潜在可观测的天体物理信号，如影子形变（shadow deformation）和引力透镜（gravitational lensing）特征。

Abstract: Traversable wormholes are among the most interesting solutions of gravitational theories, but within General Relativity they generally require exotic matter violating the null energy condition. Modified gravity theories with matter-geometry coupling provide a promising framework in which wormhole geometries may instead be supported by effective gravitational contributions. Motivated by this possibility, we investigate rotating traversable wormholes in $f(R,T)$ gravity, where $R$ is the scalar curvature and $T$ is the trace of the energy-momentum tensor, within the slow-rotation approximation. We construct stationary and axisymmetric wormhole solutions supported by an anisotropic fluid and show that the obtained geometries are regular, asymptotically flat, horizonless, and satisfy the flare-out condition at the throat. A central result is that the matter sector satisfies both the null and strong energy conditions, indicating that traversable rotating wormholes can be supported without exotic matter. We further analyze particle motion, frame dragging, and non-geodesic effects arising from matter-geometry coupling, together with shadow deformation and gravitational lensing signatures induced by rotation. A preliminary stability analysis based on sound-speed conditions indicates the physical viability of the solutions. These results demonstrate that rotating wormholes in $f(R,T)$ gravity constitute physically consistent compact configurations with potentially observable astrophysical signatures.

</details>


### [92] [Improving the resolution of double white dwarf systems with spaceborne gravitational wave observatories using a robust astrophysical prior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01236)
*Shao-Dong Zhao,Xue-Hao Zhang,Soumya D. Mohanty,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在迭代式引力波源提取流程GBSIEVER中引入基于双白矮星（DWD）质量极限与频率-频率导数关系强天体物理先验，使LISA和LISA-Taiji网络数据中可可靠解析的源数量分别提升约7.3%和14.6%，并提高参数估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间引力波天文台（如LISA、Taiji）数据中双白矮星（DWD）双星数量庞大，可分辨源的提取是一大分析挑战。现有迭代式方法计算高效但多采用忽略天体物理先验的频率学派框架，限制了源提取性能。

Method: 在迭代式源提取管线GBSIEVER中，融入一个强天体物理先验（astrophysical prior），该先验来源于孤立白矮星的质量极限，并将引力波信号频率$f$与其时间导数$\dot{f}$相关联。该方法应用于模拟的LISA单独数据和LISA-Taiji联合网络数据。

Result: 引入先验后，LISA数据可可靠解析源数量增加约7.3%，LISA-Taiji联合网络增加约14.6%，且参数估计精度提升。该改进在多种真实DWD种群实现中均保持有效，包括低频混淆主导区域。

Conclusion: 天体物理信息引导的先验在迭代式源提取中具有鲁棒性和实用价值，能有效提升可解析源数量与参数估计精度，且对观测配置和种群实现不敏感。

Abstract: Resolving the crowded population of double white dwarf (DWD) binaries in data from spaceborne gravitational wave (GW) observatories (e.g., LISA, Taiji) remains a major analysis challenge. Comparable performance on addressing this problem has been achieved with two main approaches: global fit, in which resolvable sources are estimated simultaneously from the data, and iterative, where sources are estimated one at a time and subtracted out from the data. While the latter is computationally efficient, methods developed under this approach have traditionally followed a frequentist framework that ignores astrophysical priors. This work incorporates a strong astrophysical prior, derived from the mass limits of detached white dwarfs and linking the GW signal frequency $f$ with its time derivative $\dot{f}$, into the iterative $\mathtt{GBSIEVER}$ pipeline. Applied to simulated LISA and LISA-Taiji network data, the method increases the number of confidently resolved sources by ${\approx}7.3\%$ (LISA-only) and ${\approx}14.6\%$ (network), respectively, and improves parameter estimation accuracy. The improvement persists across multiple realistic DWD population realizations, including in the low-frequency confusion-dominated regime, demonstrating the robustness and practical utility of astrophysically informed priors in iterative source extraction.

### [93] [Analytical Solutions to the Wheeler-DeWitt Equation in Rosen-Lagrangian Cosmology via the Eisenhart Lift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01500)
*Narakorn Kaewkhao,Suparat Marit,Phongpichit Channuie*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Rosen拉格朗日框架，将宇宙学常数推广为随尺度因子演化的动力学量Λ(a)=Λ₀a^λ，利用共形Killing方程和Eisenhart提升形式将惠勒-德维特方程转化为可解析求解的形式，为量子宇宙学与动力学暗能量提供统一几何描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准ΛCDM模型中的宇宙学常数为常数，无法解释暗能量的动力学演化。本文旨在通过Rosen拉格朗日框架引入尺度因子依赖的宇宙学常数，并利用几何方法（共形Killing方程与Eisenhart提升形式）将量子宇宙学（quantum cosmology）中的惠勒-德维特方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）转化为可解析求解的形式。

Method: 将宇宙学常数推广为尺度因子（scale factor）的函数Λ(a)=Λ₀a^λ；运用共形Killing方程（conformal Killing equations）确定共形因子F(a)，并将其表示为有效势Veff及其导数V'eff的函数；采用Eisenhart提升形式（Eisenhart lift formalism）引入辅助场χ，将宇宙学动力学重构为纯动力学提升作用量。

Result: 惠勒-德维特方程被转化为可解析求解的形式，在宇宙学常数主导的宇宙时期（包括早期宇宙暴胀阶段和晚期加速膨胀阶段）获得了解析解（analytic solutions）。

Conclusion: 该框架为将几何方法（geometrical methods）、量子宇宙学和动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）统一在单一描述中提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: The Rosen Lagrangian framework promotes the cosmological constant to a scale-factor-dependent quantity, $Λ(a)=Λ_{0}a^λ$, thereby providing a dynamical dark energy scenario for $λ\neq 0$. In the special case $λ=0$, the model naturally reduces to the standard $Λ$CDM cosmology. Within this framework, the conformal Killing equations are employed to determine the conformal factor $\mathcal{F}(a)$, which is expressed in terms of the effective potential $V_{\rm eff}$ and its derivative $V'_{\rm eff}$. Furthermore, the Eisenhart lift formalism introduces an additional field $χ$, allowing the cosmological dynamics to be reformulated through a purely kinetic lifted action. This geometrical construction provides a powerful approach to quantum cosmology by transforming the Wheeler-DeWitt equation into a tractable form that admits analytic solutions. Such solutions are particularly relevant in cosmological epochs dominated by the cosmological constant, including both the inflationary era of the early Universe and the late-time accelerated expansion. Consequently, this framework offers a promising avenue for connecting geometrical methods, quantum cosmology, and dynamical dark energy within a unified description.

### [94] [Gravitational-wave astronomy with a space-based optical clock network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01516)
*Dhruva Ganapathy,Divya Singh,Sammith Singamsetty,Shimon Kolkowitz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于空间原子钟网络（space-based atomic clock networks）的单向多普勒跟踪技术，用于探测毫赫兹至赫兹频段的引力波信号，并展示了其与传统探测器（如LISA）协同工作以提取双星引力波源关键天体物理信息的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文开发了天基原子钟网络中的专用测量协议（measurement protocols），分析了主导噪声源（dominant noise sources），并在模拟引力波信号上进行了初步参数估计（preliminary parameter estimation）。该方法基于单向多普勒跟踪（one-way Doppler tracking）技术，并与LISA等探测器协同运行。

Result: 研究表明，基于原子钟的引力波探测器能够在从毫赫兹到赫兹甚至更高频段的宽频带内实现灵敏测量。初步参数估计表明，这些探测器可以有效提取双星引力波源的关键天体物理信息。

Conclusion: 基于空间原子钟的引力波探测器具备独特且互补于传统光学干涉仪的能力，有望与LISA协同拓展引力波观测的频段覆盖，并为双星引力波源的天体物理研究提供重要信息。

Abstract: Since the first detection of a merging binary black hole system a decade ago, gravitational-wave astronomy has emerged as a powerful tool for astrophysics. Future space-based observatories, such as the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA), will unlock the millihertz (mHz) band, which remains entirely inaccessible to ground-based detectors due to terrestrial noise. In parallel, proposed atom-based gravitational-wave detectors, specifically those based on space-based optical clocks and atom interferometers, offer capabilities that are unique and complementary to traditional optical interferometers. Their highly tunable character enable sensitive measurements across a broad frequency band extending from the mHz up to and possibly even above the Hz regime. In this work, we investigate the use of one-way Doppler tracking in space-based atomic clock networks operating in concert with detectors like LISA. We develop dedicated measurement protocols, analyze dominant noise sources, and perform preliminary parameter estimation on simulated gravitational-wave signals. Ultimately, we demonstrate how these detectors could be used to extract critical astrophysical information about binary gravitational-wave sources.

### [95] [Pitching Cosmic Curveballs: Environmental Effects on Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals with Spinning Secondaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01569)
*Leif Lui,Lisa V. Drummond,Alejandro Torres-Orjuela*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次提出在极端质量比旋进（EMRI）中，旋转次级体在气体环境中运动时会受到马格努斯力（Magnus force）和升力（lift force）等自旋-环境耦合效应的影响。通过费希尔矩阵分析（Fisher matrix analysis）表明，气体阻力（gas drag）能够打破次级体自旋大小与倾角之间的真空投影简并（vacuum-projection degeneracy），从而紧缩参数约束，并增强自旋参数的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对极端质量比旋进（EMRI）的研究多基于真空环境假设，忽略了旋转次级体与周围气体介质的相互作用。本研究旨在建立首个考虑自旋-环境耦合效应（spin-coupled environmental effects, EEs）的演化框架，探索这些效应如何影响引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）信号的相位演化与参数推断。

Method: 论文构建了包含马格努斯力、升力和标准阻力（drag force）在内的自旋-环境耦合模型，将其纳入EMRI的动力学演化方程中。采用费希尔矩阵分析（Fisher matrix analysis）评估这些环境效应对引力波信号参数估计精度的影响，特别是自旋大小和倾角之间的简并解除情况。

Result: 自旋-环境耦合效应会在空间引力波探测器数年的观测窗口内，在信号中留下独特且可区分的失相（dephasing）特征。费希尔矩阵分析表明，气体阻力能有效打破真空假设下存在的次级体自旋大小与倾角之间的简并，从而显著提高参数约束的精度。

Conclusion: 在EMRI建模中纳入环境效应不仅是必要的模型修正，更是一种增强次级体固有自旋可探测性的有力工具。该方法有望成为探测超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）周围吸积流（accretion flow）的新型探针。

Abstract: Much like the aerodynamic deflection of a spinning curveball, a rotating secondary in an extreme-mass-ratio inspiral (EMRI) experiences Magnus and lift forces, in addition to the standard drag force, when traversing a gaseous environment. We present the first framework that incorporates these specific spin-coupled environmental effects (EEs) into the evolution of EMRI. Over the multi-year observation windows of space-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, these interactions imprint a unique, distinguishable dephasing signature on the signal. Crucially, a Fisher matrix analysis reveals that gas drag breaks the fundamental vacuum-projection degeneracy between the secondary's spin magnitude and inclination, thereby tightening parameter constraints. Thus, accounting for EEs is not merely a modeling necessity, but a powerful tool for enhancing the detectability of the secondary's intrinsic spin, and could serve as a novel probe of accretion flows harboring massive black holes.

### [96] [Ellis-Bronnikov Wormhole Shadows with Spherically Symmetric Accretion Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01699)
*Mikiya M. Takahashi,Keisuke Nakashi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过广义相对论辐射转移（GRRT）模拟，比较了Ellis-Bronnikov（EB）虫洞与Schwarzschild黑洞（BH）的观测图像差异，发现EB虫洞的阴影区和光子环均更亮，且两者均与M87*的事件视界望远镜（EHT）观测结果基本吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 区分虫洞与黑洞的观测特征是天体物理中的一个重要问题。本文旨在通过模拟探究EB虫洞与Schwarzschild黑洞在射电波段观测图像上的可区分性。

Method: 采用球对称稳态吸积流模型，结合同步辐射（synchrotron emission）机制，进行广义相对论辐射转移（GRRT）模拟，分别计算EB虫洞和Schwarzschild黑洞的辐射图像。

Result: 两类天体的模拟图像均呈现中心阴影区（shadow region）和明亮的光子环（photon ring）。EB虫洞的阴影区和光子环都比Schwarzschild黑洞更亮。该差异源于EB虫洞不存在事件视界（event horizon），喉部（throat）附近及以外区域的吸积物质辐射能够到达观测者。两类模型均与M87*的EHT观测结果合理一致。

Conclusion: EB虫洞与Schwarzschild黑洞在模拟图像上存在可观测的亮度差异，但当前EHT观测精度尚不足以区分二者；未来更精细的观测可能有助于检验虫洞假说。

Abstract: We investigate the observational differences between the Ellis--Bronnikov (EB) wormhole and the Schwarzschild black hole (BH) by performing general relativistic radiative transfer (GRRT) simulations. We consider a spherically symmetric steady-state accretion flow and perform GRRT simulations incorporating synchrotron emission. For both the EB wormhole and the Schwarzschild BH, the simulated images consist of a central shadow region and a bright photon ring. We find that both the shadow region and the photon ring of the EB wormhole are brighter than those of the Schwarzschild BH. These differences arise from the absence of an event horizon in the EB wormhole, allowing the emission from the accreting matter around and beyond the throat to contribute to the observed intensity. We also compare the simulated images with the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observations of M87* and find that both the EB wormhole and the Schwarzschild BH are in reasonable agreement with the current EHT results.

</details>


### [97] [The gravitational wave-black hole imaging correspondence for modified black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01915)
*David Díaz-Guerra,Ángel Rincón,Diego Rubiera-Garcia,Diego Saez-Chillon Gomez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文阐明并检验了黑洞电磁成像与引力波光谱之间在eikonal极限下的对应关系，发现即使对于低多极数ℓ，该对应关系在多个修改引力球对称黑洞几何中仍具有惊人的准确性，并讨论了其对未来联合多信使观测的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞可以通过电磁成像（electromagnetic imaging）和引力波光谱（ringdown GW spectroscopy）两种本质上不同的观测渠道进行研究，二者探测同一区域但编码不同的物理信息。已有文献指出某些物理量在eikonal极限下存在对应关系，但该对应的实际识别和精度尚未被系统澄清。

Method: 首先阐明在几何光学近似（geometric-optics approximation）的eikonal极限（即多极数ℓ取大值）下，黑洞准正则模（quasi-normal modes）的实部与虚部分别与临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）和Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）之间的对应关系。然后针对文献中提出的多个修改球对称黑洞几何模型，测试该对应在低ℓ值下的准确性。

Result: 对于所有测试的修改球对称黑洞几何模型，即使对于低多极数ℓ，该对应关系在关联准正则模的实部和虚部与近束缚光轨迹的临界碰撞参数和Lyapunov指数方面均表现出惊人的准确性。

Conclusion: 该结果对单一信使内部以及未来结合两种信使的黑洞检验均具有适用性，为联合多信使观测提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Black holes (BHs) can be studied via fundamentally different observational channels that probe complementary aspects of their physics. While BH imaging provides access to the quasi-static space-time geometry via the strong bending of light rays, gravitational wave (GW) observations probe the dynamical response of the space-time to time-dependent processes in the inspiral, merger and ringdown phases. Both messengers -- electromagnetic imaging probes and ringdown GW spectroscopy --, provide access to essentially the same region -- the one between the BH event horizon and the photon region --, but they do it via conceptually different methods, encoding different physical information. However, it has been shown in the literature that physical quantities supposedly exclusive of each such messenger are actually tightly related to each another via a correspondence that occurs in the eikonal limit (i.e. large values of the multipole number $\ell$) of the geometric-optics approximation. In this paper we clarify the actual identification of observables within such a correspondence and test its accuracy for a bunch of modified spherically symmetric BH geometries proposed in the literature. We find that even for low values of $\ell$ the correspondence is surprisingly accurate in relating the real and imaginary parts of quasi-normal modes in the GW ringdown phase with the critical impact parameter and Lyapunov exponent of nearly-bound light trajectories for every such model analyzed. We discuss the applicability of such a result both for each messenger individually, and also for foreseeable tests of BHs combining both messengers.

</details>


### [98] [Photon spheres in dynamical space-times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01916)
*David Díaz-Guerra,Ángel Rincón,Diego Rubiera-Garcia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新的协变方法（covariant approach）来描述动态球对称时空（dynamical spherical space-times）中的光子区域（photon region）与光子曲面（photon surface），该方法能够涵盖静态极限下的已知结果，并适用于恒星坍缩、吸积/蒸发等非稳态场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光子区域对于理解黑洞等致密天体附近的辐射行为至关重要，但以往研究主要局限于静态时空（stationary space-times），难以处理坍缩、吸积、蒸发等动态黑 hole 以及玻色子星等含时构型（time-dependent configurations）。因此，需要一种能够处理动态背景的通用描述框架。

Method: 作者发展了一种新协变方法（covariant approach）用于描述动态球对称时空中的辐射。该方法给出了光子曲面及其动力学的一般性数学描述，并在静态极限下恢复已知表达式的形式，同时澄清了其物理含义。

Result: 通过对恒星坍缩（stellar collapse）与吸积/蒸发模型（accreting/evaporating models）等多个动态场景的示例分析，验证了该方法的有效性，并展示了其在非静态时空中的适用性。同时，论文讨论了当前框架在这些场景中仍存在的未解决困难（open caveats）。

Conclusion: 该协变方法为研究动态球对称时空中的光子曲面提供了统一的描述框架，拓展了光子区域理论从静态到动态场景的适用范围，并为理解黑洞形成与演化过程中的辐射行为提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: The characterization of the photon region -- i.e. the region of space-time filled with unstable bound null geodesics -- is critical to understand the behavior of radiation near a compact-enough object, such as black holes. However, its study has been typically focused on stationary space-times that leave outside interesting theoretical and phenomenological scenarios such as collapsing, accreting, or evaporating black holes, besides time-dependent configurations such as those found in some boson star models. In this work, we present a novel covariant approach to describe radiation in dynamical spherical space-times. This allows a general description of photon surfaces and their dynamics in non-static space-times, recovering well known expressions in the static limit and clarifying their meanings. Furthermore, we illustrate our results via several examples of dynamical scenarios in stellar collapse and accreting/evaporating models, and discuss the open caveats regarding such scenarios.

### [99] [Astrophysical Applications of the Physics presented in the Film Interstellar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01921)
*Harleen Dhingra,Sanjeev Dhurandhar,Sanjit Mitra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于广义相对论（general relativity）计算，论证电影《星际穿越》中一颗行星在超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）附近轨道上产生的极端时间膨胀（extreme time dilation）现象在物理上是可能的。研究表明，只有快速旋转的克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）才能支持位于视界（event horizon）与内最稳定圆轨道（ISCO）之间的稳定束缚轨道，从而实现1小时对7年的时间比例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释并验证电影《星际穿越》中极端时间膨胀（time dilation）场景背后的真实物理学基础，分析其是否与广义相对论（general relativity）兼容。

Method: 基于广义相对论框架，分别针对非旋转的史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）和快速旋转的克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）进行轨道计算，检验极端时间膨胀所需轨道的存在条件。

Result: 对于非旋转的史瓦西黑洞，内最稳定圆轨道（ISCO）位于三倍史瓦西半径处，ISCO与视界之间不存在束缚轨道。但对于快速旋转的黑洞，广义相对论允许此类极端轨道存在。

Conclusion: 快速旋转的超大质量黑洞能够支持行星在视界附近运行，从而实现电影中1小时对应7年的极端时间膨胀效果。该计算结果不仅本身具有理论意义，还可能蕴含重要的天体物理学（astrophysical）启示。

Abstract: The film Interstellar is grounded in real physics calculations. A key requirement in the film is that of a planet orbiting a supermassive black hole such that one hour on the planet corresponds to seven years on Earth. Such extreme time dilation is possible only if the planet orbits the black hole very close to its horizon. For a non-rotating (Schwarzschild) black hole, the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) lies at three times the Schwarzschild radius; a bound orbit between the ISCO and the event horizon is not possible. Surprisingly, general relativity allows such orbits to exist if the black hole is spinning rapidly. In this work, we present computations that are non-trivial and interesting in themselves, but more importantly, they may have useful astrophysical implications.

</details>


### [100] [Effective dynamics of a homogeneous and isotropic universe with quantum curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01930)
*Ilkka Mäkinen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准圈量子宇宙学模型在描述均匀各向同性宇宙时仍存在改进空间，尤其是在哈密顿量中如何更自然地引入空间曲率效应。该工作试图通过量子约化圈引力（quantum-reduced loop gravity）中单顶点模型（one-vertex model）的启发式论证，构造一种新的LQC模型，以探索宇宙动力学在更一般框架下的表现。

Method: 在标准圈量子宇宙学的哈密顿量中添加一个与空间流形标量曲率对应的洛伦兹项，该新项的表达源自量子约化圈引力中单顶点模型对标量曲率算符形式的启发式推导；基于修正后的哈密顿量推导有效动力学方程。

Result: 新模型的有效动力学与标准LQC不完全相同，但定性再现了所有关键动力学特征；经典宇宙奇点被量子反弹所取代，有效动力学轨迹在时间上关于反弹对称；与标准LQC相比，反弹发生在显著更低的体积值处。

Conclusion: 通过引入基于量子约化圈引力启发的洛伦兹修正项，所提出的新LQC模型在保持标准模型核心定性特征的同时，展现出定量差异（尤其是反弹体积显著降低），表明该模型是有前景的替代框架，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: We consider the effective dynamics of a new, tentative model of a homogeneous and isotropic universe in loop quantum cosmology. The new model consists of modifying the standard Hamiltonian of loop quantum cosmology by adding a Lorentzian term corresponding to the scalar curvature of the spatial manifold. The expression of the new Lorentzian term is motivated by a heuristic argument based on the form of an operator representing the scalar curvature in the one-vertex model of quantum-reduced loop gravity. The effective dynamics of the new model is not identical to standard LQC but all the key features of the dynamics are qualitatively reproduced. The classical cosmological singularity is resolved by a "quantum bounce" and the effective dynamics trajectory as a function of time is symmetric around the bounce; however, in comparison with the standard LQC scenario the bounce takes place at a significantly lower value of the volume.

### [101] [Stress-energy tensor of quantized scalar fields in thermal states on a zero-tidal wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01980)
*Shun Jiang,Xiangdong Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了零潮汐力虫洞喉部上量子有质量标量场在热态下的应力-能量张量，发现Morris-Thorne条件仅在标量场质量处于特定有界区间内且温度低于质量依赖的临界温度时才能满足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态可穿越虫洞（static traversable wormhole）的构造需要满足Morris-Thorne条件的奇异物质（exotic matter），而量子能量-动量张量长期以来被认为是最有希望的候选者。本文旨在通过首个数值计算检验这一候选方案的有效性。

Method: 针对位于零潮汐力虫洞（zero-tidal-force wormhole）喉部上的量子有质量标量场（quantum massive scalar field），计算其在热态（thermal states）下的应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor），并系统扫描标量场的无量纲温度（dimensionless temperature）和无量纲质量（dimensionless mass）参数空间。

Result: Morris-Thorne条件仅在标量场质量落于特定的有界区间（bounded interval）内时才能被满足。对于该区间内的任意质量，均存在一个依赖于质量的临界温度（critical temperature）：只有当温度低于此临界阈值时，Morris-Thorne条件才得以成立。

Conclusion: 量子有质量标量场在热态下可以充当虫洞所需的奇异物质，但其参数选择受到严格约束——质量和温度必须同时满足特定限制条件。

Abstract: The construction of a static traversable wormhole requires exotic matter that satisfies the Morris-Thorne conditions. Quantum energy-momentum tensors have long been considered the most promising candidate for such exotic matter. In this paper, we present the first calculation of the stress-energy tensor for a quantum massive scalar field in thermal states localized on the throat of a zero-tidal-force wormhole. By varying the dimensionless temperature and dimensionless mass of the scalar field, we find that the Morris-Thorne conditions can only be satisfied when the scalar field mass falls within a specific bounded interval. Furthermore, for any scalar field mass within this interval, there always exists a mass-dependent dimensionless critical temperature: the Morris-Thorne conditions are fulfilled only if the temperature remains below this critical threshold.

### [102] [3d Summation-by-Parts scheme for Linear Wave Equations on Hyperboloidal Slices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02051)
*Anuraag Reddy,Shalabh Gautam,Prayush Kumar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在闵可夫斯基背景下的超双曲切片上，针对一类线性波动方程推导了一个完全三维的求和-分部（Summation-By-Parts, SBP）格式。该格式在球极坐标下构建，通过紧致化与重标度处理奇点，可证明稳定，并给出了耗散算子的抽象处理与新的范数收敛测试方法，有望应用于完全非线性系统（如爱因斯坦场方程）的引力波提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数值格式在球极坐标下处理原点、z轴坐标奇点以及未来零无穷（future null infinity）边界时缺乏稳定性保证；且线性测试的成功结果难以直接推广至非线性引力系统。本文旨在构建一个可证明稳定、能处理上述奇点与无穷远边界的三维SBP格式，为后续完全非线性系统（如爱因斯坦场方程）的引力波数值提取奠定基础。

Method: 采用球极坐标（spherical polar coordinates）下的三维求和-分部（Summation-By-Parts, SBP）格式；通过紧致化（compactification）后引入重标度（rescaling）将无穷远边界纳入计算域。在约束添加项上发现保持对称双曲性（symmetric hyperbolicity）的条件；使用二阶精度的有限差分方法（finite-difference methods）进行数值实现，并可推广至高阶或谱精度。耗散算子（dissipation operators）在曲线坐标下进行抽象定义，使其在整个域（含边界点）满足能量范数中的耗散性质（dissipative property, DP）；当退化为笛卡尔网格内部时，该算子即为标准的Kreiss-Oliger耗散算子。

Result: 重标度因子与紧致化因子之间建立了简化的方程关系；发现了维持对称双曲性的约束添加项条件。耗散算子被推广至曲线坐标含边界点的情形，并在能量范数下满足DP性质。提出了新的范数收敛测试（norm convergence tests）方法，可获得更精确的输出结果。

Conclusion: 该格式可证明稳定并成功处理坐标奇点与无穷远边界，数值实验取得了有前景的结果。这为将来应用于完全非线性系统（如爱因斯坦场方程）并提取无系统误差或规范歧义（gauge ambiguities）的引力波提供了可能性。

Abstract: We derive a fully 3-dimensional Summation-By-Parts scheme for a class of linear wave equations on hyperboloidal slices that meet future null infinity on a Minkowski background. The scheme is derived in spherical polar coordinates, with a major strength being that it is provably stable and allows having grid points at the origin and on the $z$-axis, despite coordinate singularities, and at infinity, by introducing compactification followed by rescaling. Reducing it to the standard Cauchy problem, or on finite spacelike slices with an outer boundary, will follow a similar procedure. Interesting relations are obtained between the rescaling and compactification factors that simplify the equations, and the conditions on constraint addition terms are discovered to maintain symmetric hyperbolicity. Numerical implementation is achieved using finite-difference methods at second-order accuracy, which can be generalized to higher-order or spectral accuracies as well. Dissipation operators are given a more abstract treatment, which makes it possible to define them everywhere in the domain, including at the boundary points, in curvilinear coordinates, such that they satisfy the dissipative property (DP) in our energy norms. These generalizations reduce to the well-known Kreiss-Oliger dissipation operators whenever defined on a Cartesian grid in the bulk and satisfy the DP in the standard $L^2$-norms. We also propose new norm convergence tests that produce more accurate outputs. Promising results are obtained, giving hope for application to fully nonlinear systems, like the Einstein Field Equations, and extracting the resulting gravitational waves free of systematic errors or gauge ambiguities.

</details>


### [103] [Near-Horizon Deformation of Metric and the Black Hole Instability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02066)
*Shi-Jie Ma,Zhan-Feng Mai,Run-Qiu Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过频域分析（frequency-domain analysis）系统研究了静态局域非正扰动下黑洞的准正则模（quasi-normal mode）谱。研究发现此类形变会诱发一个新的纯虚模式，当形变靠近视界时，该模式的虚部增大并进入上半复频率平面，标志着黑洞不稳定性（instability）的触发。数值结果揭示了不稳定性临界距离与扰动强度之间的标度关系（scaling relations），并给出了严格的频域证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期时域分析（time-domain analysis）表明，黑洞稳定性可能对近视界局域几何形变（localized near-horizon geometric deformations）敏感，但背后的谱机制（spectral mechanism）尚不明确。本文旨在澄清这一不稳定的谱起源。

Method: 采用频域框架（frequency-domain framework），系统研究了静态局域非正扰动（static localized non-positive perturbations）下的准正则模谱（quasi-normal mode spectrum）。结合数值计算与严格数学证明。

Result: 局域形变会诱发一个全新的纯虚模式（purely imaginary mode）。当形变靠近视界时，该模式虚部增加并进入上半复频率平面（upper half complex-frequency plane），触发不稳定性。不稳定性临界距离与形变强度之间存在清晰的标度关系。

Conclusion: 黑洞在长尺度下的稳定性对近视界度规（metric）的局域形变具有条件敏感性，本文建立了一个统一的谱框架（spectral framework）来理解这类形变诱发的不稳定性。

Abstract: Recent time-domain analyses suggest that black hole stability may be sensitive to localized near-horizon geometric deformations, while the underlying spectral mechanism remains unclear. In this work, we systematically investigate quasi-normal mode spectra under static localized non-positive perturbations within a frequency-domain framework. We find that such deformations generically induce a new purely imaginary mode. As the deformation approaches the horizon, the imaginary part of this mode increases and eventually enters the upper half complex-frequency plane, signaling the onset of black hole instability. Numerical results reveal clear scaling relations between the critical distance for instability and the deformation strength. We further derive rigorous proofs for our discoveries in frequency domain. These results demonstrate that black hole stability under long scale is conditionally sensitive to localized deformation of metric near the horizon and establish a unified spectral framework for understanding their induced instabilities.

</details>


### [104] [Spectral suppression of black hole ringdown tails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02146)
*Jose Antonio León Vega,Alejandro Svyatkovskyy Kholyavka,Sayak Datta,Xisco Jiménez Forteza*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文揭示并量化了Price定律晚期幂律尾在数值相对论双黑洞并合波形中缺失的物理机制：振荡源的光谱结构会指数级抑制分支切割激发系数，抑制程度由载波频率与谱宽之比决定。解析导出的首阶和次阶尾系数与数值拟合在10%以内吻合，首次从第一性原理解释了准圆并合中尾的缺失以及正碰和偏心并合中尾的增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Price定律预测的晚期幂律尾（power law tail）是黑洞微扰论（black hole perturbation theory）的普遍特征，但在数值相对论（numerical relativity）的双黑洞并合波形中却大量缺失。该矛盾长期缺乏物理解释，因此有必要揭示其背后的抑制机制。

Method: 通过分析振荡源（oscillatory sources）的光谱结构，引入载波频率ν与特征宽度σ，推导分支切割激发系数（branch-cut excitation coefficient）的抑制因子α=σν。对高斯脉冲（Gaussian pulse），抑制为指数形式e^{-α^2/2}，并通过时域Regge-Wheeler演化验证其精确性。

Result: 分支切割激发系数被因子α=σν抑制；对高斯脉冲，抑制程度为e^{-α^2/2}，该结果经Regge-Wheeler时域演化精确确认。解析推导出首阶（leading-order）与次阶（next-to-leading-order）尾系数，与数值拟合的偏差在10%以内。

Conclusion: 控制黑洞响应从宽带（broadband）到频率选择性（frequency selective）转变的同一参数也负责尾的抑制。该工作从第一性原理（first principle）解释了准圆并合（quasi-circular mergers）中尾的缺失以及正碰（head-on）和偏心（eccentric）并合中尾的增强。

Abstract: The late-time power law tail predicted by Price's law is a generic feature of black hole perturbation theory, yet it is largely absent in numerical relativity waveforms of binary black hole mergers. We show that this suppression arises from the spectral structure of oscillatory sources. For a generic perturbation with carrier frequency $ν$ and characteristic width $σ$, the branch-cut excitation coefficient governing the tail is suppressed by $α=σν$. For a Gaussian pulse, the suppression $\sim e^{-α^2/2}$. This suppression is exact and confirmed by the time domain Regge Wheeler evolutions. The same parameter that controls the transition from broadband to frequency selective black hole response is also responsible for the tail suppression. Moreover, we analytically derive the leading- and next-to-leading-order tail coefficients, finding agreement with numerical fits below the $\sim10\%$ level. Our results provide a first principle explanation for the absence of tails in quasi-circular mergers and their enhancement in head-on and eccentric ones.

</details>


### [105] [Poincaré asymptotic expansion in black hole theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02205)
*Giampiero Esposito,Marco Refuto*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文综述了黑洞理论中通过分离变量法和主张量（principal tensor）将场方程径向部分分离的方法，并利用庞加莱渐近级数展开（Poincaré asymptotic series expansion）研究场在类空无穷远（spacelike infinity）处的行为，得到了可计算至任意精度的级数解，最终应用于拟正则模（quasinormal modes）分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在黑洞理论中，场在类空无穷远邻域内的行为因该区域的非正则（irregular）性质而难以精确求解，仅能得到近似解。作者旨在通过庞加莱渐近级数展开这一工具，获取可任意精度的径向解，从而更深入地分析这一具有挑战性的时空区域。

Method: 首先回顾了Petrov-D度规中主张量（principal tensor）的存在性如何支撑分离变量法（separation of variables），从而将完整解中的径向部分孤立出来。随后引入庞加莱渐近级数展开（Poincaré asymptotic series expansion），对径向解在类空无穷远邻域进行渐近展开，生成可计算至任意精度的级数。

Result: 获得了一个可计算至任意精度的级数展开形式，从而能够对类空无穷远这一难以解析处理的空间区域进行更深入的定量分析。

Conclusion: 该渐近级数方法为黑洞场方程在类空无穷远处的行为提供了可任意精度的描述，并最终被应用于拟正则模（quasinormal modes）的研究中。

Abstract: In studying the dynamics of fields in black hole theory, the method of separation of variables makes it possible to isolate the radial part of the full solution in many important physical cases. This is possible thanks to the existence of the principal tensor in Petrov-D metrics. We first review this mathematical result in order to introduce several cases where it is possible to study the radial solution via the Poincaré asymptotic series expansion, a tool exploited in recent work by the authors in order to investigate the behaviour of the field at spacelike infinity, a point in the neighbourhood of which only approximate solutions are computable by virtue of its irregular nature. We obtain a series which can be computed to any degree of accuracy, allowing for a deeper analysis of this challenging spacetime region. An application to quasinormal modes is eventually provided.

</details>


### [106] [Equivalence Principle violation in metric-affine gravity and finite-temperature effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02329)
*Emmanuele Battista,Roberto Campagnola,Salvatore Capozziello,Giuseppe Fiorillo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在度规-仿射引力（metric-affine gravity）框架下研究等效原理（equivalence principle）的可能违反，将其与有限温度效应相联系，并引入广义Fermi-Walker导数以揭示等效原理在非黎曼几何下的几何特征性破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨等效原理在度规-仿射引力中可能存在的违背，并阐明其与有限温度效应之间的内在联系，从而拓展对引力基本定律的检验范围。

Method: 在黎曼几何框架下评估量子场论导出的粒子动力学热修正，并将其延伸至度规-仿射引力；通过引入广义Fermi-Walker导数（Fermi-Walker derivative），分析非度规张量（non-metricity tensor）对牛顿引力定律的修正及正交标架传播的几何约束。

Result: 有限温度效应会导致引力质量与惯性质量之比的偏移，度规-仿射引力中的非度规张量以类似方式修正牛顿定律；广义Fermi-Walker导数表明无法沿观测者世界线传播正交标架（orthonormal tetrad），从而在几何层面显示等效原理的现代表述不再成立。

Conclusion: 尽管度规-仿射引力在规范理论的基本物质形式层面可实现点态（pointwise）的爱因斯坦等效原理，但新引入的几何算符表明该原理在现代表述下并不普遍保留，并讨论了相关效应的潜在实验检验途径。

Abstract: Possible violations of the equivalence principle are investigated within the framework of metric-affine gravity and their connection to finite-temperature effects are highlighted. Thermal corrections to particle dynamics, originally derived in a quantum-field-theory setting, can be evaluated in a purely Riemannian framework and lead to a shift in the gravitational-to-inertial mass ratio. We show that the ensuing departure from universality of free fall can be also formulated in metric-affine gravity, where the presence of the non-metricity tensor modifies the Newtonian law in a way that closely parallels the finite-temperature scenario. Furthermore, we introduce a generalized Fermi-Walker derivative adapted to non-Riemannian contexts, which naturally reveals that no orthonormal tetrad can be propagated along an observer worldline. Although metric-affine gravity admits a pointwise realization of the Einstein equivalence principle in its gauge-theoretic, elementary-matter form, the new operator offers a direct geometric signature that this principle, in its modern formulation, is not retained in general. Potential tests of the analyzed effects are also discussed.

</details>


### [107] [Black Bounce via Gravitational Tension Screening Acting as an Analogue of Schwinger Corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02393)
*Milko Estrada*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于引力张力饱和（gravitational tension saturation）的新型几何正则化机制，用以生成黑跳时空（black bounce spacetimes）。通过引入类似Schwinger饱和效应的有效引力张力屏蔽，尺度函数获得与张力相关的修正，从而动态产生正则反弹结构，无需引入人为的正则核心。该机制可生成球对称、平面和双曲横截面的正则几何，涵盖正则黑洞（RBHs）、极端RBHs和可穿越虫洞（traversable wormholes）。反弹位置由引力张力与几何屏蔽之间的相互作用动态决定，饱和效应不仅影响致密天体短尺度的内部结构，还可能改变其全局几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑跳时空构造通常需引入人为的正则核心（ad hoc regular core），缺乏自洽的动力学起源。本文旨在提出一种基于引力张力饱和的几何正则化机制，使反弹结构从张力与几何屏蔽的动力学相互作用中自然涌现。

Method: 假设与真空几何相关的引力张力在高曲率短尺度区域不会无限增长，而是动态趋近一个有限临界值，从而引入类似Schwinger饱和效应的有效引力张力屏蔽。尺度函数由此获得与张力相关的修正项，驱动几何自动形成反弹结构。

Result: 该机制可生成球对称、平面和双曲三种横截面的正则几何（正则黑洞、极端正则黑洞和可穿越虫洞）。反弹位置由引力张力与几何屏蔽的相互作用动态决定，可能出现在短尺度区域或被推向更大有限尺度区域。双曲和平面正则黑洞在反弹附近可能满足标准能量条件（energy conditions）；双曲几何还呈现负质量构型等独特特征。虫洞几何的支撑物质源在喉部附近违反能量条件。

Conclusion: 饱和效应不仅能修改致密天体在短尺度上的内部结构，还能改变其全局几何，表明该机制为黑跳时空提供了一种自洽的动力学正则化途径。

Abstract: We provide a novel geometric regularization mechanism for black bounce spacetimes based on an effective gravitational tension screening inspired by Schwinger like saturation effects. The construction assumes that the gravitational tension associated with the vacuum geometry does not grow indefinitely in high curvature and short scales regimes, but dynamically approaches a finite critical value. As a result, the scale function acquires tension dependent corrections, giving rise to a regular bounce structure without introducing ad hoc regular cores. The mechanism generates regular geometries with spherical, planar, and hyperbolic transverse sections, describing regular black holes (RBHs), extremal RBHs, and traversable wormholes. A key result is that the bounce location emerges dynamically from the interplay between gravitational tension and geometric screening. Depending on the regime, the bounce may remain associated with short distance scales or be displaced toward larger finite scale regions, indicating that saturation effects can modify not only the inner structure of compact objects at short scales but also their global geometry. Hiperbolic and planar RBHs may satisfy the standard energy conditions near the bounce. Moreover, the hyperbolic geometry exhibits distinctive features, including regular negative mass configurations and a strong dependence of the energy conditions on the system parameters. In contrast, the matter sources supporting wormhole geometries, as expected, violate the energy conditions near the throat.

</details>


### [108] [Dyonic Quark Stars in Quasi-Topological Electromagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02511)
*Michael Gammon,Nicola De Kock,Robert B. Mann,Amos Kubeka*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索刘等人提出的准拓扑电磁学（QTEM）——一种暗能量（dark energy）形式——在夸克星（quark star）解中的表现，以理解该非线性理论在双荷电荷情形下产生的非平凡动力学效应。

Method: 在纯QTEM框架下考虑双荷（dyonic）电荷分布，通过求解相应的引力场方程获得夸克星解，并扫描参数空间以分析不同双荷电荷比下的星体结构演化。

Result: 双荷电荷分布使夸克星特征性的“钩状”（hook）M-R曲线向更大质量和半径偏移；在双荷电荷比较小的情形下，系统出现第二个分支，对应于具有负压外壳与正压核心的极大质量、大半径星体。随着参数变化，两分支在M/R空间中合并，并在大电荷比下演化为“回形针”（paperclip）形状。

Conclusion: 准拓扑电磁学的非线性效应在双荷电荷情形下能显著改变夸克星的结构，产生多分支的M-R关系，这为进一步检验该暗能量模型提供了可能的观测特征。

Abstract: In this paper we consider quark star solutions to Liu et al.'s \cite{Liu_2019} quasi-topological electromagnetism (QTEM), a recently proposed form of dark energy. Since the QTEM contribution is trivial for pure electric/magnetic charge, we consider the dyonic case in pure QTEM which does induce (dark) non-trivial dynamics from the non-linear theory. Besides the introduction of a dyonic charge distribution generally pushing the characteristic quark star `hook' shape to larger masses and radii, it also induces a second branch at very large mass and radius for stars with a small dyonic charge ratio. This second set of solutions have a negative pressure envelope surrounding a positive pressure core. As we explore the parameter space these features interact and evolve in interesting ways, with the two branches eventually merging in $M/R$ space before settling into a characteristic `paperclip' shape as the dyonic charge ratio becomes large.

</details>


### [109] [Teleocosmology and quantum post-selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02514)
*Paul C. W. Davies,João Magueijo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出宇宙加速膨胀并非源于宇宙常数（cosmological constant）或新场，而是纯量子力学（quantum mechanics）中的边界条件效应：通过对宇宙波函数（wave function of the universe）施加初态和末态边界条件（pre- and post-selection），在无宇宙学常数（Λ=0）的哈密顿量下依然产生加速行为，该效应可被经典模型误读为幻影暗能量（phantom dark energy, w<-1）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙加速膨胀的物理起源尚存争议，主流解释依赖非零真空能或新场，作者希望提出一种无需引入额外常数或局域源的替代机制。

Method: 将实验室量子力学中的前选择与后选择（pre- and post-selection）概念推广至微超空间量子宇宙学（minisuperspace quantum cosmology）；先用自由非相对论粒子的波包进行类比演示，再用量子宇宙学中的联络变量（connection variables）和单模时间（unimodular time）构造类似的双边界振幅（two-boundary amplitude），其中前向波包描述纯辐射，末态选为可归一化的陈-西蒙斯孤子（Chern-Simons soliton）。

Result: 双边界振幅下的波包峰值会离开辐射轨迹并进入加速区域，而前向哈密顿量中Λ=0。经典模型若要模拟该轨迹，必须引入一个在过渡区近似w≃-1、外推后变为强幻影行为（w<-1）的有效成分。

Conclusion: 该加速效应更自然的解释是量子边界条件效应，而非局域经典源；文中还讨论了陈-西蒙斯孤子作为干净末态的理由、初末态重叠小等问题及潜在的可观测特征。

Abstract: Although cosmic acceleration is well established, its physical origin remains contentious. Most explanations invoke either a non-zero vacuum energy, i.e. a cosmological constant, or new fields. We propose instead a mechanism arising purely from quantum mechanics, without additional constants or local sources. The key point is that quantum theory permits both initial and final boundary conditions on a state, here the wave function of the universe. Pre- and post-selected systems are familiar in laboratory quantum mechanics; we extend the idea to minisuperspace quantum cosmology. As a warm-up, we show that a free non-relativistic particle, initially in a semiclassical wave packet and conditioned on a final quantum state, can have an intermediate peak which accelerates even though the Hamiltonian is free. A semiclassical observer would infer a contrived classical force. We then implement the analogous construction in quantum cosmology using connection variables and unimodular time. A forward semiclassical packet, taken for simplicity to describe pure radiation, is post-selected by a normalizable Chern-Simons soliton. The resulting two-boundary amplitude has a peak which leaves the radiation trajectory and enters an accelerating regime, while the forward Hamiltonian has $Λ=0$. A classical model can mimic this trajectory only by introducing a contrived effective component: near the transition it resembles $w\simeq -1$, but when extrapolated it evolves towards strongly phantom behaviour, $w<-1$. The acceleration is therefore more naturally interpreted as a quantum boundary-condition effect than as a local classical source. We also discuss why the Chern-Simons soliton is a clean final state, the small overlap between initial and final states, and possible tell-tale signatures.

</details>


### [110] [COSMOS: A numerical relativity code specialized for PBH formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02053)
*Chul-Moon Yoo,Hirotada Okawa,Albert Escrivà,Tomohiro Harada,Hayami Iizuka,Taishi Ikeda,Yasutaka Koga,Daiki Saito,Masaaki Shimada,Koichiro Uehara*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍了COSMOS，一个用于模拟原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes, PBHs）形成的C++数值相对论（numerical relativity）求解器。它通过非笛卡尔尺度变换坐标、固定网格细化（mesh-refinement）以及OpenMP并行化，求解3+1维爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations），支持无质量标量场（massless scalar field）和线性状态方程完美流体（perfect fluid）作为物质场，且无外部依赖，安装简便。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（PBHs）形成于早期宇宙、不经过恒星演化，其标准形成过程涉及超视界（super-horizon）且初始振幅非线性地大的原初涨落（primordial fluctuations）。为模拟这种非线性引力动力学，必须依赖数值相对论（numerical relativity）求解器来近似求解爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations），但现有工具在易用性和资源占用上仍存在不足。

Method: COSMOS采用C++语言，在3+1维框架下求解爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）。为分辨塌缩区域，实现了非笛卡尔尺度变换坐标（non-Cartesian scale-up coordinates）和固定网格细化（fixed mesh-refinement）程序；物质场方面支持无质量标量场（massless scalar field）和具有线性状态方程（linear equation of state）的完美流体（perfect fluid）；利用OpenMP实现并行化以提升计算速度，且无其他外部依赖以便于安装。

Result: COSMOS提供了模拟原初黑洞（PBHs）形成的简单工具集，通过非笛卡尔坐标和网格细化有效分辨塌缩区域，借助OpenMP并行化获得了可接受的计算速度，同时无外部依赖的特点降低了安装复杂度。

Conclusion: COSMOS是一个针对原初黑洞（PBH）形成模拟而设计的轻量级数值相对论（numerical relativity）求解器，兼具分辨率、并行效率和易安装性，有望为相关研究提供实用的计算工具。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) are black holes generated in the early universe without having gone through stellar evolution. In the standard formation process, PBHs are formed from super-horizon primordial fluctuations with non-linearly large initial amplitude. In order to simulate the non-linear gravitational dynamics of PBH formation, one has to rely on numerical relativity solvers to approximate the solution of the Einstein equations. COSMOS is a C++ package for solving the Einstein equations in 3+1 dimensions, providing simple tools for the simulation of PBH formation. In order to resolve the collapsing region, non-Cartesian scale-up coordinates and a fixed mesh-refinement procedure are implemented. In COSMOS, a massless scalar field and a perfect fluid with a linear equation of state are implemented as matter fields. To achieve a practically acceptable computational speed, OpenMP is used for the parallelization. COSMOS has no other dependencies, which makes for an easier installation.

</details>

### [111] [A Cohesive $\infty$-Topos with a Quantum Modality from Finite-Dimensional $C^{*}$-Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02269)
*Joey Woo*

Main category: math.CT

TL;DR: 本文在函子∞-意象 Fun(C*Alg_fd, H_sm) 中构建了一个带有量子模態（quantum modality）的凝聚∞-意象，该模態由中心函子誘導的餘代數給出，並證明了 Day 卷積給出乘法直覺線性邏輯（multiplicative intuitionistic linear logic）的非退化仿射模型，同時證明了合成不可克隆定理（synthetic no-cloning theorem），為凝聚線性同倫類型論提供了首個具體模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有凝聚∞-意象框架和線性同倫類型論均無具體模型；本文旨在填補這一空白，構造一個具體的凝聚線性∞-意象模型，並在該模型中檢驗量子信息論中的核心概念，如退相干（decoherence）和不可克隆定理（no-cloning theorem）。

Method: 以光滑凝聚∞-意象 H_sm 為基礎，選取有限維 C*-代數（finite-dimensional C*-algebra）範疇 C*Alg_fd 作為指標範疇，構造函子∞-意象 Fun(C*Alg_fd, H_sm)；利用中心函子（centre functor）的前復合定義量子餘單子 Q^◇（quantum comonad）；在 Day 卷積（Day convolution）么半結構下分析其代數性質。

Result: Q^◇ 是強么半餘單子（strong monoidal comonad）；其餘代數範疇通過 Gelfand 對偶等價於離散經典場論意象 Fun(FinSet^op, H_sm)；Day 卷積給出乘法直覺線性邏輯（multiplicative intuitionistic linear logic, MILL）的非退化仿射模型；證明了合成不可克隆定理。

Conclusion: 本文提供了凝聚線性框架（cohesive linear framework）的首個嚴格實例，解決了凝聚線性同倫類型論（cohesive linear homotopy type theory）的開放模型問題；同時指出中心模態在表示量子信道（quantum channel）時存在侷限。

Abstract: We construct a cohesive $\infty$-topos $\mathbf{H}_{\mathbb{Q}}$ equipped with a \emph{quantum modality} -- an idempotent product-preserving comonad $Q^{\diamond}$ with right adjoint $Q_{\bullet}$ satisfying the Beck--Chevalley compatibility conditions with the cohesive structure $(Π,\flat,\sharp)$. The model is the functor $\infty$-topos $\operatorname{Fun}(\mathbf{C}^{*}\mathbf{Alg}_{\mathrm{fd}},\; \mathbf{H}_{\mathrm{sm}})$, where $\mathbf{H}_{\mathrm{sm}}$ is the smooth cohesive $\infty$-topos and $\mathbf{C}^{*}\mathbf{Alg}_{\mathrm{fd}}$ is the category of finite-dimensional $C^{*}$-algebras with centre-preserving $*$-homomorphisms. Cohesion is lifted pointwise from $\mathbf{H}_{\mathrm{sm}}$; the quantum comonad is precomposition with the centre functor. We endow the topos with the Day convolution monoidal structure $\otimes_{\mathrm{Day}}$ induced by the tensor product of $C^{*}$-algebras and prove that $Q^{\diamond}$ is a strong monoidal comonad. The category of $Q^{\diamond}$-coalgebras is equivalent, via Gelfand duality, to the topos $\operatorname{Fun}(\mathbf{FinSet}^{\mathrm{op}},\mathbf{H}_{\mathrm{sm}})$ of discrete classical field theories. The comonad is interpreted as decoherence. This yields a cohesive linear $\infty$-topos in which the cartesian linear-logic structure degenerates, while the Day convolution provides a non-degenerate affine model of multiplicative intuitionistic linear logic. We also prove a synthetic no-cloning theorem and discuss the limits of the centre modality for representing quantum channels. This work provides the first rigorous instance of the cohesive linear framework and settles the open problem of finding a concrete model for cohesive linear homotopy type theory.

</details>

### [112] [Bragg-enhanced time-domain Brillouin scattering from a propagating acoustic grating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02012)
*O. S. Ken,D. O. Horiachyi,V. L. Korenev,A. V. Trifonov,I. A. Akimov,D. R. Yakovlev,M. Bayer*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过1 GHz高频激光脉冲串在半导体中产生并探测传播的一维声学光栅，实现了相干声子光谱的塑造以及布里渊光散射在选定探测波长处的显著共振增强，在GaAs和(Cd,Zn)Te单晶中观察到10–30倍信号增强，并预期通过进一步光谱窄化可实现约100–150倍的增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用飞秒光脉冲在半导体中产生并探测相干声子（coherent phonons）是实现对其电子性质进行高频声学调控的有效手段，因此有必要发展能够塑造相干声子光谱并增强声光相互作用的新方法。

Method: 采用重复频率为1 GHz的高重频激光脉冲串对半导体进行带隙以上（above-band-gap）激发，在体材料中形成传播的一维声学光栅（acoustic grating）；结合泵浦-探测（pump-probe）配置测量时域布里渊光散射（time-domain Brillouin light scattering）信号。

Result: 在5 K低温下，于体单晶GaAs和(Cd,Zn)Te中观察到时域布里渊光散射振幅在离散探测波长处出现共振峰，源于探测光被传播的声学光栅的布拉格反射（Bragg reflection）；在GaAs和(Cd,Zn)Te中分别实现了10–30倍的信号共振增强，受限于探测脉冲的有限光谱宽度。

Conclusion: 通过进一步光谱窄化，预期可实现约100–150倍的增强，该上限由样品内声学光栅中的应变脉冲数目N决定，并最终受限于材料参数和样品厚度。

Abstract: Generation and detection of coherent phonons in semiconductors by femtosecond optical pulses is a powerful tool for high-frequency acoustic control of their electronic properties. Here, we demonstrate a propagating one-dimensional acoustic grating in bulk semiconductors using above-band-gap excitation by a train of laser pulses with high repetition rate of 1 GHz. This approach enables shaping of the coherent acoustic phonon spectrum and leads to a significant enhancement of Brillouin light scattering at selected probe wavelengths in pump-probe configuration. We demonstrate this effect at a cryogenic temperature of 5 K in prototypical semiconductor systems, namely bulk crystalline GaAs and (Cd,Zn)Te, which serve as benchmark materials for the proposed method. The spectral dependence of the time-domain Brillouin light scattering amplitude exhibits resonant peaks at discrete probe wavelengths arising from Bragg reflection of the probe light by the propagating acoustic grating. A 10-30-fold resonant enhancement of the signal amplitude is observed for GaAs and (Cd,Zn)Te, determined by the finite spectral width of the probe pulse. With further spectral narrowing, enhancements of the order ~ 100-150 are expected, set by the number N of strain pulses in the acoustic grating within the sample and ultimately limited by the material parameters and sample thickness.

### [113] [Ultrafast internal dynamics of chiral domain walls probed by time-resolved XRMS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02154)
*Dmitriy Ksenzov,Flavio Capotondi,Nicolas Jaouen,Raphael Gruber,Vincent Cros,Mathias Kläui,Matteo Pancaldi,Emanuele Pedersoli,Nicolas Reyren,Christian Gutt*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究回纹条纹畴中手性Néel型畴壁在皮秒时间尺度上的超快动力学，特别是畴壁内部模式的响应行为。

Method: 采用时间分辨X射线共振磁散射（time-resolved XRMS）技术，结合螺旋度求和与二向色信号分析，测量激光激发后条纹畴的动力学响应。

Result: 螺旋度求和信号呈现超快退磁、恢复及弱振荡（源于相干表面声子）；二向色信号呈现强振荡响应，频率随泵浦通量增大而降低，表明畴壁内禀模式的软化。

Conclusion: 时间分辨XRMS能够有效隔离畴壁特异性动力学，揭示无序条纹织构中内部畴壁运动的皮秒时间尺度信息，为研究畴壁内禀模式提供实验途径。

Abstract: We measure picosecond dynamics of labyrinthine stripe domains with chiral Néel-type domain walls using time-resolved x-ray resonant magnetic scattering (XRMS). At the stripe-domain wavevector, the helicity-summed signal shows ultrafast demagnetization, recovery, and a weak oscillatory contribution that we identify as a signature of laser-launched coherent surface phonons. In contrast, the dichroic signal, which is sensitive to the in-plane magnetization inside the Néel walls, shows a strong oscillatory response whose frequency decreases with increasing pump fluence. We attribute this softening to pump-induced changes in the effective anisotropy and saturation magnetization, which modify the restoring field of an internal domain-wall mode. Time-resolved XRMS thus isolates wall-specific dynamics and provides access to internal domain-wall motion in disordered stripe textures on picosecond time scales.
