### [114] [Linear Motility Maps in Nonlinear Viscous Fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00063)
*Yishun Zhou,Shai Revzen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文证明，低雷诺数流体中的线性运动性映射（linear motility map）可推广至幂律流体（power-law fluid），但在Carreau-Yasuda流体中该线性关系可被打破，从而在不依赖非互易变形（non-reciprocal deformation）的条件下产生净位移，甚至可通过改变运动速度切换方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于Purcell的扇贝定理（Scallop Theorem）指出，在低雷诺数流体中，互易变形无法产生净位移。该定理依赖于流体阻力的线性速度关系，但许多生物体液在中等剪切范围内呈非线性（如幂律或Carreau-Yasuda流体），因此需要检验该定理是否仍然成立。

Method: 本文通过理论分析将线性速度-运动性映射推广到Ostwald--de Waele幂律流体，并利用包含两个不等质量与不等阻力系数的“尺蠖模型（inchworm model）”在Carreau-Yasuda流体中进行数值或解析验证，检验互易形状变化能否产生净运动。

Result: 在幂律流体中，线性速度-运动性映射仍然成立，扇贝定理依然有效。但在Carreau-Yasuda流体中，该线性关系被破坏，互易变形也能产生净位移，且运动方向可通过改变速度进行切换。

Conclusion: 几何力学（geometric mechanics）中的线性运动性映射可用于分析和设计在幂律流体中的运动；而Carreau-Yasuda等非线性阻力关系则可被利用来产生看似违反扇贝定理的净运动行为。

Abstract: Systems moving in low Reynolds number fluid regimes are known to be governed by a ``motility map'' which linearly relates their shape change rates to they body frame velocity moving through the fluid. A consequence of this is ``Purcell's Scallop Theorem'' -- a locomotion system that undergoes shape changes that follow the same path forward and backward in time (reciprocal body deformations) cannot achieve net displacement, regardless of pacing of those changes.We show that linear-in-velocity motility maps extend to any power law viscosity (a.k.a. Ostwald--de Waele fluid), and therefore to many biological fluids in intermediate shear ranges. We also show that the linear-in-velocity property can be violated in Carreau-Yasuda fluids to produce net motion using an ``inchworm'' model consisting of two unequal masses with unequal drag coefficients performing reciprocal motions. Interestingly, the direction of motion can be switched by changing speeds. Our results show that the linear motility map of geometric mechaincs can be used to analyze and design locomotion in power-law fluids, and that some nonlinear drag relationships such as Carreau-Yasuda can be exploited to generate net locomotion in seeming violation of the ``scallop theorem''.

Result: 提供了刘维尔–阿诺德定理在C0和C1哈密顿量下的原型示例（prototype examples），表明即使在超曲面上光滑性降低的情况下，仍可构造出具有良好可积性行为的系统。

Conclusion: 将经典可积性理论推广至更广的光滑性条件，拓展了哈密顿力学中可积性概念的适用范围，为处理含非光滑势能的物理系统提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We consider natural Hamiltonian systems with potentials that are $C^0$ or $C^1$ on a hypersurface and $C^{\infty}$-smooth in the complement and introduce and study corresponding notions of their integrabilty and non-integrability. As a motivating example, we derive and analyze models of bungee jumping. We provide prototype examples of the Liuoville-Arnol'd theorem for $C^0$ and $C^1$ Hamiltonians.

### [116] [Non-equilibrium glassy arrest and discontinuous transitions at avoided quantum critical points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00580)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究受外约束场影响的序参量在无序凝聚态系统中的非平衡动力学行为，特别是揭示避免临界性附近出现耗散峰和玻璃态阻滞的微观机制。

Method: 采用空间扩展的Belitz-Kirkpatrick-Vojta（BKV）理论框架，分析宏观自由能平坦化与微观无序诱导钉扎的相互作用，并推导解析标度关系。

Result: 发现避免临界性处出现非单调耗散峰；在该区域，涨落-耗散定理被有效破坏，系统最终进入玻璃态阻滞；更高场强下系统发生不连续相变，绕开平坦自由能区域。

Conclusion: 这些解析标度结果建立了一个无序凝聚态系统中非平衡阻滞的通用机制。

Abstract: The non-equilibrium dynamics of an order parameter confined by an external constraint field are investigated within a spatially extended Belitz-Kirkpatrick-Vojta framework. A generic non-monotonic dissipation peak arises at avoided criticality due to the interplay between macroscopic free-energy flattening and microscopic disorder-induced trapping. Near this regime, suppressed deterministic forces enhance activated trapping, leading to an effective violation of the fluctuation-dissipation theorem and ultimate glassy arrest. At higher fields, the system undergoes a discontinuous phase transition that bypasses this flat free-energy region. These explicit analytical scalings establish a generic mechanism for non-equilibrium arrest in disordered condensed matter systems.

### [117] [Wasserstein-2 gradient flows and the geometry of entropy production in classical and quantum stochastic thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00698)
*Olga Movilla Miangolarra,Ralph Sabbagh,Artemy Kolchinsky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于Wasserstein-2度量和自由能梯度流，为经典和量子热力学中的熵产生提供了统一的几何描述，将耗散与保守动力学纳入同一黎曼几何框架，并建立了与热力学长度和最优协议的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学第二定律不仅规定了演化方向，还赋予了非平衡变换内在的几何结构。现有方法缺乏统一视角来刻画经典与量子系统中耗散与保守动力学共同作用下的熵产生几何。

Method: 基于自由能梯度流（gradient flow of free energy）诱导的Wasserstein-2结构，作者统一描述了过阻尼扩散、细致平衡马尔可夫链（detailed-balanced Markov chain）和耗散林德布拉德动力学（dissipative Lindblad dynamics）中的熵产生，并通过推广Wasserstein-2度量引入哈密顿动力学，建立了耗散-保守混合系统的几何框架。

Result: Wasserstein-2距离可界定额外熵产生，给出第二定律的有限时间精化（finite-time refinement）。建立了纯耗散与哈密顿-耗散几何之间的等价性界限，量化了惯性或相干动力学对耗散的降低效应。在平衡分布限制下恢复了线性响应热力学长度（thermodynamic length），包括量子热力学长度。

Conclusion: 该工作将热力学的黎曼纲领（Riemannian program）进一步推广至非平衡区域，为超越过阻尼情形的最优协议设计提供了几何基础，并将最优输运、热力学长度和反绝热协议（counterdiabatic protocol）统一在同一框架中。

Abstract: The second law does more than set the direction of thermodynamic evolution: it endows nonequilibrium transformations with an underlying geometry. In this work, we provide a unified geometric description of entropy production in classical and quantum thermodynamics based on Wasserstein-2 structures arising from gradient flows of free energy. We review how relaxation to equilibrium, in overdamped diffusions, discrete detailed-balanced Markov chains, and dissipative Lindblad dynamics, can be formulated as a gradient flow on the space of states. The associated Wasserstein-2 distance bounds entropy production, yielding a finite-time refinement of the second law. We extend this framework beyond purely dissipative dynamics by introducing generalized Wasserstein-2 metrics that incorporate conservative (Hamiltonian) dynamics in both classical inertial systems and open quantum systems, yielding intrinsic distances that exactly characterize minimal entropy production under fixed dissipative mobilities. We establish equivalence bounds between purely dissipative and Hamiltonian-dissipative geometries, explicitly quantifying how inertial or coherent dynamics can reduce dissipation. Finally, when restricted to equilibrium distributions, we recover the thermodynamic length of linear response-including the quantum thermodynamic length-thereby linking optimal transport, thermodynamic length, and counterdiabatic protocols within a single geometric framework. All in all, our results extend the Riemannian program of thermodynamics further from equilibrium and provide a geometric foundation for optimal protocols beyond the overdamped setting.

</details>


### [118] [Pre-failure response spectra predict finite-amplitude fragility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00789)
*Surachate Limkumnerd*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出通过线性化响应谱的广度（response-spectrum breadth）来预测非线性系统的有限振幅脆弱性（finite-amplitude fragility），无需遍历所有扰动方向即可估计脆弱性曲线（fragility curve），并在高维非正规网络和交通流崩溃中验证了该机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统失效理论（failure theories）通常只关注单一主导失效路径（如最不稳定模态、最弱链路、最小作用量逃逸路径或最优扰动），但有限振幅敏感度（finite-amplitude susceptibility）不仅取决于最近的危险方向，还取决于扰动空间中靠近危险方向的总“体积”。该工作旨在捕捉这一“脆弱性（fragility）”维度，即系统失效方向分布的广度。

Method: 定义每条扰动方向的失效距离（failure distance）及全体方向上的脆弱性曲线（fragility curve）。不直接进行多方向非线性试验，而是证明该曲线可由单个失效前（pre-failure）量的尾部预测：边界归一化脆弱性增益（boundary-normalized fragility gain），该增益可从线性化响应（linearized response）中计算得到。响应谱的广度决定了除最强方向外共存多少近危险路径。

Result: 在高维非线性非正规网络（non-normal network）中，固定最强方向增益时，响应通道广度（response-channel breadth）更广的系统具有更大的非线性脆弱性曲线，从而将广度与最坏方向效应分离开。在确定性交通流崩溃（deterministic traffic breakdown）的独立标量测试中，响应广度降低标定拥堵阈值（calibrated jam thresholds），且残余裕度（residual margins）仅起屏蔽作用而不逆转该效应。

Conclusion: 响应谱广度成为超越最强路径的有限振幅脆弱性的一种失效前坐标（pre-failure coordinate），为预测多方向失效风险提供了新框架。

Abstract: Failure theories often identify a single leading route to failure: the most unstable mode, weakest link, minimum-action escape path, or optimal perturbation. Yet finite-amplitude susceptibility depends not only on the nearest route but on how much of perturbation space lies near dangerous directions. We cast this distinction as a fragility problem: for each perturbation direction, the failure distance is the smallest amplitude that crosses a prescribed boundary, and the fragility curve is the fraction of directions that fail below a given amplitude. Measuring this curve directly requires nonlinear trials over many directions; instead, we show that it is predicted, before any failure occurs, by the tail of a single pre-failure quantity: the boundary-normalized fragility gain computed from the linearized response. The breadth of the associated response spectrum sets how many near-dangerous pathways coexist beyond the strongest direction. We demonstrate the mechanism in a high-dimensional nonlinear non-normal network with the strongest directional gain held fixed: the system with broader response-channel breadth has a larger nonlinear fragility curve, isolating breadth from the worst direction. An independent scalar test in deterministic traffic breakdown confirms the predicted sign: response breadth lowers calibrated jam thresholds once the strongest response is matched, with residual margins screening but never reversing the effect. Response-spectrum breadth thus emerges as a pre-failure coordinate for finite-amplitude fragility beyond the strongest path.

</details>


### [119] [High Resolution Study of the 2D ANNNI Model Using a Two-replica Cluster Algorithm and Population Annealing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00882)
*Shane Keiser,Jon Machta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 利用群体退火（population annealing）结合双副本团簇算法（two-replica cluster algorithm），成功解析了二维轴向次近邻伊辛（ANNNI）模型中表征有限尺寸非公度漂浮相的尖锐比热峰序列，并证明了该算法在平衡系统方面优于单副本团簇方法和Metropolis算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维轴向次近邻伊辛（ANNNI）模型中的有限尺寸非公度漂浮相（incommensurate floating phase）具有尖锐的比热峰序列，此前难以被充分解析；现有算法（单副本团簇方法或Metropolis算法）结合群体退火（population annealing）时，平衡系统的效率不足。

Method: 采用群体退火（population annealing）与双副本团簇算法（two-replica cluster algorithm）相结合的方法对二维ANNNI模型进行模拟。

Result: 1) 成功完全解析了表征有限尺寸非公度漂浮相的尖锐比热峰序列；2) 双副本团簇算法结合群体退火在平衡系统方面比单副本团簇方法或Metropolis算法结合群体退火更有效。

Conclusion: 新算法的高效性源于其能够将缺陷线组（groups of defect lines）在副本之间移动，并结合群体退火（population annealing）中的重采样过程去除含有较多缺陷线的副本。

Abstract: The axial next-nearest-neighbor Ising (ANNNI) model in two dimensions is studied using population annealing combined with a two-replica cluster algorithm. We are able to fully resolve the sequence of sharp specific heat peaks that characterize the finite-size incommensurate floating phase. We also show that the two-replica cluster algorithm is much more effective in equilibrating the system than either single-replica cluster methods or the Metropolis algorithm when these are combined with population annealing. We argue that effectiveness of the new algorithm is due to its ability to move groups of defect lines between replicas combined with resampling in population annealing, which removes replicas from the population that have larger numbers of defect lines.

</details>


### [120] [Tandem Exclusion Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01568)
*Ngo Phuoc Nguyen Ngoc,Lam Thi Nhung,Huynh Anh Thi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一维随机格点模型“串联排斥过程（TEP）”，该模型受蚂蚁串联奔跑行为启发。通过两种合作性局部跃迁（领头前进和跟随恢复），证明了稳态测度为Gibbs测度，并利用转移矩阵方法得到了稳态流和空间关联的精确闭式解。结果表明，串联协作机制能在中高密度下显著提升集体输运效率，其粒子流在密度大于1/2处取得最大值，且当q>1时超出TASEP的流值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在建立并分析一个能够刻画蚂蚁串联奔跑中集体输运机制的随机格点模型，以理解无需信息素介导的长程通信时，局部协作行为如何影响集体输运效率。

Method: 定义了一个一维排斥过程（tandem exclusion process, TEP），包含两种合作性跃迁：领头前进（110→101, 速率α）和跟随恢复（101→011, 速率β）。通过证明稳态测度为Gibbs测度形式，并运用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix methods）推导了稳态流和空间关联的精确闭式表达式。

Result: 稳态流在粒子–空穴交换（ρ↦1-ρ）下不对称，最大值出现在密度严格大于1/2处，不同于TASEP的对称流ρ(1-ρ)。当q=β/α>1时，协作动力学使流超越TASEP值并产生强空间聚集；在q→∞极限下，流趋近J→αρ，对应近乎无约束的集体输运。

Conclusion: 串联协调（tandem coordination）本身即可在中高密度下显著提升集体输运效率，即使缺乏信息素介导的长程通信也能实现高效输运。

Abstract: We introduce the \emph{tandem exclusion process} (TEP), a one-dimensional stochastic lattice model motivated by tandem running in ants. Particles evolve through two cooperative local transitions, $110\to101$ at rate $α$ (leader advancement) and $101\to011$ at rate $β$ (follower recovery). We prove that the stationary measure on the dynamically active sector is the Gibbs measure $π\propto q^{H(η)}$, where $q=β/α$ and $H(η)$ counts neighboring occupied pairs, and derive exact closed-form expressions for the stationary current and spatial correlations using transfer-matrix methods. The current is asymmetric under particle--hole exchange $ρ\mapsto1-ρ$, with its maximum occurring at densities strictly larger than $1/2$, in contrast to the symmetric current $ρ(1-ρ)$ of the totally asymmetric simple exclusion process (TASEP). For $q>1$, cooperative dynamics enhances the current above the TASEP value and generates strong spatial clustering; in the limit $q\to\infty$, the current approaches $J\toαρ$, corresponding to nearly unconstrained collective transport. These results suggest that tandem coordination alone can substantially enhance collective transport efficiency at moderate and high densities, even without pheromone-mediated long-range communication.

</details>


### [121] [Significance of time-convolutionless mode-coupling theory in capturing the dynamics of glass-forming liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01696)
*Michio Tokuyama*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文论证了新近提出的无时间卷积模式耦合理论（time-convolutionless mode-coupling theory, TMCT）在描述玻璃形成液体动力学中的重要性，并从统一视角全面探讨了理想MCT与TMCT之间的主要差异来源。TMCT对电流密度应用时间卷积（time-convolution, TC）公式，对数密度应用无时间卷积（time-convolutionless, TCL）公式，而理想MCT对两者均应用TC公式，导致二者在玻璃转变附近的物理量预测存在显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示理想模式耦合理论（mode-coupling theory, MCT）与TMCT之间根本差异的起源，澄清两种投影算子方法在不同时空尺度下的适用性，并展示TMCT在描述玻璃形成液体动力学方面的优势。

Method: 在Heisenberg绘景下分别回顾了Mori提出的时间卷积（TC）公式和Tokuyama-Mori提出的无时间卷积（TCL）公式两种投影算子方法；依据相关变量的时空尺度进行框架选择，TMCT对电流密度应用TC公式、对数密度应用TCL公式，而理想MCT对两者均应用TC公式；将完整的TMCT方程转化为简化的递归方程以促进数值分析。

Result: TMCT与理想MCT的基本差异源于对电流密度和数密度选择了不同的投影算子公式：TMCT对长时空尺度的数密度使用TCL公式，而理想MCT对两者均使用TC公式，导致TMCT的控制方程为无时间卷积形式，理想MCT为时间卷积形式。这一根本差异显著影响了玻璃转变附近各种物理量的预测结果。

Conclusion: TMCT通过合理选择投影算子框架，能够更准确地捕捉玻璃形成液体的动力学行为；其最终方程可转化为递归形式便于数值分析，且关键预测与理想MCT存在显著差异。

Abstract: This paper demonstrates the significance of the recently proposed time-convolutionless mode-coupling theory (TMCT) in capturing the dynamics of glass-forming liquids. The origin of the primary differences between ideal MCT and TMCT is comprehensively explored from a unified perspective. First, we review two distinct projection operator methods in the Heisenberg picture: the time-convolution (TC) formulation proposed by Mori and the time-convolutionless (TCL) formulation proposed by Tokuyama and Mori. We show that the appropriate choice between these frameworks fundamentally depends on the space-time scales of the relevant variables. In TMCT, the TC formulation is applied to the current density, whereas the TCL formulation is applied to the number density because the latter operates on a significantly longer space-time scale. In contrast, ideal MCT applies the TC formulation to both densities. Consequently, the governing equation in TMCT is timeconvolutionless, whereas the ideal MCT equation features a time-convolution form. This fundamental difference significantly affects various physical quantities near the glass transition. Finally, the full TMCT equation is transformed into a simplified recursion equation to facilitate numerical analysis, and the key predictions of TMCT are compared with those of ideal MCT

</details>


### [122] [Role of System-Bath Interaction in Non-Markovian Quantum Brownian Otto Cycles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01750)
*Haena Shim,Joonhyun Yeo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过精确求解海森堡-朗之万方程（Heisenberg-Langevin equations），研究了以谐振子为工质、由卡尔代拉-莱格特模型（Caldeira-Leggett model）描述布朗运动的有限时间量子奥托循环（quantum Otto cycle），分析非马尔可夫强耦合效应，发现等容过程中相互作用能的变化同时贡献于功和热，且会降低引擎的功输出，其功率-效率关系低于马尔可夫边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于马尔可夫近似（Markovian approximation）下的林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation）描述量子奥托循环的演化，缺乏对非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）和强耦合效应（strong-coupling effects）系统分析。本文旨在通过精确解析方法填补这一空白，揭示相互作用能在有限时间量子奥托循环中的热力学角色。

Method: 工质为简谐振子（harmonic oscillator），接触热浴的等容过程由卡尔代拉-莱格特模型描述。通过解析求解精确的海森堡-朗之万方程，获得系统变量及系统与热浴相互作用能的时间演化，进而研究非马尔可夫强耦合效应下的量子奥托循环。周期性稳态的获取使热力学分析成为可能，并与马尔可夫极限下的林德布拉德方程结果进行对比。

Result: 等容过程中相互作用能的变化同时贡献于功和热，对循环的热力学行为起着关键作用。当奥托循环作为引擎运行时，相互作用能会降低功输出。非马尔可夫引擎在给定效率下的功率低于马尔可夫量子奥托引擎的功率-效率权衡边界（power-efficiency trade-off bound）。

Conclusion: 非马尔可夫强耦合效应在量子奥托循环中不可忽略，相互作用能的变化是决定热力学行为的关键因素；非马尔可夫引擎的功率-效率表现逊于马尔可夫情况下的理论界限。

Abstract: We study finite-time quantum Otto cycles whose working medium is a harmonic oscillator undergoing a quantum Brownian motion described by the Caldeira-Leggett model when the oscillator is in contact with heat baths in isochoric processes. The time evolution of the Otto cycle is studied by analytically solving the exact Heisenberg-Langevin equations for the system variables and the interaction energy between the system and the bath. This enables us to investigate non-Markovian strong-coupling effects on the quantum Otto cycle. We obtain cyclic steady states and study the thermodynamic properties of the Otto cycle for various values of the parameters describing the heat baths and the coupling between the system and the bath. We compare our results with those obtained in the Markovian limit, where the time evolution is described by the Lindblad equation. We find that the change in the interaction energy during the isochoric process contributes to both work and heat, and plays a crucial role in determining thermodynamic behavior of the cycle. In particular, we find that when the Otto cycle operates as an engine, the effect of the interaction energy is to reduce the work output. We also compare our results with the power-efficiency trade-off relation recently proposed for the Markovian quantum Otto engine. We find that the power of our non-Markovian engine for a given efficiency value falls below the Markovian power-efficiency bound.

### [123] [Can the Brownian diffusion coefficient be reconstructed from Lyapunov exponents?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01887)
*I. G. Marchenko,I. I. Marchenko,D. Ivashchenko,J. Łuczka,J. Spiechowicz*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文发现，在非零温度下由交流驱动粒子在周期对称势中表现出的准周期扩散系数，可通过零温确定性系统的最大李雅普诺夫指数（maximal Lyapunov exponent）精确重建，并提出了一个近似公式，该公式与数值模拟吻合良好，但在扩散系数局部极大值附近存在偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）与布朗扩散（Brownian diffusion）之间尚无通用关系，但近期研究表明扩散系数是外部驱动振幅的准周期函数。本文旨在探索是否能从确定性系统的李雅普诺夫指数重建非零温度下的准周期扩散系数。

Method: 研究了一个在空间周期对称势中受交流驱动的粒子系统。通过对比零温确定性系统的最大李雅普诺夫指数与非零温度下的扩散系数，提出了一个近似公式用于重建准周期扩散系数，并通过数值模拟验证其有效性，同时考察了该相关性对系统参数变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 该近似公式能准确重建非零温度下的准周期扩散系数，与数值模拟结果总体吻合良好。然而，在扩散系数局部极大值附近观察到一定偏差。此外，扩散系数与李雅普诺夫指数之间的相关性对系统参数变化具有一定的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 零温确定性系统的最大李雅普诺夫指数可用于预测非零温度下布朗扩散的准周期行为，尽管在扩散峰值区域存在偏差，但该方法为连接确定性与随机动力学提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We consider an ac-driven particle moving in a spatially periodic and symmetric potential. In the zero- temperature limit, for the analyzed parameter set, its dynamics is non-chaotic and the particle does not manifest diffusive properties. At non-zero temperatures, the asymptotic long-time motion follows normal (Brownian) diffusion. Recent studies have shown that within tailored parameter regimes, the diffusion coef- ficient is a quasiperiodic function of the external driving amplitude [1]. Although no general relation between Lyapunov exponents and Brownian diffusion exists, we demonstrate that the quasiperiodic diffusion coefficient at non-zero temperature can be accurately reconstructed from the maximal Lyapunov exponent of the corresponding deterministic system (at vanishing temperature). We propose an approximate formula for this purpose, which shows good agreement with numerical simulations, although some discrepancies are detected in the vicinity of the local maxima of the diffusion coefficient. Finally, we examine the robustness of the correlation between diffusion and the Lyapunov exponent under variations of the system parameters.

### [124] [Localization of Active Particles on Random Arrays of Parallel Filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00286)
*Owen Santoso,Elena Koslover*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了淬火无序环境中，颗粒在随机取向丝状体阵列上的输运与定域化行为，发现颗粒会聚集在丝状体极性收敛区域，定域化在中等游走长度时最强，揭示了主动输运与淬火无序相互作用产生的涌现空间组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受哺乳动物树突中平行微管（microtubule）混合极性排列的启发，探索淬火无序（quenched disorder）环境如何改变主动和被动物系中颗粒的输运动力学，特别是无序丝状体阵列如何调控在扩散输运（diffusive transport）和持续输运（processive transport）之间切换的间歇运动颗粒的分布。

Method: 在快速附着-解离极限下，将无序系统映射为一个含噪声的一维有效能量势垒（effective energy landscape），其结构近似为随机游走（random walk）。势阱的深度和宽度表达为输运动力学和系统几何参数的函数。

Result: 无序丝状体阵列会导致颗粒定域化（localization）在丝状体极性收敛区域。定域化在中等游走长度（run-length）时最强——此时偏向性输运足以感知淬火丝状体极性，但又不足以使颗粒逃离局部陷阱。

Conclusion: 研究证明了颗粒在随机丝状体网络上的稳健定域化，突显了主动输运与淬火无序相互作用所产生的涌现空间组织（emergent spatial organization）。

Abstract: Quenched disorder in the environment can fundamentally alter transport dynamics in both active and passive systems. We explore how disordered arrays of filaments govern the distribution of intermittently moving particles which switch between diffusive and processive transport. Motivated by the mixed-polarity arrangements of parallel microtubules observed in mammalian dendrites, we show that such arrays tend to result in localization of particles at regions of convergent filament orientation. In the rapid attachment-detachment limit, the disordered system can be described by a noisy one-dimensional effective energy landscape, whose structure is approximated by a random walk. The depth and width of wells on this landscape are expressed as a function of the transport kinetics and system geometry. Localization is shown to be strongest at intermediate run-lengths, where biased transport persists long enough to sense the quenched filament polarity but not so long as to facilitate escape from local traps. These results demonstrate robust localization of particles moving on random filament networks, highlighting the emergent spatial organization that arises from an interplay of active transport and quenched disorder.

### [125] [The Longest Increasing Subsequence Problem revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01501)
*Silvio Franz,Roberto Mulet*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过引入温度参数，揭示了最长递增子序列（LIS）问题丰富且类似热力学（thermodynamics）的相图，包括一个肖特基型（Schottky-like）交叉和凝聚转变（condensation transition），并证明即使基态存在多项式时间算法，低温下的局部蒙特卡洛动力学（local Monte Carlo dynamics）会表现出典型的玻璃态（glassy）特征，如两步松弛、持续动力学重叠和老化（aging），从而指出热力学稀疏性（thermodynamic sparsity）而非能量障碍是导致局部搜索动态困难的根本原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典组合优化问题“最长递增子序列（Longest Increasing Subsequence, LIS）”与统计力学（statistical mechanics）之间具有深刻联系，但以往研究主要关注基态（ground state）的多项式时间算法，对其整体热力学景观（thermodynamic landscape）及动力学困难性的理解尚不充分。本文旨在通过引入温度参数，系统刻画LIS问题的热力学与动力学行为，探索优化问题与玻璃态自旋玻璃现象（glassy spin-glass phenomenology）之间的桥梁。

Method: 本文采用统计力学框架，为LIS问题引入温度参数以定义配分函数（partition function）；通过分析两种不同的能量尺度，识别出肖特基型交叉（Schottky-like crossover，特征温度T_cross）和凝聚转变（condensation transition，特征温度T_cond）。此外，论文采用局部蒙特卡洛动力学（local Monte Carlo dynamics）模拟低温快速淬火（sudden quenches）后的弛豫过程，并与对数退火（logarithmic annealing）进行对比。

Result: 研究发现两个不同的能量尺度：在T_cross处出现肖特基型交叉，在T_cond处发生凝聚转变，低于该温度时最大长度构型的数量相对于系统尺寸呈亚指数增长。低温快速淬火后，局部蒙特卡洛动力学陷入亚稳态（metastable state），表现出典型的玻璃态特征：两步松弛（two-step relaxation）、持续动力学重叠（persistent dynamical overlaps）以及老化（aging）现象。相比之下，对数退火（logarithmic annealing）能够沿平衡路径追踪至基态。

Conclusion: 本文得出结论：热力学稀疏性（thermodynamic sparsity）——而非传统认知中的能量障碍（energetic barriers）——是导致局部搜索动力学在计算上难以处理（dynamically intractable）的根本原因。这些结果将LIS问题定位为精确可解优化（exactly solvable optimization）与玻璃态自旋玻璃现象（glassy spin-glass phenomenology）之间的桥梁，为理解组合优化问题的动力学复杂性提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The Longest Increasing Subsequence problem - a classic combinatorial challenge with deep connections to statistical mechanics- exhibits a rich thermodynamic landscape. Introducing a temperature we identify two distinct energy scales: A Schottky-like crossover at T_cross and a condensation transition at T_cond, below which the number of maximum-length configurations becomes sub-exponential in system size. We also show that despite the existence of polynomial-time dynamic programming algorithms for the ground state, local Monte Carlo dynamics, after sudden quenches at low temperatures, become trapped in metastable state configurations displaying characteristic glassy signatures: two-step relaxation, persistent dynamical overlaps and aging. On the other hand, logarithmic annealing tracks equilibrium down to the ground state. These results establish that thermodynamic sparsity - not energetic barriers - can render local search dynamically intractable, positioning the LIS problem as a bridge between exactly solvable optimization and glassy spin-glass phenomenology.

</details>

### [126] [Co-condensation and multivalency enable acetylation-sensitive, concentration-robust assembly of BRD4 condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02275)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Biomolecular condensates must assemble at specific locations and times inside living cells to perform their biological functions. However, it remains unclear how condensate formation achieves high spatiotemporal precision, responding sensitively to local chemical modifications while remaining robust to fluctuations in protein concentration. Here we study chromatin-associated BRD4 condensates to identify a physical mechanism that enables this combination of sensitivity and robustness. Using an ultra-coarse-grained molecular-dynamics model, we show that co-condensation of BRD4 with chromatin enables rapid assembly below the bulk coexistence concentration, thereby suppressing off-chromatin condensation and enhancing spatial selectivity. Multivalent binding between BRD4 and acetylated histone tails sharpens the dependence of co-condensation on acetylation density through combinatorial effects, increasing contrast between highly acetylated regions and weakly acetylated background chromatin. This mechanism explains how co-condensation and multivalent binding jointly enable sensitive yet robust spatiotemporal targeting by chromatin-associated condensates.

### [127] [Design and modelling of compliant mechanisms with invertible Poisson's ratio effect for growing biological cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00434)
*Manu Sebastian,Sreenath Balakrishnan,Safvan Palathingal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文提出一种基于可调柔顺微机构（tunable compliant micro mechanisms）的新型基底，能够在细胞生长过程中原位改变其弹性性质（elastic properties），特别是实现了可逆的泊松比（invertible Poisson's ratio）效应——在两种构型下分别呈现正泊松比和负泊松比，且大小可调。作者推导了几何参数与输入/输出位移比之间的解析表达式，并通过有限元分析（finite element analysis）和介观尺度原型实验进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物细胞的行为依赖于其所附着基底的力学性质（如弹性模量和泊松比）。传统的可调材料（如聚丙烯酰胺凝胶和水凝胶）无法在细胞生长过程中原位改变其弹性性质，限制了相关研究。

Method: 提出一种基于可调柔顺微机构的基底方案，采用内凹结构（re-entrant structure）形状的机构，通过改变两个内部点之间的刚度来实现泊松比的正负可逆切换及大小调节。为两种构型推导了联系几何参数与输入/输出位移比的解析表达式。

Result: 解析建模通过有限元分析和两种构型的介观尺度设计原型实验得到了验证。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种能够在细胞生长过程中原位调控基底弹性性质（特别是可逆泊松比效应）的新方法，为研究细胞与基底力学相互作用提供了替代途径。

Abstract: The behaviour of biological cells depends on the mechanical properties, such as Elastic Modulus and Poisson's ratio, of the substrate they adhere to. Tunable materials such as polyacrylamide gels and hydrogels were previously used as substrates to understand this dependence. However, these substrates do not facilitate changing their elastic properties in situ while cells are growing on them. This work presents an alternate approach that enables this--substrates based on tunable compliant micro mechanisms.
  In particular, the mechanism proposed here has an invertible Poisson's ratio effect. In the first configuration, the effect is positive, and in the second, it is negative, with any desired magnitude. We achieve this by changing the stiffness between two internal points of a mechanism with the shape of a re-entrant structure. An increase in stiffness causes the direction of deformation along the lateral axis to reverse for a given reference load along the horizontal axis.
  We derive analytical expressions that relate the geometric parameters to the ratio of input and output displacements for both mechanism configurations. The analytical modelling is verified with finite element analysis and experiments on mesoscale design prototypes of both configurations.

</details>


### [128] [Semiflexible Ring Polymers on Active Motor Beds: Nonequilibrium Dynamics and Conformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00608)
*Sandip Roy,Abhishek Chaudhuri,Anil Kumar Dasanna*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过粗粒化朗之万模拟，系统探究了位于马达蛋白（motor protein）基底上的半柔性环状聚合物（semiflexible ring polymer）的旋转与构象动力学，发现其活性（activity）与持续性（processivity）依赖的非平衡响应显著不同于线性链；均方位移呈现交叉动力学，直径自相关函数表现出与相干旋转相关的阻尼振荡，傅里叶模式分析揭示了非单调非球性（asphericity）源于半径模与椭圆模的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由马达蛋白驱动的活性环状聚合物在细胞骨架等生物系统中普遍存在，但相较于广泛研究的线性链，环状拓扑对活性系统动力学的影响尚不清晰，亟需系统刻画其非平衡行为。

Method: 采用粗粒化朗之万模拟（coarse-grained Langevin simulations），模型包含弯曲弹性（bending elasticity）、排除体积相互作用（excluded-volume interactions）以及随机的马达附着、步进和解离过程；通过改变活性（Péclet数）、马达持续性和链刚性来映射非平衡响应。

Result: 均方位移（mean-squared displacement）呈现交叉动力学：低活性下为亚扩散到扩散行为，高活性下出现中间弹道区间；柔性增加使短时响应趋近Rouse极限。直径自相关函数展现与相干旋转相关的阻尼振荡，旋转频率随活性和持续性增加而升高，高持续性下去相关时间呈非单调变化。傅里叶模式分析表明，半径模（k=0）与椭圆模（k=2）的竞争导致非球性的非单调行为。

Conclusion: 活性环状聚合物的旋转与构象动力学无法被线性链行为所涵盖，揭示了环状拓扑特有的非平衡响应机制，包括活性诱导的相干旋转以及模间竞争导致的非单调构象涨落。

Abstract: A semiflexible ring polymer on a motor-protein bed exhibits activity- and processivity-dependent rotational and conformational dynamics that are not captured by linear-chain behavior. Using coarse-grained Langevin simulations with bending elasticity, excluded-volume interactions, and stochastic motor attachment, stepping, and detachment, we vary activity (Peclet number), motor processivity, and chain stiffness to map the nonequilibrium response. The mean-squared displacement shows crossover dynamics, with semiflexible rings displaying subdiffusive-to-diffusive behavior at low activity and an intermediate ballistic regime at higher activity, while increasing flexibility shifts the short-time response toward a Rouse-like limit. Diameter autocorrelations exhibit damped oscillations associated with coherent rotation; the rotational frequency increases with activity and processivity, whereas the decorrelation time is non-monotonic at high processivity. Fourier mode analysis identifies competition between the radius (k=0) and elliptic (k=2) modes as the origin of the non-monotonic asphericity.

</details>


### [129] [Polymer-Regulated Freezing of Water Droplets Revealed by Synchrotron X-ray Imaging and Raman Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01251)
*Hyeonjun An,Bomi Kim,Jae Kwan Im,Min Woo Kim,Seob-Gu Kim,Jae-Hong Lim,Kitae Kim,Joonwoo Jeong*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过同步辐射X射线与拉曼成像，发现冷冻液滴中的聚合物（PVA）因冷冻诱导分离（freeze-induced segregation）而空间异质重分布，导致冻结前沿传播减慢、气泡捕获减少及尖端钝化，为冷冻铸造与低温保存等应用提供新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究关注聚合物降低凝固点（freezing point）的整体效应，但对聚合物如何影响液滴冷冻过程中外部形状与内部结构的空间机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用同步辐射X射线断层成像（synchrotron X-ray tomography）与拉曼光谱成像（Raman spectral mapping），对聚乙烯醇（polyvinyl alcohol, PVA）水溶液液滴在不同浓度与分子量下的冷冻过程进行实时观测与成分分析。

Result: 聚合物浓度增加导致冻结前沿（freezing front）传播减慢、气泡捕获减少、顶部尖端更圆钝；X射线与拉曼成像一致表明冷冻液滴内部与表面形成PVA富集区，证实冷冻诱导聚合物分离。

Conclusion: 冷冻诱导聚合物分离而非整体物性改变，是调控冷冻液滴外部形态与内部结构的关键机制；该发现为冷冻铸造（freeze-casting）与低温保存（cryopreservation）等涉及冷冻的过程提供空间解析的理论框架。

Abstract: Adding a polymer to a sessile water droplet not only lowers its freezing point but also suppresses the tip singularity that forms during its freezing on cold substrates. Here, we employ synchrotron X-ray and Raman imaging to elucidate the spatiotemporal mechanism underlying tip suppression in an aqueous polyvinyl alcohol (PVA) solution, a model polymer solution. As the polymer concentration increases, we observe slower propagation of the freezing front, reduced bubble entrapment, and a progressively more rounded apex across the volumes and molecular weights examined. X-ray tomography reveals that frozen PVA droplets retain low X-ray transmittance domains in their interiors and at the surface, and Raman spectral mapping confirms that these domains correspond to PVA-enriched regions, providing direct evidence of freeze-induced polymer segregation. These findings indicate that PVA is redistributed heterogeneously during water solidification rather than shifting bulk properties homogeneously, providing a spatially resolved framework for interpreting the observed tip blunting and the suppression of discrete bubble entrapment. Our work identifies freeze-induced polymer segregation as a pathway by which a dissolved polymer regulates both the external shape and the internal structure of a freezing droplet, and these findings shed light on potential applications in freezing-based processes such as freeze-casting and cryopreservation.

### [130] [Particle Force-Based Continuum Model for Multicomponent Size Segregating Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01327)
*Soniya Kumawat,Anurag Tripathi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过连续介质模型（continuum model）与离散元法（Discrete Element Method, DEM）模拟，将二元颗粒混合物中基于力的分离模型系统扩展到三元及四元体系，构建了能预测多组分颗粒流中尺寸分选时空演化的连续介质框架，并在中等尺寸比下与DEM数据吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际颗粒流系统（如工业输送与地质过程）常涉及三种及以上不同尺寸组分的混合物，但现有分离模型主要针对二元体系，缺乏适用于多组分的一般性理论框架。

Method: 将基于颗粒力的二元分离模型推广至多组分，通过计算各组分在其他所有组分存在下的净力以避免依赖经验渗流速度（percolation velocity）。该模型与混合物流变学（mixture rheology）模型耦合，纳入物种输运方程和动量平衡方程，构建一维连续介质模型。通过DEM模拟对三元和四元混合物在不同组分比和溜槽倾角下进行验证。

Result: 在中等尺寸比下，连续模型对三元和四元混合物在多种组分比和倾角下的浓度与速度场预测与DEM吻合良好；较大尺寸比下定性趋势正确但定量偏差增大。初始构型中大颗粒在下、小颗粒在上时会引发瑞利-泰勒型（Rayleigh-Taylor like）不稳定性，导致早期二维浓度场演化。

Conclusion: 所提出的多组分连续分离模型在中等尺寸比范围内具有良好预测能力；对于大尺寸比和早期不稳定性现象，需将一维连续模型扩展至二维才能准确描述。

Abstract: We investigate size difference driven segregation in dense granular flows of multicomponent mixtures down a periodic chute using continuum model and Discrete Element Method (DEM) simulations. A previously developed particle force-based segregation model for binary mixtures is systematically extended to mixtures comprising three or more particle species differing in size. The generalized model accounts for inter-species interactions by computing the net force on each component in the presence of all others, without relying on empirical percolation velocity. This segregation model is coupled with a mixture rheology model and incorporated into the species transport and momentum balance equations to develop a continuum model that predicts the spatial and temporal evolution of species concentration and velocity fields. The continuum model predictions are found to be in agreement with DEM simulation data for ternary and quaternary mixtures over a wide range of mixture compositions and chute inclinations at moderate size ratios for well-mixed and small-near-base configurations. For larger size ratios, the one dimensional model predictions capture the qualitative segregation trend while showing relatively larger quantitative differences from DEM data. For an initial configuration, having large particles near base and small particles near the free surface, a Rayleigh-Taylor like instability at early times is observed. Due to the presence of this instability, two dimensional evolution of the species concentration fields is present for initial part of the flow. Predictions of such features requires the extension of the one dimensional continuum model to two dimensions.

### [131] [Resonant Coupling and the Non-Phononic Flat Band in Amorphous Solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01593)
*Matteo Baggioli,Bingyu Cui*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过重访共振耦合模型（resonant-coupling model），论证该最小化框架能自然复现非晶固体动力学结构因子中非声子平带（non-phononic flat band）的主要特征，并阐明其与玻色峰（boson peak）之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期实验与模拟发现二维和三维非晶固体（amorphous solids）的动力学结构因子中出现非声子平带，该特征与玻璃的玻色峰相关且表现出若干普适特性，但其理论解释尚不明确。本文旨在利用共振耦合模型厘清该平带的起源及其与玻色峰的关系。

Method: 本文采用共振耦合模型，这是一种单模简谐实现（single-mode harmonic realization）的软势情景（soft-potential scenario），其中声学声子（acoustic phonons）与单频率准局域振动（quasi-localized vibrations）发生相互作用。

Result: 该最小模型自然再现了非声子平带的三个主要特征：近无色散（dispersionless）且能量接近玻色峰频率；强度在临界波矢（约为第一衍射峰量级）以下可忽略；约化强度与静态结构因子（static structure factor）存在强关联。

Conclusion: 共振耦合模型能够从理论上解释非声子平带的起源，并澄清其与玻色峰之间的关联，为非晶固体中这一普遍现象提供了简洁的理论框架。

Abstract: Recent experiments and simulations provide compelling evidence for the emergence of a non-phononic flat band in the dynamical structure factor of two- and three-dimensional amorphous solids. This feature has been suggested to be connected to the excess in the reduced vibrational density of states of glasses, commonly known as the boson peak, and displays several apparently universal characteristics. First, it is nearly dispersionless, with an energy close to the boson-peak frequency. Second, its intensity is negligible below a critical wave vector of the order of the first diffraction peak. Third, its reduced intensity exhibits a strong correlation with the static structure factor. Here, we revisit the resonant-coupling model, a single-mode harmonic realization of the soft-potential scenario in which acoustic phonons interact with single frequency quasi-localized vibrations. We show that this minimal framework naturally reproduces the main features of the observed flat band and clarifies its connection to the boson peak.

### [132] [Stress relaxation in fiber networks via force-dependent stochastic severing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01752)
*Prathamesh Kulkarni,Anatoly B. Kolomeisky,Fred C. MacKintosh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过二维三角格点模拟，研究了随机、力依赖的切断（severing）对弹簧和纤维网络应力松弛及刚性转变（rigidity transition）的影响，揭示了张力抑制型和张力增强型两种切断反馈机制对网络刚性和松弛行为的差异化调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纤维网络（fiber networks）在从细胞到组织的多种生物系统中维持力学稳定性，而切断（severing）会降低网络连通性并破坏其刚性。理解应力与切断之间的力依赖反馈机制如何影响网络的应力松弛（stress relaxation）和刚性转变（rigidity transition）是该研究的核心动机。

Method: 采用基于二维三角格点（2D triangular lattice）的计算机模拟方法，建立了考虑应力切断力学化学反馈（mechanochemical feedback）的计算模型，并探索了不同反馈极限下网络行为的变化。

Result: 张力抑制型切断（tension-suppressed severing）会延缓应力松弛，并将刚性转变推向弯曲主导（bending-dominated）的低连通性区域；张力增强型切断（tension-enhanced severing）则加速松弛，并将转变推向高连通性区域。该偏移幅度依赖于外加剪切应变（applied shear strain）和反馈强度。

Conclusion: 理论分析阐明了这些现象的微观机制，表明理解应力-切断反馈机制可为通过调控反馈来设计具有预期力学响应的系统提供有价值的研究思路。

Abstract: Fiber networks contribute to the mechanical stability of various biological systems, from cells to tissues. Such systems have been modeled by networks of springs or fibers that exhibit rigidity transitions as a function of either connectivity or applied strain. For a fiber network under constant applied strain, severing can reduce the connectivity and destabilize an initially rigid structure. Here, we investigate stress relaxation in spring and fiber networks in the presence of stochastic, force-dependent severing. A computational model to predict stress relaxation with mechanochemical feedback of stress on severing is developed. We also examine the effects of severing on the network topology and onset of rigidity transition. Using 2D triangular lattice-based computer simulations, we explore different limits of the feedback and demonstrate the shift in the onset of rigidity depending on the limit. The limit of tension-suppressed severing delays stress relaxation and shifts the transition into the bending-dominated regime to lower-than-expected connectivity. In contrast, tension-enhanced severing accelerates relaxation and shifts the transition to higher-than-expected connectivity. It is also found that the magnitude of this shift depends on the applied shear strain and the strength of the feedback. Our theoretical approach clarifies some microscopic aspects of these phenomena. Understanding the impact of such feedback mechanisms can provide valuable insights into designing systems by tuning the feedback to the desired response.

</details>


### [133] [Dynamical frustration in space-time metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01797)
*Rupesh Mahore,Oleksandr Gamayun,Guillaume Noetinger,Romain Fleury,Corentin Coulais,Benjamin Apffel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出“动力学阻挫”（dynamical frustration）概念，指基态简并（ground state degeneracy）被非互易自振荡状态（non-reciprocal self-oscillating state）取代的现象。通过时间参数驱动与空间调制的超材料（metamaterials），实现了拓扑保护的相位位错（topologically protected phase dislocations）的单向传播与全局自组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统几何阻挫（geometrical frustration）源于局部约束无法同时满足，导致基态简并。本文旨在探索当基态简并被非互易自振荡状态取代时，是否涌现出新的物理现象，即动力学阻挫。

Method: 构建时间参数驱动且空间调制的超材料：参数泵浦（parametric pumping）引发周期倍化（period doubling），进而导致离散对称性破缺（discrete symmetry-breaking）；结合空间调制，强制产生拓扑保护的相位位错，并自发相位破缺连续对称性。通过镶嵌一维阻挫回路得到二维超材料。

Result: 实现了相位位错的单向自发传播；在二维超材料中，相位位错自组织为全局同步的非互易相位缺陷（non-reciprocal phase defects）。

Conclusion: 动力学阻挫可在从冷原子（cold atoms）、超导电路（superconducting circuits）到声学（acoustics）与射频电路（RF circuits）等任意尺度上实现，只要时空调制能够推动系统超越线性稳定性（linear stability）边界。

Abstract: From spin ice and crumpled paper to cold atoms lattices and metamaterials, geometrical frustration occurs generically whenever local constraints cannot be satisfied all at once. The result is a ground state degeneracy, where many equivalent states, each of which contains unsatisfied constraints, coexist. Here, we introduce dynamical frustration, where the ground state degeneracy makes way to a non-reciprocal self-oscillating state instead. To create dynamical frustration, we construct metamaterials that are driven parametrically in time and modulated in space. The parametric pumping leads to period doubling and in turn to a discrete symmetry-breaking. This symmetry breaking, together with the spatial modulation enforces the existence of topologically protected phase dislocations, which propagate unidirectionally with a spontaneous phase that breaks a continuous symmetry. Tesselating 1d frustrated loops, one obtains a 2d metamaterial where phase dislocations self-organize into globally synchronized non-reciprocal phase defects. We expect dynamical frustration to be broadly applicable at any scale, from cold atoms and superconducting circuits to acoustics and RF circuits -- anywhere where space-time modulation can be pushed beyond linear stability.

</details>


### [134] [Stretching and bending of (really) thick elastic plates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01889)
*Shiheng Zhao,Pierre A. Haas*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过计算厚弹性板在中线微小变形下的有效拉伸与弯曲模量，发现尽管模量随板厚增加而软化，但两者比值近似恒定，从而为将薄板理论中的拉伸-弯曲分离图像应用于厚板（如生物细胞片层）提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 薄板假设下弹性板的机械能可分离为拉伸能（stretching energy）和弯曲能（bending energy），这一分离在渐近薄板情形下严格成立，却出奇地适用于厚板。本文旨在揭示这一悖论背后的原因，即为厚板应用薄板拉伸-弯曲图像提供理论正当性。

Method: 考虑厚弹性板，对其中线施加渐近微小的变形，通过解析计算推导出板的有效拉伸模量（effective stretching modulus）和有效弯曲模量（effective bending modulus）。

Result: 有效拉伸模量和有效弯曲模量均随板厚增加而软化（soften），但两者的比值近似保持恒定，不受厚度变化的影响。

Conclusion: 该计算结果为将薄板拉伸-弯曲的分离图像扩展应用于厚板（如生物细胞片层）提供了理论上的合理解释。

Abstract: The mechanical energy of an elastic plate separates into stretching and bending energies. This is a result for asymptotically thin plates, but it is often a surprisingly accurate approximation for thick plates, too. Here, we address this conundrum: We compute the deformations of a thick elastic plate resulting from imposed, asymptotically small deformations of its midline to discover effective stretching and bending moduli. They soften with increasing plate thickness, but, strikingly, their ratio remains approximately constant. In this way, our calculations provide a justification for applying the thin-plate picture of stretching and bending to thick plates such as biological cell sheets.

</details>


### [135] [Molecular-to-polymeric crossover in ion diffusion in glyme-based electrolytes: from vehicular to hopping transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01978)
*Aicha Jani,Simon Gravelle,Pawel Wzietek,Mehdi Zeghal,Patrick Judeinstein*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过核磁共振、电导率测量和分子动力学模拟，揭示了甘醇二甲醚基电解质中离子输运随聚合物链长从短链到长链的转变机制，发现当重复单元数n≈8时存在一个交叉区域，短链以载体机制（vehicular mechanism）伴随强烈离子关联为主，长链则通过快速配位交换解耦于聚合物运动，并伴随阴离子主导的电荷输运。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 甘醇二甲醚基电解质中的离子输运受到溶剂化结构、离子关联和聚合物链长的复杂相互作用影响，但目前缺乏从短链到长链跨越分子到聚合物尺度的系统性理解。

Method: 结合脉冲梯度场核磁共振（pulsed-field gradient nuclear magnetic resonance, PFG-NMR）、离子电导率测量和分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，研究单价阳离子（Li⁺, Na⁺, Cs⁺）和TFSI⁻阴离子在从单甘醇二甲醚到长链聚环氧乙烷（poly(ethylene oxide, PEO)）的宽分子量范围内的扩散行为。

Result: 识别出在重复单元数n≈8处存在一个交叉区域，将离子输运分为两个截然不同的机制：短链区域以载体机制为主且伴有显著离子关联；长链区域中离子输运与聚合物运动解耦，通过快速配位交换进行。该转变伴随着离子簇减少和阴离子迁移率增强，导致电荷输运逐渐由阴离子主导。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了跨越分子到聚合物转变过程中离子输运的分子图像，强调了溶剂化壳层动力学和聚合物弛豫在甘醇二甲醚基电解质中离子动力学中的核心调控作用。

Abstract: Ion transport in glyme-based electrolytes arises from a complex interplay between solvation structure, ion correlations, and polymer chain length. Here, combining pulsed-field gradient nuclear magnetic resonance (PFG-NMR), ionic conductivity measurements, and molecular dynamics (MD) simulations, we investigate the diffusion of monovalent cations (Li$^+$, Na$^+$, Cs$^+$) and TFSI$^-$ anions across a wide molecular-weight range, from monoglyme to long poly(ethylene oxide) (PEO) chains up to 4000~g/mol, corresponding to $n$ up to 88, where $n$ is the number of ethylene oxide repeat units. We identify a crossover region at $n \approx 8$ separating two transport regimes. For short chains, ion motion is consistent with a vehicular mechanism, accompanied by pronounced ion correlations. For longer chains, ion transport decouples from polymer motion and proceeds via rapid coordination exchanges within a slowly relaxing matrix. This transition is accompanied by reduced ion clustering and enhanced anion mobility, leading to increasingly anion-dominated charge transport. Overall, our results provide a molecular picture of ion transport across the molecular-to-polymeric transition and highlight the central role of solvation shell dynamics and polymer relaxation in governing ion dynamics in glyme-based electrolytes.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [136] [Quantum Ergodicity and Thermalization in Interval Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00749)
*Abbas Edalat*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将黎曼谱典型性定理（Reimann's spectral typicality theorem，即量子遍历性的现代表述）与区间量子力学（Interval Quantum Mechanics, IQM）相结合，证明了在IQM框架下，由有限精度测量定义的量子包裹（quantum parcels）中，任何有界观测量的期望区间在大多数晚时刻会集中到微正则值附近，并进一步分析了双包裹情形下的分离保持与模糊测量更新性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子遍历性理论通常假定量子态由精确点态密度矩阵表示，但实际实验中观测者只能通过有限精度的宏观可观测量测量获得有限信息。因此，需要一种数学框架来精确刻画这种认识论（epistemic）知识的不确定性，并在此框架下建立热化行为的严格结果。

Method: 利用黎曼谱典型性定理作为核心工具，结合IQM中量子包裹（量子态由密度矩阵构成的弱开凸集表示）的数学结构，分析包裹内所有态的有效维度（effective dimension）对可观测量期望区间演化的影响。对于双包裹情形，引入守恒量Q^*的支撑条件来分析分离保持与模糊测量更新。

Result: 对于单个量子包裹，若其中每个态的有效维度足够大（确保热化条件），则任何有界观测量的期望区间在大多数晚时刻会集中到微正则值附近，且渐近界仅依赖于包裹内的最小有效维度而非包裹的具体形状。对于双包裹情形，两个包裹的期望区间均趋于微正则值，分离被精确保持，且模糊测量后的更新包裹仍然有效。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了有限精度测量下量子态集合的热化行为与量子遍历性之间的严格数学联系，为区间量子力学提供了热化定理的理论基础，并展示了如何在保持态间分离的条件下处理模糊测量更新，对理解宏观量子系统的统计行为有重要意义。

Abstract: We combine Reimann's spectral typicality theorem -- a modern formulation of quantum ergodicity -- with the framework of Interval Quantum Mechanics (IQM). In IQM, quantum states are represented not by points but by \emph{quantum parcels}: weak open convex sets of density matrices defined by finitely many expectation intervals. Such parcels are the exact mathematical representation of the epistemic knowledge obtained from finite-precision measurements of macroscopic observables.
  We prove that for a single parcel in which every state has large effective dimension (a condition that ensures thermalization), the expectation interval of any bounded observable becomes concentrated around the microcanonical value for most late times. The asymptotic bound depends only on the minimal effective dimension within the parcel, not on its detailed shape.
  For a double parcel \((O_1,O_2)\) with both components contained in an energy shell, separated by a conserved quantity \(Q^*\) that is supported on the range of the measurement projector, we show that the expectation intervals of both parcels become concentrated near the microcanonical values of bounded observables, the separation is preserved exactly, and the updated double parcel after a fuzzy measurement remains valid.

</details>


### [137] [Pauli-structured preconditioning for quantum linear system solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01733)
*Hantao Nie,Zhijian Lai,Dong An*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在量子线性系统（QLS）求解器中，利用泡利结构（Pauli-structured）表示进行预处理（preconditioning）的有效性，提出通过对泡利乘积进行代数重组（algebraic regrouping）来降低预处理算子的泡利系数权重，从而改善QLS算法的复杂度参数，而非仅仅改善经典条件数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典线性系统求解器中预处理是加速的基本技术，但在量子线性系统（QLS）算法中，由于系统矩阵与预处理器的块编码（block-encoding）组合会产生归一化开销（normalization overhead），预处理可能无法带来优势。这一限制引出了一个问题：是否可以利用额外的代数结构使预处理在量子访问模型中变得有效。

Method: 论文提出，当系统矩阵和预处理器均具有泡利结构（Pauli-structured）表示时，可以通过对泡利乘积进行代数重组（algebraic regrouping）来访问预处理后的算子。这种重组可降低预处理算子的泡利系数权重（Pauli coefficient weight），从而改变与量子算法相关的归一化参数。作者推导了重组后泡利表示的显式大小和系数权重边界。

Result: 理论分析表明，泡利结构预处理能够降低QLS算法的有效复杂度参数，而不仅仅是改善经典条件数。数值实验在一个有限维合成基准上验证了该方法在范数感知（norm-aware）直接块编码诊断指标和随机化QLS每样本深度代理（per-sample depth proxy）上的改进。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了泡利结构预处理在何种条件下能够切实降低QLS算法的复杂度，为评估量子线性代数的实际资源需求提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Preconditioning is a fundamental technique for accelerating classical linear system solvers, and understanding when its benefits persist in quantum linear system (QLS) solvers is important for assessing the practical resource requirements of quantum linear algebra. In QLS algorithms, however, the potential advantage of preconditioning may be offset by the normalization overhead incurred by composing separate block-encodings of the system matrix and the preconditioner, as observed in recent work. This limitation leaves open whether additional algebraic structure can make preconditioning effective in quantum access models. Motivated by this question, we show that Pauli-structured representations of both the system matrix and the preconditioner allow the preconditioned operator to be accessed through regrouped Pauli expansions. In this setting, algebraic regrouping of Pauli products can reduce the Pauli coefficient weight of the preconditioned operator, thereby altering the normalization parameters relevant to quantum algorithms. We derive explicit size and coefficient-weight bounds for the regrouped Pauli representations, and we trace their consequences for both direct block-encoding constructions and randomized Pauli linear system solvers. These results identify when Pauli-structured preconditioning can reduce the effective complexity parameters of QLS algorithms, rather than merely improving the classical condition number. Numerical experiments on a finite-dimensional synthetic benchmark show reductions in norm-aware direct block-encoding diagnostics and in the randomized QLS per-sample depth proxy.

</details>


### [138] [Trajectories of Critical Unstable Qubits in and on the Bloch Sphere](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01405)
*Snehit Panghal,Apostolos Pilaftsis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将之前关于“临界不稳定量子比特（Critical Unstable Qubits, CUQs）”的研究推广到混合态情形，使用密度矩阵（density matrix）形式分析了布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）上的轨迹演化，首次给出了纯态与混合态CUQ轨迹的显式几何构造，并识别了其在共衰变系（co-decaying frame）中的不动点（stationary points）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究关注了一类称为CUQ的新型不稳定两能级系统，其在共衰变系中展现出不同于厄米系统（Hermitian system）拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）的非简谐与相干性-退相干振荡等奇特现象；但此前对混合态以及布洛赫球上轨迹的几何性质尚缺乏系统分析。

Method: 采用密度矩阵形式描述混合态的动力学演化，通过布洛赫矢量（Bloch vector）的时间演化研究量子态在布洛赫球上的轨迹，并首次给出纯态与混合态CUQ轨迹的显式几何构造。

Result: 明确了CUQ在共衰变系中的不动点位置，即态不再随时间演化的特殊点；获得了纯态与混合态在布洛赫球上轨迹的几何构造。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解非厄米哈密顿量（non-Hermitian Hamiltonian）下的不稳定两能级系统提供了几何视角，其发现对于粒子宇宙学（particle cosmology）和非厄米哈密顿量的量子模拟具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We extend previous studies on a novel class of unstable two-level systems which were called Critical Unstable Qubits (CUQs). In an appropriately defined co-decaying frame, the CUQs exhibit striking phenomena of indefinite anharmonic oscillations between two states and coherence-decoherence oscillations of mixed states. These features are distinct from the usual Rabi oscillations observed in the Hermitian counterpart of two-level systems, which are harmonic and preserve the coherence of the quantum state. We employ the density matrix formalism to study these phenomena for mixed states and delve into the nature of the trajectory traversed by these states in the Bloch sphere by studying the time evolution of the Bloch vector that describes the quantum state of the unstable qubit. In particular, we provide for the first time explicit geometric constructions to obtain trajectories of both pure and mixed CUQs in and on the Bloch sphere. This enables us to identify the stationary points of CUQs, at which the states do not evolve in time in the co-decaying frame. The potential implications of our findings for particle cosmology and quantum simulations of non-Hermitian Hamiltonians are discussed.

</details>


### [139] [Correlated Quantum Sensing at the Seemingly Classical Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01673)
*K. P. Athulya,Sreenath K. Manikandan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在弱相互作用辐射场（包括引力波和引力子）中，使用高质量谐振量子探测器在经典极限（大量量子）下探测量子统计效应的可能性，提出了相关计数、零差和外差探测策略，并设计了基于对称关联器的统计检验方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱相互作用辐射场的不可分量子（indivisible quanta）及其量子统计（quantum statistics）的探测极具挑战性，本文旨在探索在看似经典极限（大量量子入射）下，通过高质量谐振探测器揭示量子效应的统计优势。

Method: 采用高质量谐振量子谐波探测器（quantum harmonic detectors），初始化于受辐射热测量术（bolometry）启发的零均值热态（thermal states）制备；提出了相关计数（correlated counting）、零差（homodyne）和外差（heterodyne）三种探测策略；并将量子光学中的辐射热测量学机制（bolometric regime）类比于量子引力中质量四极谐振子（mass quadrupole oscillators）的类似机制。

Result: 提出了用于两个和三个低功能谐振质量探测器的对称关联器（symmetric correlators）简单统计检验方法，能够在桌面实验中揭示引力子（gravitons）的互补量子噪声特征（complementary quantum noise characteristics）。

Conclusion: 高质量谐振探测器在弱相互作用辐射场的量子统计探测中具有统计优势；所提出的对称关联器统计检验为在桌面实验中探测引力子量子特性提供了可行路径。

Abstract: It is a difficult task to detect the indivisible quanta of weakly interacting radiation fields, and even more challenging to probe their quantum statistics. Nevertheless, if barely functional high-quality resonant detectors are feasible for weakly interacting radiation fields, they do come with certain statistical advantages to probe quantum effects at the seemingly classical limit of a large number of quanta of the incoming radiation field. We present correlated counting, homodyne, and heterodyne detection strategies using high-quality resonant quantum harmonic detectors operating at this limit, initialized in bolometry-inspired zero-mean preparations such as thermal states. We compare the bolometric regime of good resonant harmonic detectors in quantum optics to the bolometric regime of barely functional resonant mass quadrupole oscillators as detectors for quantum gravity. Simple statistical tests are proposed using symmetric correlators for two and three such barely functional resonant mass detectors that could reveal the complementary quantum noise characteristics of gravitons in tabletop experiments.

</details>


### [140] [Hidden $\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$ symmetry and Jordan chains in a resonant ghostly three-dimensional model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02290)
*Andreas Fring,Ian Marquette*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类三维“鬼”哈密顿量实现的全简并共振六阶Pais-Uhlenbeck振子，揭示了经典相流中的非对角化约当链（Jordan chain）结构、量子化后隐藏的$\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$谱生成代数、伴随的约当结构不变子空间，以及三哈密顿量（tri-Hamiltonian）形式；该模型体现了共振高阶导数系统中隐藏对称性、经典与量子约当结构及多哈密顿量几何的共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高阶导数共振系统中经典与量子层面约当结构（Jordan structure）的来源，以及隐藏对称代数与多哈密顿量几何如何在该类系统中共同作用。

Method: 基于三维鬼哈密顿量实现（ghostly Hamiltonian realisation）的六阶Pais-Uhlenbeck振子，从经典相流分析其非对角化的约当链分解；运用量子化与交织算子（intertwining operators）构造隐藏$\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$谱生成代数；利用Lie点对称性导出三哈密顿量形式。

Result: 经典相流分解为两条复共轭的三节约当链（Jordan chains of length three），解释含长期项（secular terms）的振荡解；量子化后隐藏$\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$代数的二次组合生成有限维不变子空间，其约当分解与$\mathfrak{sl}_2$子模分解一般不一致；三哈密顿量族中不存在正定线性组合能恢复相同动力学；高阶中心化子候选$Q$可约且不产生独立守恒量。

Conclusion: 该模型展示了一种共振高阶导数系统中隐藏$\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$对称性、经典与量子约当结构及多哈密顿量几何共存的情形。

Abstract: We investigate a three-dimensional ghostly Hamiltonian realisation of the fully degenerate resonant sixth-order Pais-Uhlenbeck oscillator. On the classical level, the phase-space flow is non-diagonalisable and decomposes into two complex-conjugate Jordan chains of length three, explaining the appearance of oscillatory solutions with secular terms.
  Upon quantisation, we construct intertwining operators whose quadratic combinations generate a hidden spectrum-generating $\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$-algebra. The associated descendant spaces are finite-dimensional invariant subspaces carrying non-trivial Jordan structure. Although these spaces admit a natural decomposition into irreducible modules of a distinguished $\mathfrak{sl}_2$-subalgebra, this decomposition does not in general coincide with the Jordan decomposition of the Hamiltonian.
  We further derive a tri-Hamiltonian formulation from Lie point symmetries of the classical flow and show that the corresponding Hamiltonians are naturally encoded by the same hidden algebra. Nevertheless, unlike in the non-resonant case, no positive-definite linear combination of them generates the same dynamics. Finally, we analyse the common centraliser of the tri-Hamiltonian family in $U(\mathfrak u(2,1))$, showing that the natural higher-order candidate $Q$ is reducible and yields no independent classical or quantum integral.
  The model thus provides a resonant higher-derivative system in which hidden $\mathfrak{u}(2,1)$ symmetry, classical and quantum Jordan structures, and multi-Hamiltonian geometry coexist.

</details>


### [141] [Topics on Foundations of Physics: From the quantum to the (semi) classical, gravity, thermodynamics, and (or beyond) our possible detections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00255)
*Ricardo Muciño*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本论文聚焦于评估和拓展量子理论，以探索其在热力学、半经典及量子引力等领域的可检验预言，并围绕“时间之箭”（the arrow of time）等基础问题展开三条相互关联的研究：物理理论中的可探测性、热力学平衡趋近机制、以及相对论性坍缩理论与自洽半经典引力模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心动机源于对世界根本基础的求知欲，特别是弥合观测/感知经验与基础量子理论之间的鸿沟。具体而言，旨在回答为何时间在我们理论中单向“流动”，以及为何自然过程在时间上不对称演化——即时间之箭（the arrow of time）问题。

Method: 采取三条独立但相互关联的研究路线：第一部分探讨物理理论中的可探测性（possible detections）；第二部分研究趋近热力学平衡（approach to thermodynamic equilibrium）的解释机制；第三部分构建相对论性坍缩理论（relativistic collapse theories）与自洽的半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）模型。

Result: 三条研究路线均取得了成功的研究成果，分别对应论文的三个独立部分。

Conclusion: 通过对量子理论在热力学、半经典与量子引力等不同场景下的评估与延伸，论文为基础物理中的时间不对称性等根本问题提供了新的理解路径，并展示了可探测的理论预言。

Abstract: The work leading to this thesis focuses on assessing and extending quantum theories in order to explore and test their implications across various regimes -- including thermodynamics, semiclassical and quantum gravity scenarios, and the in principle detectable predictions of such theories. The general motivation stems from a basic desire to understand the world form its very foundations. For instance, how can we bridge the gap between what we observe or `perceive' and the fundamental quantum nature in our theories. In particular, this work originated from the search to a better understanding of the nature of time according to our physical theories and the common perception that it invariably `flows' to the future, or, in other words, why do we observe distinct natural processes evolving asymmetrically in time? These motivations led to three distinct, yet interconnected and successful, lines of research, presented here in three separate parts: I. On Possible Detections within Physical Theories; II. On Explaining the Approach to Thermodynamic Equilibrium; and III. Relativistic Collapse Theories and a Self-Consistent Model of Semiclassical Gravity.

</details>


### [142] [Information Hierarchy in Many-Body Berry Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02155)
*Kai Watanabe*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了相互作用多体基态的几何信息是否能从有限数量的局域关联中推断出来。基于Resta公式，本文将log z视为累积量母函数，建立了累积量阶次之间的信息层级。结果表明，对于N粒子系统，即使知道所有直到N-1阶的密度关联函数，通常也无法唯一确定Berry相位；在热力学极限下，任何有限局域关联函数集都不足以确定整体和乐。本文还识别了两种例外情况（准自由模型和对称性约束模型），并讨论了该结果对数值方法（包括机器学习）研究拓扑相的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体拓扑（many-body topology）是现代固体理论的核心概念，识别能够捕捉这一概念的有效的自由度在基础研究和实际应用中都具有重要意义。本文旨在澄清局域自由度方法在多体和乐（many-body holonomy）研究中的局限性，并区分全局和乐何时编码于局域关联之中、何时不能。

Method: 从Resta公式 $z=\left\langle \exp\!\left(\frac{2πi}{L}\hat X\right)\right\rangle$ 出发，将 $\log z$ 视为累积量母函数（cumulant generating function），建立跨累积量阶次的通用信息层级（information hierarchy）。该方法不依赖于具体的微观哈密顿量，属于解析论证。

Result: 对于N粒子系统，即使已知所有直到N-1阶的密度关联函数（density correlators），通常也无法唯一确定Berry相位 $\gamma=\operatorname{Im}\log z \, (\mathrm{mod}\ 2\pi)$。在热力学极限下，任何有限局域关联函数集都不足以确定全局和乐（global holonomy）。存在两种例外情况：准自由模型（quasi-free models）中所有累积量由两点关联函数决定；对称性约束（symmetry-enforced constraints）可将无限累积量和约化为有限信息。

Conclusion: 本文结果阐明了基于局域自由度的多体和乐研究方法的局限性，提供了判断全局和乐是否编码于局域关联中的最小框架。该工作对未来的数值研究（包括基于机器学习的拓扑相搜索方法）具有启示意义，并可能推广至量子信息论中的量子边际问题（quantum marginal problem）和多体散射问题等其它领域。

Abstract: Many-body topology is a central concept in modern theories of solids, and identifying effective degrees of freedom that capture it is important both fundamentally and practically. This work studies the extent to which geometric information of an interacting many-body ground state can be inferred from a finite number of local correlations. Starting from the Resta formula, $ z=\left\langle \exp\!\left(\frac{2πi}{L}\hat X\right)\right\rangle$, we view $\log z$ as the cumulant generating function and establish a generic information hierarchy across cumulant orders. We show that, for an $N$-particle system, even complete knowledge of all density correlators up to order $N-1$ does not, in general, uniquely determine the Berry phase $γ=\operatorname{Im}\log z \, (\mathrm{mod}\ 2π)$. In the thermodynamic limit, the statement becomes stronger: no finite set of local correlators suffices to determine the global holonomy. We also identify two exceptional yes-go cases in which the hierarchy is broken. First, for quasi-free models, all cumulants are determined by the particle two-point correlation function. Second, symmetry-enforced constraints can reduce the infinite cumulant sum entering $\log z$ to finite information. The argument is analytic and does not rely on a specific microscopic Hamiltonian. Our results clarify a limitation of approaches based on local degrees of freedom for many-body holonomy and provide a minimal framework for distinguishing when global holonomies are encoded in local correlations and when they are not. We also comment on the possibility of analogous hierarchies in other contexts, such as the quantum marginal problem in quantum information theory and many-body scattering problems. Finally, we discuss implications for future numerical work, including machine-learning approaches to the search for topological phases.

</details>


### [143] [Dynamics of the Density Cube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02421)
*Nabin Bhatta,Djordje Minic,Tatsu Takeuchi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将密度矩阵（density matrix）扩展为密度立方体（density cube），引入第三个指标 $ρ_{ijk}$，并基于三元南部动力学（ternary Nambu dynamics）的量子化推导出其运动方程，发现三路径干涉（triple-path interference）的配对会在演化中相互振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子密度矩阵 $ρ_{ij}$ 只能描述双路径干涉（double-path interference），无法刻画非典型的三路径干涉（triple-path interference）现象。本文旨在通过引入密度立方体理论，将密度矩阵推广到三指标形式，从而扩展对量子干涉结构的描述能力。

Method: 将密度矩阵的指标从两个扩展为三个，得到密度立方体 $ρ_{ijk}$；通过对三元南部动力学的量子化操作，推导出密度立方体所满足的运动方程（equation of motion）。

Result: 密度立方体中具有两个相同指标的元素 $ρ_{iij}$ 和 $ρ_{ijj}$ 分别对应密度矩阵非对角元 $ρ_{ij}$ 的实部和虚部，描述双路径干涉；具有三个不同指标的元素则描述非规范的三路径干涉。运动方程进一步表明，三路径干涉的配对会相互振荡。

Conclusion: 密度立方体理论为描述超越标准密度矩阵框架的量子干涉（特别是三路径干涉）提供了新的动力学框架，其三路径干涉配对间的振荡行为揭示了更丰富的量子相干演化模式。

Abstract: Density cube theory extends the canonical quantum density matrix $ρ_{ij}$ with the addition of an extra index to $ρ_{ijk}$. The elements of the density cube with two different indices, $ρ_{iij}$ and $ρ_{ijj}$, correspond to the real and imaginary parts of the off-diagonal element $ρ_{ij}$ of the density matrix and describe double-path interference, while those with three different indices describe non-canonical triple-path interference. In this letter, we propose an equation of motion for the density cube, obtained from the quantization of ternary Nambu dynamics, and find that pairs of triple-path interferences oscillate into each other.

### [144] [Information scrambling in all-to-all interacting models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02207)
*Abhik Kumar Saha,Tanay Pathak,Masaki Tezuka*

Abstract: Information scrambling is a hallmark of quantum chaos and thermalization in isolated quantum many-body systems. We investigate scrambling dynamics in the all-to-all interacting spin Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK)-$q$ model using both pure- and mixed-state entanglement measures. We show that von-Neumann and Rényi entropies exhibit rapid growth followed by saturation near Haar-random values, signaling efficient scrambling. The scrambling rate reveals a nontrivial dependence on the interaction order, system size, and Hamiltonian scaling. We further employ mixed-state entanglement as a powerful probe of information scrambling. We numerically find a universal relation between the Rényi-1/2 mutual information and entanglement negativity for minimal interaction order in the early growth regime. Furthermore, entanglement negativity displays a Page-curve-like behavior under unequal subsystem partitioning, characterized by the birth, spread, and eventual death of quantum correlations. Our results provide a generic description of information scrambling using entanglement dynamics in all-to-all interacting spin systems with multi-body interactions.

### [146] [Smooth velocity shuttling for suppressing valley excitations in disordered Si/SiGe quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01541)
*Ryo Nagai,Takashi Takemoto,Hiroyuki Mizuno*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种平滑速度穿梭协议（smooth velocity shuttling protocol），通过将速度剖面设计映射到信号处理中的窗函数设计问题，利用基于Tukey窗的调频栅压抑制电子穿梭过程中的谷激发（valley excitation），显著降低硅量子比特中的自旋不保真度（spin infidelity），为大规模硅量子处理器的高保真自旋输运提供了一种无需昂贵数值优化的简洁控制方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将时域穿梭速度剖面（velocity profile）的设计映射为信号处理中窗函数（window functions）的设计问题，从而建立解析且直观的设计准则，无需昂贵的数值优化。具体采用基于Tukey窗的调频栅压（frequency-modulated gate voltage）来抑制速度频谱的高频旁瓣（high-frequency sidelobes）。

Result: 数值模拟表明，在包含实际谷景观空间随机性（spatial randomness of the valley landscape）的条件下，所提出的平滑速度控制在中等至低无序区域（$|Δ_0|/σ_Δ\simeq \mathcal{O}(1)$）显著降低了平均自旋不保真度。此外，在具有大确定性谷耦合（deterministic valley coupling）$|Δ_0|$的器件中，结合该平滑技术可增强对谷无序（valley disorder）的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该控制层面的速度塑形（velocity shaping）方法简单有效，为大规模硅量子处理器中的高保真自旋输运提供了一条稳健的路径。

Abstract: Coherent electron shuttling is a key requirement for realizing scalable silicon quantum computing architectures. However, in silicon qubits, the existence of nearly degenerate conduction-band valleys poses a significant challenge because non-adiabatic transitions to excited valley states cause spin dephasing via spin-valley mixing. In this paper, we propose a smooth velocity shuttling protocol to suppress these valley excitations. By mapping the time-domain design of the shuttling velocity profile onto the design problem of window functions in signal processing, we establish an analytical and intuitive design guideline that does not require computationally expensive numerical optimization. We demonstrate that the high-frequency sidelobes of the shuttling velocity spectrum can be effectively suppressed by applying a frequency-modulated gate voltage based on the Tukey window. Through numerical simulations incorporating realistic spatial randomness of the valley landscape, we show that the proposed smooth velocity control significantly reduces the average spin infidelity in the moderate-to-low disorder regime ($|Δ_0|/σ_Δ\simeq \mathcal{O}(1)$). Furthermore, we clarify that in devices designed with a large deterministic valley coupling $|Δ_0|$, combining it with this smoothing technique improves robustness against valley disorder. Our results underscore that this simple, control-level velocity shaping provides a robust pathway toward high-fidelity spin transport in large-scale silicon quantum processors.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该理论建立了从二维关联环境的多体自旋响应到约化双量子比特动力学模拟的直接路径，揭示了自旋液体环境的实用价值受磁化率介导交换与退相干之间竞争关系的支配，为狄拉克自旋液体量子互联提供了可操作的分析框架。

Abstract: We develop a susceptibility-based open-system theory for two localized qubits coupled through a candidate two-dimensional $\mathrm{U}(1)$ Dirac-spin-liquid-like bath. The central input is the gauge-invariant retarded physical spin susceptibility $\Chi^R(q,ω)$ of the bath. We show that this single response kernel controls both coherent and dissipative qubit dynamics: its real part generates the nonlocal mediated exchange, while its absorptive part determines relaxation and dephasing through the equilibrium noise spectrum. This gives a unified reduced two-qubit description in which the usefulness of the bath as an entanglement bus is governed by the competition between susceptibility-mediated exchange and bath-induced decoherence. As an analytically transparent benchmark, we evaluate the spinon mean-field Dirac susceptibility and recover the static algebraic exchange $J_{\mathrm{eff}}(R)\propto J_{\rm local}^2/(v_F R^3)$, together with pseudogap-suppressed relaxation $Γ_1\propto J_{\rm local}^2ω_0^3/v_F^4$. We then formulate a beyond-mean-field extension in which gauge-field dressing and other interaction effects are absorbed into a dressed physical susceptibility, without changing the reduced qubit-sector mapping. The resulting framework provides a direct route from the many-body spin response of a correlated two-dimensional bath to reduced-dynamics simulations of entanglement generation, coherence loss, and the operational phase space of a candidate Dirac spin-liquid quantum interconnect.

Abstract: We propose a quantum probability-flow principle for deriving local learning rules in associative memory. *Christopher Mastandrea,Chih-Chun Chien*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过哈伯德哈密顿量（Hubbard Hamiltonian）控制的一维双粒子连续时间量子行走（continuous-time quantum walks），研究了空间分离区域之间以及两个可区分或不可区分粒子之间的纠缠度量；分析了不同初始态下的纠缠增长，发现不可区分情形与可区分情形在类似初始态下表现相似，但长时间极限下纠缠度量随局域排斥强度增加呈非单调变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多粒子量子动力学中，纠缠度量（entanglement measures）的计算和演化行为尚不完全清晰，尤其是对于不可区分粒子（indistinguishable particles）与空间区域之间纠缠的对比研究较少，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用哈伯德哈密顿量描述一维双粒子连续时间量子行走；通过左-右纠缠（left-right entanglement）度量空间区域间的纠缠（基于粗粒化态的熵，统计格子左右两半的粒子数），以及通过粒子-粒子纠缠（particle-particle entanglement）度量粒子间的纠缠（基于时间演化Fock态奇异值的熵）；分别采用可分离（separable）、纠缠（entangled）和双重占据（doubly occupied）三种初始态进行数值计算。

Result: 不可区分粒子情形的纠缠度量与可区分粒子情形在类似初始态下表现相似；长时间极限下，纠缠度量随局域排斥（onsite repulsion）强度增加呈非单调（non-monotonic）变化。

Conclusion: 本文为多粒子量子动力学中的纠缠研究提供了新视角，指出纠缠度量的长时间行为受局域相互作用强度的非平凡影响，对未来的相关研究具有参考意义。

Abstract: We present entanglement measures between spatially separated regions and between two distinguishable or indistinguishable particles in one-dimensional two-particle continuous-time quantum walks governed by the Hubbard Hamiltonian. The left-right entanglement checks the entropy of coarse-grained states counting the numbers of particles on the left and right halves of the lattice while the particle-particle entanglement is based on the entropy of the singular values of the time-evolved Fock state. With separable, entangled, and doubly occupied initial states, we examine initial entanglement and the following growth in different entanglement measures. While the entanglement measures of the indistinguishable cases resemble those of the distinguishable cases when the initial states are comparable, the long-time limits of the entanglement measures are typically non-monotonic as the onsite repulsion increases. We also discuss possible implications for future research of entanglement in multi-particle quantum dynamics.

</details>


### [151] [Strong-to-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02555)
*Chong Wang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了强到弱自发对称性破缺（SW-SSB）这一概念，将其从混合态对称性破缺的基本思想出发，扩展为联系拓扑序、涌现流体动力学以及物相信息论表征的统一视角，并为开放系统（量子和经典）中的物相研究提供了鸟瞰式概述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为理解开放系统（open systems）中量子或经典物相提供统一框架，连接拓扑序（topological orders）、涌现流体动力学（emergent hydrodynamics）和物相的信息论表征（information-theoretic characterization）等不同物理思想。

Method: 从对称性破缺扩展到一般混合态（mixed states）的基本思路出发，借鉴统计力学（statistical mechanics）中正则系综与巨正则系综的等价性，建立强到弱自发对称性破缺（SW-SSB）概念，并以此为主线串联多个物理领域。

Result: SW-SSB 发展为一个统一视角，能够将拓扑序、涌现流体动力学及物相信息论表征等不同研究方向联系起来。

Conclusion: 这篇综述对 SW-SSB 相关近期进展进行了鸟瞰式总结，表明该概念为开放系统中的物相研究提供了有价值的统一框架。

Abstract: Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SW-SSB) has recently emerged as a useful framework for studying phases of matter in open systems, quantum or classical. Beginning with the simple idea of extending symmetry breaking to general mixed states, and the familiar equivalence between canonical and grand-canonical ensembles in statistical mechanics, the concept has grown into a unifying perspective connecting many different ideas in physics, including topological orders, emergent hydrodynamics, and information-theoretic characterization of phases of matter. This review provides a bird's-eye view of some of these recent developments.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该问题受椭圆限制性三体问题启发，其中洛伦兹力对应科里奥利力，库仑力被重力替代，外部源的电场力由离心力和其他天体的引力组合而成。该设置是一个奇异的欧拉-哈密顿系统版本，奇点源于电子与质子的碰撞（或两质量体的碰撞），因此需要进行正则化处理。

Method: 采用变分方法，分别在非局部拉格朗日（non-local Lagrangian）设定和非局部哈密顿（non-local Hamiltonian）设定中探测周期碰撞解。

Abstract: In this article we study periodic orbits of an electron attracted by a proton subject to Lorentz, electric, and Euler forces where each of them is allowed to depend periodically on time. This setup is motivated by the elliptic restricted three-body-problem where the Lorentz force corresponds to Coriolis force, the Coulomb force is replaced by the gravitational force, and the electric force of an external source is a combination of centrifugal forces and gravitational forces of other bodies. This is a singular version of a Euler-Hamilton system as discussed in [FW26b]. The singularity is due to collisions of the electron with the proton, respectively of two masses. Due to the possibility of collisions this problem has to be regularized. We show how periodic collisional solutions of this problem can be detected variationally in a non-local Lagrangian setup as well as in a non-local Hamiltonian setup.

### [153] [Eigenvalue formulation of Stochastic Inflation and application to large perturbation generating inflationary features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00176)
*Swagat S. Mishra,Edmund J. Copeland,Anne M. Green*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种自洽的本征值技术（eigenvalue technique），用于求解随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）中描述大尺度扰动概率分布函数（PDF）的邻接福克-普朗克方程（adjoint Fokker-Planck Equation），并在无漂移和有恒定漂移两种情形下分析了随机e-折叠数（${\cal N}$）的PDF结构，特别发现了PDF在指数尾部与峰值之间存在幂律行为（$P({\cal N}) \propto {\cal N}^{-3/2}$）的中间区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机暴胀是计算可能坍缩形成原初黑洞（Primordial Black Holes）的大尺度暴胀扰动概率分布函数（PDF）的重要工具。该PDF满足邻接福克-普朗克方程（adjoint Fokker-Planck Equation），需要发展新的求解方法以更深入地理解其结构。

Method: 提出一种新的自洽本征值技术（eigenvalue technique）来求解随机e-折叠数（${\cal N}$）的概率分布函数（PDF）。首先应用于平坦势（flat potential）上无经典漂移（classical drift）的量子扩散，随后推广到具有恒定漂移（constant drift）的暴胀情形，并在窄阱（narrow-well）和宽阱（broad-well）极限下分别处理。

Result: 在无漂移情形下，恢复了先前用特征函数（characteristic functions）方法得到的含指数尾部（exponential tail）的PDF，并新发现峰值与指数尾部之间存在幂律行为（$P({\cal N}) \propto {\cal N}^{-3/2}$）的中间区间。在窄阱极限下，PDF与无漂移情形相似，尾部受到轻微抑制。在宽阱极限下，需分段构造本征谱（spectrum），PDF在定性上不同：峰值增强而尾部被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 发展的本征值技术可以有效求解随机暴胀中的PDF，揭示了在指数尾部与峰值之间存在尚未被强调的幂律中间区间，并在不同漂移条件下展示了PDF结构的显著差异。

Abstract: Stochastic inflation is a powerful technique for calculating the probability distribution function (PDF) of large inflationary perturbations, which may collapse to form Primordial Black Holes. The PDF, $P({\cal N})$, of the stochastic number of e-folds, ${\cal N}$, satisfies an adjoint Fokker-Planck Equation. We develop a new self-contained eigenvalue technique which can be used to determine $P({\cal N})$. First we apply this method to the simple case of quantum diffusion along a flat potential without any classical drift. We recover the expression for the PDF that has previously been found using characteristic functions, with an exponential tail. We also identify an intermediate regime between the peak and the exponential tail of the PDF, which has not been emphasized in earlier studies, where it exhibits a power-law behaviour, $P({\cal N}) \propto {\cal N}^{-3/2}$. Finally we apply the method to constant drift inflation, in the narrow- and broad-well limits. In the narrow-well limit, there is an analytic solution and the PDF is similar to the drift-free case, with a mildly suppressed tail. In the broad-well limit, determining the full set of eigenvalues and eigenfunctions requires a piecewise construction of the spectrum, and the broad-well PDF is qualitatively different, with an enhanced peak and a strongly suppressed tail.

</details>

Abstract: In this paper, we provide a short review on the Quintom dark energy theory. Firstly, we discuss the No-Go theorem associated with dynamical dark energy, then present some examples of models in which the equation of state (EoS) evolves with time and can cross $w=-1$ . Secondly, we discuss the bouncing universe and emergent universe with Quintom matter. Finally, we discuss the possibility of studying the nature of dark energy by measuring the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) polarization rotation angle.

### [155] [JWST's Little Red Dots as collapsed Supermassive Dark Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02539)
*Cosmin Ilie*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出超重暗星（SMDS）路径可自然满足类恒星（quasi-star）形成所需的结构与能量条件，从而解释JWST观测到的“小红点”（LRDs）现象，且无需传统超重星（SMS）路径所需的严格环境限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测揭示的“小红点”（Little Red Dots, LRDs）现象是当前天体物理学的重大谜题之一，现有类恒星（quasi-star）模型虽可解释其光谱与形态，但依赖极为严苛的超重星（supermassive star, SMS）形成条件，亟需寻找更普适的形成路径。

Method: 本文从理论上论证了超重暗星（supermassive dark star, SMDS）——一种由暗物质湮灭（dark matter annihilation）而非核燃烧供能的恒星——可同时满足类恒星（quasi-star）形成所需的结构与能量条件，并系统分析该路径相较于传统超重星（SMS）路径在环境约束上的放松效应。

Conclusion: 超重暗星（SMDS）路径能够统一解释JWST“小红点”（LRDs）的观测特征，同时消除了传统超重星（SMS）路径对强Lyman-Werner背景、高速持续气体流入和旋转支撑等条件的依赖，为理解早期宇宙超大质量黑洞的形成提供了新范式。

Abstract: The nature of the ``Little Red Dots'' (LRDs) is one of the most profound mysteries posed by the JWST data. One promising class of models that can reproduce the observed LRDs spectra and morphology are quasi-stars: massive envelopes surrounding accreting black holes formed via the collapse of supermassive stars (SMSs). However, the canonical SMS pathway relies on a highly restricted set of environmental and structural conditions: strong Lyman--Werner (LW) backgrounds to suppress H$_2$ cooling, high and sustained gas inflow rates to enforce entropy stratified envelopes, and assume non-zero rotational support in order to prevent GR instability collapse before $\sim 10^6 M_{\odot}$. Here we show that supermassive dark stars (SMDSs), powered by dark matter (DM) annihilation rather than nuclear burning, naturally satisfy the key structural and energetic requirements for quasi-star (QS) formation while relaxing {\it all} of those restrictive conditions listed above. Moreover, quasi-stars formed through the SMDS pathway are born with prompt BH masses ($\gtrsim 10\%$) of the progenitor mass. They therefore enter directly into a late-stage quasi-star regime; subsequently the envelope expands and cools until its photosphere reaches the zero-metallicity opacity limit $(T_{\rm eff}\sim3000$-$6000\,{\rm K}$). Those cool, optically thick, unresolved photospheres can reproduce key features of many JWST LRDs.
