### [156] [Photostationary Lifshitz transition in High Tc superconductor Bi2Sr2CaCu2O8+δ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00185)
*Ji Dai,Lukas Hellbrück,Michele Puppin,Alberto Crepaldi,Francesco Barantani,Thomas LaGrange,Arnaud Magrez,Edoardo Martino,Neven Barisic,László Forró,J. Hugo Dil,Marco Grioni,Henrik M. Rønnow,Siham Benhabib,Fabrizio Carbone*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报道通过超快光学激发（ultrafast optical excitation）可在高温铜氧化物超导体Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈+δ中诱导出长寿命的光稳态激发态，该态在高泵浦通量下发生费米面（Fermi surface）Lifshitz转变，拓扑结构由空穴型转变为电子型，其效果与化学掺杂（chemical doping）高度类似，揭示了一种涉及电荷转移、有效电子关联重整化和缺陷辅助电荷俘获的高效光掺杂（photodoping）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用超快光激发驱动Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈+δ；利用时间分辨和角分辨光电子能谱（time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, tr-ARPES）测量能带演化，并结合单带紧束缚（single-band tight-binding）计算进行理论支持。

Result: 在足够高的泵浦通量下，光激发诱导的稳态经历费米面Lifshitz转变（Lifshitz transition），拓扑从空穴型（hole-like）变为电子型（electron-like）。1.6 eV光激发引起的能带结构演化与化学掺杂高度类似。高效光掺杂机制包含电荷转移、有效电子关联重整化（renormalization of effective electronic correlations）以及缺陷辅助电荷俘获（defect-assisted charge trapping）。

Conclusion: 该发现对铜氧化物中与激光重复周期相当时间尺度上的热化过程（thermalization processes）提出了基本追问。更广泛而言，超快光学控制通过调节泵浦通量，能够进入传统方法难以达到的相图区域。

Abstract: To date, controlling the steady-state electronic band structure in high-Tc cuprate superconductors has been achieved primarily through chemical doping or magnetic fields. Here, we present that ultrafast optical excitation can instead drive the electronic band structure of Bi2Sr2CaCu2O8+δ into a photostationary, long-lived excited state. At sufficiently high pump fluences, this state undergoes a Lifshitz transition of the Fermi surface, characterized by a change in topology from hole-like to electron-like. Time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, supported by single-band tight-binding calculations, reveals that 1.6 eV photoexcitation induces band-structure evolutions closely analogous to those produced by chemical doping. These results point to an efficient photodoping mechanism involving cooperative effects, including charge transfer, renormalization of effective electronic correlations, and defect-assisted charge trapping. Our findings raise fundamental questions regarding thermalization processes occurring on timescales comparable to the laser repetition period in cuprates. More broadly, ultrafast optical control enables access to otherwise inaccessible regions of the phase diagram by tuning the pump fluence.

### [157] [Extracting central charge from ground-state overlaps of spatially deformed Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00214)
*Chen Bai,Xinyu Sun,Liang-Hong Mo,Hong-Hao Tu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种直接从基态波函数重叠（wave-function overlap）中提取 $(1+1)$ 维共形场论（conformal field theory, CFT）中心荷（central charge）的方法。通过构造 $q$-Möbius 形变下的精确重叠公式，并基于该结果构建仅依赖基态重叠的晶格估计量，在临界量子链和二维陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）的无能隙边缘模中验证了该方法的有效性与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法提取共形场论中的中心荷等共形数据通常需要复杂的计算或特定的边界条件（boundary conditions）。本文旨在提供一种更简单、仅基于基态波函数重叠的方法，以便在微观模型和拓扑边缘模中直接探测共形数据。

Method: 1) 推导了 $q$-Möbius 形变下变形基态与未变形基态之间的精确波函数重叠公式，其指数仅依赖于中心荷。2) 基于该重叠公式，构造了一个仅利用基态重叠的晶格估计器（lattice estimator）。3) 将该估计器应用于代表性临界量子链（critical quantum chains）和二维陈绝缘体的无能隙边缘模（gapless edge modes）进行数值验证。

Result: 数值结果表明，构建的基态重叠能够简单且鲁棒地探测微观模型中的中心荷。此外，变形后的基态在其纠缠谱（entanglement spectra）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropies）中保留了普适的几何结构（universal geometric structures）。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一条基于基态波函数重叠的简单路径，用于探测临界系统中的共形数据（conformal data）和拓扑边缘模（topological edge modes）的共形性质。

Abstract: We show that the conformal anomaly of a $(1+1)$-dimensional conformal field theory can be extracted directly from a ground-state wave-function overlap associated with a spatial conformal deformation. Focusing on the $q$-Möbius deformation, we derive an exact overlap formula between the deformed and undeformed ground states, whose exponent depends only on the central charge. Motivated by this result, we construct a lattice estimator based solely on ground-state overlaps and apply it to representative critical quantum chains and the gapless edge modes of a two-dimensional Chern insulator. Numerical results demonstrate that the resulting overlaps provide a simple and robust probe of the central charge in microscopic models. We further demonstrate that the deformed ground states retain universal geometric structures in their entanglement spectra and entanglement entropies. These results provide a simple wave-function-based route to probing conformal data in critical systems and topological edge modes.

### [158] [Electron vs. hole doping in infinite-layer nickelates: electronic structure, magnetism and correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00223)
*Ezra Day-Roberts,Fabio Bernardini,Harrison LaBollita,Yi-Feng Zhao,Andres Cano,Antia S. Botana*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）与动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）相结合，研究了无限层镍酸盐（infinite-layer nickelates）在空穴掺杂和电子掺杂两种条件下的电子结构演化。发现Ni-d_{x^2-y^2}能带的自掺杂效应存在显著不对称性：空穴掺杂抑制该效应，而电子掺杂则增大R(5d)电子口袋但不有效空穴掺杂Ni-d能带。这种不对称性导致磁性响应差异——空穴掺杂迅速抑制反铁磁，电子掺杂则保持反铁磁基态。尽管如此，两个掺杂区间的电子关联均由Ni d_{x^2-y^2}轨道主导，表明单带描述在两种掺杂条件下均可能适用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 未掺杂无限层镍酸盐中观测到的超导电性挑战了现有理解，亟需重新审视该类材料的电子结构（electronic structure）。目前研究集中于空穴掺杂（hole-doped）区域，而对几乎未探索的电子掺杂（electron-doped）区域的系统研究至关重要。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory）与动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）相结合的第一性原理计算方法，研究无限层镍酸盐在空穴掺杂和电子掺杂两种掺杂区间下电子结构的演化。

Result: 发现Ni-d_{x^2-y^2}能带因R(5d)态产生的自掺杂（self-doping）效应存在显著不对称性：空穴掺杂强烈抑制该效应，电子掺杂则增大R(5d)电子口袋尺寸但未对Ni-d_{x^2-y^2}能带产生有效空穴掺杂。磁性响应方面，空穴掺杂迅速压制反铁磁（antiferromagnetism），而电子掺杂下反铁磁仍保持为基态。

Conclusion: 尽管两种掺杂区间的电子结构存在显著不对称性，电子关联（electronic correlations）均由Ni d_{x^2-y^2}轨道主导，表明单带描述（single-band description）对无限层镍酸盐在电子掺杂和空穴掺杂两个区间均可能是合适的。

Abstract: The observation of superconductivity in undoped infinite-layer nickelates $R$NiO$_2$ ($R$ = rare earth) challenges our current understanding and calls for a re-examination of the underlying electronic structure of this family of materials. In this context, it is particularly important to extend the investigation of $R$NiO$_2$ compounds from the intensively studied hole-doped regime to the almost unexplored electron-doped one. Here, we use a combination of density-functional theory and dynamical mean-field theory to study the evolution of the electronic structure of infinite-layer nickelates in these two doping regimes. We find a striking asymmetry in the self-doping of the Ni-$d_{x^2-y^2}$ band due to the $R(5d)$ states: while this effect is strongly suppressed upon hole doping, electron doping instead leads to an increase in the size of the $R(5d)$ electron pockets, but without effectively hole-doping the Ni-$d_{x^2-y^2}$ band. This asymmetry has an important impact on the magnetic response as antiferromagnetism is rapidly suppressed upon hole doping, whereas it remains the ground state upon electron doping. Despite these differences, electronic correlations on both sides of the phase diagram are dominated by the Ni $d_{x^2-y^2}$ orbital, suggesting that a single-band description may be appropriate for infinite-layer nickelates in both the electron- and hole-doped regimes.

</details>


### [159] [Imaging the Magnetically Driven Reconstruction of the Electronic States in the Antiferromagnetic Topological Insulator EuSn$_2$As$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00337)
*Luka Khizanishvili,Erekle Jmukhadze,Anika Raisa,Divyanshi Sar,Mingda Gong,Tetiana Romanova,Dariusz Kaczorowski,Wei-Cheng Lee,Pegor Aynajian*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究利用变温扫描隧道显微镜/谱学（STM/STS）与密度泛函理论（DFT）相结合，在反铁磁（AFM）拓扑绝缘体EuSn₂As₂中观测到两种与磁性相关的能隙，并揭示了Sn空位对镜面对称性保护的破坏是Dirac点质量能隙形成的可能机制，为轴子绝缘体（axion insulator）的实现提供了实空间证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁拓扑绝缘体中轴子绝缘体相的实现常受晶体对称性（crystal symmetries）的阻碍，即便时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）已破缺。本文旨在通过实空间电子结构表征，探究反铁磁拓扑绝缘体EuSn₂As₂在Néel相变附近的局域电子结构及其与磁有序的耦合机制。

Method: 采用变温扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）和扫描隧道谱学（scanning tunneling spectroscopy, STS），并结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，对EuSn₂As₂的(001)表面进行局域电子结构表征，覆盖其Néel温度（T_N = 24 K）以上的顺磁态与以下的反铁磁态。

Result: 在(001)表面观测到大量本征Sn空位（Sn vacancies），引入纳米尺度的电子不均匀性和p型掺杂。降温至T_N以下后，解析出两个不同的磁驱动能隙：费米能级附近约100 meV的能隙和ARPES观测到的Dirac点处约50 meV的能隙。前者归因于反铁磁布里渊区折叠（AFM Brillouin-zone folding）与杂化；后者则指向Sn空位导致镜面对称性（mirror symmetry）保护被解除，进而使Dirac点产生质量能隙（mass gapping），但AFM折叠杂化的贡献无法完全排除。

Conclusion: 研究提供了局域磁矩（localized moments）与巡游拓扑态（itinerant topological states）之间强耦合的实空间证据，表明易剥离的EuSn₂As₂是构建基于轴子绝缘体（axion insulator）器件的潜在候选材料。

Abstract: The realization of the axion insulator phase in magnetic topological insulators is often hindered by crystalline symmetries that protect gapless surface states, even when time-reversal symmetry is broken. Here, we use variable-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) and spectroscopy (STS), complemented with density functional theory (DFT), to investigate the local electronic structure of the antiferromagnetic (AFM) topological insulator EuSn$_2$As$_2$ across its Néel transition at $T_N = 24$ K. On the (001) surface, we observe a substantial density of intrinsic Sn vacancies that introduce nanoscale electronic inhomogeneity and p-type doping. Upon cooling below $T_N$, we resolve the emergence of two distinct magnetically driven gaps: a $\sim$100 meV gap near the Fermi level and a $\sim$50 meV gap at the ARPES-resolved Dirac point. We attribute the former gap to AFM Brillouin-zone folding and hybridization. The characteristics of the 50 meV gap point toward the lifting of mirror-symmetry protection by Sn vacancies and the consequent mass gapping of the Dirac point, although contributions from AFM-induced folding hybridization cannot be entirely ruled out. Our findings provide real-space evidence for strong coupling between localized moments and itinerant topological states, highlighting exfoliable EuSn$_2$As$_2$ as a potential candidate for realizing axion-insulator-based devices.

### [160] [Magnetic self-frustration from spontaneous structural distortion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00339)
*T. Vignau Costa,G. L. Rossini,D. C. Cabra,S. A. Grigera,R. A. Borzi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过经典模型和蒙特卡洛模拟，展示了在kagomé晶格上，最近邻Ising铁磁相互作用与磁弹耦合相结合，可以诱导出一种称为“磁性自挫”（magnetic self-frustration）的磁结构相变，导致呼吸状晶格畸变和残余熵，而非传统的有序基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在受挫磁性（frustrated magnetism）中，磁弹耦合（magnetoelastic coupling）介导的晶格畸变通常被视为摆脱简并（degeneracy）走向有序基态乃至多铁性（multiferroicity）的途径。本文旨在展示相反的现象——磁性自挫，即磁性与晶格自由度相互作用反而阻止了有序化。

Method: 作者构建了一个最小经典模型（minimal classical model），在kagomé晶格上考虑最近邻Ising铁磁相互作用（nearest-neighbor Ising ferromagnetism）和磁弹耦合。采用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行数值研究，并对磁弹耦合常数α做一阶解析分析。

Result: 模拟发现系统发生磁结构相变（magnetostructural transition），进入呼吸状（breathing-like）相，表现为沿三条kagomé方向的不规则键二聚化（bond dimerization）。一个子晶格的等边三角形自发畸变为等腰三角形，其形状对α一阶不敏感，像刚性积木一样决定第二个子晶格的几何构型。磁性部分可映射为有效反铁磁三角晶格（antiferromagnetic triangular lattice），在低温下保持无序，残余熵为Wannier熵的三分之一。该自挫相存在于中等α值区间，分离了弱耦合下的未畸变铁磁相与强耦合下的规则二聚化上-上-下-下反铁磁有序相。

Conclusion: 该模型揭示了磁弹耦合在特定条件下可以产生全新的自挫无序相，而非促进有序，为理解受挫磁性系统中结构与磁性的相互作用提供了新的视角。

Abstract: In frustrated magnetism, lattice distortions mediated by magnetoelastic coupling are commonly invoked as an escape route from extensive degeneracy toward an ordered ground state and, in some cases, the onset of multiferroicity. Here we present a minimal classical model that illustrates the converse phenomenon, which we term ``magnetic self-frustration''. Monte Carlo simulations reveal that a kagomé lattice with trivial magnetic interactions -- namely, nearest-neighbor Ising ferromagnetism -- undergoes a magnetostructural transition into a breathing-like phase, characterized by irregular bond dimerization along the three kagomé directions. Structurally, the equilateral triangles belonging to one of the two kagomé sublattices spontaneously distort, expanding into isosceles triangles. An analysis to first order in the magnetoelastic coupling constant $α$ shows that the shape of these triangles is remarkably robust. Acting like rigid building blocks in a puzzle, their vertices determine the geometry of the second sublattice, giving rise to contracted ferromagnetic triangles with a variety of shapes. The magnetic sector can be mapped onto an effective antiferromagnetic triangular lattice, which remains disordered down to low temperatures and retains a finite residual entropy of one third of that of Wannier. This self-frustrated phase takes place at intermediate values of $α$, separating the conventional undistorted ferromagnetic phase at weak coupling from a strongly coupled ordered phase characterized by a regular dimerized up-up-down-down antiferromagnetic pattern along the three kagomé directions, built from ferromagnetic triangles and hexagons.

### [161] [Surface Reconstruction in Low-Temperature ARPES Spectra of Charge-Ordered EuAl$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00453)
*Hao Liu,Bo Chen,Chen Zhang,Qi-Yi Wu,Sheng-Tao Cui,Zhe Sun,Zhong-Tuo Fu,Ying Zhou,Yang Luo,Jun Liu,Yu-Xia Duan,Jian-Qiao Meng*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用光子能量依赖、温度依赖和劈裂历史依赖的ARPES，结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），将本征体相能带（intrinsic bulk bands）与来自表面的谱权重（surface-derived spectral weight）分离。

Result: 高温劈裂表面上测得的谱（160 K及冷却至10 K）与计算的三维体相电子结构高度吻合；而低温劈裂表面则出现额外的类电子能带、类似费米面复制的轮廓以及几乎与kz无关的表面衍生特征，这些特征在体相计算中不存在，并在升温时被逐渐抑制，而体相衍生能带在CDW转变前后基本不变。

Conclusion: 分析表明，低温重构的谱权重主要来源于热力学上脆弱的表面重构（surface reconstruction），而非本征体相CDW引起的能带折叠。该结果为EuAl₄中的歧义提供了解决，并为区分BaAl₄族关联半金属中的表面重构与体相电荷有序效应提供了光谱判据。

Abstract: Charge ordering in EuAl$_4$ has been widely discussed in connection with band reconstruction, magnetism,and topological electronic states, yet the microscopic origin of the complex low-temperature ARPES spectra remains unresolved. Here we combine photon-energy-, temperature-, and cleavage-history-dependent ARPES with firstprinciples calculations to separate intrinsic bulk bands from surface-derived spectral weight. Spectra measured on high-temperature-cleaved surfaces, both at 160 K and after cooling to 10 K, are well described by the calculated three-dimensional bulk electronic structure, whereas low-temperature-cleaved surfaces exhibit additional electron-like bands, replica-like Fermi-surface contours, and nearly kz-independent surface-derived features that are absent from the bulk calculations. These extra features are progressively suppressed upon warming, whereas the bulk-derived bands remain largely unchanged across the charge-density-wave transition within the experimental resolution. The combined analysis of photon-energy dependence, temperature evolution, and cleavage history identifies the reconstructed low-temperature spectral weight as arising predominantly from a thermally fragile surface reconstruction rather than from intrinsic bulk CDW-induced band folding. These results resolve an important ambiguity in EuAl$_4$ and provide spectroscopic criteria for distinguishing surface reconstruction from bulk charge-order effects in BaAl$_4$-family correlated semimetals.

### [162] [Complexity of tensor network simulation for noisy quantum circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00474)
*Yuguo Shao,Zishuo Zhao,Song Cheng,Zhengwei Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文严格证明了局域噪声（local noise）如何影响基于张量网络（tensor-network）方法的量子动力学经典可模拟性（classical simulability）。通过算子纠缠熵（operator entanglement entropy, OEE），给出了不同噪声模型、电路类型和精度要求下，张量网络所需键维数（bond dimension）的上界与下界，建立了噪声、电路结构与经典可模拟性之间的严格联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对于局域噪声如何影响量子动力学的经典可模拟性缺乏严格的理论保证。本文旨在从数学上回答：在何种噪声模型和电路结构下，张量网络方法能够以多项式资源高效模拟含噪声的量子演化。

Method: 以算子纠缠熵作为核心分析工具，对四种场景进行严格证明：(1) 任意电路上的单比特去极化噪声（single-qubit depolarizing noise）在绝对误差和相对误差下的键维数边界；(2) 一维局域电路中的全轨迹误差有界矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operator, MPO）存在性；(3) 一维砖墙电路（brickwall circuits）中一般单比特噪声下OEE的平台期（plateau）行为与最坏情况分析，涉及随机二设计（random two-design）门与收缩系数（contraction coefficient）c；(4) 高维情形下投影纠缠对算符（projected entangled pair operator, PEPO）的边界键维数均匀有界性。

Result: (1) 任意电路下，固定Hilbert-Schmidt绝对误差时$\order{1}$深度内poly(n)键维数足够，相对误差则限制在$\order{\log n}$深度，且该边界是最优的。(2) 一维局域电路在任意深度下存在poly(n)键维数的全轨迹误差有界MPO。(3) 一维砖墙电路中，随机二设计门在$c<1/3$时以高概率出现$\order{1}$的OEE平台期，任意门在$c<1/48$时最坏情况OEE为$\order{\log n}$。(4) 高维情形下，去极化噪声在绝对或相对精度下，以及一般噪声在强收缩和绝对精度下，PEPO在每个切割处的平均边界键维数均为均匀的poly(n)。

Conclusion: 本文建立了噪声模型、电路类型与经典可模拟性之间的严格对应关系：特定噪声（如去极化噪声）和强收缩性电路中，张量网络方法可在多项式资源内模拟任意深度的量子演化，提供了噪声辅助经典模拟的严格理论基础。

Abstract: We aim to rigorously address how local noise affects classical simulability of quantum dynamics benchmarked by tensor-network methods. Using operator entanglement entropy (OEE), we prove the following: (1) For single-qubit depolarizing noise on arbitrary circuits, tensor networks with $\mathrm{poly}(n)$ bond dimension suffice for fixed absolute Hilbert-Schmidt error after $\order{1}$ depth, while relative error demands $\order{\log n}$ depth; and this bound is optimal. (2) For single-qubit depolarizing noise on 1D local circuits, the existence of whole-trajectory error-bounded matrix product operator (MPO) of $\mathrm{poly}(n)$ bond dimension at all depths. (3) For general single-qubit noise in 1D brickwall circuits, random two-design gates with contraction coefficient $c<1/3$ yield an $\order{1}$ OEE plateau with probability $1-Te^{-Ω(n)}$, while arbitrary gates with $c<1/48$ give $\order{\log n}$ OEE in the worst case. (4) In higher dimensions, these bounds yield uniform-in-depth $\mathrm{poly}(n)$ average boundary-bond dimensions for projected entangled pair operators~(PEPO) across every cut -- under depolarizing noise at either absolute or relative accuracy, and under general noise with strong contraction at absolute accuracy. Our results establish a rigorous connection between certain noise models, circuit types, and their classical simulability.

</details>


### [163] [Supersymmetric quantum criticality with discrete symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00657)
*Teng-Yue Wang,Shuai Yin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，证明在(2+1)维Gross-Neveu-Yukawa理论中，当离散$Z_n$各向异性阶数$n>3$时，体系可涌现出$\mathcal{N}=2$ Wess-Zumino超对称临界点，并在有序相中发现由危险无关各向异性导致的第二特征长度尺度$\xi'$，验证了标度关系$\nu'/\nu= 1+|y_n|/p$（$p=2$）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称性（supersymmetry）在凝聚态体系的量子临界点处可能涌现，但现有理论多关注连续对称性模型，而实际材料受限于微观离散对称性（discrete symmetry）。因此，有必要研究离散各向异性对涌现超对称性的影响。

Method: 采用泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，分析(2+1)维Gross-Neveu-Yukawa理论中耦合Dirac费米子（Dirac fermion）与具有$Z_n$离散各向异性的复序参量（complex order parameter）的系统。

Result: 对于$n>3$，各向异性扰动在不动点处为无关（irrelevant）算符，体系呈现$\mathcal{N}=2$ Wess-Zumino超对称临界点。在有序相中，危险无关（dangerously irrelevant）各向异性产生第二特征长度尺度$\xi'$。对$Z_4$、$Z_5$和$Z_6$模型，标度关系$\nu'/\nu= 1+|y_n|/p$（$p=2$）成立。

Conclusion: 离散$Z_n$各向异性不会破坏$n>3$时超对称临界点的涌现，且危险无关各向异性导致的多尺度行为可由普适的标度关系描述，为在具有离散对称性的真实材料中观测涌现超对称性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Supersymmetry, originally proposed in high-energy physics, can emerge as a remarkable low-energy structure in condensed matter systems. While emergent supersymmetry at quantum critical points is widely discussed in models with continuous symmetries, real materials are constrained by microscopic discrete symmetries. To address this, we investigate (2+1)-dimensional Gross-Neveu-Yukawa theories coupling Dirac fermions to a complex order parameter with discrete $Z_n$ anisotropy. Using the functional renormalization group, we find that for $n>3$, the anisotropic perturbations are irrelevant at the fixed point, yielding a $\mathcal{N}=2$ Wess-Zumino supersymmetric critical point. In the ordered phase, this dangerously irrelevant anisotropy gives rise to a second characteristic length scale, $ξ'$, alongside the usual correlation length, $ξ$. By tracking mass thresholds along symmetry-broken renormalization group trajectories, we extract the exponents $ν'$ and $ν$ without imposing prior scaling assumptions. For the $Z_4$, $Z_5$, and $Z_6$ models, our results support the scaling relation $ν'/ν= 1+|y_n|/p$ with $p=2$ in the isotropic framework used here.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于具有DM相互作用（Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction）的海森堡模型（Heisenberg model），在保持六方对称性（hexagonal symmetry）的周期性变形Kagome晶格（deformed Kagome lattice）上进行分析，晶胞（unit cell）被扩大，从而获得更复杂的能带结构。

Result: 反铁磁（anti-ferromagnetic）耦合情形下，经典基态（classical ground state）中存在自旋空间对称性（spin-space symmetry），导致拓扑平庸态（topologically trivial states）；铁磁（ferromagnetic）情形下该对称性被经典基态自发破缺，能带展现出丰富拓扑特征，包括多次拓扑相变（topological transitions）以及陈数范围从+2到-2的能带。

Conclusion: 变形磁体（deformed magnets）能够承载新奇且丰富的拓扑物理现象，其拓扑结构比未变形情形更为多样。

Abstract: We study the band structure and topology of magnons for a Heisenberg model with DM interaction on a deformed Kagome lattice. For simplicity, we focus on a periodically deformed lattice with hexagonal symmetry and an enlarged unit cell. This enlarged unit cell gives rise to a richer band structure than in the undeformed case. Analyzing band topology, there is a distinction between the topologically trivial case with anti-ferromagnetic coupling and the topologically rich case with ferromagnetic coupling. In the anti-ferromagnetic case, a spin-space symmetry, also present in the classical ground state, enforces these topologically trivial states. In the ferromagnetic case, this symmetry is spontaneously broken by the classical ground state. Consequently, the band structure also hosts rich topological features. Specifically, we observe many topological transitions and bands with Chern numbers ranging from $+2$ to $-2$, which makes the system richer than in the undeformed case. This emergent rich topological structure demonstrates that deformed magnets can host new and exciting physics.

</details>


### [165] [Low-Temperature Suppression of Intertwined Orders in La$_{1/3}$Sr$_{2/3}$FeO$_{3}$ Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00769)
*Mayia A. Conclusion: 研究提出，该有序态抑制的可能原因是薄膜中畴的降维效应（reduced dimensionality）。该发现为理解强关联材料（strongly correlated materials）中竞争相互作用（competing interactions）的影响，特别是具有耦合序的系统，提供了新的见解。

Abstract: The strong coupling between spin, charge, and lattice degrees of freedom in perovskite oxides leads to an array of exotic phenomena, giving these materials rich phase diagrams that can include coupled orders. This is exemplified by the A-site doped ferrite La$_{1/3}$Sr$_{2/3}$FeO$_{3}$ (LSFO), which exhibits a coupled paramagnetic-antiferromagnetic and charge ordering phase transition at $\sim$190 K that has been well studied in thin films, bulk, and polycrystalline samples. However, the low temperature behavior of LSFO thin films below $\sim$100 K has not been thoroughly explored. This work uses several X-ray scattering and spectroscopy techniques to directly probe LSFO's magnetic and charge order down to low temperature. Using resonant X-ray scattering, we observe a complete suppression of LSFO's known antiferromagnetic and charge order below $\sim$25 K. Further spectroscopy and coherent scattering measurements provide insight into LSFO's electronic structure and domain dynamics in this new low temperature phase, and we propose possible explanations for the observed order suppression based on reduced dimensionality of domains in our thin films. Our findings provide insight into the effects of competing interactions in strongly correlated materials, particularly those with coupled orders.

### [166] [Locality-Induced Hierarchical Backflow Wavefunctions for Correlated Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00924)
*Yu-Tong Zhou,Zheng-Wei Zhou,Wen-Yuan Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出层级反流（hierarchical backflow, HB）波函数族，利用局域性（locality）作为自然原则对反流波函数进行层级化组织。HB波函数通过路径深度 $K$ 系统性地提升表达能力，在半填充和空穴掺杂条件下均展现出高能量精度和可扩展性，并能自然地实现局域-非局域分解，架起通往神经量子态（neural quantum states）的桥梁，为关联费米子系统的大规模可解释模拟提供了新框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反流（backflow）波函数在描述关联费米子系统中具有重要作用，但其组织结构缺乏清晰的层级化原则，限制了其表达能力的系统提升和大规模应用。局域性（locality）作为物理系统中的自然属性，尚未被用于系统性地组织反流波函数。

Method: 提出层级反流（hierarchical backflow, HB）波函数族，通过路径深度 $K$ 参数控制反流关联的范围，从而系统性地提升波函数的表达能力。HB波函数还支持局域-非局域分解（local-nonlocal decomposition），连接神经量子态（neural quantum states），同时保持紧凑表示和高效优化。

Result: 在半填充（half-filling）条件下，$K=1$ 的HB波函数已在 $4\times4$ 到 $10\times10$ 的系统尺寸上达到约 $0.5\%$ 的能量精度。在空穴掺杂（hole doping）$n_h=0.125$ 时，该方法高效扩展至 $12\times16$ 和 $16\times16$ 系统；随着 $K$ 增加，能量精度系统性地提升，并呈现出清晰的条带相（stripe phase）。

Conclusion: 局域性是反流波函数的自然组织原则，HB波函数为大规模关联费米子系统模拟提供了具有系统可改进性（systematic improvability）和可解释性（interpretability）的新框架。

Abstract: We show that locality provides a natural principle to hierarchically organize backflow wavefunctions. This leads us to propose a family of variational fermionic states, termed hierarchical backflow (HB) wavefunctions. The expressive power of HB is systematically improvable, controlled by a path depth $K$ which reflects the range of backflow correlations. At half-filling, the HB with $K=1$ already achieves high energy precision, with an accuracy around $0.5\%$ for system sizes from $4\times 4$ to $10\times 10$. At hole doping $n_h=0.125$, the method scales efficiently to $12\times16$ and $16\times16$ systems, and the energy systematically achieves higher accuracy with $K$ increasing, yielding a clear stripe phase. The HB further enables a local-nonlocal decomposition, naturally bridging to neural quantum states, while featuring compact representations and efficient optimization. Our work reveals locality as a natural organizing principle of backflow wavefunctions, opening a new framework with systematic improvability and interpretability for large-scale simulations of correlated fermion systems.

### [168] [Microscopic Theory of the Phonon Thermal Hall Effect in Chiral Mott Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01876)
*Junha Kang,Taekoo Oh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在赝自旋莫特绝缘体（chiral Mott insulators）中建立了声子热霍尔效应（phonon thermal Hall effect, PTHE）的微观理论，推导了有效拉曼相互作用（effective Raman interaction）的精确解析形式，揭示了其强度正比于标量自旋手征性（scalar spin chirality），并在kagome晶格上明确展示了本征PTHE。该理论揭示了同位素替换下输运行为随温度变化的交叉行为，并建立了定量分离声子贡献与背景信号的比例定律（scaling law），为隔离微观热载流子提供了实验标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热霍尔效应（thermal Hall effect, THE）可以探测绝缘体中的电中性激发，而声子已被发现能在量级上与自旋贡献相当的大热霍尔效应，这表明声子在热输运中扮演关键角色。然而，目前尚缺乏对声子热霍尔效应的完全微观理论推导，尤其是在赝自旋莫特绝缘体这类体系中。

Method: 首先推导了半满莫特绝缘体中有效拉曼相互作用的精确解析形式，证明其强度直接正比于标量自旋手征性；随后在kagome晶格上显式展示了本征声子热霍尔效应（intrinsic PTHE）。

Result: 发现同位素替换下输运行为存在随温度变化的交叉（temperature-dependent crossover）；基于此建立了可将声子对热霍尔效应的贡献与其他背景信号进行定量分离的比例定律（scaling law）。

Conclusion: 该工作首次提供了声子热霍尔效应的完全微观推导，并为在赝自旋莫特绝缘体中隔离微观热载流子确立了明确的实验标准。

Abstract: The thermal Hall effect (THE) probes charge-neutral excitations in insulators, where the charge gap blocks electronic transport. Recently, phonons have been shown to induce a THE comparable in magnitude to the spin contribution, underscoring their critical role in thermal transport. Here, we develop a microscopic theory of the phonon thermal Hall effect (PTHE) in chiral Mott insulators. First, we derive the exact analytic form of the effective Raman interaction in half-filled Mott insulators, showing that its strength is directly proportional to the scalar spin chirality. Next, we demonstrate the intrinsic PTHE explicitly on the kagome lattice. Crucially, our formulation reveals a temperature-dependent crossover in the transport behavior under isotopic substitution. Using this result, we establish a scaling law that quantitatively separates the phonon contribution to the THE from other background signals. Our results not only provide the first fully microscopic derivation of the PTHE, but also establish a definitive experimental standard for isolating microscopic heat carriers in chiral Mott insulators.

### [169] [Spin Dynamics from Niu-Kleinman Adiabatic Approach and Slave Boson Mean Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01984)
*Xuan Yang,Tianyang Xie,Shaohang Shi,Kun Jiang,Jiangping Hu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文结合Niu-Kleinman形式与Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子理论发展了一套自旋动力学的绝热理论，在线性化运动方程中提取贝里曲率矩阵和能量海森矩阵，计算自旋波激发。在单轨道哈伯德模型和La2NiO4双轨道模型上验证表明，该方法在保持计算效率的同时，相比传统弱耦合方法大幅提升了与基准结果的吻合度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋波激发是研究强关联材料中磁序和电子关联的核心探针，但传统弱耦合方法（如随机相位近似，RPA）在强关联体系中精度不足，而精确方法（如行列式量子蒙特卡洛）计算成本高昂。因此，需要一种既能有效纳入强关联效应、又保持计算效率的实用框架。

Method: 将Niu-Kleinman形式与Kotliar-Ruckenstein奴隶玻色子理论（NK+KRSB）相结合，构建自旋动力学的绝热理论（adiabatic theory）。对于每个冻结的自旋构型，自洽求解约束奴隶玻色子鞍点，从而直接提取线性化绝热运动方程中的贝里曲率矩阵（Berry-curvature matrix）和能量海森矩阵（energy Hessian）。

Result: 在半满单轨道哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）上，所得自旋波色散与行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）基准相比，显著优于随机相位近似（random phase approximation），并接近含时古茨威勒近似（time-dependent Gutzwiller approximation）的结果。进一步在La2NiO4双轨道模型中验证了方法对真实多轨道强关联体系的适用性。

Conclusion: 该方法仅需磁基态附近的鞍点解，计算高效且纳入超越传统弱耦合描述的强关联效应，为研究关联量子材料中的低能自旋激发提供了一种实用框架。

Abstract: Spin-wave excitations provide a central probe of magnetic order and electronic correlations in strongly correlated materials. In this work, we develop an adiabatic theory of spin dynamics by combining the Niu-Kleinman formalism with Kotliar-Ruckenstein slave-boson theory (NK+KRSB). For each frozen spin configuration, the constrained slave-boson saddle point is solved self-consistently, allowing the Berry-curvature matrix and energy Hessian entering the linearized adiabatic equations of motion to be extracted directly. Applied to the half-filled single-orbital Hubbard model, the resulting spin-wave dispersion shows substantially improved agreement with determinant quantum Monte Carlo benchmarks compared with the random phase approximation and closely approaches results from the time-dependent Gutzwiller approximation. We further extend the method to a two-orbital model of $\mathrm{La}_2\mathrm{NiO}_4$, demonstrating its applicability to realistic multi-orbital correlated systems. Because the approach only requires saddle-point solutions near the magnetic ground state, it remains computationally efficient while incorporating strong-correlation effects beyond conventional weak-coupling descriptions, providing a practical framework for studying low-energy spin excitations in correlated quantum materials.

### [170] [Decomposition of Anomalous Diffusion in two-state random walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00149)
*Abhijit Bera,Kevin. E. Bassler*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种两态随机游走（TSRW）模型，该模型在连续时间随机游走（CTRW）的静止态与标准莱维游走（LW）的运动态之间切换，并展示了约瑟夫效应、诺亚效应和摩西效应的共存现象，揭示了随机切换如何重塑反常扩散（anomalous diffusion）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂系统中广泛存在着两态随机模型（two-state stochastic models），其中运动在两种不同的动力学模式之间交替。当前研究旨在理解这种随机切换如何影响反常扩散行为，特别是多重重尾效应（heavy-tailed effects）的共存机制。

Method: 采用反常扩散分解（anomalous diffusion decomposition）方法，分析TSRW在CTRW静止态与LW运动态之间以幂律分布（power-law）驻留时间进行切换的动力学行为。

Result: TSRW表现出约瑟夫效应（Joseph effect，相关性效应）、诺亚效应（Noah effect，重尾增量效应）和摩西效应（Moses effect，老化效应）的共存。尽管经典莱维游走仅具有约瑟夫效应，但由于与CTRW态的随机切换，诺亚效应和摩西效应在TSRW中同时显现。

Conclusion: 动力学位态之间的耦合能够从根本上重塑驱动反常扩散的机制。该模型为异质性和间歇性切换环境中的输运行为提供了一个简约而强大的理论框架。

Abstract: Two-state stochastic models, where motion alternates between distinct dynamical modes, are widely observed in complex systems. Here we study the Two-State Random Walk (TSRW), which switches between a continuous-time random walk (CTRW) rest state and a standard L'evy walk (LW) motion state, each with power-law distributed sojourn times. Using anomalous diffusion decomposition, we show that TSRWs exhibit a generic coexistence of Joseph (correlation), Noah (heavy-tailed increments), and Moses (aging) effects. Strikingly, although classical L'evy walks alone possess only the Joseph effect, both Noah and Moses effects emerge in TSRWs solely due to stochastic switching with the CTRW phase. Our results demonstrate that coupling between dynamical states can fundamentally reshape the mechanisms driving anomalous diffusion, offering a minimal yet powerful framework for transport in heterogeneous and intermittently switching environments.

### [171] [Ferrofluids: Modeling and Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01392)

Conclusion: 该工作为铁磁流体模型提供了从热力学原理到数值求解的完整框架，所提格式具有理论收敛保证与数值可行性。

Abstract: Starting from Maxwell's and linear momentum balance equations, we derive a ferrofluid model using the generalized Onsager's principle. ### [172] [Explaining the $B \to Kμ^+μ^-$ Anomaly in the Left-Right Inverse Seesaw Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00513)
*David Delepine,Shaaban Khalil*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 基于左右反跷跷板（Left-Right Inverse Seesaw, LRIS）模型，通过带电标量/重中微子箱图（box diagram）的非退耦（non-decoupling）机制，成功解释了稀有衰变 B→Kll 中矢量 Wilson 系数ΔC₉≈-1而轴矢系数ΔC₁₀≈0的长期反常，且满足所有味物理与对撞机约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀有衰变 B→Kll 的实验和全局分析显示矢量 Wilson 系数 ΔC₉ 存在显著的负偏移，而轴矢系数 ΔC₁₀ 保持为零，这一反常模式长期未获满意解释。论文旨在 LRIS 模型框架内为该反常提供自然且自洽的理论机制。

Method: 在 LRIS 模型中引入带电标量（charged scalar）与重右手中微子（heavy right-handed neutrino）的箱图贡献，利用右手耦合在重中微子极限下的非退耦效应产生 ΔC₉ 的未压低贡献，同时左手 Dirac Yukawa 耦合自动导致 ΔC₁₀≈0 的抵消；通过右手夸克混合矩阵中的 GIM 类相位结构压低 Bₛ–\bar{B}ₛ 混合的大贡献。

Result: 数值参数空间扫描识别出与所有当前味物理（含 b→sγ，安全余量约两个数量级）及对撞机约束一致的可行区域。该区域同时产生 ΔC₉≈-1 和 ΔC₁₀≈0 的反常模式。

Conclusion: LRIS 模型能够自然地解释 B→Kll 反常，并为 LHC 及未来高亮度实验提供了针对带电标量和重右手中微子的关联搜寻目标。

Abstract: We investigate the long-standing anomaly in the rare decay B into Kll within the Left-Right Inverse Seesaw (LRIS) model. Global analyses of the B into s mu mu data consistently indicate a significant negative shift in the vector Wilson coefficient, $ΔC{9} \approx -1$, while the axial coefficient $ΔC{10}$ remains consistent with zero. We show that a charged-scalar/heavy-neutrino box diagram in the LRIS model naturally generates this pattern through a \emph{non-decoupling} mechanism: the right-handed coupling
  produces a contribution to $ΔC{9}$ that is unsuppressed in the heavy-neutrino limit, while the simultaneous presence of a comparable left-handed Dirac Yukawa coupling ensures the automatic cancellation $ΔC{10} \approx 0$. The otherwise large contribution to $B_s$--$\bar{B}_s$ mixing is suppressed by several orders of magnitude through a GIM-like phase structure in the right-handed quark mixing matrix. A numerical scan over the model parameter space identifies a viable region, consistent with all current flavor and collider constraints. The $b \to sγ$ constraint is satisfied with two orders of magnitude to spare throughout the viable band. These results motivate correlated searches for the charged scalar and the heavy right-handed neutrinos at the LHC and future high-luminosity experiments.

</details>

This BSM scenario is used as an illustrative example of the potential of using only low-level calorimeter information enhanced by advanced Deep Learning (DL) methodologies in searching for this channel, which can achieve a statistical significance of approximately $4.5σ$, for an integrated luminosity of 300 fb$^{-1}$ at the CERN machine.

Notably, the $D_{s1}\bar D_{s2}^*$ state with $J^{PC}=2^{+-}$ possesses exotic spin-parity quantum numbers forbidden for conventional mesons, providing a clean experimental signature for exotic hadrons. Moreover, the $D_{s2}^*\bar D_{s2}^*$ state with $J^{PC}=4^{++}$ is a rare high-spin hadronic molecule. We then extend the same framework to discuss the binding properties of the $T_s T_s$ systems and construct the mass spectrum of corresponding doubly-charm doubly-strangeness molecular tetraquarks. The promising candidates are $D_{s1}D_{s1}$ ($J^P=2^+$), $D_{s1}D_{s2}^*$ ($J^P=3^+$), and $D_{s2}^*D_{s2}^*$ ($J^P=4^+$), all of which are absolutely flavor-exotic. ### [178] [Semi-analytical two-loop QCD corrections to $e^+e^-\to J/ψ+χ_{cJ}$ at B factories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02182)
*Hao-Yang Liu,Cong Li,Wen-Long Sang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在非相对论量子色动力学（NRQCD）因子化框架下，计算了B工厂中$e^+e^-\to J/ψ+χ_{cJ}$过程的NNLO QCD修正，通过渐近展开方法获得了高精度的螺旋度振幅，并给出了非极化截面和角分布参数的预言。结果表明$χ_{c0}$的NNLO结果与Belle和BaBar实验数据在$2σ$内一致，而角分布参数$α^0_θ$与Belle测量存在明显偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算B工厂中双粲偶素产生过程$e^+e^-\to J/ψ+χ_{cJ}$的高阶QCD修正，以检验NRQCD因子化框架的有效性，并解释与实验数据之间可能存在的偏差。

Method: 在NRQCD因子化框架内，计算该过程的NNLO QCD修正；利用围绕$r=0$和$r=1$（其中$r=16m_c^2/s$）的渐近展开（asymptotic expansions）获得螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）。

Result: 渐近展开结果在整个$0\le r\le 1$范围内与精确数值结果高度一致，相对误差低于$10^{-5}$；大对数项（large logarithmic terms）被解析获得。$χ_{c0}$的$\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$修正达LO截面的33%，显著降低了标度不确定性；$χ_{c1}$和$χ_{c2}$的$\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$修正分别为-15%和-38%。$χ_{c0}$的NNLO预言与Belle测量一致，且在$2σ$内与BaBar数据符合；角分布参数$α^0_θ$的理论值与Belle测量存在显著差异。

Conclusion: NNLO QCD修正对双粲偶素产生过程至关重要，尤其是$χ_{c2}$中高阶修正间的大幅抵消将NNLO截面拉回接近LO预言。$α^0_θ$的理论与实验偏差需要进一步研究，而对$χ_{c1}$和$χ_{c2}$角分布参数的未来测量将提供对理论框架的重要检验。

Abstract: In this work, we compute the next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) QCD corrections to the process $e^+e^-\to J/ψ+χ_{cJ}$ at B factories within the NRQCD factorization framework. The helicity amplitudes are obtained via asymptotic expansions around $r=0$ and $r=1$, with $r=16m_c^2/s$. Our asymptotic expressions reproduce the exact numerical results with high accuracy across the entire range $0\le r \le 1$, achieving a relative error below $10^{-5}$, which is sufficient for phenomenological applications. Notably, the large logarithmic terms are obtained analytically. We compute the unpolarized cross sections. The $\mathcal{O}(α_s)$ correction is found to be large, while the $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$ correction for $χ_{c0}$ production amounts to $33\%$ of the leading-order (LO) cross section, significantly reducing the scale uncertainties. For $χ_{c1}$, the $\mathcal{O}(α_s)$ and $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$ corrections correspond to $35\%$ and $-15\%$, respectively. For $χ_{c2}$, the corresponding corrections are $25\%$ and $-38\%$. The large cancellation between the corrections for $χ_{c2}$ brings the NNLO cross section close to the LO prediction. Our prediction for $χ_{c0}$ is consistent with the {\tt Belle} measurement and agrees with the {\tt BaBar} data within $2σ$. We also predict the angular distribution parameters $α^J_θ$, which are independent of nonperturbative inputs. A sharp discrepancy between the theory and the {\tt Belle} measurement is observed for $α^0_θ$, calling for further experimental and theoretical investigations. Moreover, future measurements of the angular distribution parameters for $χ_{c1}$ and $χ_{c2}$ will provide important tests of the theoretical framework.

### [179] [Comment on "QCD-factorization amplitudes from flavour symmetries: beyond the $SU(3)$ symmetric case''](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02538)
*Bhubanjyoti Bhattacharya,David London*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文对 arXiv:2604.19612 中声称 EWP-树关系（EWP-tree relations, ETRs）无效的观点提出反驳，指出 ETRs 在 SU(3) 味对称性未破缺且忽略弱有效哈密顿量中微小 Wilson 系数 c_{7,8} 的条件下是群论上严格的数学结果，并非依赖于强子计算，并指出了该论文形式体系中的若干缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两篇论文对 B→PP 衰变（P∈{π,K,η,η'}）的拟合结果存在矛盾：arXiv:2604.19612 采用拓扑图与 QCD 因子化（QCD factorization）结合的方法获得了良好拟合，而另一篇基于 SU(3) 味对称性的拟合结果却很差。本文旨在澄清这一分歧的根源——即 EWP-树关系（ETRs）的有效性问题，并驳斥该论文关于 ETRs 无效的论断。

Method: 本文采用群论（group theory）论证方法，从数学严格性出发证明 ETRs 的正确性。核心逻辑链为：若 SU(3) 味对称性未破缺，且弱有效哈密顿量中微小的 Wilson 系数 c_{7,8} 可忽略，则 ETRs 自动成立且精确成立。该方法不依赖任何强子计算（hadronic calculations），完全基于群论推导。

Result: 本文论证了 ETRs 是群论上严格的数学结果，而非依赖于强子模型的近似关系。此外，指出了 arXiv:2604.19612 所采用形式体系中的若干薄弱环节（weaknesses）。通过澄清 ETRs 的有效性，解释了为何先前基于 SU(3) 对称性并应用 ETRs 的拟合结果是可靠的，而对方论文声称 ETRs 无效从而导致拟合方法不可靠的断言是错误的。

Conclusion: ETRs 在 SU(3) 对称性成立且忽略小 Wilson 系数 c_{7,8} 的极限下是群论上精确成立的关系，并非无效近似。因此，使用 ETRs 的分析方法具有可靠性，arXiv:2604.19612 对其有效性的否定是不正确的。

Abstract: Recently, a fit to $B \to PP$ decays ($P \in \{π, K, η, η'\}$) was performed (arXiv:2604.19612, "QCD-factorization amplitudes from flavour symmetries: beyond the $SU(3)$ symmetric case''}) using a formalism that combines topological diagrams with QCD factorization, and a good fit was found. We also recently performed such a fit, under the assumption that the $B \to PP$ amplitudes are related by flavour SU(3) symmetry, but we found a very poor fit. The two results therefore disagree with one another. The source of this disagreement is that we applied EWP-tree relations (ETRs). These were derived $\sim 30$ years ago, and relate different topological diagrams or reduced matrix elements, thus reducing the number of unknown parameters in the fit. In their paper, it is asserted that ETRs are invalid, so that analyses that use them are unreliable. We are writing this Comment to explain why this assertion is incorrect. The key point is that ETRs are mathematically rigorous, group theoretically. If SU(3) is unbroken, and the small Wilson coefficients $c_{7,8}$ in the weak effective Hamiltonian are neglected, ETRs follow automatically and are exact. That is, this is a group theory result -- no hadronic calculations are involved. In this Comment, we also point out several weaknesses of their formalism.

</details>


### [180] [New Windows on Heavy Dark Matter: Mineral Melt Modelling and X-Ray Readout for Muscovite Mica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02579)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 白云母作为古探测器为探测重复合暗物质提供了可行且灵敏的新途径；新开发的快速X射线荧光成像和热尖峰建模方法可有效识别和校准亚微米损伤特征；以往蚀刻云母的暗物质排除约束存在方法论缺陷，需要重新评估其可靠性。

Abstract: Muscovite mica is a translucent, layered silicate mineral whose basal cleavage, low radiogenic background, gigayear exposures, and demonstrated track retention over geological timescales make it a compelling target for rare particle searches. In this work, we develop a new framework for detecting heavy composite dark matter using muscovite mica as a paleodetector. We model melt track formation by heavy composite dark matter transiting through mica using a Sedov-Taylor thermal spike formalism, and validate the sub-micron regime with SRIM/TRIM simulations of nuclear recoil cascades, which also calibrate the phonon efficiency governing local energy deposition. We demonstrate a novel readout method using rapid X-ray fluorescence mapping with a copper backing contrast technique, capable of identifying micron-scale damage features in cleaved mica sheets over macroscopic scan areas, and calibrate the minimum detectable track size using laser-ablated defect regions. We present projected sensitivities for opaque and diffuse composite dark matter, including a sub-melt hole-channel detection mode for large composites substantially attenuated by overburden. We also revisit prior dark matter exclusions from etched mica searches, identifying shortcomings that compromise the robustness of these constraints.

### [181] [Matter-Wave Interferometers as Open-System Dark Matter Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00237)
*Leonardo Badurina,Kathryn M. Zurek*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Schwinger-Keldysh形式论构建了物质波干涉仪（matter-wave interferometer, MWI）的开路有效场论（open effective field theory），用以描述暗物质（dark matter, DM）散射引起的退相干（decoherence）与相位（phase）效应，揭示了两种探测通道之间的结构不对称性，并涵盖了从马尔可夫（Markovian）到非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）的动力学范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物质波干涉仪提供了一条独特的量子途径来探测暗物质（dark matter, DM），即使在能量沉积或可分辨反冲可忽略的条件下，暗物质也能通过分离波包间的相位（phase）和退相干（decoherence）显现自身。现有理论框架在描述这些量子效应时仍不完善，需要建立统一的场论描述。

Method: 采用Schwinger-Keldysh形式论（Schwinger-Keldysh formalism）构建物质波干涉仪的开路有效场论（open effective field theory），在其中统一处理暗物质弹性散射导致的相位和退相干效应，并保留暗物质相干时间（coherence time）以跨越马尔可夫（Markovian）与非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）动力学。

Result: 弹性自旋无关暗物质散射（elastic spin-independent DM scattering）中，退相干通道呈现出新颖的玻色增强（Bose enhancement）或泡利阻塞（Pauli blocking）因子，而相位通道最多与暗物质占据数（occupation number）呈线性关系。该框架系统地组织了对重探针极限（heavy-probe limit）之外的修正。

Conclusion: 该有效场论框架揭示了相位与退相干两种探测通道之间存在结构不对称性（structural asymmetry），并能够描述从马尔可夫到非马尔可夫的大范围暗物质质量尺度下的动力学行为，为重探针极限以外的暗物质探测提供了系统化的理论工具。

Abstract: Matter-wave interferometers (MWIs) offer a uniquely quantum route to dark matter (DM) detection: DM can reveal itself through phase and decoherence between spatially separated wavepackets, even when negligible energy deposition or resolvable recoil occurs. We formulate these effects in an open effective field theory for MWIs using the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, which highlights a structural asymmetry between the two detection channels. For elastic spin-independent DM scattering, decoherence inherits novel Bose enhancement or Pauli blocking factors, while the phase is at most linear in the DM occupation number. By retaining the DM's coherence time, this framework spans Markovian and non-Markovian dynamics across a wide range of DM masses, and systematically organizes corrections beyond the heavy-probe limit.

</details>

Method: 聚焦于包含未观测的半硬胶子的主导半包容道（semi-inclusive channel），对横向能量-能量关联子（transverse energy-energy correlator）可观测量中的软胶子辐射进行全阶重求和（all-order resummation），同时考虑初态和末态辐射效应，并分析重夸克对产生及喷注轴定义的影响。

Abstract: We calculate the azimuthal angular decorrelation of diffractive dijets in ultra-peripheral heavy-ion, $ep$, and $eA$ collisions to probe non-perturbative diffractive transverse momentum-dependent distributions. Focusing on the dominant semi-inclusive channel with an unobserved semi-hard gluon, we perform an all-order resummation of soft gluon emissions for the transverse energy-energy correlator observable, accounting for both initial and final state radiation. We also analyze heavy-quark pair production and demonstrate the sensitivity of the decorrelation to the jet axis definition. Finally, we provide numerical predictions for relevant kinematics at LHC UPCs, HERA, and the future EIC. ### [184] [On the spanning cuts consistency problem in the IBP reductions of Feynman integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02485)
*Zihao Wu,Yingxuan Xu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文揭示了跨切割IBP约化中的“一致性问题”机制，指出切割下隐藏项的费曼规则参数被忽略导致IBP关系被违反，而切割引入的缩并奇点（pinch singularities）使这些隐藏项变为有限，从而产生误差。文章还提供了发现线性隐藏关系的算法与实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 跨切割方法（spanning cuts method）能有效降低计算费曼积分（Feynman integrals）时IBP约化的复杂度，但其应用受限于所谓的一致性问题（consistency problem）：不同切割之间的IBP约化系数为何会相互不一致，此前原因不明。

Method: 通过分析切割下IBP关系中被忽略的隐藏项（hidden terms）与费曼规则参数（Feynman prescription parameters）的相互作用，揭示不一致性的机制，并设计算法来发现传播子之间的线性隐藏关系（linear hidden relations）。

Result: 发现切割引入的缩并奇点（pinch singularities）会抵消隐藏项中“消失”的费曼规则参数，使本应可忽略的隐藏项变为有限大小，从而造成误差；同时指出切割下的缩并奇点与传播子之间的隐藏关系相关。

Conclusion: 提供了解决跨切割IBP约化一致性问题的理论基础，并给出了检测隐藏关系的算法与实现，有助于扩大跨切割方法在费曼积分计算中的适用范围。

Abstract: The spanning cuts method is a powerful approach to reduce the cost of IBP reduction while computing Feynman integrals. However, its usage is limited due to the so-called consistency problem. It was unclear why the IBP reduction coefficients can be inconsistent with each other between different cuts. In this paper, we report a mechanism behind this inconsistency. We found that the IBP relations can be violated under the cuts, if we blindly erase the hidden terms that are proportional to the ``vanishing'' Feynman prescription parameters in the relations. In some cases, the cut introduces pinch singularities, which cancel the vanishing Feynman prescription parameters, making the hidden terms finite. In various cases, the error comes from omitting such finite hidden terms. We also claimed that the pinch singularity under the cuts are related to some hidden relations between the propagators. In this paper, we provide an algorithm and its implementation to find the linear hidden relations.

</details>

### [185] [Creating and Probing Spin-Squeezed States of Molecules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02500)
*Connor M. Holland,Callum L. Welsh,Yukai Lu,David Wellnitz,Xing-Yan Chen,Ana Maria Rey,Lawrence W. Cheuk*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在极性CaF分子的光镊阵列中实验实现了自旋压缩态（spin-squeezed states），获得了最高3.0 dB的计量增益，并展示了该纠缠态在均匀和空间变化场中的灵敏度增强、非经典关联特性以及长达100 ms的存储寿命，确立了分子光镊阵列作为可扩展量子增强传感平台的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性分子（polar molecules）因其强长程偶极相互作用（dipolar interactions）和对电磁场及超出标准模型（Standard Model）物理的广泛敏感性，是量子增强传感（quantum-enhanced sensing）和基础物理精密检验的理想平台；然而，在分子体系中产生具有计量学价值的纠缠态此前尚未实现。

Method: 将自旋自由度编码在由偶极交换相互作用（dipolar exchange interactions）直接耦合的转动能级（rotational levels）中，利用动态去耦方案（dynamical decoupling schemes）和Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）操控相互作用哈密顿量，并在具有位点和自旋分辨测量能力的CaF分子光镊阵列中实现与表征自旋压缩态。

Result: 观测到来自直接交换相互作用的计量增益最高达3.0(3) dB（测量校正后），并成功将自旋压缩态转移至长寿命、非相互作用的超精细态（hyperfine states）中，计量增强可持续长达100 ms；实验还观测到双粒子纠缠与爱因斯坦-波多尔斯基-罗森（Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen, EPR）导引等强非经典关联。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在分子体系中实现具有计量学价值的纠缠态，表明分子光镊阵列是可扩展的分子纠缠态产生、控制、表征与存储平台，为量子增强传感和基础物理精密检验开辟了新的可能性。

Abstract: Polar molecules are a promising platform for quantum-enhanced sensing and precision tests of fundamental physics, owing to their strong long-range dipolar interactions, broad sensitivity to electromagnetic fields, and sensitivity to potential physics beyond the Standard Model. However, the creation of metrologically useful entangled states in molecular systems has remained elusive. Here, we report the first observation of a class of metrologically useful entangled states - spin-squeezed states - in polar CaF molecules trapped in an optical tweezer array. The spin degree of freedom is encoded in rotational levels which are directly coupled by dipolar exchange interactions. By harnessing appropriate dynamical decoupling schemes we observe up to 3.0(3)dB of metrological gain, (2.2(3)dB without measurement correction) from direct exchange interactions. Using Floquet engineering, we further realize richer Hamiltonians that preserve spin squeezing while enabling the development of longer-range quantum correlations. Using site- and spin-resolved measurements we demonstrate that these entangled states enhance sensitivity to both homogeneous and spatially varying fields, and reveal strong non-classical correlations, including bipartite entanglement and Einstein-Podolsky-Rosen steering. Finally, we transfer the spin-squeezed states into long-lived and non-interacting hyperfine states, where the metrological enhancement persists for up to 100ms. Our results establish molecular optical tweezer arrays as a scalable platform for generating, controlling, characterizing, and storing entangled states of molecules, opening new opportunities for quantum-enhanced sensing and precision tests of fundamental physics.

</details>


### [186] [A Mid-Infrared Platform Based on Strontium Tweezer Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02560)
*Aaron Holman,Ximo Sun,Bojeong Seo,Joshua Corn,Zezheng Zhu,Yuan Xu,Jiahao Wu,Nanfang Yu,Dmytro Filin,Marianna Safronova,Sebastian Will*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用$^{88}$Sr原子在光镊阵列（optical tweezer arrays）中实现亚波长原子阵列，通过访问2,923 nm的中红外跃迁并识别597.14(3) nm的魔幻陷阱波长（magic trapping wavelength），实现了高保真度的单原子制备和成像，以及分辨边带冷却（resolved-sideband cooling），为研究集体发射现象和偶极多体物理等提供了平台。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用$^{88}$Sr原子在光镊阵列中，利用波长为2,923 nm的中红外跃迁（$5s5p\:^{3}P_{2} \rightarrow 5s4d\:^{3}D_{3}$）来增大发射波长；确定了一个魔幻陷阱波长（magic trapping wavelength）为597.14(3) nm以抑制陷阱对原子能级的扰动；采用2,923 nm的光进行分辨边带冷却（resolved-sideband cooling）以降低原子温度。

Result: 成功实现了对光镊中锶原子的高保真度单原子制备与成像，并演示了分辨边带冷却。确定了魔幻陷阱波长的具体数值为597.14(3) nm。

Conclusion: 该平台不仅能够支持灵活排列原子阵列中的集体发射现象研究，还为偶极多体物理（dipolar many-body physics）、对里德伯动力学（Rydberg dynamics）的增强控制以及锶精细结构量子比特（fine-structure qubit）的操控提供了新的机会。

Abstract: Subwavelength atomic tweezer arrays, in which atoms can be positioned at distances smaller than their emission wavelength, have been proposed as a versatile platform to study collective emission phenomena, such as superradiance and subradiance. Experimentally, the realization of such arrays has been a challenge as typical emission wavelengths in the visible or near-infrared are short compared to typical tweezer spacings in the micrometer range. Here, we use $^{88}$Sr atoms in optical tweezer arrays to access a mid-infrared transition at 2,923 nm ($5s5p\:^{3}P_{2} \rightarrow\, 5s4d\:^{3}D_{3}$). We identify a magic trapping wavelength at 597.14(3) nm and demonstrate single-atom preparation and imaging with high fidelity. In addition, using 2,923 nm light, we demonstrate resolved-sideband cooling of tweezer-trapped strontium. Beyond enabling studies of collective emission phenomena in flexible arrangements of atoms, our platform opens novel opportunities for dipolar many-body physics and enhanced control over Rydberg dynamics and the strontium fine-structure qubit.

### [187] [Identifying sensitivity-dominant parameters via active subspaces in reduced-order modeling of fluid dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02315)
*Dewu Yang,Rui Wang,Pengyu Lai,Junjie Wang,Feng Wang,Hui Xu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出POD-AS-PRS框架，结合本征正交分解（POD）、主动子空间（AS）与多项式响应面（PRS），对复杂流动系统的状态空间和参数空间进行双重降维，实现高效、高保真的感兴趣量（QoI）近似重构；在周期性及混沌钝体绕流中验证了高精度与显著加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全阶模型（FOM）在模拟复杂系统动力学时计算成本过高，亟需发展高效的降阶模型（ROM）方法。现有方法多基于模态能量选择主导模态，但未能直接反映感兴趣量（QoI）的敏感性，限制了降维的效率与精度。

Method: 首先利用本征正交分解（POD）从CFD快照中提取低维系数；然后将这些系数作为残差神经网络（ResNet）的输入学习其到QoI的非线性映射，并采用反向模式自动微分（AD）高效计算系数梯度；接着利用主动子空间（AS）在POD系数空间中进行敏感性驱动的降维；最后基于AS所得主动变量构建多项式响应面（PRS）代理模型，仅保留高影响POD系数以重构QoI。

Result: 在周期性及混沌钝体绕流中，该方法以极少的参数实现了高精度QoI重构；AD梯度计算相比有限差分方法提速两个数量级；敏感性分析表明，高影响系数与模态能量并不成正比，揭示了关键流动物理结构。

Conclusion: POD-AS-PRS能够识别由敏感性主导的低维流形，揭示关键流动物理结构及其与控制参数的耦合关系，从而实现对QoI的高效、精确重构。

Abstract: Reduced-order models (ROMs) are widely employed to describe complex system dynamics when simulations with full-order models (FOMs) are computationally prohibitive. This study presents POD-AS-PRS, a novel model-reduction framework based on the active subspaces (AS) technique, which performs dimensionality reduction in both the state and parameter spaces, enabling efficient and high-fidelity approximations of quantities of interest (QoI). The approach employs proper orthogonal decomposition (POD) to extract low-dimensional coefficients from CFD snapshots, which are inputs to a residual neural network (ResNet) with linear layers to learn their nonlinear mapping to QoI. Reverse-mode automatic differentiation (AD) is utilized to compute gradients with respect to the coefficients, enabling AS analysis to identify influential modes by shifting the analysis to the POD coefficient space, thereby achieving a dual-stage dimensionality reduction driven by QoI sensitivity rather than modal energy. A surrogate model is subsequently constructed using a polynomial response surface (PRS) based on AS-derived active variables, retaining only the highly influential POD coefficients to ensure accurate and efficient QoI reconstruction. The framework is validated on periodic and chaotic bluff-body flows, demonstrating high accuracy with few influential parameters, while AD-based gradients achieve a two-order-of-magnitude speed-up over finite-difference approximations. Sensitivity analysis further reveals that the influential coefficients are not necessarily proportional to modal energy, highlighting the critical flow structures. Consequently, POD-AS-PRS identifies a low-dimensional manifold of sensitivity-dominant parameters that govern the QoI, elucidating the essential flow structures and their coupling with control parameters, thereby enabling efficient and accurate QoI reconstruction.

</details>


<div id='nucl-th'></div>

# nucl-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [188] [Quantum dominance of coherent bremsstrahlung in $\isotope[124]{Sn} + \isotope[124]{Sn}$ scattering at 25 MeV/u](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01623)
*Sergei~P. ~Maydanyuk,Ju-Jun Xie,Peng-Ming~Zhang,Li-Ping~Zou*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文对124Sn+124Sn在25 MeV/u能量下的轫致辐射（bremsstrahlung）进行了量子力学计算，首次定量确定了光子谱中非相干与相干发射之比。该比值极小（10⁻¹¹–10⁻⁴），表明相干发射主导整个测量能区，与质子-核散射中非相干发射占优形成鲜明对比。这一发现揭示了核反应中一个此前未被探索的量子轫致辐射区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，质子-核散射中的轫致辐射主要由非相干发射主导（源于核子磁矩的突出作用），而重离子碰撞中可能存在不同的发射机制。本研究旨在通过定量计算非相干-相干比（incoherent-to-coherent ratio），统一解释两类碰撞体系中光子谱的差异，并探索重离子碰撞中的相干效应。

Method: 采用量子力学计算方法对124Sn+124Sn在25 MeV/u能量下的轫致辐射进行模拟，将计算结果与实验测量的全能量范围光子谱进行对比验证。通过定量计算光子谱中非相干成分与相干成分的比值，分析两种发射机制的相对贡献。

Result: 首次定量确定了非相干-相干比，该比值在10⁻¹¹至10⁻⁴之间，表明相干发射在整个测量能区占绝对主导地位。与之对比，p+¹⁹⁷Au碰撞中该比值达到10³–10⁵（TAPS合作组数据，质子束能量190 MeV），非相干发射主导。两类体系的光子谱形态差异得到了统一解释：质子-核散射呈现明显的隆起结构，而锡-锡碰撞的光子谱单调递减并接近对数形状。

Conclusion: 本研究识别出一个此前未被探索的核反应轫致辐射量子区域，为重离子碰撞中的相干效应研究开辟了新途径。非相干-相干比的定量分析为理解不同碰撞体系中光子谱的差异提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We present quantum-mechanical calculations of bremsstrahlung in the $^{124}$Sn+$^{124}$Sn at 25 MeV/u reproducing the measured photon spectrum over the full energy range. For the first time, we quantitatively determine the incoherent-to-coherent ratio in the photon spectrum. This ratio is extremely small, ranging from $10^{-11}$ to $10^{-4}$, which demonstrates that coherent emission dominates throughout the measured energy range. This behavior is in sharp contrast to proton--nucleus scattering, where incoherent emission dominates because of the leading role of nucleon magnetic moments. This contrast is illustrated by the TAPS Collaboration data for $p + ^{197}{\rm Au}$ collisions at a proton beam energy of 190~MeV, where the corresponding ratio reaches $10^{3}$--$10^{5}$. We find that incoherent-to-coherent ratios explain the difference between the two spectra in unified picture: (1) In proton--nucleus scattering, the spectrum contains a pronounced hump, (2) In $\isotope[124]{Sn} + \isotope[124]{Sn}$ scattering, the spectrum decreases monotonically and has a nearly logarithmic shape. Our results identify a previously unexplored quantum regime of bremsstrahlung emission in nuclear reactions and open a new route for studying coherent effects in heavy-ion collisions.

</details>


### [189] [Hydrodynamics without a relaxation gap: memory effects, nonlocality, and superdiffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01805)
*Lorenzo Gavassino,Sukanya Mitra,Rajeev Singh*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该研究通过一个具有上无界能量依赖弛豫时间的相对论粒子传播模型，证明长期记忆效应会导致非流体动力学（non-hydrodynamic）模式的持续存在，从而使梯度展开发散，并最终破坏流体动力学局部性（hydrodynamic locality），在某些极端条件下甚至导致普通扩散失效并出现超扩散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在具有无间隙非流体动力学谱（gapless non-hydrodynamic sector）的系统中，长期记忆（long-term memory）如何阻碍局部流体动力学（local hydrodynamics）的出现。

Method: 研究一个相对论粒子在具有能量依赖且上无界弛豫时间（relaxation time）的背景介质中传播的简单模型；在弛豫时间近似（RTA, relaxation time approximation）匹配框架（matching frame）下分析梯度展开（gradient expansion）的性质。

Result: 全梯度展开在大多数流（flows）中一般是发散的，即使对于傅里叶模式（Fourier modes）也是如此；任何重求和（resummation）必然保留无限多个慢速非流体动力学自由度（slow non-hydrodynamic degrees of freedom）；足够奇异的弛豫谱（relaxation spectra）可能使普通扩散（ordinary diffusion）失效，导致扩散率发散、晚期动力学转变为超扩散（superdiffusive）。

Conclusion: 梯度展开的发散反映了由持续非流体动力学记忆（persistent non-hydrodynamic memory）引起的更根本的流体动力学局部性失效；在极端条件下系统由本质上非局域的本构关系（intrinsically nonlocal constitutive relations）主导。

Abstract: By studying a simple model of relativistic particles propagating through a background medium with an energy-dependent relaxation time that is unbounded from above, we investigate how long-term memory obstructs the emergence of local hydrodynamics in systems with a gapless non-hydrodynamic sector. In the RTA matching frame, we show that the full gradient expansion is generically divergent in most flows, even for Fourier modes, and that any resummation necessarily retains an infinite set of slow non-hydrodynamic degrees of freedom. The divergence of the gradient expansion therefore reflects a more fundamental breakdown of hydrodynamic locality caused by persistent non-hydrodynamic memory. We finally show that sufficiently singular relaxation spectra can invalidate ordinary diffusion itself. In these regimes, the diffusivity diverges, and the late-time dynamics become superdiffusive, governed by intrinsically nonlocal constitutive relations.

</details>

### [190] [Timelike ideal boundary of non-positively curved Lorentzian spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02496)
*Saúl Burgos,Mauricio Che,Miguel Prados-Abad*

Main category: math.MG

TL;DR: 该论文在洛伦兹长度空间（Lorentzian length space）中引入了“类时理想边界”（timelike ideal boundary）的概念，将其定义为未来或过去定向类时测地射线（timelike geodesic rays）的渐近类集合，并为其配备了自然的锥拓扑（cone topology）和角度度量（angular metric），建立了该度量空间的上曲率界（upper curvature bounds），最后通过广义锥（generalized cones）模型研究了类时理想边界与纤维的度量理想边界及扭曲函数渐近行为之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 类时理想边界的构造是对Geroch-Kronheimer-Penrose因果边界（causal boundary）的补充，类似于度量空间（metric space）中理想边界（ideal boundary）的概念，旨在为洛伦兹几何提供一种新的边界理论。

Method: 作者将洛伦兹长度空间中未来或过去定向的类时测地射线按渐近性分类，定义类时理想边界；接着在该边界上构造了自然锥拓扑和角度度量，并证明了所得度量空间满足上曲率界；最后以广义锥作为模型，分析了类时理想边界与纤维度量理想边界以及扭曲函数（warping function）渐近行为之间的关联。

Result: 成功定义了类时理想边界并赋予其锥拓扑与角度度量结构；证明了该度量空间具有上曲率界；揭示了广义锥模型下，类时理想边界与纤维的度量理想边界及扭曲函数渐近行为之间的联系。

Conclusion: 类时理想边界为洛伦兹长度空间提供了一种与因果边界互补的边界构造，具有自然的几何结构（锥拓扑与角度度量）且满足上曲率界，为广义锥等模型中的渐近分析提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We introduce the notion of timelike ideal boundary of a Lorentzian length space as the set of asymptotic classes of future or past-directed timelike geodesic rays, a construction complementary to the causal boundary in the sense of Geroch-Kronheimer-Penrose and akin to the concept of ideal boundary of a metric space. We endow such a timelike ideal boundary with a natural cone topology and an angular metric, and establish upper curvature bounds for the resulting metric space. Finally, we consider generalized cones as a model and study the relation between the timelike ideal boundary and both the metric ideal boundary of the fiber and the asymptotic behaviour of the warping function.

Method: 借鉴熔融物理学（physics of melting），将网络中的已巩固知识建模为受保护的“固体”，未利用的容量建模为可适应的“液体”；通过一个“潜热”（latent heat）调节旋钮控制固-液边界的扩张，数学上冻结已学习的内部区域。

Result: 该方法将遗忘（forgetting）降低至接近零，在不存储原始数据（raw data）的条件下，达到了与依赖大量记忆的基线方法（memory-heavy baselines）相当的性能。

Conclusion: Stefan-CL 提供了一条基于物理学（physics-grounded）的优雅路径，用于解决持续学习中的稳定性-可塑性困境，展现出在无数据回放场景下实现近零遗忘的潜力。

Abstract: Continual learning struggles to balance retaining past knowledge with absorbing new tasks. Stefan-CL elegantly resolves this stability-plasticity dilemma through the physics of melting. It frames consolidated knowledge as a protected "solid" and unused capacity as an adaptable "liquid." As the network learns, this boundary expands, governed by a "latent heat" tuning dial. By mathematically freezing the learned interior, Stefan-CL cuts forgetting to near zero, matching memory-heavy baselines without storing raw data, forging a beautiful, physics-grounded path for AI.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: This study presents an iterative AI-guided workflow that accelerates graphite-based anode development by improving both formulation feasibility and process robustness. Sequential learning via AI/ML-guided multiobjective inverse design for anode optimization was implemented using the Citrine Platform. Starting from a noisy, incomplete dataset, the Citrine Platform was used to generate early surrogate models, which despite low predictive certainty highlighted missing process constraints. By iteratively adding feasibility labels and boundary condition failures, the workflow rapidly converged toward manufacturable, higher-performing formulations. Fabrication reliability improved from frequent process failures to 100% successful cell production, while the fraction of cells delivering $\geq$ 350 mAh g$^{-1}$ increased from 28.4% to 84.8%, with capacity retention rising from 42.1% to 97.3%. ### [193] [Speculative Sampling For Faster Molecular Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02455)
*Arthur Kosmala,Stephan Günnemann,Meng Gao,Brandon Wood*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Langevin推测动力学（Langevin Speculative Dynamics, LSD），一种分布式、模型无关的推测性采样方法，通过草稿模型快速建议模拟步骤并由目标模型并行验证，在不引入额外相对误差的前提下加速分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟，实验获得3–9倍加速比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）虽为模拟原子系统动力学的关键工具，但其固有的串行特性使得通过并发计算提升单系统吞吐量十分困难。

Method: 受语言建模与扩散建模中推测方法的启发，LSD采用草稿模型（draft model）快速提出模拟步骤，再通过较慢的目标模型（target model）并行验证；同时引入从草稿分布到目标分布的传输映射（transport map），并将推测采样（speculative sampling）推广至二阶朗之万动力学（second-order Langevin dynamics）。

Result: 推导了以物理参数表达的可达加速比函数；实验表明LSD在不同系统和草稿-目标组合下具有泛化能力，实现3–9倍加速；理论和实证均证实LSD从目标模型分布中采样轨迹（trajectories）。

Conclusion: LSD在不增加相对误差的条件下有效加速MD模拟，且采样轨迹忠实于目标模型分布。

Abstract: Molecular dynamics (MD) is a key tool for simulating the dynamical behavior of atomic systems. However, MD is inherently serial, which makes it difficult to increase single-system throughput with concurrent compute. To address this, we introduce Langevin Speculative Dynamics (LSD), a distributed and model-agnostic speculative sampler for accelerating MD without adding relative error. Inspired by speculative methods in language and diffusion modeling, LSD uses a draft model to propose fast simulation steps and verifies them in parallel with a slower target model, applying a transport map from the draft to the target distribution. We extend speculative sampling to second-order Langevin dynamics, derive the achievable speedup as a function of physical parameters, show that LSD generalizes across different systems and draft-target combinations with a 3-9x speedup, and confirm theoretically and empirically that LSD samples trajectories from its target model distribution.

</details>

### [194] [Chirality routing non-polaritonic vacuum correlations in Landau polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00165)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用量子信息（quantum information）方法，基于多模Hopfield模型（multimode Hopfield model）分析Landau极化激元（Landau polaritons）中的手性超强耦合系统，利用从多模Landau极化激元系统提取的参数计算高斯失谐（Gaussian discord）等量子关联指标。

Result: 精确手性电荷将主导的异常关联、压缩和光-物质纠缠路由到相反偏振方向；手性路由将回旋共振与有限动量磁等离子体激元通过高斯失谐关联起来，但成对物质-物质纠缠缺失；预测了修饰真空电场涨落的偏振各向异性作为该手性路由的特征。

Conclusion: 手性（chirality）可作为组织超强耦合真空的对称性原理，量子信息工具是揭示Landau极化激元显著性质的有效框架。

Abstract: Ultrastrong coupling between matter and cavity vacuum fields can turn the electromagnetic vacuum into a structured quantum environment, thereby opening passive routes for modifying and manipulating material properties. Recent work has identified light--matter entanglement as an important ingredient in these property changes, which raises the question of where the relevant vacuum correlations actually reside. Landau polaritons provide chiral ultrastrong coupling systems in which one circular cavity polarization forms the bright polariton branches. Here, using a quantum information approach, we show that an exact chiral charge in a multimode Hopfield model routes the dominant anomalous correlations, squeezing, and cavity--matter entanglement into the opposite polarization. We find that, using parameters extracted from a multimode Landau polariton system, this hidden sector correlates the cyclotron resonance with finite momentum magnetoplasmons through Gaussian discord, while pairwise matter--matter entanglement remains absent. We further predict a polarization anisotropy of dressed vacuum electric field fluctuations as a signature of this chiral routing. These results identify chirality as a symmetry principle for organizing ultrastrong coupling vacua and show that quantum information tools provide a powerful framework for revealing the salient properties of Landau polaritons.

The flow rate of potassium ions, however, under an applied electric field is almost the same in metallic and semiconducting nanotubes. We propose a simple physical picture to understand these experimental results by examining the effects of screening by conduction electrons in electrically conducting carbon nanotubes on the friction experienced by protons, water molecules, and ions flowing through the nanotube.

### [196] [Individually tunable Si/SiGe quantum dot operating voltages via gate-biased illumination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00446)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体量子点（quantum dot）qubit 常需要每个栅极施加差异很大的电压才能达到正确工作点，这增加了复杂性和不可控性，因此需要一种能可控且可重复地改变界面 trapped charge 分布的方法来统一工作电压。

Method: 在施加栅极电压（gate voltages）的同时，使用近红外光（near-infrared light）照射器件，从而逐栅极地调控氧化物-半导体界面处的纳米尺度 trapped charge 分布；通过自洽薛定谔-泊松模拟（self-consistent Schrödinger-Poisson simulations）解释其物理机制。

Result: 在 Si/SiGe 量子点器件上成功演示该方法，工作电压可被调控并变得均匀；将三重量子点（triple quantum dot）调谐到 (1,1,1) 电荷组态下具有均匀且低的工作电压；该方法改变工作电压后测得的电荷噪声（charge noise）未发生变化。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种逐栅极调节量子点工作点的有效途径，能显著提升电压均匀性且不引入额外的电荷噪声，为半导体量子点 qubit 的实用化调控提供了新手段。

Abstract: Semiconductor quantum dot qubits often require very different voltages on each gate to bring them to a correct operating point. Here, we present a method by which one can controllably and repeatably alter the nanoscale trapped charge distribution at an oxide-semiconductor interface. We demonstrate this method on a Si/SiGe quantum dot device, and we find that the operating voltages can be controlled and made much more uniform. The method relies on illumination with near-infrared light in the presence of applied gate voltages, and it enables the tuning of the device operating point on a gate-by-gate basis. We present an explanation of the underlying physics using self-consistent Schrödinger-Poisson simulations. As an application of this method, we tune a triple quantum dot to have uniform and small operating voltages in the (1,1,1) charge configuration. Importantly, we show that shifting the operating voltages in this way does not change the measured charge noise.

### [197] [Wilson Holonomy and Spectral Monodromy in Spin-Orbit Rings: Effective Gauge Connections and Loop Observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01029)
*N. Bolivar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文严格区分了自旋-轨道（spin-orbit）哈密顿量中的两种环状对象——与能量无关的Wilson和乐（Wilson holonomy）和与能量相关的单值性（monodromy），建立了从规范场论（gauge theory）的环/和乐表示到凝聚态自旋-轨道输运（spin-orbit transport）之间的可计算桥梁。通过狄拉克环和Rashba-Dresselhaus环两个实例，展示了分离后的和乐与单值性如何精确地给出谱量子化条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献常将自旋-轨道系统中的两种环状对象——Wilson和乐与单值性——混为一谈，导致概念模糊和计算困难。本文旨在通过严格分离这两种对象，为规范场论与凝聚态自旋-轨道输运之间构建一个精确且可计算的桥梁。

Method: 首先将自旋-轨道哈密顿量映射为有效的$U(1)$加上内部非阿贝尔联络（non-Abelian connection），将其约化为一阶输运问题；然后从和乐、单值性、曲率（curvature）和本征相位（eigenphase）数据中读取物理预言。通过两个环系统（狄拉克环与Rashba-Dresselhaus环）使分离过程具体化。

Result: 对于具有Rashba耦合和Aharonov-Bohm通量的狄拉克（石墨烯）环，总和乐精确分解为一个对易的$U(1)$通量相位乘以一个内部自旋/赝自旋和乐，谱由和乐本征值条件给出。对于Rashba-Dresselhaus环，在$α=\pmβ$纯规范（pure-gauge）点以外，内部$SU(2)$输运是真正非阿贝尔的，曲率控制路径排序（path ordering）；谱量子化需要通过对二阶Schrödinger问题进行相空间加倍（phase-space doubling）获得显式一阶约化。

Conclusion: 严格分离Wilson和乐与单值性能够为自旋-轨道系统提供清晰的谱量子化方案。非阿贝尔Stokes公式和Magnus展开仅作为排序诊断（ordering diagnostics）工具，而非谱工具。自旋网络（spin-network）概念仅作为历史的几何动机，而非自旋电子学中的动力学引入。

Abstract: A spin-orbit Hamiltonian with an effective gauge structure carries two distinct loop objects that are routinely conflated: an energy-independent Wilson holonomy, which organizes interference and internal spin transport, and an energy-dependent monodromy, which quantizes the spectrum. We show that cleanly separating these objects supplies a precise, computable bridge between the loop/holonomy representation of gauge theories and condensed-matter spin-orbit transport. The construction maps a spin-orbit Hamiltonian to an effective $U(1)$ plus internal non-Abelian connection, reduces it to a first-order transport problem, and reads physical predictions from holonomy, monodromy, curvature, and eigenphase data. Two rings make the separation explicit. For a Dirac (graphene) ring with Rashba coupling and Aharonov-Bohm flux, the total holonomy factorizes exactly into a commuting $U(1)$ flux phase times an internal spin/pseudospin holonomy, and the spectrum follows from a holonomy-eigenvalue condition. For a Rashba-Dresselhaus ring, the internal $SU(2)$ transport is genuinely non-Abelian away from the $α=\pmβ$ pure-gauge locus, where curvature controls path ordering; spectral quantization then requires an explicit first-order reduction obtained by phase-space doubling of the second-order Schrödinger problem. A non-Abelian Stokes formulation and Magnus expansion serve as ordering diagnostics rather than spectral tools. Spin-network ideas enter only as historical geometric motivation, not as a dynamical import into spintronics.

*Shiyu Chen,Yan He*

TL;DR: 本文基于Uhlmann相位研究高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulators）在有限温度下的拓扑性质，以Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes（BBH）模型为例，通过Uhlmann相位的量子化及其跳变确定有限温度拓扑相变的临界温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前高阶拓扑绝缘体（HOTIs）的拓扑性质主要在零温下被研究，而有限温度下的拓扑行为尚不明确。本文旨在利用Uhlmann相位这一有限温度拓扑工具，探索HOTIs在有限温度下的拓扑相变。

Method: 采用Uhlmann相位（Uhlmann phase）作为有限温度下的拓扑不变量，该相位是Uhlmann重叠（Uhlmann overlap）的相位角。以BBH模型为例，其哈密顿量由满足Clifford代数（Clifford algebra）的Gamma矩阵构造，利用该代数结构导出的Uhlmann相位量子化（$0$或$\pi$）特性，将相位的跳变视为非平庸拓扑相的标志，并据此确定临界温度。

Result: Uhlmann相位在BBH模型中量子化为$0$或$\pi$，其跳变可作为有限温度下非平庸拓扑相的指示。通过跳变的消失确定了拓扑相变发生的临界温度。在特殊参数选择下，Uhlmann重叠和临界温度可以解析计算。

Conclusion: Uhlmann相位能够有效刻画高阶拓扑绝缘体在有限温度下的拓扑相变，为有限温度拓扑研究提供了可行的方法。

Abstract: We have studied the finite-temperature topology of higher-order topological insulators (HOTIs) based on the Uhlmann phase, which is a phase angle of the Uhlmann overlap. As an example of HOTIs, the Hamiltonian of the Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes (BBH) model is constructed from Gamma matrices satisfying the Clifford algebra. This specific algebraic structure underpins the model's higher-order topological properties, including the quantization of the Uhlmann phase to $0$ or $π$. This quantization enables us to treat the abrupt jumps of the Uhlmann phase as an indication of the nontrivial topological phase of the BBH model at finite temperature. From the disappearance of these jumps, we determine the critical temperature at which the topological transition occurs. For a special choice of parameters, the Uhlmann overlap and the critical temperature can be computed analytically.

### [199] [Non-Hermiticity-induced chirality imbalance of Weyl Landau levels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00615)
*Sachin Vaidya,Alaa Bayazeed,André Grossi Fonseca,Adolfo G. Grushin,Marin Soljačić,Christina Jörg*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验展示了在合成光子外尔半金属中，非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）如何重塑由尼尔森-仁科定理（Nielsen-Ninomiya theorem）强制的全局手征性约束。通过轴向磁场将补偿性手征通道空间分离，并利用辐射边界损耗选择性地抑制表面态，实现了可观测的手征性失衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 外尔半金属（Weyl semimetals）受尼尔森-仁科定理约束，其净手征拓扑电荷及手征谱流必须为零。作者旨在实验探究非厄米性能否调控甚至放宽这一基本约束，从而实现对传统上被禁阻的谱响应的访问。

Method: 在一维多层结构中利用工程规范场（gauge fields）构建合成光子外尔半金属，分别实现均匀磁场和轴向磁场，直接探测由此产生的朗道能级（Landau-level）谱。通过引入辐射边界损耗（radiative boundary loss）选择性地抑制表面态，并在降低损耗后恢复隐藏的手征通道。

Result: 均匀磁场产生手征平衡的第零朗道能级；轴向磁场则将补偿性手征通道空间分离：共传播的体能赝朗道能级携带一种手征性，相反手征性局域在边界表面态中。辐射边界损耗选择性抑制表面态，产生可观测的手征性失衡；降低损耗后恢复该隐藏通道并确认其表面态起源。

Conclusion: 非厄米性天然存在于光子学系统中，能够控制和放宽拓扑系统中的基本手征性约束，从而实现原本被禁阻的谱响应。

Abstract: Weyl semimetals obey a global chirality constraint: the net chiral topological charge and any associated chiral spectral flow must vanish, as required by the Nielsen-Ninomiya theorem. Under magnetic fields, this constraint manifests through counter-propagating zeroth Landau levels associated with Weyl nodes of opposite chirality. Here, we experimentally demonstrate how non-Hermiticity can reshape this balance in a synthetic photonic Weyl semimetal. Using engineered gauge fields in one-dimensional multilayer structures, we realize both homogeneous and axial magnetic fields and directly probe the resulting Landau-level spectra. While a homogeneous field produces the expected chirality-balanced zeroth Landau levels, an axial field spatially separates the compensating chiral channels: co-propagating bulk pseudo-Landau levels carry one chirality, whereas the opposite chirality resides in boundary-localized surface states. We show that radiative boundary loss selectively suppresses these surface states, removing them from the long-lived observable spectrum and producing an experimentally accessible chirality imbalance. By reducing boundary loss, we recover the hidden chiral channel and reveal its surface-state origin. These results show that non-Hermiticity, present naturally in photonics, can control and relax fundamental chirality constraints in topological systems, enabling access to otherwise forbidden spectral responses.

### [200] [Optically programmable and erasable cryogenic flash memory on an undoped Si/SiGe heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00711)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在未掺杂 Si/SiGe 异质结场效应晶体管（heterojunction field-effect transistor, HFET）中，利用光激发（optical excitation）与栅偏压（gate bias）的相互作用实现非易失性存储；器件利用高界面陷阱密度（interface trap density, $D_{it} > 1.6 \times 10^{12}$ eV$^{-1}$cm$^{-2}$），结合氧化物厚度与介电常数，将阈值电压（threshold voltage）“锁定”到所施加的栅偏压上。

Abstract: Scalable cryogenic memory is a critical yet unresolved requirement for large-scale quantum computing architectures, particularly for computing-in-memory schemes. We exploit the interplay between optical excitation and gate bias in an undoped Si/SiGe heterojunction field-effect transistor (HFET) to realize non-volatile memory functionality. The device exploits a high interface trap density ($D_{it} > 1.6 \times 10^{12}$~eV$^{-1}$cm$^{-2}$), which, in conjunction with the oxide thickness and dielectric constant, enables effective "locking" of the threshold voltage to the applied gate bias over a wide voltage range. Two of these states can be selected for binary operation, while the availability of multiple stable states within the same device enables multibit data storage. Robust cycling endurance ($>~10^3$ cycles) and long-term state retention ($>~10^4$~s) of the memory states at 1.5 K confirm the suitability of this approach for integration into Si/SiGe-based quantum computing architectures.

### [203] [Ultrafast formation of a large dynamic magnetic soliton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00849)
*Ondřej Wojewoda,Sina Mayr,Miela J. Gross,Jan Klíma,Jaganandha Panda,Jakub Krčma,Jakub Holobrádek,Kristýna Davídková,Andrii V. Chumak,Igor Gerasimchuk,Roman Verba,Philipp Pirro,Markus Weigand,Simone Finizio,Morris Lindner,Carsten Dubs,Qi Wang,Sebastian Wintz,Caroline A. Ross,Michal Urbánek*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究报道了在具有垂直磁各向异性的铁磁性石榴石（ferrimagnetic garnet）薄膜中，由微波磁场驱动的动态磁孤子（dynamic magnetic soliton）的超快形成过程。实验发现该孤子在线性自旋波频带内形成，尺寸可达数十微米，并通过自限幅机制（self-limiting mechanism）解释其形成；时间分辨测量显示孤子形成存在微小延迟，而长程相干振荡在40微米范围内几乎同时出现。该结果确立了微波驱动孤子作为一种稳健的非线性现象（nonlinear phenomenon），并为快速、非局域的磁态调控与新型计算方案提供了可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性磁化动力学（nonlinear magnetization dynamics）中存在从双稳态到混沌的丰富现象，但其中的动态磁孤子的超快形成机制及其与线性自旋波的相互作用仍未得到充分理解。本研究旨在揭示微波磁场驱动下薄膜铁磁体中动态磁孤子的形成过程、物理机制及其独特性质。

Method: 实验采用微带天线（microstrip antenna）的微波磁场驱动具有垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy）的铁磁性石榴石薄膜。利用时间分辨布里渊光散射显微镜（time-resolved Brillouin light scattering microscopy）和扫描透射X射线显微镜（scanning transmission X-ray microscopy）直接追踪大角度进动态（large-angle precession state）的建立过程。

Result: 观测到的孤子具有两个关键特征：(i) 在线性自旋波频带（linear spin-wave frequency band）内部形成；(ii) 尺寸异常大，可达天线范围外几十微米。远离驱动源时，孤子塌缩并通过几乎瞬时的空间波数转换（spatial wavenumber conversion）发射短波自旋波。时间分辨测量显示孤子形成存在微小有限延迟，而长程相干振荡在40微米距离内几乎同时出现。

Conclusion: 孤子形成由正非线性频移（positive nonlinear frequency shift）引发的自限幅机制以及天线的近场空间范围（spatial extent of the near-field）共同解释。这些结果确立了微波驱动孤子作为薄膜石榴石中一种稳健的非线性现象，并为快速、非局域的磁态操控以及新型计算方案的应用提供了可能性。

Abstract: Nonlinear magnetization dynamics offers a rich variety of phenomena ranging from bistability to chaos. Here, we report the ultrafast formation of a dynamic magnetic soliton in thin ferrimagnetic garnet films with perpendicular magnetic anisotropy, driven by the microwave magnetic field of a microstrip antenna. Using time-resolved Brillouin light scattering microscopy and scanning transmission X-ray microscopy, we directly track the build-up of the large-angle precession state. The observed soliton is distinct from other nonlinear magnetic excitations in two key aspects: (i) it forms inside the linear spin-wave frequency band, and (ii) it is exceptionally large, reaching tens of microns beyond the antenna. We explain the soliton formation by the self-limiting mechanism upon a positive nonlinear frequency shift and the spatial extent of the near-field of the antenna. At large distances from the drive, the soliton collapses and emits short-wavelength spin waves via almost instantaneous spatial wavenumber conversion. Time-resolved measurements further reveal a small finite delay during soliton formation, while coherent long-range oscillations appear essentially simultaneously over distances up to 40 micrometers. These results establish microwave-driven solitons as a robust nonlinear phenomenon in thin-film garnets and suggest opportunities for fast, nonlocal manipulation of magnetic states and for applications in novel computational schemes.
