### [204] [Electronic Hall viscosity: hidden indicator for antiferromagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01003)
*Ding Li,Tao Qin,Jianhui Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了电子霍尔粘度（electronic Hall viscosity）与布洛赫能带（Bloch bands）的四极贝里曲率（quadruple Berry curvature）之间的密切关系，证明其受d轨道因子调制的量子体积（quantum volume）二阶矩的约束，并推导了非零电子霍尔粘度的对称性条件。通过第一性原理计算，在d波交变磁体（altermagnet）RuO₂和非共线Mn₃Sn两种典型反铁磁材料中验证了关键结论，为反铁磁自旋电子学器件设计提供了基于非常规霍尔粘度的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体（antiferromagnet）因杂散场可忽略且自旋动力学超快，在低功耗自旋电子学（spintronics）和拓扑电子学（topological electronics）中至关重要。然而，由于磁化强度和反常霍尔电导（anomalous Hall conductivity）消失，对非平庸贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的探测和调控极为受限，亟需新的表征方法。

Method: 理论推导了电子霍尔粘度与四极贝里曲率及量子体积二阶矩之间的数学约束关系，导出了非零电子霍尔粘度的对称性条件。通过第一性原理计算（first-principle calculations），在d波交变磁体RuO₂和非共线反铁磁体Mn₃Sn中进行了数值验证。

Result: 发现电子霍尔粘度紧密关联于布洛赫能带的四极贝里曲率，且受d轨道因子调制的量子体积二阶矩所限制；即使在反常霍尔线性响应被禁止时，电子霍尔粘度仍能表征反铁磁有序（antiferromagnetic ordering）。第一性原理计算在两种典型反铁磁材料中证实了上述发现。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一种描述通用反铁磁体的新型量子几何量（quantum geometry quantity），并提供了一种通过非常规霍尔粘度（unconventional Hall viscosity）设计反铁磁自旋电子学器件的广泛适用方法。

Abstract: The antiferromagnets with negligible stray fields and ultrafast spin dynamics play a crucial role in the fields of energy-efficient spintronics and topological electronics. However, the detection and control of the underlying nontrivial Berry curvature become extremely limited by the vanishing magnetization and anomalous Hall conductivity. Here, we show the electronic Hall viscosity is closely related to the quadruple Berry curvature of Bloch bands and is bounded by the $d$-orbit factor modulated second moment of the quantum volume. Moreover, we derive the symmetry requirement for nonzero electronic Hall viscosity that could characterize antiferromagnetic ordering even when the linear anomalous Hall response gets forbidden. We further examine our key findings in two archetypal antiferromagnets: $d$-wave altermagnet $\mathrm{RuO}_{2}$, and noncollinear $\mathrm{Mn_{3}Sn}$ through direct first-principle calculations. Thus, our work reveals a new and fundamental quantum geometry quantity of generic antiferromagnets and offers a broadly applicable way to design antiferromagnetic spintronics devices via unconventional Hall viscosity.

</details>


### [205] [Hot carrier diffusion-assisted ideal carrier multiplication in monolayer MoSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01125)
*Joonsoo Kim,Hong-Guk Min,Sehwan Park,Jin Cheol Park,Junhyeok Bang,Youngkuk Kim,Ji-Hee Kim*

TL;DR: 本研究通过超快瞬态吸收光谱和第一性原理计算，证明单层MoSe2能够达到能量-动量守恒原理允许的理论最大载流子倍增效率，其关键在于抑制了载流子-晶格散射导致的能量耗散，并利用2Eg能带嵌套提供了丰富的CM路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 载流子倍增（carrier multiplication, CM）有望突破光伏应用中的Shockley-Queisser极限，但长期以来没有材料实现理想的CM效率，主要原因是载流子-晶格散射（carrier-lattice scattering）造成的显著能量损失。

Method: 采用超快瞬态吸收光谱（ultrafast transient absorption spectroscopy）解析热载流子的无散射弹道输运（scatter-free ballistic transport），并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证实验结果。

Result: 单层MoSe2达到了能量-动量守恒原理（energy-momentum conservation principle）所允许的理论最大CM效率；相较于体相MoSe2，单层MoSe2因更优的热载流子扩散和额外的CM路径而表现出增强的CM效率。

Conclusion: 单层MoSe2是实现高性能光电器件和下一代能量转换技术的候选材料，其优异的CM特性源于抑制载流子-晶格散射和2Eg能带嵌套提供的丰富CM通道。

Abstract: Carrier multiplication (CM), the process of generating multiple charge carriers from a single photon, offers an opportunity to exceed the Shockley-Queisser limit in photovoltaic applications. Despite extensive research, no material has yet achieved ideal CM efficiency, primarily owing to significant energy losses from carrier-lattice scattering. In this study, we demonstrate that monolayer MoSe2 can attain the theoretical maximum CM efficiency permitted by energy-momentum conservation principle, using ultrafast transient absorption spectroscopy. By resolving the scatter-free ballistic transport of hot carriers and validating our findings with first-principles calculations, we identify the cornerstone of optimal CM in monolayer MoSe2: superior hot-carrier dynamics characterized by suppressed energy dissipation via minimized carrier-lattice scattering, and the availability of abundant CM pathways facilitated by 2Eg band nesting. Comparative analysis with bulk MoSe2 further emphasizes the enhanced CM efficiency in the monolayer, attributed by superior hot-carrier diffusion and access to additional CM pathways. These results position monolayer MoSe2 as a promising candidate for high-performance optoelectronic applications, providing a robust platform for next-generation energy conversion technologies.

### [206] [Signatures of Rashba-Cavity-Induced Berry-curvature redistribution in the Spin-Hall Conductivity of Semiconductor Artificial Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01373)
*Maryam Mansouri,Vram Mughnetsyan,Armen Harutyunyan,Albert Kirakosyan,Vidar Gudmundsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了远红外腔场（far-infrared cavity field）与Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit interaction）对人造石墨烯（artificial graphene）能带结构和输运性质的联合影响。结果表明两类狄拉克点（type-I和type-II）对Rashba耦合响应不同，且腔与Rashba的协同作用可调控狄拉克点物理、自旋霍尔电导（spin-Hall conductivity）及拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索远红外腔场与Rashba自旋-轨道耦合在人造石墨烯（基于准二维InAs/GaAs量子点）中的联合效应，以揭示其对能带结构和输运性质的调控机制。

Method: 将腔-光子耦合建模为电子希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）与福克空间（Fock space）张量积的完备基；在柱面腔（cylindrical cavity）和线形腔（linear cavity）两种几何构型下进行理论计算。

Result: 在线形腔中预测了type-I和type-II两类狄拉克点（Dirac points），其区别在于对Rashba耦合的响应：type-II狄拉克点打开能隙，而type-I保持无隙。两类腔中均观察到电子-光子混合态（electron-photon hybrid states）和能带间拉比振荡（Rabi oscillations）。狄拉克带副本（Dirac-band replicas）之间出现多重劈裂、交叉与反交叉，导致自旋霍尔电导呈现强各向异性（anisotropy）和振荡行为，且受腔几何与极化调控。

Conclusion: Rashba耦合与腔耦合的相互作用主导了狄拉克点物理，为实现可调极化激元输运（polaritonic transport）和工程纳米结构中的拓扑相（topological phases）提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the combined effect of a far-infrared cavity field and Rashba spin-orbit interac- tion on the band structure and transport properties of artificial graphene composed of quazi-2D InAs/GaAs quantum dots. The coupling to cavity photons is modeled by constructing a complete basis as the tensor product of the electronic Hilbert space and the Fock space. Our calculations for the system embedded in a linear cavity predict the existence of both type-I and type-II Dirac points which can be distinguished by their response to Rashba interaction. Namely, Rashba coupling opens a gap at type-II Dirac points, while type-I Dirac points remain gapless. For both cylindrical and linear cavities, we demonstrate the formation of electron-photon hybrid states and Rabi oscillations between energy minibands. Multiple splittings, crossings, and anticrossings between Dirac-band replicas produce pronounced modifications of the spin-Hall conductivity, including strong anisotropy and oscillatory behavior controlled by cavity geometry and polarization. Our results show that the interplay between Rashba and cavity couplings governs Dirac-point physics and provides a route toward tunable polaritonic transport and topological phases in engineered nanostructures.

### [207] [Quantized orbital and spin Hall transport: interplay between $sp$-hybridization, altermagnetism and spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01404)
*Saikat Saha,Banasree Sadhukhan,Tanay Nag*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过二维模型哈密顿量，研究了超越L-S耦合的轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）与自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），发现当交错磁序（altermagnetic order, AM order）强度超过或Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）强度低于sp-杂化标度时，轨道和自旋霍尔响应分别在费米能窗口内呈现量子化。该量子化源于费米面激活的轨道与自旋贝里曲率（Berry curvature），且轨道（自旋）量子化不受Rashba SOC（AM序）影响。温度升高会显著破坏自旋霍尔量子化。轨道与自旋能斯特系数（Nernst coefficients）的尖峰-谷结构为实验探测提供了信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索源自超越L-S耦合的轨道与自旋霍尔效应的涌现机制，并阐明轨道间杂化（inter-orbit hybridization）、相对论性Rashba自旋-轨道耦合与非相对论性SOC（即交错磁序）三者之间的相互作用。

Method: 构建二维模型哈密顿量，在其中同时引入轨道间杂化、Rashba SOC以及交错磁序（作为非相对论性SOC）；通过计算轨道与自旋霍尔电导及相应的能斯特系数，并结合费米面附近的能带结构与贝里曲率分析，研究量子化响应及其温度依赖性。

Result: 当AM序强度超过sp-杂化标度或Rashba SOC强度低于该标度时，轨道与自旋霍尔响应分别在特定费米能窗口内呈现量子化。轨道霍尔量子化不受Rashba SOC影响，自旋霍尔量子化不受AM序影响；费米面附近能带具有有限轨道矩（orbital moment）但自旋矩（spin moment）可忽略。量子化窗口宽度受轨道内耦合强度（intra-orbital coupling）强烈调控。自旋霍尔量子化随温度升高显著退化；轨道与自旋能斯特系数中出现的尖峰-谷结构可作为量子化存在的实验可探测信号。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了一种不依赖于传统L-S耦合的、由交错磁序与Rashba SOC共同调控的轨道与自旋霍尔效应量子化机制，且两种量子化相互独立。这一发现为在无强自旋-轨道耦合材料中实现纯轨道或自旋输运的量子化提供了新途径，并给出了可实验验证的能斯特信号作为参考。

Abstract: We here explore the emergence of orbital and spin Hall effects, originating beyond the $L$-$S$ coupling, and investigate the interplay between inter-orbit hybridization, relativistic Rashba spin-orbit coupling (SOC), and non-relativistic SOC, namely altermagnetic (AM) order, in a two-dimensional model Hamiltonian. The orbital (spin) Hall responses are remarkably found to be quantized within a window of Fermi energy when the strength of AM order (Rashba SOC) exceeds (falls below) the scale set by $sp$-hybridization. Importantly, orbital and spin Hall quantizations are independent of Rashba SOC and AM order, respectively, while the uniform profiles of finite orbital and vanishingly small spin moments of bands around the Fermi energy. The microscopic origin of such quantization comes from the Fermi surface-activated orbital and spin Berry curvatures. The extent of the quantized regime is strongly controlled by the intra-orbital coupling strength. As the temperature increases, the quantization is significantly compromised in the spin Hall case. We extend our analysis to the orbital and spin Nernst coefficients where the pronounced dip-peak structures signal the existence of the quantization leading to experimental relevance.

### [208] [Quantum Statistics and Structural Topology Govern Thermal Transport in Two-Dimensional Monolayer Amorphous Carbon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01408)
*Gizem Kurt,Haldun Sevincli*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文运用三种非晶化算法生成二维单层非晶碳（MAC）的各种构型，通过局域键序参数q₃量化非晶度并结合全量子力学框架计算热导率（TC），发现室温下TC值在3.5–10 W/m/K范围内，且经典处理会显著高估热导率，尤其在低温下偏差可达近一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二维非晶固体中结构拓扑、非晶化程度和量子统计效应对热传导的贡献，并定量预测二维单层非晶碳（monolayer amorphous carbon, MAC）的热导率（thermal conductivity, TC）以解释近期实验观测。

Method: 采用三种不同的非晶化算法生成多种MAC构型（从Zachariasen型连续随机网络到嵌入随机网络的纳米晶粒）；利用局域键序参数q₃量化结构非晶度；在完全量子力学框架下计算TC作为q₃和温度的函数。

Result: 室温下TC预测值为3.5–10 W/m/K，与近期实验一致。振动模式虽可归类为传播子（propagons）、扩散子（diffusons）和局域子（locons），但极化特性呈现不同行为。量子TC在室温下不足经典值的一半，在低温下比经典值低近一个数量级。

Conclusion: 结构非晶度与量子统计效应对二维非晶碳的热传导具有决定性影响；经典处理会严重高估其热导率，必须采用全量子力学描述才能准确预测二维非晶固体的热输运性质。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum thermal conductivity (TC) of two-dimensional monolayer amorphous carbon (MAC). We employ three distinct amorphization algorithms to generate various possible MAC configurations, ranging from Zachariasen-type continuous random networks to nanocrystallites embedded in random networks. The local bond order parameter, q3, is used to quantify the amorphousness of the structures, and TC is computed as functions of q3 and temperature. This framework enables us to assess how structural topology, degree of amorphization, and quantum statistics contribute to heat conduction in a two-dimensional amorphous solid. At room temperature, TC values are predicted to range between 3.5 to 10 W/m/K, in agreement with recent experiments. Analysis of vibrational modes reveals that, while the modes of these 2D amorphous structures fall into the usual categories, namely, propagons, diffusons, and locons, their polarization characteristics display distinct behavior. Owing to the fully quantum mechanical framework, we examine both low- and high-temperature characteristics of this 2D amorphous system. By examining the classical limit, we show that classical treatments substantially overestimate the TC of MAC; namely, the quantum TC is less than half of the classical value at room temperature and up to nearly an order of magnitude lower at low temperatures.

### [209] [Universal Right-Hand Chirality of Evanescent Vector Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01585)
*Yilin Qing,Ji Zou,Yi-Pu Wang,Gerrit E. W. Bauer,Tao Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了任何无源（source-free）矢量场在传播方向 $\hat{\bf q}$ 与衰减方向 $\hat{\bf n}$ 上，若存在自旋（spin），则自动满足刚性右手锁定的手性（chirality）关系，且该手性指数存在由自旋-传播方向夹角决定的基本上界。这一普遍性否定了左手衰减场的存在，体现了镜像构型的根本非对等性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在光学、磁学、等离激元学和声学等领域的倏逝波或表面波中广泛观察到传播方向 $\hat{\bf q}$、自旋 $\hat{\bf S}$ 与界面法向 $\hat{\bf n}$ 之间的锁定现象（即手性），但尚不明确该现象是否具有普遍性，抑或受限于特定条件。本文旨在证实这种锁定的普适性。

Method: 从无源矢量场的普遍性质出发，基于传播方向 $\hat{\bf q}$ 和衰减方向 $\hat{\bf n}$ 的几何约束，引入手性指数 $C_{\bf q}\equiv \hat{\bf n}\cdot(\hat{\bf S}\times \hat{\bf q})$，并推导其在任意传播-自旋夹角 $\hat{\bf q}\cdot \hat{\bf S}\equiv η\in [-1,1]$ 下的基本上界 $C_{\bf q}\le \sqrt{1-η^2}$。

Result: 任何无源矢量场的自旋自动强制 $\hat{\bf q}$、$\hat{\bf S}$ 与 $\hat{\bf n}$ 之间形成严格的右手锁定（$C_{\bf q}>0$），且手性指数受限于 $C_{\bf q}\le \sqrt{1-η^2}$。左手衰减无源场在普遍意义上不存在。

Conclusion: 该普遍规律表明镜像构型在物理上具有根本的非等价性，这一原则与宇称破坏（parity violation）、手性分子中对映异构体的天然过剩以及DNA的固定手性等现象内在呼应。

Abstract: A locking between propagation direction $\hat{\bf q}$, spin $\hat{\bf S}$, and surface or interface normal $\hat{\bf n}$ -- a phenomenon broadly termed \textit{chirality} -- pervades evanescent or surface waves in optics, magnetism, plasmonics, and acoustics. Yet, it is not known whether the phenomenon is universal or bound to conditions. Here, we unveil that any \textit{source-free} vector field that propagates along $\hat{\bf q}$ and is evanescent along $\hat{\bf n}$, the existence of a spin automatically enforces a rigid, right-handed locking among $\hat{\bf q}$, $\hat{\bf S}$, and $\hat{\bf n}$, that is characterized by a chirality index $C_{\bf q}\equiv \hat{\bf n}\cdot(\hat{\bf S}\times \hat{\bf q})>0$. For an arbitrary propagation direction defined by $\hat{\bf q}\cdot \hat{\bf S}\equiv η\in [-1,1]$, i.e., not necessarily transverse spin, we derive a fundamental upper bound $C_{\bf q}\le \sqrt{1-η^2}$. The universal absence of left-handed evanescent (source-less) vector fields underscores the fundamental physical non-equivalence of mirror-image configurations -- a principle echoed by parity violation, the natural excess of enantiomers in chiral molecules, and the fixed chirality of DNA.

</details>


### [210] [Integer quantum Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01744)
*Hideo Aoki*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论和实验角度系统综述了整数量子霍尔效应（integer quantum Hall effect），重点关注其在拓扑系统（topological systems）视角下的新理解，并涵盖了石墨烯、氧化物、窄带隙半导体等不同材料中的量子霍尔效应进展，以及Floquet拓扑绝缘体（Floquet topological insulator）这一非平衡拓扑系统的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 整数量子霍尔效应作为拓扑系统（topological systems）的首个实现，其研究已拓展至更广泛的拓扑物理领域。本文旨在提供一个更新的综述，从拓扑系统的新视角重新审视量子霍尔效应，并涵盖该领域在多种材料和新兴非平衡系统中的最新进展。

Method: 本文采用理论分析与实验回顾相结合的综述方法。在理论上，从拓扑系统（topological systems）的视角重新解读量子霍尔效应的基本物理；在实验上，汇总了量子霍尔效应在石墨烯、氧化物、窄带隙半导体等不同材料中的实现，以及Floquet拓扑绝缘体（Floquet topological insulator）中零磁场反常量子霍尔效应的实验验证。

Result: 量子霍尔效应（QHE）最初在强磁场下的二维电子气（two-dimensional electron gas）中被观测到，表现为霍尔电导率量子化为整数倍$e^2/h$。该效应已在石墨烯、氧化物和窄带隙半导体等多种材料中被观察到，并与分数量子霍尔效应（fractional quantum Hall effect）存在关联。理论预测并经实验验证，在圆偏振激光照射下的石墨烯中可实现零磁场下的反常量子霍尔效应，构成Floquet拓扑绝缘体（Floquet topological insulator）这一非平衡拓扑系统的新范式。

Conclusion: 量子霍尔效应不仅是拓扑系统（topological systems）的历史性发端，也是一种重要的电阻标准（resistance standard）并在新的国际单位制（SI system）中发挥作用。Floquet拓扑绝缘体（Floquet topological insulator）作为非平衡拓扑系统的范例，为在零磁场下实现反常量子霍尔效应开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Integer quantum Hall effect, which is the Hall effect quantized into integer times $e^2/h$ ($e$: elementary charge, $h$: Planck's constant) observed first in two-dimensional electron gases in strong magnetic fields, is reviewed from both theoretical and experimental standpoints. Basic physics underlying the phenomenon is explained. Specifically in this new edition we have a fresh look at how the quantum Hall effect is captured in a perspective of topological systems, since, while the quantum Hall effect is historically the first realization of the topological systems, the field has been delved into a much wider realm of physics of topological systems. We also mention diverse advances such as the quantum Hall effect (QHE) in various materials and contexts that include graphene, oxides and narrow-gap semiconductors, a relation with the fractional quantum Hall effect, and the quantum Hall effect as the resistance standard and further roles in the new SI system. We also expound the Floquet topological insulator (a light-matter coupled system) as a new paradigm in nonequilibrium topological systems, where an anomalous quantum Hall effect in zero magnetic field is realized as theoretically predicted to occur in graphene illuminated by a circularly-polarized laser and experimentally verified recently.

</details>


### [211] [Voltage-driven transition from steady-state fluctuations to phase-transition noise in nanoscale VO$_2$ devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01872)
*Sebastian Werner Schmid,Zoltán Balogh,Botond Sánta,Tímea Nóra Török,Zsombor Sinóros-Szabó,György Molnár,János Volk,László Pósa,András Halbritter*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过噪声谱分析与二维电阻网络模拟，揭示了纳米尺度的二氧化钒（VO₂）莫特忆阻器中电场驱动的金属-绝缘体相变（MIT）噪声增强机制，指出噪声源于渗流阈值附近金属与绝缘体畴的动态重组，并表明电流噪声决定了开关阈值电压变异性的下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究纳米尺度VO₂莫特忆阻器中电场驱动的金属-绝缘体相变（MIT）附近的电流噪声行为及其物理起源，为理解非平衡相变过程提供关键见解。

Method: 采用噪声谱学（noise spectroscopy）实验测量外加电压接近阈值时绝缘相与金属相的相对电流噪声变化，并结合二维电阻网络模拟（two-dimensional resistor network simulations）捕捉相变随机动力学过程。

Result: 在set转变和reset转变点附近均观测到相对电流噪声增加约一个数量级；模拟表明噪声增强来源于渗流阈值（percolation threshold）附近金属与绝缘体畴的竞争导致的相涨落放大以及导电路径的动态重构；前驱电流涨落与重复开关周期中的阈值电压变异性一致，表明噪声设定了可达方差的下界。

Conclusion: 噪声增强源于渗流阈值附近的相涨落，且电流噪声对开关阈值的变异性施加了基本下限，为电刺激下纳米VO₂器件中的非平衡相变过程提供了关键理解。

Abstract: We investigate the electrically driven metal-to-insulator transition (MIT) in nanoscale vanadium dioxide (VO$_2$) Mott memristor through noise spectroscopy and two-dimensional resistor network simulations. Our experiments focus on both the insulating phase as the applied voltage approaches the threshold voltage (set transition) and the metallic phase as the voltage is reduced toward the reset voltage (reset transition). In both regimes, we observe an order of magnitude increase in relative current noise near the transition points. To analyze the origin of this noise enhancement, we use simulations that capture the stochastic dynamics of the phase transition. The simulations indicate that the increased noise stems from amplified phase fluctuations near the percolation threshold, where competing metallic and insulating domains lead to dynamic reconfiguration of the conduction paths. In addition, we show that the precursor current fluctuations observed near the switching threshold are consistent with the threshold voltage variability measured in repeated switching cycles, indicating that the noise sets a lower bound on the achievable variance. These findings offer key insights into the non-equilibrium processes governing phase transitions in nanoscale VO$_2$ devices under electrical stimuli.

</details>


### [212] [Magnetic control of electron scattering in silicene quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01938)
*Mohamed El Azar,Elmustapha Feddi,Pablo Díaz,David Laroze,Ahmed Jellal*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了硅烯量子点（silicene quantum dot, SQD）在垂直磁场中通过自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）产生的能隙增强电子局域化的机制，证明该体系可实现鲁棒且自旋选择性的电子束缚。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于克莱因隧穿效应（Klein tunnel effect），无质量纳米结构中载流子无法被永久束缚；外加恒定磁场虽可形成准束缚态（quasi-bound states），但局域化不够理想。本文旨在利用硅烯特有的自旋-轨道耦合所产生固有能隙来增强电子在量子点中的空间局域化。

Method: 首先推导低能狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）的解；其次通过在硅烯量子点界面施加连续性条件，得到扩散系数的精确表达式；最后利用这些结果绘制散射效率图以及概率密度和电流密度的空间分布。

Result: 模拟结果表明，固有能隙（intrinsic gap）的存在显著增强了硅烯量子点中心的电子俘获效率；此外，外加磁场与自旋-轨道耦合的相互作用打破了自旋对称性（spin symmetry），实现了鲁棒且自旋选择性的局域化。

Conclusion: 硅烯量子点在垂直磁场下，利用自旋-轨道耦合产生的能隙可有效增强电子局域化，并实现自旋选择性束缚，为自旋电子学（spintronics）等应用提供了新的思路。

Abstract: The Klein tunnel effect phenomenon makes it impossible to permanently confine charge carriers in massless nanostructures. However, applying a constant magnetic field allows these electrons to be temporarily localized, thus forming quasi-bound states. In this study, we analyze the mechanism of electron diffusion through a silicene quantum dot (SQD) subjected to a perpendicular magnetic field. To enhance spatial localization, we exploit the spin-orbit coupling (SOC) specific to silicene, which generates a natural energy gap by acting as an effective mass. We first derive the solutions to the Dirac equation at low energy. Subsequently, by imposing the continuity conditions at the SQD interfaces, we obtain exact expressions for the diffusion coefficients. These results are then used to map the scattering efficiency together with the spatial distributions of probability and current densities. Our simulations demonstrate that the presence of this intrinsic gap significantly enhances electron trapping at the center of the SQD. Finally, we prove that the interplay between the external field and SOC breaks spin symmetry, thereby enabling robust and spin-selective confinement.

### [213] [Ferroelectric hysteresis in singly aligned graphene-hBN moiré superlattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02338)
*Bao Q. Tu,Tanweer Ahmed,Garen Avedissian,Suzanne Lancaster,Mayank Sharma,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Fèlix Casanova,Marco Gobbi,Luis E. Hueso*

TL;DR: 本研究在单层石墨烯（SLG）与六方氮化硼（hBN）形成的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）中观测到了铁电响应，揭示了其电滞行为源于莫尔超晶格能带（moiré superlattice band）导致的异常电荷屏蔽（abnormal charge screening）。通过霍尔测量估算了自发极化强度，并验证了该电滞行为在2K至室温范围内的稳定性，为高迁移率超薄非易失性器件提供了新机遇。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用霍尔测量（Hall measurements）定位电滞行为（hysteretic behavior）的来源，将其归因于莫尔超晶格能带引发的异常电荷屏蔽；通过电学测量估算莫尔超晶格结构中的自发极化（spontaneous polarization）强度，并开展变温测量以考察电滞行为的温度依赖性。

Result: 成功在SLG-hBN莫尔超晶格中观测到铁电响应；电滞行为的根源是莫尔超晶格能带导致的异常电荷屏蔽；自发极化强度得以估算；变温实验证实该电滞行为在2K至室温范围内均稳定存在。

Conclusion: 本文明确证实了非中心对称单层石墨烯-hBN莫尔超晶格中存在铁电响应，其宽温区（2K–室温）的稳定性为开发高迁移率（high-mobility）、超薄（ultrathin）非易失性器件（non-volatile devices）开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials have the unique ability to maintain an electric polarization which can be reversed under an external applied electric field. This property makes them valuable for applications such as non-volatile random-access memories, transducers, actuators and electro optic modulators. Recently, emergent unconventional ferroelectricity has been demonstrated in moiré superlattices of bilayer graphene and hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) hosting non centrosymmetric stacking order. Whether this phenomenon is also present in noncentrosymmetric single layer graphene (SLG)-hBN moiré superlattices is still under debate. Here we demonstrate a ferroelectric response in an SLG-hBN moiré superlattice. Through Hall measurements, we pinpoint the origin of the hysteretic behavior to abnormal charge screening due to the moiré superlattice band and estimate the spontaneous polarization magnitude in the moiré superlattice structure. Temperature dependent measurements confirm that the hysteretic behavior persists from 2K up to room temperature, opening opportunities for high-mobility, ultrathin non-volatile devices

### [214] [BBH-Genesis: Disentangling Binary Black Hole Formation Channels with GWTC-4](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00234)
*Shaunak Padhyegurjar,Suvodip Mukherjee*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文基于引力波数据（GW data）中的双黑洞（BBH）事件，开发了一个新的推理管线 BBH-Genesis，并应用于第四代引力波目录（GWTC-4），发现当前数据最强证据支持双通道形成场景，暗示存在非孤立双黑洞形成通道，并可能有第三个通道（如活动星系核 AGN 形成通道）的较弱支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测到的双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）种群为揭示其形成与演化历史提供了可能，但天体物理模拟的复杂性使预测不同形成通道的关键特征变得困难。因此，需要通过数据驱动的方法从探测到的引力波事件中识别不同形成通道的存在。

Method: 开发了一个新的统计推断管线 BBH-Genesis，并以数据驱动的方式将其应用于第四代引力波目录（GWTC-4），用于识别是否存在多个内在不同的双黑洞子种群。

Result: GWTC-4 中所有双黑洞事件的最强证据支持仅需双通道场景即可解释，暗示存在非孤立双黑洞形成通道。该子种群可进一步划分为第三个通道，但支持力度较弱，该通道指向活动星系核（active galactic nucleus, AGN）中的形成，并表现出略微不同的有效自旋（effective spin）与质量比（mass ratio）相关性。

Conclusion: 未来随着更多引力波事件的探测，将能更清晰地判断是否至少需要三个形成通道来解释引力波观测到的双黑洞事件。

Abstract: The detected population of binary black holes (BBHs) from the gravitational wave (GW) data has made it possible to decipher their formation and evolution history over cosmic time. The complexity of astrophysical modeling of binary mergers makes it challenging to predict key signatures for different formation channels. As a result, one of the major avenues to discover the presence of different channels from detected GW events is through a data-driven way which can isolate different scenarios. In this spirit, we developed a new inference pipeline BBH-Genesis and applied it on the fourth GW catalog (GWTC-4) to identify the presence of multiple underlying distinct populations. We find that the current population of all the binary events in GWTC-4 can be explained with the strongest evidence for only a two-channel scenario, hinting at the presence of a non-isolated binary formation channel. This sub-population can be further divided into a third channel with mild support towards formation in AGN exhibiting a slightly different effective spin and mass ratio correlation. In the future, with the detection of more events, it will be clearer whether it is necessary to consider at least three channels to explain the BBH events detected using GW observations.

### [215] [The First Detection of Sub-Populations in the Delay-Time Distribution of Binary Black Holes in GWTC-4 of LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02318)
*Shaunak Padhyegurjar,Suvodip Mukherjee*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究首次从LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次引力波目录（GWTC-4）中测量了双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）的延迟时间分布（delay-time distribution）与致密天体源性质之间的关联，识别出三个具有不同并合率行为的子种群，并发现高质量源（>45 M☉）的延迟时间分布显著依赖于质量比（mass-ratio）和自旋（spin），从而否定了所有引力波探测到的BBH具有统一并合率的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同形成通道的双黑洞会在延迟时间分布与源性质（如质量、质量比、自旋等）之间留下关联印记。检测这种潜在关联有助于揭示BBH的形成通道与演化历史，但此前尚未有相关测量。

Method: 基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次引力波目录（GWTC-4）的数据，通过对延迟时间分布与致密天体源性质之间的相关性进行分析，识别出三个具有不同并合率行为的子种群。

Result: 质量大于45 M☉的引力波源的延迟时间分布与质量较小的源显著不同，且强烈依赖于质量比和自旋：接近相等质量和接近零有效自旋的源具有更长的延迟时间。三个子种群在红移z=0处的并合率在0.6–12 Gpc⁻³ yr⁻¹之间变化。

Conclusion: 研究结果排除了所有引力波探测到的双黑洞具有统一并合率的可能性，证实了延迟时间分布与源性质之间存在依赖关系，表明至少存在三个与源性质相关的并合率子种群。

Abstract: The imprint of different formation channels of binary black holes (BBHs) is encoded in the distribution of time delays between BBH mergers and the formation of their progenitor stars, along with their source properties such as component mass, mass-ratio, spin, and more. This makes it possible for the presence of a potential correlation between the delay-time distribution and compact-object source properties. We report the first measurement of this inevitable signature from the fourth gravitational wave (GW) catalog (GWTC-4) of LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA and identified three sub-populations that show distinct merger rate behavior as a consequence of this. We find that the delay-time distribution of the sources above a mass of $45$ M$_\odot$ is significantly different from the ones below and exhibits strong dependence on the mass-ratio and spin, indicating that GW sources close to equal masses and close to zero effective spin are more delayed in comparison to the values otherwise. Our analysis identifies the presence of at least three source property dependent sub-population of merger rates with the merger rate at redshift $z=0$ varying from $\sim 0.6- 12$ Gpc$^{-3}$ yr$^{-1}$ for the three different sub-populations and hence rule out a Universal merger rate for all the BBHs detected using GW.

### [217] [Weyl-type theorems in Galilei and Carroll geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00799)
*Philip K. Schwartz,James Read,Quentin Vigneron*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推广了Weyl经典定理——Weyl度量由共形结构（conformal structure）和射影结构（projective structure）唯一确定——到Galilei与Carroll几何中的共形结构，这些几何分别对应洛伦兹几何的“非相对论性”（non-relativistic）和“超相对论性”（ultra-relativistic）极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Weyl在1921年证明了伪黎曼度规（pseudo-Riemannian metric）的经典定理，表明Weyl度量可由其共形结构和射影结构唯一确定。本文旨在将这一结果推广到Galilei几何和Carroll几何中适当定义的共形结构，这两类几何分别对应于洛伦兹几何（Lorentzian geometry）的非相对论极限和超相对论极限。

Method: 本文采用对称性分析方法，在Galilei几何和Carroll几何框架下定义合适的共形结构概念，并研究其与射影结构之间的唯一确定性关系，类似于Weyl定理中伪黎曼情形的论证思路。

Result: 对于Galilei几何和Carroll几何中适当定义的共形结构，得到了与Weyl定理类似的结果，即无挠线性联络（torsion-free linear connection）在相容于共形结构的意义下可由其射影结构唯一确定。

Conclusion: Weyl关于共形结构与射影结构唯一确定度量的经典定理可以自然推广到非相对论性和超相对论性极限下的时空几何，表明该结果在更广泛的几何框架中仍成立。

Abstract: A classic theorem of Weyl (1921) states that a Weyl metric -- a natural generalisation of a pseudo-Riemannian metric -- is uniquely determined by its conformal and projective structures (i.e. by its conformal structure and its set of unparametrised geodesics). An equivalent formulation of Weyl's result is that a torsion-free linear connection compatible with a pseudo-Riemannian conformal structure is uniquely determined by its projective structure. We discuss analogous results for suitably defined notions of conformal structure for Galilei and Carroll geometry, i.e. for spacetime geometries arising as the `non-relativistic' and `ultra-relativistic' limits of Lorentzian geometry.

</details>


### [218] [The 2D Smorodinsky--Winternitz II system and the Laguerre--Heun algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00903)
*Vutha Vichea Chea,Luc Vinet,Alexei Zhedanov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文确定了二维Smorodinsky–Winternitz II系统的二次对称代数（quadratic symmetry algebra）与一类具有Laguerre型合流Heun代数（Laguerre-type confluent Heun algebra）之间的等价关系。该系统在笛卡尔坐标和抛物坐标下均可分离，其互补笛卡尔分离算子为Laguerre型，抛物积分作为其代数Heun伙伴，共同构成超可积（superintegrable）的Laguerre–Heun代数实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究目的是揭示二维Smorodinsky–Winternitz II系统的对称性代数结构，并阐明其与特殊函数（Laguerre型合流Heun代数）之间的内在联系。

Method: 通过分析该系统在笛卡尔坐标和抛物坐标下的可分离性，识别互补分离算子Y（Laguerre型）与抛物积分W（代数Heun伙伴），并利用对易关系定义二次对称代数，其中H为中心元素（central element）。

Result: 推导出二次对称代数的定义对易关系：[Y,Z]=16ω²W−2bY和[W,Z]=6Y²−4HY+2bW+8ω²(1−c²)，其中Z=[Y,W]。这一代数结构直接对应超可积的Laguerre–Heun代数实现。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了二维Smorodinsky–Winternitz II系统的对称代数与Laguerre–Heun代数之间的精确对应，为超可积系统与特殊函数理论的交叉提供了新的代数框架。

Abstract: We identify the quadratic symmetry algebra of the two-dimensional Smorodinsky--Winternitz II system with a Laguerre-type confluent Heun algebra. The system is separable in Cartesian and parabolic coordinates. The complementary Cartesian separation operator \[
  Y=\partial_y^2-ω^2y^2+\frac{1/4-c^2}{y^2} \] is of Laguerre type, while the parabolic integral \(W=L_2\) is its algebraic Heun partner. With \(Z=[Y,W]\), the defining relations are \[
  [Y,Z]=16ω^2W-2bY,\qquad
  [W,Z]=6Y^2-4HY+2bW+8ω^2(1-c^2), \] where \(H\) is central. This gives a direct superintegrable realization of the Laguerre--Heun algebra.

</details>


### [219] [A first-order formulation for axisymmetric Willmore surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01001)
*Z. C. Tu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入两个独立的第一积分（first integrals），将轴对称Willmore曲面（axisymmetric Willmore surfaces）的控制方程约化为一阶常微分方程，并给出了生成曲线切角ψ与旋转轴距离ρ之间的解析表达式，从而为旋转Willmore曲面提供了分类框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Willmore曲面在微分几何和变分问题中具有重要地位，但轴对称情形下的方程通常为高阶非线性常微分方程，求解和分类困难。作者试图通过第一积分方法降低方程阶数，简化分析并促进曲面分类。

Method: 作者从轴对称Willmore曲面出发，利用两个独立的第一积分（first integrals）组合，推导出生成曲线的切角ψ满足的一阶常微分方程。该方程以距离ρ（距旋转轴的距离）和Ψ=sinψ为变量，包含两个积分常数C₁和C₂。

Result: 得到了一个关于Ψ和ρ的一阶常微分方程，该方程将原始的轴对称Willmore方程（axisymmetric Willmore equation）降阶为一阶形式。球面（sphere）和克利福德环面（Clifford torus）作为特例被验证，证实了该公式的正确性。

Conclusion: 该一阶形式为Willmore旋转曲面（Willmore surfaces of revolution）提供了一个便捷的分类方案，能够系统地区分和构造不同类型的轴对称Willmore曲面。

Abstract: We show that axisymmetric Willmore surfaces admit a first-order formulation obtained by combining two independent first integrals. If $ρ$ denotes the distance from the axis of revolution and $Ψ=\sinψ$, where $ψ$ is the tangent angle of the generating curve, then the profile satisfies \begin{equation*} \frac{\left[Ψ(ρΨ'-Ψ)^2+2(ρΨ'-Ψ)+2C_1ρ\right]^2}{1-Ψ^2} +\left[(ρΨ'-Ψ)^2-2\right]^2=C_2, \end{equation*} where $C_1$ and $C_2$ are constants of integration and the prime denotes differentiation with respect to $ρ$. This equation reduces the axisymmetric Willmore equation to a first-order ordinary differential equation and provides a convenient classification scheme for Willmore surfaces of revolution. The sphere and the Clifford torus are discussed as elementary checks of the formulation.

</details>

Method: 回顾余伴随轨道方法（coadjoint orbit method）及其在自旋相对论性粒子中的应用；陈述并证明两个关键定理，用于为预量子流形赋予辛结构与接触结构；基于此推导狄拉克方程与概率流守恒；利用卡鲁扎-克莱因理论系统构造电荷共轭（charge conjugation）、宇称变换（parity transformation）和时间反演（time reversal）对称性。

Conclusion: 通过严格证明关键定理，补充了Souriau几何量子化框架中的理论空白，并为相对论性自旋粒子提供了更系统的对称性构造方案。

Abstract: The aim of this paper is to revisit, in Souriau's book "Structure of Dynamical Systems", the chapter devoted to the geometric quantization where the justifications of important results and formulae are not given and are difficult to prove. After recalling the coadjoint orbit method and its application to the relativistic particle with spin, we state and prove two keystone theorems that allow to equip its prequantum manifold with the symplectic and contact structures. We apply them to the relativistic particle with spin 1/2, leading to the Dirac equation and the conservation of the probability current. We propose also an identity of conservation of the spin current and, invoking the Kaluza-Klein theory, a systematic construction of the symmetries of charge conjugation, parity transformation and time reversal which seems to us more convenient and readable than that of the classical presentations.

### [221] [The Schwinger-Dyson equations for random fuzzy geometries coupled to matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01343)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从(0,1)型随机模糊几何（random fuzzy geometries）与费米子或玻色子耦合的矩阵积分出发，研究其Schwinger-Dyson方程和鞍点方程，以理解此类双迹厄米矩阵系综（bi-tracial Hermitian matrix ensembles）的解析性质。

Method: 采用复分析（complex analytic）技术从鞍点方程（saddle point equation）推导Schwinger-Dyson方程；对任意势能（包括玻色子或费米子贡献）进行迭代求解；在高斯模型情形下，分别针对单玻色子和单费米子情况，用椭圆积分（elliptic integrals）严格推导自由能和第一矩公式。

Result: 对于包含玻色子或费米子贡献的任意势能，Schwinger-Dyson方程可通过迭代求解；高斯模型中，单玻色子和单费米子情形的自由能和第一矩均可用椭圆积分（elliptic integrals）严格表达；玻色子情形的解与Hoppe模型和三色模型（three-colour model）密切相关。

Conclusion: 本研究为(0,1)型随机模糊几何耦合系统的矩阵积分提供了系统的解析框架，并揭示了玻色子情形与已知随机矩阵模型之间的深层联系。

Abstract: In this work we study the Schwinger-Dyson equations and saddle point equations of matrix integrals that come from type $(0,1)$ random fuzzy geometries coupled to fermions or bosons. Such random fuzzy geometries are bi-tracial Hermitian matrix ensembles with a determinant contribution in the integrand. We derive the Schwinger-Dyson equations using complex analytic techniques from the saddle point equation. For arbitrary potentials with either bosonic or fermionic contributions, their Schwinger-Dyson equations can be solved iteratively. For both the Gaussian models with either one boson or fermion we rigorously derive the formula for the free energy and first moment in terms of elliptic integrals. In the bosonic case this solution is closely related to the Hoppe model and the three-colour model.

Abstract: We study the exact spectrum of the XX spin chain with constrained non-diagonal boundary fields, which can be analyzed by solving the associated Bethe Ansatz equations. Based on numerical observations, we analyze the Bethe root configurations for the ground state and the first excited state. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将Deift–Zhou非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest-descent method）应用于关联的Riemann–Hilbert问题（Riemann–Hilbert problem, RH problem）；通过局域Painlevé XXXIV参数化（Painlevé XXXIV parametrix）处理临界区域中驻相点与分支切割端点的碰撞；将离散谱（呼吸子（breathers））纳入渐近分析框架。

Result: 得到了解在临界区域中一致成立的长时渐近展开，误差阶为$\mathcal{O}(t^{-1/2})$；首项包含有限亏格代数-几何背景以及呼吸子（breathers），且呼吸子的参数受到背景解的缓慢调制。

Abstract: We investigate the Cauchy problem for the focusing modified Korteweg--de Vries (mKdV) equation with finite-genus algebro-geometric quasi-periodic initial data. By applying the nonlinear steepest-descent method of Deift--Zhou to the associated Riemann--Hilbert (RH) problem, we derive the long-time asymptotics of the solution in the critical regime where complex stationary phase points coalesce with the endpoints of the finite-genus branch cuts. The collision is resolved via a local Painlevé XXXIV parametrix, and the discrete spectrum (breathers) is incorporated into the analysis. The resulting expansion is valid uniformly up to an error of order $\mathcal{O}(t^{-1/2})$. In this critical region, the leading-order term comprises the finite-genus algebro-geometric background together with breathers, whose parameters are slowly modulated by the background solution.

### [225] [Higher-Rank Orthogonal Twists, APS Boundary Conditions, and $O(2)$-Equivariant Spectral Flow on a Warped Cylinder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02186)
*Taro Kimura,Sanchita Sharma*

Main category: math-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对具有O(2)对称性的Dirac算子，传统整值谱流（integer-valued spectral flow）无法捕捉完整的表示论信息。本文旨在建立取值于实表示环$RO(O(2))$的谱流公式，从而更精细地刻画等变谱流（equivariant spectral flow）的结构。

Method: 在配备固定可容许正规化APS边值条件的有穷翘曲圆柱上研究$O(2)$-等变谱流。将扭转丛复化并对角化正交扭转后，Dirac方程分解为标量Fourier模径向方程，包含运动旋转块和静止中性块。将共轭块和反射配对块重组后，交叉贡献定义实$RO(O(2))$-类，并在标准自伴Fredholm、端点可逆性和正则交叉假设下，通过组装各分离块的局部交叉贡献得到最终公式。

Result: 得到了$RO(O(2))$-值谱流（spectral flow）的显式分块公式，该公式在标准假设和固定中性区约定下成立。讨论了秩三情形，包括固定中性区的作用以及相应的端点$\eta$/APS指标解释。

Conclusion: 该公式细化了普通整值谱流，并明确展示了维数映射$RO(O(2))\to\mathbb Z$如何丢失表示论信息。这为具有O(2)对称性的Dirac算子的谱流分析提供了更丰富的代数拓扑工具。

Abstract: We study $O(2)$-equivariant spectral flow for Dirac operators on a finite warped cylinder equipped with fixed admissible regularized APS boundary conditions. The twisting bundle is a real higher-rank orthogonal bundle, and reflection symmetry is implemented by a fiber involution. After complexifying the twisting bundle and diagonalizing the orthogonal twist, the Dirac equation decomposes into a scalar Fourier-mode radial equation, with moving rotating blocks and stationary neutral blocks. After regrouping conjugate and reflection-paired blocks, the crossing contributions define real $RO(O(2))$-classes. Consequently, we obtain an explicit blockwise formula for the $RO(O(2))$-valued spectral flow of the resulting regularized APS family. Under the standard self-adjoint Fredholm, endpoint-invertibility, and regular-crossing hypotheses, together with a fixed neutral-sector convention, this formula is obtained by assembling the local crossing contributions of the separated blocks. It refines ordinary integer-valued spectral flow and shows explicitly how the dimension map $RO(O(2))\to\mathbb Z$ loses representation-theoretic information. We also discuss the rank-three case, including the role of the fixed neutral sector, and the corresponding endpoint $η$/APS index interpretation.

### [226] [Exponential thermalisation of viscous fluids on negatively curved manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02286)
*Samuel L. Braunstein,Zhi-Wei Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在严格负Ricci曲率的紧致黎曼流形上建立了随机Navier-Stokes方程，通过拓扑方法（Poincaré引理）从耗散算子唯一确定涨落-耗散关系，证明了谱截断系统的唯一平稳分布是Gibbs测度（吉布斯测度），且以指数速度收敛到平衡态，收敛速率受曲率控制；在负曲率空间中，速度-速度关联函数呈指数衰减，区别于平坦空间的代数衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性不可压缩Navier-Stokes方程在物理上是不完备的：任何有限温度的粘性流体必须包含热涨落（thermal fluctuation），且其形式由涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）决定。作者旨在将这一物理完备化推广到负曲率流形上，并建立严格的统计力学基础。

Method: 在严格负Ricci曲率的紧致黎曼流形上，利用运动学选择的变形拉普拉斯算子（deformation Laplacian）构造随机Navier-Stokes方程；通过Poincaré引理（Poincaré lemma）这一拓扑论证，从粘性算子唯一导出噪声项，从而确定涨落-耗散关系。对谱截断系统（spectrally truncated system）进行严谨分析。

Result: 谱截断系统的唯一平稳分布是Gibbs测度（Gaussian in mode amplitudes），非线性对流项保持能量；收敛到平衡态的速率至少为$2νλ_\Def$，其中$λ_\Def$为变形拉普拉斯算子的谱隙（spectral gap）。当$\Ric \leq -κ^2 g$时，谱隙满足$λ_\Def \geq κ^2$，且与区域体积无关。平衡态速度-速度关联函数在测地距离（geodesic distance）上呈指数衰减，而平坦空间为代数衰减。

Conclusion: 该工作为负曲率流形上的粘性流体提供了严格的统计力学基础，阐明了流形几何不仅控制确定性动力学，还控制热平衡的趋近过程。平坦空间对应的热化率（thermalisation rate）在无穷体积极限下趋于零，凸显了负曲率的独特作用。

Abstract: The deterministic incompressible Navier-Stokes equations are physically incomplete: any viscous fluid at finite temperature must exhibit thermal fluctuations whose form is dictated by the fluctuation-dissipation relation. We formulate the stochastic Navier-Stokes equations with the kinematically selected deformation Laplacian on compact Riemannian manifolds with strictly negative Ricci curvature. The fluctuation-dissipation relation, derived from a topological (Poincaré lemma) argument, uniquely determines the noise from the viscous operator. For the spectrally truncated system, we prove that the unique stationary distribution is the Gibbs measure (Gaussian in the mode amplitudes, because the nonlinear convective terms preserve energy), and that convergence to equilibrium is exponentially fast with rate at least $2νλ_\Def$, where $ν$ is the kinematic viscosity and $λ_\Def$ is the spectral gap of the deformation Laplacian. The spectral gap satisfies $λ_\Def \geq κ^2$ when $\Ric \leq -κ^2 g$, and is independent of the volume of the domain. On flat space, the analogous thermalisation rate vanishes in the infinite-volume limit. The equilibrium velocity-velocity correlation function decays exponentially in geodesic distance, in contrast to the algebraic decay on flat space. These results provide a rigorous statistical-mechanical foundation for viscous fluids on negatively curved manifolds and illustrate how the geometry of the domain controls not only the deterministic dynamics but also the approach to thermal equilibrium.

</details>


### [227] [There Are No Dirac Mass Terms with de Sitter Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02477)
*Craig McRae*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在德西特群（de Sitter group）的旋量表示（spinor representation）中，满足宇称算符（parity operator）和时间反演算符（time reversal operator）必要性质的唯一算子必然导致费米子自耦合（fermion self-couplings）为宇称奇（parity odd），从而排除了任何德西特对称的自旋-1/2费米子理论中标准的狄拉克质量项（Dirac mass term）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 洛伦兹正交群（Lorentzian orthogonal groups）的表示论中，宇称算符 $\mathcal{P}$ 与时间反演算符 $\mathcal{T}$ 分别被实现为线性（linear）与反线性（anti-linear）算符，这是经典结论（Wigner, 1932）。本文旨在检验这一结论在德西特群旋量表示框架下是否仍然成立，并探讨其对费米子质量项的影响。

Method: 作者在德西特群的旋量表示中，系统地考察了满足宇称算符和时间反演算符所需性质的算符结构，并分析这些算符对费米子自耦合项形式的约束。

Result: 满足这些性质的唯一算符必然使得费米子自耦合项为宇称奇，即无法构造宇称偶（parity even）的自耦合项。这意味着在德西特对称的自旋-1/2费米子理论中，标准的狄拉克质量项（通常为宇称偶）被排除。

Conclusion: 在德西特对称框架下，自旋-1/2费米子的理论不允许存在标准的狄拉克质量项，这一发现对德西特时空中的量子场论（quantum field theory）和宇宙学模型（cosmological models）具有重要约束意义。

Abstract: In the representation theory of Lorentzian orthogonal groups there are well known arguments as to why the parity operator $\mathcal{P}$ and the time reversal operator $\mathcal{T}$ should be realized as linear and anti-linear operators respectively (Wigner 1932). In this paper it is shown that the only operators satisfying the requisite properties for the spinor representation of the de Sitter group lead to fermion self-couplings which are necessarily parity odd, ruling out standard Dirac mass terms from any de Sitter symmetric theory of spin-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ fermions.

</details>

### [228] [Ergodicity for a class of stochastic Hasegawa-Mima equations with dissipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00325)
*Federico Butori,Ciro Campolina,Franco Flandoli*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究有界域中加性噪声驱动的随机耗散Hasegawa-Mima方程的遍历性（ergodicity），并利用渐近耦合技术（asymptotic coupling technique）证明了不变测度（invariant measure）的唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hasegawa-Mima方程是等离子体物理中的重要模型，探讨其随机版本的遍历性有助于理解系统长期统计行为，而遍历性质（ergodic property）是随机动力系统（stochastic dynamical system）理论中的核心问题。

Method: 采用渐近耦合技术（asymptotic coupling technique）来证明不变测度（invariant measure）的唯一性，该方法通过构造两个轨道的耦合过程并控制其渐近距离，从而推导出测度的唯一性。

Result: 在加性噪声（additive noise）扰动下，有界域中的随机耗散Hasegawa-Mima方程存在唯一的不变测度（invariant measure）。

Conclusion: 该结果表明系统具有遍历性（ergodicity），即长时间后系统的统计行为可由唯一不变测度刻画，为后续动力学分析提供了基础。

Abstract: This work deals with the ergodicity for the stochastic dissipative Hasegawa-Mima equations in a bounded domain and perturbed by additive noise. The uniqueness of the invariant measure is obtained by the asymptotic coupling technique.

</details>


### [229] [Singular central limit theorems for the spherical ensemble and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00330)
*Djalil Chafaï,David García-Zelada,Yuan Yuan Xu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了球系综（spherical ensemble）中对数格林奇点（logarithmic Green singularities）的涨落问题，发现光滑可观测量表现出索博列夫（Sobolev）或高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）的涨落，而对数奇点则在对数尺度上产生更大涨落，并在高维中渐近解耦为显式的白噪声（white-noise）极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解球系综这一二维球面随机离散化系统中，对数格林奇点（与对数势和特征多项式相关）的涨落行为，尤其是其与光滑可观测量涨落之间的尺度差异。

Method: 将球面视为二维球面（two-sphere）的随机离散化，通过分析对数格林奇点的涨落尺度及其在高维极限下的渐近行为，推导出显式的白噪声极限。

Result: 光滑可观测量呈现通常的索博列夫或高斯自由场涨落；对数奇点在对数尺度上产生更大涨落，并在高维中渐近解耦，收敛为白噪声。

Conclusion: 给出了对数势和特征多项式的精确渐近表达式，其中常数通过球面上的弦几何（chordal geometry）来描述。

Abstract: We study the fluctuations of logarithmic Green singularities in the spherical ensemble, viewed as a random discretization of the two-sphere. Smooth observables exhibit the usual Sobolev or Gaussian free field fluctuations, whereas logarithmic singularities live on a larger logarithmic scale and asymptotically decouple in high-dimension, producing an explicit white-noise limit. The result gives precise asymptotics for logarithmic potentials and characteristic polynomials, with constants expressed through chordal geometry on the sphere.

</details>


### [230] [Stationary fluctuations for an exclusion process with mass and energy conservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.01937)
*Hugo Da Cunha,Makiko Sasada*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种具有质量和能量两个守恒律（conservation laws）的排斥过程（exclusion process），旨在在相互作用粒子系统框架内模拟连续系统的关键特征。通过应用非线性涨落流体力学（NFH），研究揭示了不同参数选择下的多种普适类（universality classes），并严格证明了在适当参数下涨落场在标度极限（scaling limit）中收敛到解耦的随机Burgers方程（SBE）。证明依赖于二阶Boltzmann-Gibbs原理、谱隙估计和系综等价性，并给出了宏观流雅可比矩阵可对角化的严格证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多物种过程仅守恒粒子数，难以模拟具有质量和能量双重守恒的连续系统。本文旨在构建一个具有两个守恒律的排斥过程，以在相互作用粒子系统框架内更真实地反映如耦合振子（interacting oscillators）等连续系统的本质特征。

Method: 采用非线性涨落流体力学（nonlinear fluctuating hydrodynamics, NFH）分析模型在不同参数下的普适类；利用二阶Boltzmann-Gibbs原理（second-order Boltzmann-Gibbs principle）、谱隙估计（spectral gap estimate）和系综等价性（equivalence of ensembles）严格证明标度极限下的收敛性；并给出宏观流雅可比矩阵（Jacobian matrix）在具有相异实特征值时可对角化的数学证明。

Result: 模型在适当参数选择下，涨落场在标度极限中严格收敛到解耦的随机Burgers方程（stochastic Burgers equations, SBE）。此外，严格证明了多组分系统中宏观流雅可比矩阵在特征值相异实数的条件下的可对角化性，即使特征向量无法显式计算。

Conclusion: 该工作为具有多个守恒律的相互作用粒子系统的涨落分析提供了严格的数学基础，特别是为广泛物理文献中通常假设的雅可比矩阵对角化性质给出了严谨证明，从而将这类模型的分析建立在更坚实的数学框架之上。

Abstract: We introduce a novel exclusion process with two conservation laws, mass and energy, designed to mimic the essential features of continuous systems like interacting oscillators within the framework of interacting particle systems. This distinguishes our model from conventional multi-species processes where only particle numbers are conserved. As a basis for our fluctuation analysis, we first show that applying nonlinear fluctuating hydrodynamics (NFH) to this model reveals a wide variety of universality classes depending on the parameter choices. The main objective of this work is to study the stationary fluctuations of these conserved quantities. For a suitable choice of parameters, we rigorously show that the fluctuation fields converge to uncoupled stochastic Burgers equations (SBE) in the scaling limit. The proof relies on the second-order Boltzmann-Gibbs principle that we establish for this model, along with the spectral gap estimate and the equivalence of ensembles. Of independent interest is our general proof of the diagonalizability of the Jacobian matrix for the macroscopic current with distinct real eigenvalues. While this property is often taken as given in the physics literature, we establish it rigorously for multi-component systems even when the eigenvectors cannot be explicitly computed, offering a firm mathematical foundation for a broad class of models.

</details>

### [231] [Proton High-Order Cumulants in Au+Au Collisions at High Baryon Density from JAM with a Centrality-Independent Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00786)
*Yongcong Xu,Zhaohui Wang,Yu Zhang,Xiaofeng Luo*

Main category: physics.data-an

TL;DR: 本文基于JAM模型，利用新提出的中心度无关本征累积量分析框架（CIGAR）系统分析了Au+Au碰撞中质子数分布的高阶累积量，有效消除了初始体积涨落，并与传统CBWC方法进行了对比，为高重子密度区域QCD临界点搜索提供了非临界动力学基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高重子密度区域中守恒量（如净重子数、净电荷、净奇异数）的事件逐事件高阶累积量（higher-order cumulants）被广泛用于实验搜寻QCD临界点（QCD critical point），但传统方法受初始体积涨落（volume fluctuations）影响，需发展更精确的分析框架以提供可靠的动力学基准。

Method: 使用JAM模型模拟Au+Au碰撞，能区为$\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}} = 3.2, 3.5, 3.9, 4.5$ GeV；采用新方法CIGAR（即中心度无关本征累积量分析框架，Centrality-Independent Genuine Cumulant Analysis fRamework）计算累积量（cumulants）、阶乘累积量（factorial cumulants）及其比值，并与传统中心度箱宽修正（CBWC, Centrality Bin Width Correction）方法进行全面比较；此外系统考察了旁观者（spectators）对累积量的影响。

Result: CIGAR方法有效消除了初始体积涨落，给出了与CBWC方法不同的累积量结果；旁观者对累积量的影响被系统量化；所得结果为高重子密度区域提供了动力学非临界基线（dynamic non-critical baseline）。

Conclusion: CIGAR方法在高重子密度区域为QCD临界点搜寻提供了优于传统方法的非临界动力学基准，有助于未来实验数据与理论模型的精确对比。

Abstract: The event-by-event higher-order cumulants of conserved quantities such as net-baryon, net-electric charge, and net-strangeness in heavy-ion collisions have been extensively utilized in experimental searches for the QCD critical point, notably in the RHIC-STAR experiment. In this study, we conduct a systematic analysis of higher-order cumulants of proton number distributions in Au+Au collisions at center-of-mass energies of $\sqrt{s_{\rm NN}} = 3.2$, $3.5$, $3.9$, and $4.5$ GeV using the JAM model. We calculate cumulants, factorial cumulants, and their ratios using a novel method, Centrality-Independent Genuine Cumulant Analysis fRamework (CIGAR), which effectively eliminates initial volume fluctuations. We comprehensively compare the CIGAR method with the traditional Centrality Bin Width Correction (CBWC) method. In addition, the effect of spectators on cumulant is systematically investigated. Our results provide a dynamic non-critical baseline in the high-baryon-density regime which is crucial for QCD critical point searches in heavy-ion collisions.

</details>

### [232] [Dependence of two-particle azimuthal correlations on the forward rapidity gap width in pPb collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 8.16 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00171)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 该论文通过测量质子-铅（pPb）碰撞中方位角分布的傅里叶系数（V_{nΔ}），探讨了小系统（如pPb、pp、电子-正电子、光子-质子碰撞）中是否也存在类似于相对论性重离子碰撞中的集体流（collective flow）现象。研究基于无质子方向粒子的pPb事件样本，排除了光子-铅（γPb）与波梅子-铅（IPb）相互作用的干扰，并通过前向快度间隙宽度、粒子横向动量及多重度等变量系统测量V_{nΔ}，最终与已有数据和现代事件生成器进行对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性重离子碰撞中观测到的集体流（collective flow）被认为是夸克-胶子等离子体（quark gluon plasma）流体行为的标志。然而，在pPb、pp等小系统碰撞中同样观测到非零傅里叶系数（V_{nΔ}），这引发了对集体流是否存在的根本性质疑。本工作的动机是通过测量pPb碰撞中无质子方向粒子的事件（富集γPb和IPb相互作用）的V_{nΔ}，来检验小系统中是否存在与重离子碰撞类似的集体流。

Method: 分析基于质心系能量（√s_NN）为8.16 TeV的质子-铅（pPb）碰撞事件样本。通过要求质子方向区域无粒子来筛选富集光子-铅（γPb）和波梅子-铅（IPb）相互作用的事件。测量随前向快度间隙宽度、粒子横向动量（transverse momentum）及事件多重度（multiplicity）变化的V_{nΔ}值，并与pp、pPb、γp+IPp碰撞的已有测量及现代事件生成器（event generators）结果进行比较。

Result: 给出了在pPb碰撞的无质子方向粒子事件样本中，V_{nΔ}随前向快度间隙宽度、粒子横向动量和多重度的系统测量结果。并将这些结果与pp、pPb及γp+IPp碰撞的测量数据以及现代事件生成器的模拟结果进行了对比。

Conclusion: 通过对pPb碰撞中特殊事件样本的V_{nΔ}测量及与多种碰撞系统和事件生成器的对比，为小系统中是否存在集体流以及其起源提供了新的实验约束，有助于进一步区分集体流机制与其他可能产生类似方位角关联的物理过程。

Abstract: One of the most striking features of relativistic heavy ion collisions is the presence of collective flow of thousands of produced particles. This flow can be characterized by the Fourier coefficients (${V_{nΔ}}$) of the azimuthal angular distributions of charged particles, and its existence can be explained by the formation of a quark gluon plasma, which behaves as a fluid. Surprisingly, the angular distributions of particles from very small systems such as proton-lead (pPb), proton-proton (pp), electron-positron, and photon-proton ($γ$p) collisions also exhibit non-zero Fourier coefficients, raising the question of whether collective flow is present. This paper presents measurements of $V_{nΔ}$ from a sample of pPb events at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 8.16 TeV that are enriched in photon-lead ($γ$Pb) and pomeron-lead ($\mathrm{\!I\!P}$Pb) interactions by requiring no particles in the proton-going region. Measurements are made as a function of the forward rapidity gap width (the rapidity range in which no particles are found), the transverse momentum of the particles, and the multiplicity of particles in the event. The results are compared to previous measurements of pp, pPb, and $γ$p+$\mathrm{\!I\!P}$p events as well as modern event generators.

</details>


### [233] [Investigation of the onset of deconfinement with the NA61/SHINE experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00597)
*A. Bazgir*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于NA61/SHINE固定靶实验对高能重离子碰撞中强相互作用物质的相变进行系统研究，通过改变束流动量和碰撞系统尺寸进行二维扫描，重点利用奇异熵比（strangeness-to-entropy ratio）这一观测量探讨去禁闭（deconfinement）的起始点，并结合SMES理论模型与实验数据对比，深化对QCD相图的理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能重离子碰撞是研究强相互作用物质相变的独特框架。NA61/SHINE实验旨在系统探索量子色动力学相图（QCD phase diagram），重点关注去禁闭转变——即从强子物质（hadronic matter）到夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma, QGP）的相变过程。

Method: 实验采用固定靶（fixed-target）装置，通过二维扫描方式改变束流动量（13A至150/158A GeV/c）和碰撞系统大小（p+p、p+Pb、Be+Be、Ar+Sc、Xe+La、Pb+Pb、O+O），以分析碰撞动力学随系统尺寸和能量的演化，并采用早期阶段统计模型（Statistical Model of the Early Stage, SMES）解释观测结果。

Result: 根据SMES理论预测，奇异熵比（strangeness-to-entropy ratio）在SPS能量范围内应呈现角状结构（horn-like structure），其中熵正比于π介子产额（pion yields）。文章将NA61/SHINE的最新结果与全球其他实验数据进行对比，从而验证该理论预测。

Conclusion: 本文通过对SMES理论框架及其假设的讨论，并结合NA61/SHINE与其它实验数据的比较，为理解QCD相变提供了更深层次的见解。

Abstract: High-energy heavy-ion collisions provide a unique framework for studying the phase transition of strongly interacting matter. The NA61/SHINE experiment, located in the North Area of CERN's SPS, is a fixed-target facility designed to perform a systematic exploration of the QCD phase diagram. This is achieved through a two-dimensional scan that varies both the beam momentum (from 13A to 150/158A GeV/c) and the size of the colliding systems (p+p, p+Pb, Be+Be, Ar+Sc, Xe+La, Pb+Pb, O+O). Such a wide scan enables detailed studies of how collision dynamics evolve with system size and energy. A central objective of the NA61/SHINE research program is to investigate the onset of deconfinement - the transition from hadronic matter to a quark-gluon plasma (QGP) - by analyzing observables such as the strangeness-to-entropy ratio, where entropy is proportional to pion yields. According to the Statistical Model of the Early Stage (SMES), this ratio is expected to exhibit a horn-like structure within the SPS energy range. This article discusses the theoretical framework of the SMES, its assumptions, and compares recent NA61/SHINE results with other experimental data worldwide, contributing to a deeper understanding of the QCD phase transition.

### [234] [Measurements of jet quenching with semi-inclusive hadron-jet correlations in Ru+Ru and Zr+Zr collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}=200$ GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.00973)
*STAR Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: STAR实验在RHIC上测量了200 GeV的Ru+Ru和Zr+Zr碰撞中，由高横动量带电强子触发的带电粒子喷注的半包容产额，观测到中心碰撞中喷注产额的压制现象，表明夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）导致的喷注淬火（jet quenching）效应及喷注内展宽（intra-jet broadening）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用中等质量原子核（intermediate-mass beams）的碰撞系统，研究喷注淬火效应的空间和时间维度特性，弥补此前仅在较小或较大碰撞系统中进行类似测量的不足。

Method: 在质心系能量为200 GeV的Ru+Ru和Zr+Zr碰撞中，基于中心度（centrality）分类，测量高横动量带电强子触发的半包容带电粒子喷注的反冲产额（recoil yield），并将中心碰撞与边缘碰撞的触发归一化产额进行比较，以量化喷注淬火效应。

Result: 中心碰撞中观测到反冲产额被压制，表明介质诱导的部分子能量损失（medium-induced partonic energy loss）；小分辨率参数与大分辨率参数的喷注产额比值在中心碰撞中相对边缘碰撞被压制，显示出介质诱导的喷注内展宽特征。

Conclusion: 中等质量碰撞系统的测量结果与较小和较大碰撞系统中的类似测量进行了比较，为喷注淬火的空间和时间特性提供了独特的理解。

Abstract: The STAR experiment at RHIC reports measurements of the semi-inclusive yield of charged-particle jets recoiling from high transverse momentum charged-hadron triggers in centrality-selected Ru+Ru and Zr+Zr collisions at the nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energy of 200 GeV. The effects of jet quenching, arising from the interaction of jets with the quark-gluon plasma, are quantified by comparing trigger-normalized recoil yields in central and peripheral collisions. Such measurements with intermediate-mass beams provide unique insight into spatial and temporal aspects of jet quenching. Suppression of the recoil yield in central collisions is observed, indicating medium-induced partonic energy loss due to quenching. The ratio of recoil jet yields for small and large resolution parameter is found to be suppressed in central relative to peripheral collisions, characteristic of medium-induced intra-jet broadening. The results are compared to similar measurements in smaller and larger collision systems.

### [235] [Centrality dependence of charged-hadron pseudorapidity distributions in oxygen-oxygen collisions at $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02285)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了在质心能量 $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV 的氧-氧（OO）碰撞中带电强子赝快度（pseudorapidity）分布的首次测量结果。实验数据由 LHC 上的 CMS 探测器在 2025 年采集，涵盖 $|η|$ $\lt$ 2.4 范围，并与铅-铅（PbPb）、氙-氙碰撞结果及多个蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）事件生成器和流体动力学模型预测进行了比较。流体动力学模型 TRAJECTUM 对数据描述最佳；中心 OO 碰撞的粒子密度与中心 PbPb 碰撞一致，但数据偏离简单的参与者与系统规模标度（scaling），凸显了轻离子碰撞中碰撞几何与有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前尚无氧-氧（OO）碰撞中带电强子赝快度分布的实验测量，而轻离子碰撞系统可作为研究碰撞几何与有限尺寸效应的敏感探针，因此需要首次实验数据以检验理论模型并完善对核-核碰撞系统规模标度行为的理解。

Method: 利用 CMS 探测器在 LHC 上采集的 2025 年 OO 碰撞数据，在 $|η|$ $\lt$ 2.4 范围内测量原初带电强子产额，并按中心度（centrality）进行分档；将结果与相近能量下的 PbPb、XeXe 碰撞数据以及多个蒙特卡洛事件生成器和流体动力学模型 TRAJECTUM 的预测进行对比分析。

Result: 中心区 ($|η|$ $\lt$ 0.5) 的带电强子赝快度密度为 $\langle$dN$_{\text{ch}}$/d$η\rangle$ = 41.8 $\pm$ 1.1 (syst)（全中心度积分）和 135.0 $\pm$ 4.0 (syst)（最中心事件）。TRAJECTUM 模型整体描述最优；中心 OO 碰撞的每参与核子粒子密度与中心 PbPb 碰撞一致。数据整体保持其他核-核碰撞的能量标度行为，但偏离简单的参与者与系统规模标度。

Conclusion: 氧-氧碰撞的首次赝快度分布测量表明，轻离子碰撞中的粒子产生机制与重离子碰撞存在一致性，但有限尺寸效应和碰撞几何因素不可忽略；TRAJECTUM 流体动力学模型能够较好地描述该系统的末态粒子产生。

Abstract: We report the first measurement of charged-hadron pseudorapidity ($η$) distributions in oxygen-oxygen (OO) collisions at a nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energy of $\sqrt{s_\mathrm{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV. The data were recorded by the CMS experiment at the LHC in 2025. Primary charged-hadron yields are measured in the range $|η|$ $\lt$ 2.4 as a function of centrality (the overlap of the two nuclei). The results are compared with previous measurements in lead-lead (PbPb) and xenon-xenon collisions at similar energies, as well as predictions from several Monte Carlo event generators and a hydrodynamic model. The charged-hadron pseudorapidity density in the midrapidity region ($|η|$ $\lt$ 0.5) is $\langle$dN$_{\text{ch}}$/d$η\rangle$ = 41.8 $\pm$ 1.1 (syst) integrated over centrality and 135.0 $\pm$ 4.0 (syst) for the most central (i.e., largest nuclear overlap) events. The hydrodynamic model TRAJECTUM provides the best overall description of the data, particularly in central collisions. The particle density at midrapidity divided by the number of nucleons participating in the interaction in central OO collisions is consistent with that observed in central PbPb collisions at similar collision energy. While the overall energy-scaling behavior observed in other nucleus-nucleus collisions is preserved, the data exhibit deviations from simple participant and system-size scaling, highlighting the role of collision geometry and finite-size effects in light ion collisions.

</details>
